[ॐ kāraguravē namaḥ ॐ hrīṁ śrīṁ arhaṁ namaḥ gautamasvāminē namaḥ]

[namōstu ṇaṁ śramaṇāya bhagavatē mahāvīrāya]

[śrīdhanēśvaramuniviracitam]

[surasundarīcaritram]


[p. 1]
suhasāmannapaïnnāsamayasamāraddhalōyakammassa
amaravaïvayaṇadhariō parikuḍilō kuntalakalāvō // SurSuCa.1

kannāsannē sōhaï jassa avatthāṇapatthaṇatthaṁva
cittabbhantararuddhappavēsakandappadūuvva // SurSuCa.2

ahavā. 

sōhaï jassa susaṅgayaübhayaṁsalulantakuntalakalāvā
muttī suvannavannā sakajjalaggavva dīvasihā // SurSuCa.3


[p. 2]
jassa paṇāmā pāvaï palayaṁ paürōpi vigghasaṅghāō
tassa risahassa paḍhamaṁ namāmi payapaṅkayaṁ payaō // SurSuCa.4

[caturbhiḥ kalāpakam]
ajiyāiṇō jiṇindē vandē jammaṁmi jēsimamarindā
rāgāiṇō vi sattū pañcattaṁ pāviyā samayaṁ // SurSuCa.5

jammaṇasamayāṇantarasumērusiharābhisēyasamayammi
sakkandaṇakayakuviyappannāsaṇē kayapayattassa // SurSuCa.6

rāgāivaïrisēṇavva jassa daṭṭhuṁ aṇannasāmatthaṁ
tharahariyā accatthaṁ sasilōccayasāyarā vasuhā // SurSuCa.7

nimmalakamanahaniyarō paḍibimbiyapaṇayatihuaṇō jassa
uvvahaï jāyagavvō kēvalanāṇassa samasīsiṁ // SurSuCa.8

jassa ya paṇāmamēttā nimmalakamaṇakkhapaḍiyapaḍibimbā
ēkkārasaguṇamuvalabbha appayaṁ harisiyā tiyasā // SurSuCa.9


[p. 3]
taṁ vandē jiṇayandaṁ dēvindanarindavindavandiyayaṁ
siddhatthanarindasuaṁ carimaṁ carimaṁ gaïṁ pattaṁ // SurSuCa.10

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
dujjayaaṇaṅgamāyaṅgabhaṅgasāraṅgapuṅgavasaricchē
sāsayasivasuhasahiē siddhē sirasā namaṁsāmi 11 // SurSuCa.11

duddhaṁsadhantaviddhaṁsadhīrasiddhantadēsaē dhīrē
pañcavihāyāraraē sirasā vandāmi āyariē // SurSuCa.12

visayasuhanippivāsē saṁsāracchēyakaraṇatallicchē
vandāmi uvajjhāē suttatthavisāraē sayayaṁ // SurSuCa.13

pañcamahavvayaduvvahapavvayaüvvahaṇapaccalē sirasā
gharavāsapāsamukkē sāhū savvē namaṁsāmi // SurSuCa.14

jīē kamakamalaṁ pāviūṇa pāvinti pāṇiṇō paramaṁ
nāṇaṁ annāṇā vi hu sā jayaï sarassaī dēvī // SurSuCa.15


[p. 4]
jāṇa pasāēṇa puṇa maēvi jaḍabuddhiṇā kahākaraṇē
līlāē payaṭṭijjaï, visēsaō tē gurū vandē // SurSuCa.16

iya pujjapaṇaïkaraṇappaṇāsiyāsēsavigghasaṅghāō
vōcchaṁ saṁvēgakariṁ kahaṁ tu surasundariṁ nāma // SurSuCa.17

annaṁ ca tassa kīraï paḍhamaṁ ciya patthaṇā khalajaṇassa
bīhēi kavijaṇō jassa mūsaō iva biḍālassa // SurSuCa.18

ahavā sahāvaücciya dōsaggahaṇammi vāvaḍamaṇassa
abbhatthaṇāsaēhi vi na khalassa khalattaṇaṁ galaï // SurSuCa.19

kuḍilattaṇaṁ na ujjhaï paricchiddagavēsaō ya dōjīhō
patthijjantō vi kavīhiṁ dujjaṇō sappasāricchō // SurSuCa.20

abbhatthiō vi vaṅkō kalusiyahiyaō suvittaparihīṇō
candōvva dujjaṇō iha dōsāsaṅgē payāsēi // SurSuCa.21


[p. 5]
laliē va niṭṭhurē vā kavvē dōsō khalēhiṁ ghēttavvō
uṭṭhamuhāō ahavā nīharaï na jīrayaṁ kahavi // SurSuCa.22

dujjaṇasahāē paḍiyaṁ nimmalakavvaṁ pi lahaï na païṭṭhaṁ
jalabinduvva sutattē āyasabhāṇammi pakkhittō // SurSuCa.23

āsajja dujjaṇaṁ kavijaṇassa abbhatthaṇā taō vihalā
na hu sakkararasasittōvi cayaï kaḍuyattaṇaṁ nimbō // SurSuCa.24

ahavā kahāpabandhō kīraï kiṁ dujjaṇāṇa saṅkāē?
jūyābhaēṇa parihāṇavimōyaṇaṁ handi! na hu juttaṁ // SurSuCa.25

dujjaṇaasaṁmayaṁ pi hu kuṇaï kavī kavvamēttha kimajuttaṁ?
uluyāṇamabhāsantōvi diṇayarō kiṁ na uggamaï? // SurSuCa.26

apatthiōvi suyaṇō kaīṇa kavvē guṇē payāsēi
dhavalēi jayaṁ sayalaṁ sabhāvaō cēva nisināhō // SurSuCa.27


[p. 6]
nindākārijaṇassa vi dōsaggāhī na sajjaṇō kahavi
kuṇaï suyandhaṁ vāsiṁ tacchijjantō vi malayaruhō // SurSuCa.28

annaṁ ca havaï hu virūvayampi hu kavvaṁ suyaṇāṇa saṅgamē laṭṭhaṁ
sippipuḍammi paviṭṭhaṁ jalampi muttāhalaṁ hōi // SurSuCa.29

abbhatthaṇārihāṁ jaṁ suyaṇā tō tē u patthimō iṇhiṁ
ēgaggamaṇā hōuṁ sāhijjantiṁ nisāmēha // SurSuCa.30

ghōrē aṇōrapārē saṁsārē jōṇilakkhapaürammi
aïdulahaṁ laddhūṇaṁ maṇuyattaṁ bhaviyalōēṇa // SurSuCa.31

dēvindacandanāgindavindamaṇuindavandiyajiṇēhiṁ
vajjariē ujjamiuṁ juttaṁ dhammammi suddhammi // SurSuCa.32

sō antarārivijaē rōgaddōsā ya antarā sattū
tavvijae cciya sōkkhaṁ tēhiṁ jiyāṇaṁ puṇō dukkhaṁ // SurSuCa.33


[p. 7]
ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē rāgaddēsāṇugayā jīvā pāvēnti vivihadukkhāiṁ
tamhā tavvijae cciya vibuhēhiṁ hōi jaïyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.34

ēyatthasāhaṇaparā sōlasaparicchēyasaṅgayā laliyā
pāiyagāhāhiṁ kahā kīraï surasundarīnāmā // SurSuCa.35

abuhajaṇabōhaṇaṁ taha dukkahalōyāṇa cittarañjaṇayaṁ
jugavaṁ ṇō sakkijjaï kavīhiṁ ubhayampi kāūṇa // SurSuCa.36

jaō sālaṅkārēṇa ghaṇakkharēṇa rañjijjaē jaṇō vibuhō
payaḍatthalaliyakavvaṁ abuhāṇaṁ bōhaṇaṁ kuṇaï // SurSuCa.37

dōṇha vi ēkkavaēcciya sakkijjaï rañjaṇaṁ na kāūṇaṁ
ēkkaṁ gēṇhantāṇaṁ avassa kira nāsaē bīyaṁ // SurSuCa.38

niyagurukamappasāyā kāvi hu sattī u jaïvi maha atthi
uvamāsilēsarūpagavaṇṇagabahulammi kavvammi // SurSuCa.39


[p. 8]
tahavi hu tayaṁ na kīraï asamatthaṁ patthuammi jaṁ atthē
tō abuhabōhaṇatthaṁ payaḍatthā kīraē ēsā // SurSuCa.40

kiñca sīsiṇimayahariyāē gurubhagiṇīē alandhavayaṇāē
sirikallāṇamaīē pavattiṇīē u vayaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.41

pāraddhā jaṁ ēsā kavittagavvēṇa nō maē tēṇa
kīraïuttāṇatthā pāiyagāhāhiṁ laliyapayā // SurSuCa.42

hu pajjattaṁ bahuṇā patthuyavigdhāvahēṇa vihalēṇa
vihavakulabāliyākayakaḍakkhavikkhēvasarisēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.43

nisuṇaha ēgaggamaṇā hōumiyāṇiṁ kahaṁ kahijjantaṁ
aḍ̣dhāijjasaēhiṁ gāhāṇaṁ kayaparicchēyaṁ // SurSuCa.44

atthēttha suvitthinnō uḍ̣dhāhōlōgamajjhayārammi
nāmēṇa tiriyalōgō vibuhāṇugaō sumēruvva // SurSuCa.45


[p. 9]
dīvō u atthi tatthavi vittharaō jōyaṇāṇa lakkhaṁ tu
jalahivalayāvagụ̄dhō jambuddīvō tti vikkhāō // SurSuCa.46

tassa ya dāhiṇabhāgē bharahaṁ nāmēṇa atthi varakhēttaṁ
vēyaḍḍhanagavarēṇaṁ duhā vihattaṁ suvitthinnaṁ // SurSuCa.47

aha dāhiṇaḍḍhabharahē gaṅgāsindhūṇa majjhayārammi
kappadumōvva dumāṇaṁ bahudēsāṇaṁ pahāṇayārō // SurSuCa.48

dhannasamiddhilapāmararāsayasaṁsaddapūriyadiyantō
avikarahamahisarāsahanāṇāvihagōhaṇāinnō // SurSuCa.49

païdiyahavahantāṇēyasāraṇīvisararēhirujjāṇō
puranagaragāmapaürō bahuriddhisamiddhasayalajaṇō // SurSuCa.50

niccaṁ pamuiyalōō nāṇāvihaücchavēhiṁ avirahiō
bhayaḍamararahiyagāmō kurutti nāmēṇa varadēsō // SurSuCa.51

[caturbhiḥ kalāpakam]

[p. 10]
aviya aṇavarayavahantāṇēyavaṇiyasatthōhavasimasayalapahō
jattha na najjaï pahi pahiṁ aḍavivasiṭhāṇayavisēsō // SurSuCa.52

annaṁ ca tammi dēsē guṇāṇa bhavaṇammi ēyamacchariyaṁ
sōarahiōvi jaṁ suṇaï jaṇavaō lōyabhaṇiyāiṁ // SurSuCa.53

aviya jattha ya gāmamahallā kararahiyā dhammavajjiyā muṇiṇō
dēsassa tassa saṁvaṇṇaṇammi kō ujjamaṁ kuṇaï? // SurSuCa.54

tatthavi ya atthi vitthinnajalahivalayāṇukāriparihāē
parapurisālaṅghāē parikkhittaṁ bhamiramayarāē // SurSuCa.55

paḍavakkhabhayuppāyaṇavisālasālēṇa parigayaṁ rammaṁ
ramaṇīyamagaratōraṇagōuradārēhiṁ parikinnaṁ // SurSuCa.56

aïnīlabahalaüvavaṇavirāyamāṇāvasāṇabhāgēhiṁ
mattālambagavakkhayajuēhiṁ varacittajuttēhiṁ // SurSuCa.57


[p. 11]
nāṇabhūmijuēhiṁ pāsāēhiṁ tusāradhavalēhiṁ
tannayaravāsijaṇajasathūhēhivva niccamaïrammaṁ // SurSuCa.58

taha avarāvaradēsāgaēṇa tannayaravāsiṇā cēva
vaṇiyakalāniuṇēṇaṁ païdiyahaṁ vaṇiyalōēṇa // SurSuCa.59

kijjantavaṇijjēhiṁ virāyamāṇaṁ aṇēgahaṭṭēhiṁ
paripūriēhiṁ antō bahumullakiyāṇagasaēhiṁ // SurSuCa.60

uttuṅgamagaratōraṇapavaṇuddhuyadhavaladhayavaḍaḍ̣dhēhiṁ
sudaṁradēvaülēhiṁ uvasōhiyasundarapaēsaṁ // SurSuCa.61

taha paṇḍupaümasaṇḍōhamaṇḍiyāṇēyagurutarasarēhiṁ
sōvāṇapantisugamāvayāravāvīsahassēhiṁ // SurSuCa.62

varatiyacaükkacaccaraārāmujjāṇadīhiyāīhiṁ
dēvāṇamavi kuṇantaṁ paē paē cittasaṁharaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.63


[p. 12]
sayalannapurapahāṇaṁ nayaraṁ sirihatthiṇāuraṁ nāma
nayaraguṇōhuvavēyaṁ saṅkāsaṁ amaranayarassa // SurSuCa.64

[daśamiḥ kulakam]
jattha ya nivasaï lōō piyaṁvaō dhammakaraṇatallicchō
dakkhinnacāyabhōgēhiṁ saṅgaō taha kalākusalō // SurSuCa.65

jattha ya purammi niccaṁ iō taō bahupaōyaṇaparēṇa
bhamirajaṇasamudaēṇaṁ dussañcārāō ratthāō // SurSuCa.66

jattha ya kōḍipaḍāyāpacchāiyasayalagayaṇamaggammi
lōō gimhadiṇēsuvi ravikaratāvaṁ na yāṇēi // SurSuCa.67

jattha ya purammi purisā gharabhittinihittamaṇimaūhēhiṁ
niccaṁ hayandhayārē gayampi rāiṁ na yāṇanti // SurSuCa.68

rammattaṇaō jassa ya palōyaṇatthaṁva āgayā dēvā
kōugavakkhittamaṇā aṇamisanayaṇattaṇaṁ pattā // SurSuCa.69


[p. 13]
dhavalaharasiharaviraïyapavaṇapahallantavējayantīō
sannanti va raviṇō sārahissa aïuccagamaṇaṭṭhā // SurSuCa.70

jattha ya purammi dīsaï pāyapahārō u raṅgabhūmīsu
daṇḍō u dhayavaḍāṇaṁ sīsacchēō juyārīṇa // SurSuCa.71

kusumāṇa sirasi bandhō sāgacchēttēsu jīvakattaṇayā
taha paṇḍiyaparisāsu pattāṇaṁ handi! bhindaṇayā // SurSuCa.72

aha ēkko cciya dōsō guṇāṇa bhavaṇammi tammi nayarammi
niddōsasāhuṇō jaṁ sayāvi dīsanti guttiṭhiyā // SurSuCa.73

aha tammi purammi pahū pabhūyakariturayarayaṇabhaṇḍārō
jahabhaṇiyanīipālaṇaāṇandiyasayasajaṇacittō // SurSuCa.74

niyabuddhisamudaēṇaṁ vasīkayāsēsasattusantāṇō
sampūriyatthisamudayamaṇapatthiyaatthavitthārō // SurSuCa.75


[p. 14]
daḍhakạdhiṇabhuyā 'parimiyaparakkamakkantasayalapaḍivakkhō
paḍivakkhabhāmiṇīvayaṇanaliṇasaṅkōyamaṇamayaṅkō // SurSuCa.76

sūrōvva pihupayāvō sīhō iva akayaparabalāsaṅkō
uyahivva sugambhīrō candō iva jaṇamaṇāṇandō // SurSuCa.77

ruvēṇa kāmadēvō buddhiē suragurussa sāricchō
nivasaï pamōyapattō rāyā siriamarakēutti // SurSuCa.78

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
tassa ya tivaggasāraṁ rajjasiriṁ sammamaṇuhavantassa
vaccanti vāsarāi indassa va dēvalōgammi // SurSuCa.79

aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō tassa
viṇayapaṇaüttamaṅgō paḍihārō bandhulō bhaṇaī // SurSuCa.80

dēva! kusaggapurāō cittayarō cittakammapattaṭṭhō
nāmēṇa cittasēṇō samāgatō ciṭṭhaï duvārē // SurSuCa.81


[p. 15]
sō dēvapāyadaṁsaṇasuhakaṅkhī icchaē iha pavēsaṁ
ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē amhaṁ dēvāēsō pamāṇanti // SurSuCa.82

tattō raṇṇā bhaṇiyaṁ lahuṁ pavēsēhi tāhē sō vihiṇā
atthāṇammi paviṭṭhō kayaviṇaō rāiṇō puraō // SurSuCa.83

uvaviṭṭhō bhūmīē rannā bhaṇiō kuō 'si taṁ bhadda!?
kēṇa va kajjēṇa ihaṁ samāgaō maha samīvammi? // SurSuCa.84

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō kusagganayarāu āgaō dēva!
cittagarō sāisayaṁ jāṇāmi ya cittakammamahaṁ // SurSuCa.85

cittappiō ya dēvō summaï vattāsuṁ tēṇa ahamēttha
cittakalaṁ payaḍēuṁ samāgaō dēvapāsammi // SurSuCa.86

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ kērisayaṁ cittakōsalaṁ tujjha?
daṁsēhi tāva majjhaṁ ālihiyaṁ kiñci vararuvaṁ // SurSuCa.87


[p. 16]
aha tēṇa kakkhadēsammi gōviyā cittapaṭṭiyā sahasā
payaḍīkāuṁ raṇṇō samappiyā hiṭṭhavayaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.88

pasarantapayaḍapulaō rāyā pulōēi tattha ālihiyaṁ
nāṇāvannayakaliyaṁ pamāṇarēhāhiṁ suvisuddhaṁ // SurSuCa.89

ahiṇavajjōvvaṇavararuvajuttamaccantamaṇaharāgāraṁ
ahiṇavasihiṇārambhaṁ kaṇṇāē ruvayaṁ pavaraṁ // SurSuCa.90

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ naranāhō cintaï ēsō hu cittakammammi
aïkusalō jaṁ lihiyaṁ aüvvaruvaṁ imaṁ rūvaṁ // SurSuCa.91

tilōkkammivi mannē ērisarūvā na itthiyā atthi
cittakalāniuṇattā adiṭṭharūvā imā lihiyā // SurSuCa.92

jaï puṇa katthavi hōjjā ērisaruvēṇa itthiyā kannā
tīē vi saṅgamō jaï tā rajjaṁ hōjja sakayatthaṁ // SurSuCa.93


[p. 17]
ēvaṁ cintēntassa ya vammahasaragōyarammi paḍiyassa
vīsariō sē appā cittē 'vakkhittacittassa // SurSuCa.94

tattō khaṇantarāō saṁmīliyalōyaṇō amarakēū
sīhāsaṇāu paḍiō mucchāē paravasō sahasā // SurSuCa.95

hā! hā! hatti bhaṇantā atthāṇagayā samuṭṭhiyā lōyā
vīyanti vīyaṇēhiṁ sīyalasalilēṇaṁ siñcanti // SurSuCa.96

vayaṇē khivanti khippa kappūraṁ taha malēnti aṅgāiṁ
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ cittasēṇō pahasiyavayaṇō daḍhaṁ jāō // SurSuCa.97

rē! rē! kōvi hu pāvō ahimararūvēṇa āgaō ēsō
kammaṇagārī jēṇiha vimōhiō amha sāmitti // SurSuCa.98

tālēha haṇaha vandhaha ēvaṁ bhaṇantēhiṁ aṅgarakkhēhiṁ
gahiō sō hammantō ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō // SurSuCa.99


[p. 18]
bhō! bhō! bhaddā! nāhaṁ duṭṭhō tā mā muhā kayatthēha
tattō ya tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kahaṁ na duṭṭhō tumaṁ pāva!? // SurSuCa.100

kammaṇakayaṁ hi cittaṁ payaṁsiyaṁ kīsa rāiṇō tumaē?
taha mucchiyammi dēvē viyasiyavayaṇō ya kiṁ jāō? // SurSuCa.101

tā kahasu kēṇa raṇṇō vahaṇatthaṁ pēsiō tumaṁ pāva!?
tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō akkhissaṁ tumha savvampi // SurSuCa.102

rannō abbhudayatthaṁ samāgaō na uṇa duṭṭhabuddhīē
ēmāi bhaṇantōvi hu baddhō sō rāyapurisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.103

ētthantarammi rāyā gayamucchō satthacēyaṇō jāō
aha naravaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ muñcaha bhō! cittagaramēyaṁ // SurSuCa.104

ucchōḍiyabandhō sō rannā bhaṇiō ya bhadda! uvavisasu
āikkhasu maha saccaṁ kēṇa tumaṁ pēsiō ēttha? // SurSuCa.105


[p. 19]
tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō nisuṇasu naranāha! ēttha paramatthaṁ
cittagaravēsadhārī samāgaō jēṇa ahamēttha // SurSuCa.106

atthēttha kusaggapuraṁ supasiddhaṁ cēva dēvapāyāṇaṁ
nayaraguṇōhuvavēyaṁ dhaṇadhannasamiddhajaṇakaliyaṁ // SurSuCa.107

paṇaïjaṇapūriyāsō rāyā ghaṇavāhaṇotti tatthāsi
pāṇappiyā sē dēvī vasantasēṇatti nāmēṇa // SurSuCa.108

tāṇa ya puttō naravāhaṇotti nāmēṇa ukkaḍapayāvō
kamalāvaïttināmā dhūyāaccantarūvavaī // SurSuCa.109

aha annayā ya rāyā dāuṁ naravāhaṇassa niyarajjaṁ
kamalāvaī ya bhagiṇī aṇurūvavarassa dāyavvā // SurSuCa.110

iya bhaṇiūṇa puttaṁ sugurusamīvammi jāyasaṁvēgō
saṁsārucchēyakaraṁ sāmannaṁ uvagaō vihiṇā // SurSuCa.111


[p. 20]
naravāhaṇōvi rāyā rajjaṁ pālēi paṇayapaḍivakkhaṁ
ciṭṭhaï kannantēuramajjhē kamalāvaï vi suhaṁ // SurSuCa.112

ēttō ya tammi nayarē nivasaï vaṇiō u sāgarō nāma
rannō bālasavayaṁsō jiṇavayaṇē gāḍhamaṇurattō // SurSuCa.113

sirimaïnāmā bhajjā aïppiyā tassa sīlasampannā
siridattō sē puttō sirikantā tahaya duhiyatti // SurSuCa.114

sirikantā aṇudiyahaṁ vaccaī kamalāvaīē pāsammi
jāyā ya garuyapīī annōnnaṁ tāṇa dōṇhampi // SurSuCa.115

itthījaṇajōgāō gahiyāō kalāō bālabhāvēvi
sagalakalāniuṇassa u pāsammi sumittasēṇassa // SurSuCa.116

rāyaduhiyāē samayaṁ cittāīyāhi vivihakīlāhiṁ
sirikantā kīlēttā vigālasamayammi ēi gihaṁ // SurSuCa.117


[p. 21]
sirikantāē samayaṁ siṇēhasārāē rāyadhūyāē
vōlīṇō bahukālō nāṇāvihakīḍaṇarayāē // SurSuCa.118

kamasō vaḍḍhantīō tiyasāṇa vi patthaṇijjarūvāō
pattāō paḍhamajōvvaṇamaṇaṅgasiṅgāraāvāsaṁ // SurSuCa.119

aha annayā ya rāyā maïsāgarasāgarēhi sañjuttō
atthāṇamaṇḍavammī āsīṇō acchaī jāva // SurSuCa.120

niyasahiyaṇasañjuttā tāva ya kamalāvaī tahiṁ āyā
bhūsaṇapasāhiaṅgī gēnduyakīlāē kīlantī // SurSuCa.121

aha sā bhagiṇī rannā pīīē nivēsiyā niucchaṅgē
tattō daṭṭhuṁ tīē rūvaṁ taha jōvvaṇamudaggaṁ // SurSuCa.122

bhaṇiō rannā mantī maïsāgara! taïya pavvayantēṇa
tāēṇa ahaṁ bhaṇiō bhagiṇī ṭhāṇammi dāyavvā // SurSuCa.123


[p. 22]
iṇhiṁ varassa uciyā jāyā ēsatti tā mahaṁ kahasu
kō aṇurūvō purisō imīē sukulappasūō ya? // SurSuCa.124

maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dēvo cciya ēttha jāṇaē uciyaṁ
tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ mē phuraī cittammi // SurSuCa.125

kīraï sayaṁvarō iha hakkārijjantu savvarāyāṇō
jō cēva hiyayaïṭṭhō taṁ cēva varēī jēṇēsā // SurSuCa.126

maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi taṁ kiccaṁ
navari sayaṁvarakaraṇaṁ sampaï uciyaṁ na kāuṁ jē // SurSuCa.127

savvēvi nivā jaïyā āyattā honti ēganaravaïṇō
tadaṇunnāēṇa tayā sayaṁvarō hōi kāyavvō // SurSuCa.128

ēgassa jaō varaṇē sēsāṇaṁ sō nivāragō hōi
sampaï puṇa rāyāṇō narinda! savvēvi ahamindā // SurSuCa.129


[p. 23]
tā tāṇamēgavaraṇē sēsā savvēvi sattuṇō honti
na ya sakkā saṅgāmē jiṇiuṁ savvēvi ēgēṇa // SurSuCa.130

tā alamimiṇā naravara! viggahamūlēṇaṇatthabahulēṇa
kamalāvaīsayaṁvarakaraṇēṇa ēttha patthāvē // SurSuCa.131

tattō raṇṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kassēsā tarihi bhadda! dāyavvā
kō va imīē iṭṭhō maṇassa iha kaha ṇu nāyavvaṁ? // SurSuCa.132

jassa va tassa va rannō dāyavvā na ya maē niyayabhagiṇī
dinnā hōi sudinnā jassa, imā tassa dāyavvā // SurSuCa.133

ēvaṁ ca jāva jampaï rāyā maïsāgarēṇa saha tattha
tāva ya duvārapālō paṇāmapaccuṭṭhiō bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.134

aṭṭhaṅganimittaviū bhūyabhavissatthapayaḍaṇapaḍiṭṭhō
suṇaīnāmō ihaïṁ samāgaō dēva! nēmittī // SurSuCa.135


[p. 24]
sō dēvadaṁsaṇatthaṁ duvāradēsammi ciṭṭhaï iyāṇiṁ
iya sōuṁ naravaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ turiyaṁ pavēsēhiṁ // SurSuCa.136

tayaṇantaraṁ ca sumaī nimmalasiyavasaṇasōhiyasarīrō
gōrōyaṇakayatilaō samāgaō rāiṇō puraō // SurSuCa.137

āsīpayāṇapuvvaṁ dāuṁ duvvakkhaē narindassa
rannā kaōvayārō uciyāsaṇagammi uvaviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.138

rannā paccayahēuṁ atīyavatthummi pucchiō ēsō
paccakkhaṁ piva savvaṁ sāhēi sō avitahaṁ jāva // SurSuCa.139

tāhē pahasiyavayaṇō rāyā naravāhaṇō imaṁ bhaṇati
bhō sumaï! majjha bhagiṇī ēsā kamalāvaī kaṇṇā // SurSuCa.140

ēīē kō bhattā hōhī maṇavallahutti vajjarasu
sumaī nirūviūṇaṁ nimittamēvaṁ samullavaï // SurSuCa.141


[p. 25]
naravara! cittē lihiyaṁ ēīē rūvayaṁ pulōēttā
mucchijjissaï jō iha hōhī bhattā imīē sō // SurSuCa.142

sayalōrōhapahāṇā tassa ya hōhī imā mahādēvī
ētthattthē ya narēsara! mā kāhisi annahābhāvaṁ // SurSuCa.143

ētthantarammi sāgarasēṭṭhī saṁlavaï sumaïnēmittiṁ
sirikantāē bhattā kō hōhī majjha dhūyāē? // SurSuCa.144

vajjaraï taō sumaī kasiṇabhuyaṅgēṇa ḍasiyamēyaṁ jō
ujjīvissaï so cciya bhattā dhūyāē tē hōhī // SurSuCa.145

ēvaṁ ca pucchiūṇaṁ uciyaṁ kāūṇa tassa uvayāraṁ
paṭṭhaviō naravaïṇā jahāgayaṁ paḍigaō sumaī // SurSuCa.146

tattō ya bhaṇaï mantī sōhaṇamahuṇā narinda! sañjāyaṁ
tā iṇhiṁ tabbhaṇiē kāyavvō ujjamō hōi // SurSuCa.147


[p. 26]
bhaṇiyaṁ rannā kō iha sāisayaṁ lihaï cittakammanti
maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ supasiddhō tāva iha nayarē // SurSuCa.148

ēkko cciya kamalāvaïujjhāyasumittasēṇanāmassa
taṇaō u cittasēṇō aïkusalō cittakammammi // SurSuCa.149

[yugmam]
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ sigghaṁ vāharaha tayanti takkhaṇēṇa ahaṁ
vāhariō sampattō bhaṇiō rannā sabahumāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.150

kamalāvaīē rūvaṁ sigdhaṁ ālihasu cittaphalahīē
jaṁ āṇavēsi bhaṇiuṁ, sōhaṇavannēhi taṁ lihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.151

dēkkhāliyaṁ ca rannō sāisayaṁ pēkkhiūṇa tō tuṭṭhō
bhaṇiō ahaṁ rannā ētthatthē taṁ siuciutti // SurSuCa.152

cittagaravēsadhārī ēyaṁ ghēttūṇa savvarāīṇaṁ
daṁsēṇu jassa mucchā jāyaï ēyaṁ pulōēuṁ // SurSuCa.153


[p. 27]
sō maha sāhēavvō sigdhaṁ āgamma, jēṇa tassēva
mahayā uvayārēṇa dijjaï kamalāvaī ēsā // SurSuCa.154

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ raṇṇā bhaṇiō tattō paṇamittu tassa payakamalaṁ
kaïvayapariyaṇasahiō kusagganayarāu nīhariō // SurSuCa.155

suggīvakittivaddhaṇapamuhāṇaṁ naravaīṇa mē ēsā
sandaṁsiyāu na puṇō jāyā iha atthasaṁsiddhī // SurSuCa.156

ajja puṇō iha nayarē samāgaō dēva! tumha pāsammi
ēyaṁ niyacchiūṇaṁ mucchā jāyā ya tumhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.157

jāyaṁ maha sāmisamīhiyaṁ ti cinttittu tēṇa naranāha!
jāō harisō majjha sumariya nēmittiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.158

ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ mucchāē tumha harisiō ahayaṁ
tā mā narinda! annahabhāvēṇa viyappasu mamanti // SurSuCa.159


[p. 28]
ii cittasēṇavayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ vigayaannaāsaṅkō
vajjaraï amarakēū vimhaïō cittarūvēṇa // SurSuCa.160

kiṁ tīē kannāē ērisayaṁ atthi rūvasōhaggaṁ?
tā bhaṇaī cittasēṇō nimēsamēttaṁ imaṁ lihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.161

kō sakkaï kusalōvi hu jahaṭṭhiyaṁ tīē rāyakannāē
nijjiyatiyasavilāsiṇīrūvaṁ rūvaṁ samālihiuṁ? // SurSuCa.162

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyahiyaēṇa rāiṇā tassa
aṅgavilaggamasēsaṁ pasāiyaṁ kaḍayavatthāiṁ // SurSuCa.163

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō āēsaṁ dēha dēva! amhāṇaṁ
naravāhaṇassa raṇṇō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ jēṇa sāhēmō // SurSuCa.164

raṇṇaṇṇunnāō sō kamēṇa pattō kusagganayarammi
naravāhaṇassa rannō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō // SurSuCa.165


[p. 29]
aha tēṇavi niyabhagiṇī pabhūyadhaṇapariyaṇēṇa pariyariyā
paṭṭhaviyā hiṭṭhēṇaṁ sayaṁvarā amarakēussa // SurSuCa.166

sirikantāisahijaṇaṁ ābhāsittā ya sayalaparivāraṁ
kamalāvaīvi caliyā harisavisāyāurā hiyaē // SurSuCa.167

icchiyavaralābhēṇaṁ sāṇandā tahaya bandhuvirahēṇaṁ
kiñci sasōgā pattā kamēṇa sā hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.168

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ sōhaṇalaggammi gurupamōēṇaṁ
kamalāvaī u rannā pariṇīyā khattakulavihiṇā // SurSuCa.169

pāṇāṇavi abbhahiyā pavarā antēurassa sayalassa
indassava indāṇī jāyā aha sā mahādēvī // SurSuCa.170

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa rāiṇō tassa
nīīē sayalabhūmiṁ niyayaṁ parivālayantassa // SurSuCa.171


[p. 30]
vaccanti vāsarāiṁ suhasamudayamasamamaṇuhavantassa
vibuhapahussava tiyasālayammi addiṭṭhadukkhassa // SurSuCa.172

tammi ya purē pasiddhō pavarō paürāṇa āsi dhaṇadhammō
sēṭṭhī nivassa iṭṭhō pattaṭṭhō savvasatthēsu // SurSuCa.173

nīsēsaatthivittharapatthiyaabbhahiyadinnavaradāṇō
ajjayapajjayajaṇayajjiyāē lacchīē 'laṅkariō // SurSuCa.174

jiṇasamayasatthavittharaviyakkhaṇō mōkkhamaggatallicchō
jiṇasāhupūyaṇaraō sāhammiyavacchalō dhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.175

avahasiyatiyasasundarirūvāisayā paīvayā dakkhā
bhajjā maṇōramanāmā tassa ya pāṇappiyā dhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.176

tāṇaṁ tivaggasāraṁ visayasuhaṁ sammamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ
niyakulamaṇḍaṇabhūō jāō aha dāraō ēkkō // SurSuCa.177


[p. 31]
vattē ya bārasāhē ammāpīīhiṁ niyayakulavihiṇā
dhaṇadēvotti ya sammaṁ nāmaṁ nivvattiyaṁ tassa // SurSuCa.178

aha pañcadhāikayavivihalālaṇō dāraō sa vaḍḍhantō
pattō kumārabhāvaṁ māupiuṇaṁ kayāṇandō // SurSuCa.179

abbhahiyaaṭṭhavarisō sammaṁ abbhasiyasayalavijjassa
ujjhāyassuvaṇīō vinnāyakalākalāvassa // SurSuCa.180

thēvēṇa vi kālēṇaṁ ahigamiyāō samatthavijjāō
sayalē kalākalāvē aha jāō sōvi pattaṭṭhō // SurSuCa.181

tattō gahiyakalāvō samāṇiō niyagharammi dhaṇadēvō
piuṇā sē ujjhāō sa pūiō vatthamāīhiṁ // SurSuCa.182

kamasō pavaḍḍhamāṇō dhaṇadēvō jōvvaṇaṁ samaṇupattō
nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvō jāō varakāmiṇīdaïō // SurSuCa.183


[p. 32]
aha sō samāṇajōvvaṇarūvāisaēhiṁ varavayaṁsēhiṁ
pariyariō āhiṇḍaï īsaralīlaṁ viḍambantō // SurSuCa.184

aha annayā kayāivi vayaṁsavisarēṇa parigaō ēsō
nayarāō nīhariō pattō ya maṇōramujjāṇē // SurSuCa.185

diṭṭhō ya tattha ēgō purisō gurusōyaparigaō tēṇa
vāvītaḍōvaviṭṭhō aṁsujalōhaliyagaṇḍayalō // SurSuCa.186

dhaṇadēvō taṁ daṭṭhuṁ purisaṁ uppannagaruyakāruṇṇō
āsannē gantūṇaṁ mahuragirāē imaṁ bhaṇati // SurSuCa.187

kō si tumaṁ kattō vā kiṁ vā tē sōyakāraṇaṁ bhadda!?
ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō sō purisō ēvamullavaï // SurSuCa.188

kaha tammi vajjarijjaï dukkhaṁ gurudukkhapīḍiyamaṇēhiṁ
na kuṇaï jō paḍiyāraṁ na ya duhiō ahava jō hōi? // SurSuCa.189


[p. 33]
tahavi hu kahēmi sundara! mā vayaṇaṁ tujjha nipphalaṁ jāu
sīhaguhānāmēṇaṁ aïvisamā atthi pallitti // SurSuCa.190

tīē ya supaïṭṭhō pallivaī tassa bhāriyā lacchī
tīē puttō jāō jayasēṇō jaṇamaṇāṇandō // SurSuCa.191

tassa ya bālaggahō ahayaṁ nāmēṇa dēvasammotti
kīlāmi ya jayasēṇaṁ tattha ahaṁ vivihakīlāhiṁ // SurSuCa.192

aha annayā ya bāhiṁ viṇiggaō gēṇhiūṇa jayasēṇaṁ
purisēhiṁ dōhi diṭṭhō tattha ahaṁ jōgirūvēhiṁ // SurSuCa.193

sambhāsiūṇa puvviṁ dinnō maha tēhiṁ pavaratambōlō
tammi samāṇiyamittē maïsaṁmōhō mahaṁ jāō // SurSuCa.194

tattō kumarasamēō tēsimaṇumaggamēva laggō haṁ
jāṇāmi nēva kiñcivi vimōhiō tēhiṁ pāvēhiṁ // SurSuCa.195


[p. 34]
tēhi samētō ahayaṁ vayāmi jā kittiyampi bhūbhāgaṁ
tāva ya tisiēṇa maē ēgammi uvavaṇaniguñjē // SurSuCa.196

bahuvihataruphalakalusaṁ pīyaṁ nīraṁ tu tappabhāvēṇa
jāō satthasarīrō vicintiyaṁ tāhi mē ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.197

rayaṇīi gahiya kumaraṁ nāsissamimāṇa pāvapurisāṇaṁ
iya cintiya caliō haṁ alakkhiō cēva saha tēhiṁ // SurSuCa.198

pattāē rayaṇīē nisuyā annōnnamullavēmāṇā
ēēṇa bālaēṇaṁ sijjhissaï jakkhiṇī amhaṁ // SurSuCa.199

tugīyapavvayammī pattā huṁṇiūṇa bālayaṁ ēyaṁ
siddhāē jakkhiṇīē pāvissāmō nihiṁ taṁ tu // SurSuCa.200

iya tēsiṁ sōūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, bhayavēvirō daḍhaṁ jāō
suttēsu tēsu ghēttuṁ jayasēṇaṁ tāhi naṭṭhō haṁ // SurSuCa.201


[p. 35]
kahakahavi hu nāsantō gavēsamāṇēhiṁ tēhiṁ haṁ pattō
bandhittu taō vasabhē samāruhēttā ihāṇīō // SurSuCa.202

ajja puṇō iha nayarē sampattō sattamāu divasāu
tanhāchuhābhibhūō mukkō haṁ ēttha ujjāṇē // SurSuCa.203

tā bhadda! imaṁ gurusōyakāraṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ maē tumha
jaï atthi kāvi sattī tā rakkhaha bālayaṁ taṁ tu // SurSuCa.204

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sampaï ciṭṭhanti kattha tē purisā?
sō bhaṇaï gahiyakumarō ēgō naggōhahēṭṭhammi // SurSuCa.205

bīō purē paviṭṭhō surāikajjēṇa sampayaṁ cēva
iya bhaṇiē dhaṇadēvō jōgiyapāsē gaō turiyaṁ // SurSuCa.206

bhaṇiō ya tēṇa ēsō ēyaṁ maha dēsu bālayaṁ bhadda!
ahayaṁ suvannalakkhaṁ tuha dēmi, na ēttha sandēhō // SurSuCa.207


[p. 36]
tō jōgiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jāva na sō ēi duiyaō jōgī
tāva maha dēsu lakkhaṁ jēṇa imaṁ dēmi tuha bālaṁ // SurSuCa.208

tattō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ samappiyaṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ tassa
dīṇāralakkhamullaṁ mukkō ya imēṇa jayasēṇō // SurSuCa.209

ghēttūṇa aṅgulīyaṁ sigghayaraṁ jōgiō taō naṭṭhō
ghēttūṇa ya jayasēṇaṁ dhaṇadēvō dēvasammassa // SurSuCa.210

pāsammi samallīṇō bhaṇiō ēsō ya ginha kumaratti
tattō ya dēvasammō pahasiyavayaṇō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.211

taṁ sāmī taṁ bandhū taṁ ciya maha jīyadāyagō suyaṇu!
kiṁ kiṁ na kayaṁ tumaē jīyaṁ kumarassa dintēṇa? // SurSuCa.212

maha sāmiyassa dinnaṁ, jīyaṁ jaṁ pāṇavallahō puttō
pāviṭṭhaduṭṭhajōgiyakayantavayaṇāu nīhariō // SurSuCa.213


[p. 37]
tattō dhavadēvēṇaṁ nīō gēhammi bhōiō sammaṁ
satthassa mēliūṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō niyayaṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.214

ēsō puṇa vuttantō vitthariō tattha puravarē sahasā
aïcāī dhaṇadēvō dēi dhaṇaṁ lakkhagannēhiṁ // SurSuCa.215

tā jattha jattha dīsaï dhaṇadēvō niyavayaṁsapariyariō
annōnnaṁ puralōō tattha imaṁ vivihamullavaï // SurSuCa.216

ēsō sō dhaṇadēvō cāī bhōgī ya taha kalākusalō
atthijaṇapatthiō jō varisaï lakkhēhiṁ dhannotti // SurSuCa.217

annē puṇa macchariṇō bhaṇanti niyacāyagavviyā tattha
kiṁ salahijjaï ēsō niyapiulacchīē khayakālō? // SurSuCa.218

taṁ dāṇamiha pasassaṁ taṁ cēva ya pōrusassa vuḍ̣dhikaraṁ
jaṁ niyaparakkamēṇaṁ viḍhaviya vilasijjaï jahicchaṁ // SurSuCa.219


[p. 38]
jaṁ puṇa ajjayapajjayajaṇayajjiyaatthamajjhaō dāṇaṁ
paramatthaō kalaṅkaṁ tayaṁ tu purisābhimāṇīṇaṁ // SurSuCa.220

bhaṇiyaṁ ca bappaviḍhaviya davvēṇaṁ kō na viḍ̣dhiraṁ kuṇaï
saïviḍhavaṇavilāsaṇayaṁ jaṇayaï viralaṁ suyaṁ nārī // SurSuCa.221

ēyaṁ jaṇappavāyaṁ nisuṇittā cintaī u dhaṇadēvō
saccaṁ bhaṇanti ēē na hu juttaṁ majjha ērisayaṁ // SurSuCa.222

tā paradēsaṁ gantu viḍhavittā bhūribhūipabbhāraṁ
vilasāmi jahicchāē dīṇā 'ṇāhāṇa avisaṅkō // SurSuCa.223

iya cintiya dhaṇadēvō māupiūṇaṁ sagāsamāgamma
viṇayapaṇaüttamaṅgō kayañjalī bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.224

tubbhēhiṁ aṇunnāō gantūṇaṁ tāya! annadēsammi
viḍhavāmi bhūridavvaṁ iya icchā sampayaṁ majjha // SurSuCa.225


[p. 39]
tā aṇujāṇaü tāō pujjantu maṇōrahā imē majjha
gacchāmi annadēsaṁ vaṇijjabuddhīē sayamēva // SurSuCa.226

bhaṇiyaṁ jaṇaṇīē taō gamaṇavayaṇampi dussahaṁ putta!
acchaü tā dūre cciya puṇa gamaṇaṁ annadēsammi // SurSuCa.227

annaṁ ca atthi lacchī tuha jaṇaēṇāvi ajjiyā putta!
jīē vilasantōvi hu antaṁ kāuṁ na sattō si // SurSuCa.228

aviya jaṇaēṇa ya tuha puttaya! atthuppattīē kāraṇaṁ jaṁ jaṁ
taṁ savvaṁ kāraviyaṁ kiṁ kajjaṁ tuha vaṇijjēṇa? // SurSuCa.229

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ jāvajjavi ammi! bālaō puttō
tāva niyajaṇaṇisihiṇē pharisantō lahaï sōhampi // SurSuCa.230

vōlīṇabālabhāvō chippaï pāvēṇa taṁ karēmāṇō
taha piulacchī jaṇaṇivva hōi susamatthaputtāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.231


[p. 40]
susamatthō vi hu jō jaṇayaajjiyaṁ sampayaṁ nisēvēi
sō ammi! tāva lōē mamaṁva uvahāsaṁ lahaï // SurSuCa.232

iya bhaṇiuṁ dhaṇadēvō aṁsujalupphuṇṇalōyaṇō sahasā
mukkalaha iha bhaṇantō paḍiō jaṇaṇīē calasēṇu // SurSuCa.233

tō dhaṇadhammō sēṭṭhī nāuṁ avasāṇa- (ya) kāraṇaṁ tassa
vajjaraï puttaṁ! kō tujjha vañchiē kuṇaï vigghanti? // SurSuCa.234

jaṇaēṇaṁ jaṇaṇī puttaviōgaṁ aṇicchamāṇīvi
kahakahavi hu saṇṭhaviyā vinnāyasuyāvamāṇēṇa // SurSuCa.235

ēvaṁ sō dhaṇadēvō māyāvittēhiṁ abbhaṇunnāō
paradēsagamaṇajōgaṁ gahiūṇa caüvvihaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ // SurSuCa.236

aṭṭhāhiyamahimāō kārāvēttā jiṇindabhavaṇēsu
sampūiya sāhujaṇaṁ saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.237


[p. 41]
sayalammi tammi nayarē kāriya āghōsaṇaṁ jaṇē miliē
nēmittiyaāiṭṭhē suhadivasē vihiyamaṅgallē // SurSuCa.238

gahiūṇa pavarasaüṇaṁ aṅgīkāuṁ kusaggavaranayaraṁ
hiyabandhuvaṇiyasahiō nīhariō niyayanayarāō // SurSuCa.239

[caturbhiḥ kalāpakam]
ēvaṁ sō dhaṇadēvō saṁvāhiyasahapayaṭṭajaṇaniyarō
lahulahupayāṇaēhiṁ vaccaï saha garuyasatthēṇa // SurSuCa.240

tattō 'ṇuvāsaraṁ sō satthō vasimaṁ aïkkamēūṇa
aha kamasō sampattō ēkkaṁ aïbhīsaṇaṁ aḍaviṁ // SurSuCa.241

jattha adīsantāṇavi ghaṇapattalapaürapāyavattaṇaō
kūiyasarasaṁsavaṇā gammaï vihagāṇa atthittaṁ // SurSuCa.242

annaṁ ta jīē lōyā nīipahāṇassa puhaïpālassa
nayarīē iva na kuṇanti kahavi ummagasañcaraṇaṁ // SurSuCa.243


[p. 42]
viyaḍāḍavīē tīē majjhaṁmajjhēṇa vayaï sō satthō
niyakōlāhalapaḍiravapaḍipūriyajunnataruvivarō // SurSuCa.244

tuṅgataruniyarasāhappasāhasañchannaambarattaṇaō
savvampi vahaï diyahaṁ alaggaravikiraṇasantāvō // SurSuCa.245

kavikaguyugarutaravōkkārasavaṇasahasuttasantabahuvasahō
uttasiyavasahavālaṇanimittapamukkahakkārō // SurSuCa.246

hakkārasaddapaḍiravasaṁsavaṇuttāsiyāṇa sayarāhaṁ
āyannantō disi disi ghūyāṇaṁ bhūrihuṅkārē // SurSuCa.247

vasahakaṇṭhapalambiraghaṇṭiyā-raṇiyapūriyabhūritarambarō
visakhurukkhayarēṇunirantarō, vayaï tattha sa vāṇiyasatthaō // SurSuCa.248


[p. 43]
sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsō ēttha samappaï aḍavipavēsassa vannaṇō nāma
surasundarināmāē kahāē paḍhamō paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 44]
[|| dvitīyaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha annavāsarammī kamēṇa bahuvōliyāē aḍavīē
gahiya jalāsayamēgaṁ aha sō āvāsiō satthō // SurSuCa.1

aha tammi satthalōē ulladdiyasayalavasahaniyarammi
jalaïndhaṇāiaṭṭhā iō taō pariyaḍantammi // SurSuCa.2

pamukkēsu disi disi caraṇatthaṁ savvavasahamahisēsu
pāraddhēsu ya takkālamuciyakiccēsu lōēṇa // SurSuCa.3

nāūṇa paṇihivasaō bhōyaṇakajjammi āulaṁ satthaṁ
satthammi tammi paḍiyā jhaḍitti bhillāṇa dhāḍitti // SurSuCa.4

[tisr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]

[p. 45]
aviya. 

navamuggavannaaḍḍaṇaḍhakkiyaājāṇubhīsaṇasarīrā
masirāsī iva kālā kuviyakayantōvva duppicchā // SurSuCa.5

kharabībhacchasarīrā palāsapattēhiṁ vihiyasēharayā
guñjāphalaratacchā ubbhaṅkharakēsamapabbhārā // SurSuCa.6

sanaddhabaddhakavayā paṭṭhipaēsā 'vaṇaddhatōṇīrā
kannāyaḍḍhiyadhaṇuhapaṭṭhadīsantabhallōḍā // SurSuCa.7

kēvi asivaggahatthā kēvi hu karagahiyalaüḍayā avarē
gumphaṇaphēraṇasuṅkāraēhiṁ jīyaṁ va avaṇēntā // SurSuCa.8

dhiṭṭhāniṭṭhurahiyayā disō disiṁ ‘māri māri’ bhaṇamāṇā
annāyā ēva kuōvi jjhatti bhillā samāvaḍiyā // SurSuCa.9

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]

[p. 46]
paḍiēsu taō tēsuṁ satthō savvō vi āulībhūō
bhillāṇa paürabhāvā vakkhēvā satthapurisāṇa // SurSuCa.10

aha tammi saraṇarahiē lhasijjantē samatthasatthammi
dappaparipūriyaṅgā hakkiya jampanti kēvi narā // SurSuCa.11

rē! rē! pisāyarūvā! katthiṇhiṁ jāha diṭṭhipahapaḍiyā
payaḍaha savvaṁ jaï atthi tumhamiha pōrisaṁ kimpi // SurSuCa.12

kēvi puṇa bhīruhiyayā varayā dasaṇaüḍagahiyaaṅguliṇō
hā! hā! rakkhaha rakkhaha ēvaṁ kaluṇāiṁ jampanti // SurSuCa.13

kēvi hu luṇṭijjantā iō taō taha pahammamāṇā ya
kīvā palāyaṇaṭṭhā tattha gavēsanti chiddāṇi // SurSuCa.14

kēvi kahakahavi pāviyachiddā gāḍhaṁ ca khasaphasēmāṇā
saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ ōsakkiūṇa līyanti gahaṇēsu // SurSuCa.15


[p. 47]
kēvi hu vēviradēhā sịdhilīkayakacchabandhaṇā dhaṇiyaṁ
pamukkapurisayārā aṅgīkayadīṇajaṇacēṭṭhā // SurSuCa.16

paricattasayalalajjā kahakahamavi mōkkhaṇaṁ vimaggantā
tēsiṁ ciya pāvāṇaṁ, kuṇanti bahucāḍukammāṇi // SurSuCa.17

kēvi hu mayamiva bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyaṁ appayaṁ payaṁsanti
kēvi hu chuhanti gaṇṭhiṁ mahīē pakkhāṇi jōēttā // SurSuCa.18

jēvi hu iō taō indhaṇāiaṭṭhā gayāsi satthāō
tēvi hu kalayalasaddaṁ sōuṁ vaccanti dūrayaraṁ // SurSuCa.19

rē! lēha haṇaha bandhaha māraha vayaṇāiṁ bharaha dhūlīē
summanti tattha satthē disi disi ēvaṁvihā saddā // SurSuCa.20

ēyāvasarammi taō pāsittu iō taō vilumpantaṁ
bhillēhiṁ satthalōyaṁ kaïvayaniyapurisapariyariō // SurSuCa.21


[p. 48]
uppāēntō tēsiṁ āgiīē cēva cittasaṅkhōhaṁ
vasunandayakhaggakarō dhaṇadēvō ēvamullavaï // SurSuCa.22

rē! rē! pāvā! jaï atthi tumha iha kāvi dappakaṇḍūī
tā havaha majjha puraō sahasā taṁ jēṇa avaṇēmi // SurSuCa.23

mā bhaṇaha jaṁ na bhaṇiyaṁ ēsa kasavaṭṭaō supurisāṇa
na hi niyajuvaïsalahiyā purisā purisattaṇamuvēnti // SurSuCa.24

hā! dhī! dhī! ēyassa u rē! duṭṭhā! tumha purisagārassa
nāsantalōyapaṭṭhīdhāvaṇaüvaladdhāpasarassa // SurSuCa.25

ēvaṁ ca nisāmittā dōccaṁ taccaṁ samullavantassa
dhaṇadēvassullāvē suhaḍāṇavi bhūribhayajaṇagē // SurSuCa.26

rē! rē! lēha imassavi phēḍēmō dhīrayaṁ kirāḍassa
ēvaṁ samullavantā valiyā tē jhatti tayabhimuhaṁ // SurSuCa.27


[p. 49]
pattā ya āhasantā dhaṇadēvassantiyaṁ samantā tē
tikkhāsikōntatōmarabhallīhi ya pahariuṁ laggā // SurSuCa.28

dhaṇadēvōvi asaṅkō tahā payaṭṭēsu tēsu bhillēsu
tāṇamuramōḍiūṇaṁ kuṇaï niyapōrisaṁ payaḍaṁ // SurSuCa.29

jaha jaha tē bhillanarā dēnti pahārē daḍhaṁ dayāhīṇā
dhaṇadēvō uṇa taha taha abbhasiyakalō pavañcēi // SurSuCa.30

aviya pharaēṇa kēvi hu iō taō kēvi kāyakaraṇēṇaṁ
kēvi hu dūrāucciya ēntē khaggābhidhāēṇa // SurSuCa.31

kahakahavi hu bhillēhiṁ gahiō pharaēhiṁ uṭṭhahēūṇa
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ rē! rē! ēsō satthāhivō vaṇiō // SurSuCa.32

tā bandhiūṇa ēyaṁ akkhayadēhaṁ tu pallināhassa
appēmō jēṇēsō dēi vaṇiō dhaṇaṁ bahuyaṁ // SurSuCa.33


[p. 50]
tattō ya tēhiṁ gantuṁ pallīvaïṇō samappiō ēsō
ētthantarammi diṭṭhō dhaṇadēvō dēvasammēṇa // SurSuCa.34

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiō sadukkhamēvaṁ tu pallināhassa
hā! hā! sāmiya! ēsō mahāṇubhāvō sa dhaṇadēvō // SurSuCa.35

jēṇa tayā tuha taṇaō jōgiyagahiōvi mōiō āsi
dāuṁ suvannalakkhaṁ nikkāraṇavacchalēṇaṁ tu // SurSuCa.36

jayasēṇakumarajīviyadāyā dhaṇadhammasēṭṭhiputtō sō
paramuvayārī sāmiya! kahaṇu ahannēhiṁ vihiutti? // SurSuCa.37

iya dēvasammabhaṇiyaṁ sōuṁ sambhantalōyaṇō sahasā
aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō muñcaha muñcaha mahābhāgaṁ // SurSuCa.38

pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ takkhaṇamucchōḍiyā ya sē bandhā
pallīvaïṇā tāhē avagụ̄dhō sāyaraṁ ēsō // SurSuCa.39


[p. 51]
tattō vihiyapaṇāmō takkālamuciyammi āsaṇē dinnē
pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ, uvaviṭṭhō tattha dhaṇadēvō // SurSuCa.40

tattō ya dīhadīhaṁ nīsasiya visāyagabbhiṇaṁ ēvaṁ
lajjāvaṇamiyavayaṇō pallivaī bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.41

paramuvagāritti tumaṁ uvēcca kilahōsi amha daṭṭhavō
navaraṁ gihāgayassavi sāgayamēvaṁvihaṁ vihiyaṁ! // SurSuCa.42

jāyaï avagāraphalō vihiō pāvāṇaṁ ahava uvayārō
sappassa jahā dinnaṁ duddhampi visattaṇamuvēi // SurSuCa.43

pāvō ahaṁ kayagdhō suyajīviyadāyagassa jēṇajja
gihamāgayassa ēyaṁ ahammakammaṁ samāyariyaṁ // SurSuCa.44

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ kīsa imaṁ vahaha guruvisāyanti
annāṇaṁ avarajjhaï, kō dōsō ēttha tumhāṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.45


[p. 52]
daṭṭhuṁ aṇannasarisaṁ bhillavaī tassa vayaṇavinnāṇaṁ
rūvaṁ taha suyaṇattaṁ puṇōvi aïrañjiō bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.46

pēcchaha ēgammi narē kēttiyaguṇasamudaō samaṁ vasaï?
bahurayaṇā hu vasumaī saccō lōyappavāō 'yaṁ // SurSuCa.47

dhī! dhī! maha purisattaṁ dhī! dhī! maha ērisāē vittīē
niyakulakalaṅkabhūyassa majjha dhī! purisajammēṇa // SurSuCa.48

dhī! majjha jīviēṇa kukammanirayassa dhammarahiyassa
ēyārisapurisāṇaṁ luṇṭaṇakammammi nirayassa // SurSuCa.49

ēttiyamēttēṇaṁ ciya dhannō 'haṁ jaṁ mahāṇubhāvassa
akkhayadēhassa imassa daṁsaṇaṁ jhatti sañjāyaṁ // SurSuCa.50

jaï puṇa hōjja vivattī samayaṁ bhillēhiṁ jujjhamāṇassa
tā kaha majjha aünnassa hōjja pāvassa nitthārō? // SurSuCa.51


[p. 0५3]
ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ appāṇaṁ nindiūṇa tō bhaṇaï
bhō! bhō! bhillā satthē jaṁ gahiyaṁ ēttha tumhēhiṁ // SurSuCa.52

taṁ savvampi samappaha imassa dhaṇadēvanāmavaṇiyassa
tēhiṁ taṇamajjāyaṁ samappiyaṁ tassa taṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.53

[yugmam]
tattō sabālavuḍ̣dhē miliē lōgammi bhayavimukkammi
vajjaraï suppaïṭṭhō dhaṇadēvaṁ nēhagabbhamiṇaṁ // SurSuCa.54

ēttō gāuyamēttē sīhaguhā nāma atthi mē pallī
tīē lahumāgacchaha ajja maha pāhuṇā hōha // SurSuCa.55

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti tāhē sō satthō
dhaṇadēvamaggalaggō sīhaguhaṁ jhatti sampattō // SurSuCa.56

āvāsiyassa tattō vasimāsannammi satthalōyassa
pallīvaïṇā nīō dhaṇadēvō niyayagahēmmi // SurSuCa.57


[p. 54]
abbhaṅgiūṇa vihiṇā sugandhatēllēhiṁ pavarajuvaīhiṁ
addhāṇaparissamanāsagēṇa varavāriṇā nhaviō // SurSuCa.58

ghaṇasārasārasirikhaṇḍacacciō tāhē pallināhēṇa
sahiō pavarāhāraṁ bhōttūṇa samuṭṭhiō kamasō // SurSuCa.59

kappūrapūrasahiē tambōlē āyarēṇa sē dinnē
vajjaraï dhaṇadēvō suhāsaṇatthō imaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.60

ēsā hu tāva pallī āvāsō nigdhiṇassa lōyassa
tubbhēvi tassa pahuṇō aṇannasōjjannadayakaliyā // SurSuCa.61

ēsō na sammajōgō ahivaïbhiccāṇa maha ṭhiyaṁ cittē
jaṁ sōyasaccadakkhinnavajjiyāṇaṁ imaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.62

bhillāṇaṁ nāhāvi hu jaṁ ērisaguṇagaṇēṇa sañjuttā
ēyaṁ maṇammi bhāvaï mahantamacchērayaṁ majjha // SurSuCa.63


[p. 55]
asarisasōjannajuyā tumhē ēyāē vasaha pallīē
uttamanarāvi hōuṁ sāhaha maha kēṇa kajjēṇa? // SurSuCa.64

tō bhaṇaï supaïṭṭhō kiṁ kahiēṇaṁ imēṇa dhaṇadēva!
vañcaṇamavamāṇaṁ ciya maïjuttō nō pagāsējjā // SurSuCa.65

tahavi hu bhaṇāmi mā hōu tujjha abbhatthaṇā imā vihalā
ēgaggamaṇō hōuṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi // SurSuCa.66

niccaṁ pamuiyanaranāriputragāmāvalīē ramaṇīō
bahudivasavannaṇijjō aṅgō nāmēṇa dēsō 'tthi // SurSuCa.67

tammi ya puraṁ purāṇaṁ pavaraṁ suranayarasarisariddhillaṁ
bhayaḍamarakaravimukkaṁ siddhatthapuranti vikkhāyaṁ // SurSuCa.68

tammi ya mayandhariukaraḍikaraḍanibbhēyaṇammi pattaṭṭhō
kambunnayasuggīvō suggīvō nāma naranāhō // SurSuCa.69


[p. 56]
sayalōrōhapahāṇā sundarasaradindubimbasamavayaṇā
buddhīē aṇannasamā kamalā nāmēṇa sē dēvī // SurSuCa.70

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa taha ya rajjadhuraṁ
puvvabhavapunnapāyavasamappiyaṁ pālayantassa // SurSuCa.71

vaccantēsu diṇēsuṁ tīē dēvīē aha ahaṁ puttō
jāō kayaṁ ca nāmaṁ vihiṇā maha suppaïṭṭhotti // SurSuCa.72

lālijjantō pañcahiṁ dhāīhiṁ kamēṇa vaḍḍhamāṇō 'haṁ
sañjāō pañcavarisō māupiūṇaṁ kayāṇandō // SurSuCa.73

ētthantarammi gimhē santāviyamahiyalē vaïkkantē
nivvaviyamahīvị̄dhō rasantasālūrasaṅghāō // SurSuCa.74

pavahantabahalavāhiṇikhalahalasaṁsaddabahiriyadigantō
gajjantagahirajalaharadaṁsaṇanaccantasihinivahō // SurSuCa.75


[p. 57]
papphullaphullasōhiyanīvōhavirāyamāṇavaṇaniyarō
mucakundakuḍayasandiyarayagabbhiṇavāiyasamīrō // SurSuCa.76

puliṇapaïṭṭhiyabālayakayavāluyadēulēhiṁ ramaṇīō
karisayajaṇapārambhiyahalaüttayacacciyabaïllō // SurSuCa.77

harisavasahasirapāmara disi disi cabbhattabhūrikēyārō
pattō vāsārattō kaddamadullaṅghamaggillō // SurSuCa.78

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
ēyārisammi navapāusammi pattammi annadivasammi
naranāhō suggīvō vihiṇā kayabhōyaṇō santō // SurSuCa.79

candaṇacacciyadēhō parihiyamiusaṇhanimmaladugūlō
tambōlavaggahatthō samāgatō dēvibhavaṇammi // SurSuCa.80

[yugmam]
sattatalē pāsāē ārụ̄dhō uvarimāē bhūmīē
dēvīē kayaviṇaō maharihasējjāē āsīṇō // SurSuCa.81


[p. 58]
khaṇamēgamacchiūṇaṁ parihāsakahāhimpiyayamāē saha
siyavasaṇacchāiyāē kōmalatūlīē pāsuttō // SurSuCa.82

tatō ya sajalajalaharagañjiyasaddēṇa naṭṭhaniddō sō
uṭṭhittuṁ saṁniviṭṭhō nijjūhagasaṇṭhiyamasūrē // SurSuCa.83

addhāsaṇē niviṭṭhā kamaladēvīvi tāhē narapahuṇō
vajjaraï taō rāyā harisavasullasiyarōmañcō // SurSuCa.84

maha (naha) saṅgamagaruyasamullasantamaṇaharapaōharā jhatti
pēccha piē! sañjāyā tujjha saricchā kubēradisā // SurSuCa.85

taralattaṁ nayaṇāṇaṁ kuḍilattaṁ sutaṇu! tujjha kēsāṇaṁ
aṇukaraï pēccha vijjū ghaṇamajjhē cigicigāyantī // SurSuCa.86

annaṁ ca piya! pēcchasu paribbhamantēhiṁ indagōvēhiṁ
najjaï pāusalacchī pacunniyā mahīyalē paḍiyā // SurSuCa.87


[p. 59]
pāusanarindanavasaṅgamammi jāyammi bhūmimahilāē
hariyaṅkuracchalēṇaṁ pēcchasu rōmañcaō jāō // SurSuCa.88

niṭṭhura karapasarēṇaṁ imēṇa santāviā imā puhaī
iya rōsēṇava ruddhō ghaṇēhiṁ sūrassa karapasarō // SurSuCa.89

maha āgamēvi piyavirahiyāṇa mahilāṇa kiṁ na phuṭṭāiṁ
hiyayāiṁ sāmarisaṁ vijjujjōēṇa jōēi // SurSuCa.90

nāuṁ maha āgamaṇaṁ tahavi hu kiṁ calliyā piyā mōttuṁ
gajjantō rōsēṇava pahiyāṇaṁ dalaï hiyayāiṁ // SurSuCa.91

dhavalabalāyādạ̄dhō vijjulayācavaladīhajīhālō
kasaṇaśarīrō dhāvaï pahiyāṇaṁ pāusapisāō // SurSuCa.92

pēccha suracāvaniggayadhārābāṇēhiṁ virahihiyayāiṁ
vindhantō uvahasaïva pañcasaraṁ pañcasarasahiyaṁ // SurSuCa.93


[p. 60]
ētthantarammi dēvī naranāhaṁ bhaṇaï harisitā santī
sēsaüūṇa naravara! abbhahiō pāusō ēsō // SurSuCa.94

mōttūṇa virahiṇijaṇaṁ suhaō jaṁ ēsa kāmuyajaṇassa
pāmaravacchataṇōsahipamuhāṇaṁ tahaya jīvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.95

aha bhaṇaï puhaïnāhō īsiṁ hasēūṇa, dēvi! taṁ saccaṁ
āhīṇaṁ sañjāyaṁ jaṁ summaï ēttha lōgammi // SurSuCa.96

dhāyā purisā pēcchanti āyārā dhāyacaṁ disāvalayaṁ
taha dēvi! tumaṁ suhiyā savvaṁ suhiyanti mannēsi // SurSuCa.97

savvēvi dēvi! uuṇō saünnalōyassa honti suhahēū
punnavihūṇāṇa puṇō pāusasamaōvi duhahēū // SurSuCa.98

ō! pēccha pēccha sundari! addhasamārammi jarakuḍīrammi
ōghasarasayavirāiyavirāiyaḍimbhasamūhē ruyantammi // SurSuCa.99


[p. 61]
niyayaghariṇīē bāḍhaṁ cōijjantō puṇō puṇō varaō
āvaraṇarahiyadēhō hammantō vāridhārāhiṁ // SurSuCa.100

uddhusiyarōmakūvō sīyalaanilēṇa saṅkuiyagattō
ēsō dariddapurisō kahakahavi samāraï kuḍīraṁ // SurSuCa.101

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
ōlambiyakannajuyaṁ hammantaṁ guruyavāridhārāhiṁ
ōluggabhaggadēulakōṇagayaṁ rāsabhaṁ niyasu // SurSuCa.102

taha pēccha imaṁ sundari! suṇahaṁ cullīē sunnagēhammi
sīēṇa kuṇukuṇantaṁ kharakharakhaḍḍaṁ khaṇēmāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.103

taha pēccha jarabaïllā jalaharadhārāvalīhi hammantā
īriyāsamiuvva muṇī vaccanti mahiṁ palōēntā // SurSuCa.104

sēvāliyabhūmitalē phillusamāṇā ya thāmathāmammi
hatthagayalaṭṭhikhaṇḍā bhikkhaṁ pariyaḍaï jararōrō // SurSuCa.105


[p. 62]
ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï dēvīē tāva kañcuī jhatti
pāyavaḍaṇuṭṭhiō aha vasudattō bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.106

dēvēṇa jō u puvviṁ paṭṭhaviō āsi campanayarīē
sirikittivammarannō dūō dāmōdarō nāma // SurSuCa.107

sō dēvapāyadaṁsaṇasuhakaṅkhī āgaō duvārammi
ciṭṭhaï, ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē dēvō pamāṇanti taṁ sōccā // SurSuCa.108

diṭṭhīē āpucchiya dēviṁ sahasatti uṭṭhiō rāyā
atthāṇamaṇḍavassa u āsannō jāva sampattō // SurSuCa.109

tāva ya vijjucamukkāraṇantaraṁ caṇḍacaḍaḍasaṁsaddō
āsannō sañjāō bhēsiyanaranārisaṅghāō // SurSuCa.110

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
tayaṇantaraṁ ca mahāhāravasaṁmīsaṁ samuṭṭhiyaṁ saddaṁ
dēvīgihammi sōuṁ sahasā valiō mahīnāhō // SurSuCa.111


[p. 63]
vajjaraï dēvidhāvī ruyamāṇī dhagdharēṇa saddēṇa
naravara! muṭṭhā muṭṭhā dēvī vijjūē daddhatti // SurSuCa.112

daṭṭhūṇa bhūmipaḍiyaṁ dēvīdēhaṁ jiēṇa paricattaṁ
hā! hā! hatti bhaṇantō rāyā mucchāvasaṁ pattō // SurSuCa.113

daṭṭhūṇa bhūmipaḍiyaṁ naranāhaṁ mucchiyaṁ vigayacēṭṭhaṁ
bhūritarō sañjātō pariyaṇaakkandasaddōvi // SurSuCa.114

pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ sīyalapavaṇāiyammi vihiyammi
rāyāvi vigayamucchō vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattō // SurSuCa.115

hā vallahi! hā sāmiṇi! hā jīviyadāyagē! visālacchi!
hā maha hiyayanivāsiṇi! hā! kattha gayā mamaṁ mōttuṁ? // SurSuCa.116

hā gōradēṁhi! hā pihupaōharē! hā sukōmalasarīrē!
hā kaha nigghiṇavihiṇā tuha uvariṁ pāḍiyā vijjū? // SurSuCa.117


[p. 64]
ghaṇasāraghusiṇacaccaṇaüciyasarīrammi kaha ṇu hayavihiṇā
vijjūnivāō vihiō majjha aünnēhiṁ pāvēṇa? // SurSuCa.118

hā dēvi tujjha virahē nāranārīsaṅkulaṁ imaṁ nayaraṁ
uvvasiṁyanayarasarisaṁ aḍavisamāṇaṁ ca paḍihāi // SurSuCa.119

kila dēvi! taṁ bhaṇantī tuha virahē acchiuṁ na sakkēmi
taṁ kaha ahaṁ ahannō tumaē sahasā pariccatō // SurSuCa.120

hā! kiṁ na kimpi jampasi kiṁvā taṁ suyaṇu! majjha ruṭṭhā si
kiṁva maē avaraddhaṁ sundari! taṁ majjha sāhēsu? // SurSuCa.121

taṁ ciya maha vallahiyā nēhō maha natthi annaïtthīsu
tujjha kaē paricattō sayalō ōrōhanārijaṇō // SurSuCa.122

tahavi tumaṁ kiṁ sundarī! nibbhararattassa dēsi nālāvaṁ?
tā pasiya pasiya sāmiṇi! uṭṭhiya maha dēsu paḍivayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.123


[p. 65]
ēmāi jāva vilavaï vivihaṁ rāyā sakaluṇasaddēṇa
tāva ahaṁ sampattō rōvantō tattha dhaṇadēva! // SurSuCa.124

ucchaṅgē viṇivēsiya mamaṁ taō gāḍhakaluṇasaddēṇa
taṁ cēva palavamāṇō sudīharaṁ ruvaï bālōvva // SurSuCa.125

ētthantarammi mantī sumaīnāmō bhaṇaï naranāha
dēva! alaṁ runnēṇa mayakiccaṁ kuṇaha dēvīē // SurSuCa.126

bhaṇaï taō naranāhō candaṇadārūṇi bāhiṁ nīṇēha
dēvīē jēṇa samayaṁ ahampi aggīē vissāmi // SurSuCa.127

tō bhaṇaï sumaïmantī kāyarajaṇacēṭṭhiēṇa kiṁ imiṇā
maraṇa 'jjhavasāaiṇaṁ, avalambasu dhīra! dhīrattaṁ // SurSuCa.128

maraṇēṇa tujjha naravara! dēsō savvōvi hōi jaṁ gammō
paḍivakkhanaravarāṇaṁ bālō taha supaïṭṭhotti // SurSuCa.129


[p. 66]
dēvāṇaṁ bambhaṇāṇa ya ligīṇaṁ taha pāgayajaṇassa
dhammakiriyāō savvā vahanti dēvē dharantammi // SurSuCa.130

mahilāmēttassa kaē na hu juttaṁ tumha uttamanarāṇa
asamañjasamāyariuṁ vinnāyajagassabhāvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.131

aviya niruvakkamakāyassavi usabhajiṇindassa āidēvassa
maraṇaṁ jāyaṁ jaïyā kā gaṇaṇā annamaṇuēsu? // SurSuCa.132

nijjiyapaḍivakkhassavi chakkhaṇḍamahīsarassa bharahassa
jaïyā jāyaṁ maraṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annamaṇuēsu // SurSuCa.133

garuyaparakkamanijjiyariubalapāikkaccakkakayarakkhā
sōṇḍīrā naravaïṇō sōmajasā ' 'iccajasapamuhā // SurSuCa.134

jaï tāva tē ya nihāyā pāvakayantēṇa nigghiṇamaṇēṇa
anivāriyapasarēṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annalōyammi? // SurSuCa.135

[yugmam]

[p. 67]
jēsimpi ya tittīsaṁ āuyamudahīṇa pavaradēvāṇaṁ
tēsimpi hōi cavaṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annasattēsu? // SurSuCa.136

bhavaṇavaïvāṇamantarajōisiyāṇaṁ vimaṇavāsīṇaṁ
jaï nāma hōi cavaṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā maṇuyalōyammi? // SurSuCa.137

sō kōvi natthi jīvō tilōyamajjhammi jō vasaṁ na gaō
maccussa pāvamaïṇō mōttuṁ siddhē suhasamiddhē // SurSuCa.138

iya kālakavaliyaṁ pēcchiūṇa sayalampi tihuaṇaṁ dēva!
jāyammi dēvimaraṇē kiṁ sōgaṁ kuṇaha vihalaṁ tu? // SurSuCa.139

jujjaï kāuṁ sōgō maraṇaṁ jaï hōjja tīē ēkkāē
sāhāraṇammi maraṇē kō sōgō kiṁva runnēṇa? // SurSuCa.140

aïtaṇutaṇaggasaṅgayajalalavatullammi jīviyavvammi
niddāsaṅgē jaṁ puṇa uṭṭhijjaï taṁ mahacchariyaṁ // SurSuCa.141


[p. 68]
iya lōyassa sarūvaṁ kuviyakayantassa ērisaṁ daṭṭhuṁ
dēvimaraṇammi naravara! na hu juttaṁ sōgakaraṇanti // SurSuCa.142

ēvaṁ ca bahuvigappaṁ bhaṇiō sō sumaïṇā naravarindō
takkāluciyaṁ savvaṁ maïkiccaṁ kuṇaï dēvīē // SurSuCa.143

kaïvayadiṇāiṁ paricattalōyasambhāvaṇāivāvārō
gahagahiō iva ciṭṭhaï rāyā dēvīē sōgēṇa // SurSuCa.144

sumaïmuhēhiṁ tāvaya nāṇāvihasōyamōyaṇapaḍūhiṁ
bōhijjantō girāhiṁ jāō kālēṇa gayasōgō // SurSuCa.145

nāūṇa aṭṭhavarisaṁ mamaṁ taō garuyaputtanēhēṇa
saṅgahiya uvajjhāyaṁ gāhēi kalāṇasandōhaṁ // SurSuCa.146

gahiē kalākalāvē gāmasahassaṁ tayā mahaṁ dinnaṁ
maha daṁsaṇēṇa rāyā sāhāraï dēvivirahampi // SurSuCa.147


[p. 0५9]
aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō jhatti
paṇamiya duvāravālō vajjaraï sūhavō ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.148

campāpurīō sāmiya! mahantaō kittidhammanaravaïṇō
dēvassa daṁsaṇatthaṁ ciṭṭhaï paḍihārabhūmīē // SurSuCa.149

sigghaṁ pavēsasutti ya bhaṇiē sō rāiṇā aṇunnāō
āgamma vihiyaviṇaō uvaviṭṭhō uciyaṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.150

tambōlāipayacchaṇapuvvaṁ sō rāiṇā samullaviō
āgamakāraṇaṁ bhō! sāhasu tō bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.151

campāē puravarīē supasiddhō cēva dēvapāyāṇaṁ
vitthāriyavimalakittī rāyā sirikittidhammō 'tthi // SurSuCa.152

nijjiyasurindasundarirūvātisayā samatthamahilāṇa
abbhahiyā sē dēvī kittimaī lōyavikkhāyā // SurSuCa.153


[p. 70]
tīya dhūyā sōhaggarūvaviṇṇāṇagāravagdhaviyā
pāyālakannayasamā kaṇayavaī nāma varakannā // SurSuCa.154

sampattajōvvaṇā sā ābharaṇavibhūsiyā piusayāsē
paṭṭhaviyā māūē taduciyavaradāṇaaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.155

āgamma pāyapaḍiyā piuṇā sā saharisaṁ niucchaṅgē
viṇivēsiya avagụ̄dhā bhaṇiyā ya imaṁ tu sā kannā // SurSuCa.156

putti! niyahiyayaïṭṭhaṁ sāmantamahantayāṇa majjhammi
sāhasu jēṇa tuhaṁ sō kijjaï bhattā, kimannēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.157

ēvaṁ piuṇā bhaṇiyā lajjāē ahōmuhī ṭhiyā bālā
puṇaruttaṁ puṭṭhāvi hu na kiñci paḍiuttaraṁ dēi // SurSuCa.158

tō cintiuṁ payattō ēyā lajjāluyā imā varaī
na hu sakkaï vajjariuṁ ēsō maha tāya! iṭṭhotti // SurSuCa.159


[p. 71]
tā cintēmi sayaṁ ciya aṇurūvamimīē pavarabhattāraṁ
vinnāṇarūvasampayakaliyaṁ varavaṁsaüppannaṁ // SurSuCa.160

khaṇamēgamacchiūṇaṁ rāyā cintāurō bhaṇaï tattō
putti! tuha rūvasarisō bhattā laddhō maē iṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.161

siddhatthapurē rāyā suggīvō nāma maha paraṁ mittaṁ
tassa tumaṁ gaccha lahuṁ sayaṁvarā, ēttha kiṁ bahuṇā? // SurSuCa.162

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiyamēttē sā kannā dēva! tumha nāmēṇa
nisuēṇaṁ ciya jāyā harisavasullasiyarōmañcā // SurSuCa.163

nāūṇa tīē bhāvaṁ rāyā sampēkkhiuṇa maha vayaṇaṁ
vajjaraï, taṁ mahābala! vaccasu siddhatthanayarammi // SurSuCa.164

ghēttuṁ sayaṁvaramimaṁ kaṇagavaïṁ bhūribhūisañjuttaṁ
kaïvayabalasañjuttō sōhaṇatihikaraṇanakkhatō // SurSuCa.165

[yugmam]

[p. 72]
jaṁ āṇavēsi bhaṇiuṁ tattō haṁ taṁ gahīya sañcaliō
jāva ya kamēṇa ēttō jōyaṇamēttammi sampattō // SurSuCa.166

ajja rayaṇīvirāmē kaïvayaturaēhiṁ vēgavantēhiṁ
uggiliya āgaō huṁ tumhāṇa piyaṁ nivēēmi // SurSuCa.167

dēva! mahamēyamāgamaṇakāraṇaṁ pucchiyaṁ hi jaṁ tumaē
ēvaṁ cavatthiyammi sampaï dēvō pamāṇanti // SurSuCa.168

harisāūriyahiyaō aha rāyā bhaṇaï pariyaṇaṁ niyayaṁ
mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ nayarē kannaṁ pavēsēha // SurSuCa.169

tō pariyaṇēṇa sammaṁ tahatti sampāḍiyammi vayaṇammi
sōhaṇalaggē rannā pariṇīyā tattha kaṇagavaī // SurSuCa.170

sā rannō kaṇagavaī kālēṇa aīva vallahā jāyā
maha māūē ṭhāṇē vihiyā aha paṭṭabaddhā sā // SurSuCa.171


[p. 73]
aïvallahampi vīsaraï māṇūsaṁ dēsakālaantariyaṁ
vallīsamaṁ hi pimmaṁ jaṁ āsannaṁ tahiṁ caḍaï // SurSuCa.172

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ maha piuṇō tīē gāḍharattassa
sịdhilīkayasēsōrōharamaṇigamaṇāicēṭṭhassa // SurSuCa.173

aha annayā kayāivi kaṇagavaīē suō samuppannō
surahotti vihiyanāmō pattō sō kumarabhāvammi // SurSuCa.174

annadiyahammi ēyaṁ ēgantē bhaṇaï kaṇagavaī dēvī
juvarāyapaē kiṁ navi ahisiccaï dēva! mē puttō // SurSuCa.175

tō bhaṇaï naravarindō jēṭṭhē puttammi suppaïṭṭhammi
vijjantē na hu juttaṁ juvarāyaṁ ṭhāviuṁ surahaṁ // SurSuCa.176

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō jēṭṭhaṭṭhavaṇē nihōḍaü kō ṇu?
jaï tujjha ahaṁ daïyā tā surahaṁ kuṇasu juyarāyaṁ // SurSuCa.177


[p. 74]
tāhē rannā bhaṇiyaṁ suṭṭhuṁ piyā taṁ sulōyaṇē! majjha
kintu imassa 'ṇurattā sāmantamahantayā savvē // SurSuCa.178

taha ēsō susamatthō ēvaṁ vihiē vihējja taṁ kimpi
avamāṇiō hu jēṇaṁ mamāvi rajjaṁ avaharējjā // SurSuCa.179

tō bhaṇaï hasiya dēvī ērisasattēṇa kaha tumaṁ vihiṇā
piyayama! rāyā vihiō navari kirāḍō kaō hontō? // SurSuCa.180

jēṇēva suppaïṭṭhō ērisaō ukkaḍō payāvēṇa
tēṇēva imaṁ sigghaṁ kaṭṭhaharē khivasu jattēṇa // SurSuCa.181

tattō ya majjha puttaṁ juvarāyaṁ ṭhāviuṁ payattēṇa
acchasu vigayāsaṅkō rajjaṁ ca mamaṁ ca māṇantō // SurSuCa.182

ēvaṁ dēvīvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ paḍiuttaraṁ adāūṇaṁ
rāyā samuṭṭhiūṇaṁ atthāṇē gantumuvaviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.183


[p. 75]
ēyaṁ ca dēvivayaṇaṁ sūhaviyānāmiyāē cēḍīē
pacchannē sōūṇaṁ savvaṁ dhaṇadēva! maha siṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.184

taṁ sōuṁ maha vigappō cittē ēyārisō samuppannō
kiṁ kaṇagavaīē vuttō karējja ēvaṁ piyā majjha? // SurSuCa.185

ahavā na gaṇanti puvvanēhaṁ na ya nīiṁ nēya lōyaavavāyaṁ
na ya bhāviāvayāō purisā mahilāṇa āyattā // SurSuCa.186

tā jā na kimpi annaṁ dēvīvayaṇāō maha piyā kuṇaï
tāva ahiṭṭhēmi sayaṁ rajjaṁ, piyaraṁ viṇāsēttā // SurSuCa.187

ahava na ēyaṁ juttaṁ vivēyajuttassa majjha kāuṁ jē
tā bandhiūṇa piyaraṁ kaṭṭhaharagayaṁ aṇucarāmi // SurSuCa.188

kiṁvā kaṇagavaïṁ ciya saha surahēṇaṁ nayāmi jamavayaṇē
kiṁvā kaṭṭhaharammi dōnnivi ghēttēmi bandhaüṁ? // SurSuCa.189


[p. 76]
ahavā kiṁ maha imiṇā pēkkhāmō tāva jaṁ piyā kuṇaï
adiṭṭhapāṇiyammi na hu juttaṁ pāṇahummuyaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.190

aha rāyā maha uvariṁ diṇē diṇē piyayamāē bhannantō
jāō sịdhilasiṇēhō kannavisaṁ jaṁ mahantavisaṁ // SurSuCa.191

sahasatti annadiyahē kimpi misaṁ dāviūṇa maha rannā
hariyaṁ gāmasahassaṁ dinnaṁ lahukhēḍayaṁ ēkkaṁ // SurSuCa.192

sañjāyaamarisēṇaṁ tāhē maē cintiyaṁ durāyāraṁ
mārēūṇa ēyaṁ rajjamahiṭṭhēmi, kiṁ bahuṇā? // SurSuCa.193

ahavā na puvvapurisēhiṁ majjhaṁ vaṁsē kayaṁ imaṁ pāvaṁ
tamahampi kaha karōmī asārarajjassa kajjēṇa? // SurSuCa.194

mahilāvayaṇēṇa imō rāgandhō kuṇaï, kuṇaü annāyaṁ
maha puṇa vivēyajuttassa handi! na hu ērisaṁ juttaṁ // SurSuCa.195


[p. 77]
tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ avamāṇaṁ tāva dūsahaṁ piuṇō
appavahōvi na juttō dēsaccāō paraṁ juttō // SurSuCa.196

gantūṇamannadēsaṁ tamhā sēvāmi annanaranāhaṁ
huṁ tampi hu nahu juttaṁ avamāṇapayaṁ hi sēvatti // SurSuCa.197

suggīvanarindasuō juyarāyā āsi ēsa riddhijuō
sampaï puṇa vaṇṭhōiva kaha sēvaṁ kuṇaï bhiccāṇa? // SurSuCa.198

ēmāivayaṇavittharavajjaraṇasamujjaēṇa lōēṇaṁ
daṁsijjantō riūṇa kahaṁ gēhēsuṁ paribhamissaṁ? // SurSuCa.199

tamhā kaïvayaniyapurisaparigaō akayaannajaṇasēvō
gantuṁ ciṭṭhāmi ahaṁ kammivi paccantadēsammi // SurSuCa.200

jā jīvaï ēsa piyā ēyammi mayammi puṇa jahā juttaṁ
taïya cciya kāhāmō kiṁ iṇhiṁ tīē cintāē? // SurSuCa.201


[p. 78]
ēvaṁ viṇicchiyamaī kaïvayapiyapariyaṇēṇa pariyariō
sāmantamantipuranāyagēhiṁ rannā ya annāō // SurSuCa.202

nīhariō tattō haṁ kamēṇa aha pāviuṁ imaṁ palliṁ
sīhaguhaṁ nāmēṇa acchiumēīē pāraddhaṁ // SurSuCa.203

miliyā majjha aṇēgē bhillā cōrā kukammanirayā ya
tēhiṁ parivāriō haṁ sampaï pallīvaī jāō // SurSuCa.204

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ tumhāṇaṁ kaha ṇu ēttha āvāsō
uttamanarāṇa pāviṭṭhalōyajōgāē pallīē? // SurSuCa.205

ēyaṁ saṅkhēvēṇaṁ kahiyamavatthāṇakāraṇaṁ ēttha
taṁ tuha dhaṇadēva! maē garuyasiṇēhēṇa savvampi // SurSuCa.206

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ avvō! jaṇaōpi ērisaṁ kuṇaï
avamāṇaṁ puttāṇaṁ dhī! dhī! saṁsāravāsassa // SurSuCa.207


[p. 79]
so cciya kajjavasēṇaṁ vallahaō hōi ēttha saṁsārē
kāraṇavasēṇa sōvi hu riuvva vēsō jaṇō hōi // SurSuCa.208

paramatthaō na kōvi hu piō va sattū va atthi lōgammi
naï māyā nēya piyā sakajjavasaō jaṇō savvō // SurSuCa.209

puttōvi sattusarisō dīsaï niyakāraṇē apujjantē
piuṇā suviṇīōvi hu dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa // SurSuCa.210

taṁ ciya kumāra! mahappā taṁ ciya pasamassa laddhaparamatthō
taṁ ciya vivēyajuttō tumae cciya maṇḍiyā vasuhā // SurSuCa.211

piuṇā 'vamāṇiōvi hu annaṁ asamañjasaṁ akāūṇaṁ
santammi balē tahavi hu dēsaccāō kaō jēṇa // SurSuCa.212

ēmāivayaṇavittharaavarōpparavaḍḍhamāṇanēhāṇaṁ
tāṇaṁ pañca va satta va vōlīṇā vāsarā jāva // SurSuCa.213


[p. 80]
tāvaya samatthasatthaṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ gamaṇaücchugībhūyaṁ
dhaṇadēvō āpucchaï gamaṇatthaṁ suppaïṭṭhaṁ taṁ // SurSuCa.214

tumha viōgō dūsahō ēsō satthō samucchugībhūō
taṁ kumārō! amha jāyaṁ ēttha taḍī ēttha vagghotti // SurSuCa.215

ēēṇaṁ ciya nēcchanti sāhavō sajjaṇēhiṁ saṁsaggiṁ
jamhā viōgavihuriyahiyayassa na ōsahaṁ annaṁ // SurSuCa.216

[yugmam]
jahavi hu vahaï na jīhā ērisavayaṇē samullavijjantē
tahavi hu bhaṇāmi muñcasu gacchāmō sampayaṁ amhē // SurSuCa.217

tā kimpi cintiūṇaṁ khaṇantaraṁ dīhara ca nīsasiuṁ
vajjaraï suppaïṭṭhō savisāyaṁ ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.218

amhārisēhiṁ gihamāgayāṇa tumhārisāṇaṁ suyaṇāṇaṁ
kō uvayārō kīraü ērisaṭhāṇē vasantēhiṁ? // SurSuCa.219


[p. 81]
tahavi hu bhaṇāmi kiñcivi kāyavvō nēva patthaṇābhaṅgō
jēṇa parakajjasāhaṇanirayā khalu sajjaṇā honti // SurSuCa.220

tattō phurantanimmalama ūhavicchu riyadasadisā ' 'bhōgō
ēkkōvi aṇēgaguṇō pavaramaṇī tassa uvaṇīō // SurSuCa.221

daṭṭhuṁ divvamaṇiṁ taṁ dīsantāṇēyalakkhaṇaṁ vimalaṁ
viyasiyalōyaṇajualō aha dhaṇadēvō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.222

ērisapavaramaṇīṇaṁ maṇussakhēttammi sambhavō natthi
navaraṁ jaï suralōgē havējja na hu annakhēttammi // SurSuCa.223

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyammivi tahavi hu kōūhalaṁ mahaṁ hiyaē
tō bhaṇasu kaha ṇu jāyā sampattī tumha ēyassa? // SurSuCa.224

tō bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumē bhadda!
māṇusakhēttasamutthō na hōi ēsō maṇī tāva // SurSuCa.225


[p. 82]
kintu suralōgajāō ēsō sampāviō jahamhēhiṁ
taṁ ēgamaṇō hōu jaï kōugamatthi tō suṇasu // SurSuCa.226

puvvaṁ ēgammi diṇē pabhāyasamayammi gahiyakōdaṇḍā
caliō kaïvayaniyapurisaparigaō migavahaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.227

uttaradisāmuhō haṁ gāumēttammi bhūmibhāgammi
ghaṇapattalataruvarasaṅkulami viyarāmi jāva vaṇē // SurSuCa.228

tāva ya nisuō saddō dūsahagurudukkhasūyaō kaluṇō
āgāsē mahilāē saghaggharaṁ rōyamāṇīē // SurSuCa.229

[yugmam]
hā! kaha majjha nimittē piyayama! atigaruyaāvayaṁ pattō?
hā! ajjaütta! iṇhiṁ tuha virahē natthi maha jīyaṁ // SurSuCa.230

tadaṇantaraṁ ca kēṇavi hakkiya aïniṭṭhuraṁ samullaviyaṁ
kattō maha vasagāē sāhārō tujjha ēēṇa? // SurSuCa.231


[p. 83]
taṁ sōūṇaṁ majjhaṁ maṇammi kōūhalaṁ samuppannaṁ
jāva ya dōṇṇi va tiṇṇi va vaccāmi payāiṁ tā nisuō // SurSuCa.232

ēgammi vaṇaniguñjē adissamāṇassa kassavi narassa
gurudukkhasūyaṇaparō mandō nitthaṇaṇasaṁsaddō // SurSuCa.233

[yugmam]
tattō mahantakōūhalēṇa tattōmuhō ahaṁ caliō
pēcchāmi sambalitaruṁ saralaṁ uttuṅgamaïgaruyaṁ // SurSuCa.234

daṁsaṇamēttuppāiyaaïgaruyabhaēhiṁ rattanēttēhiṁ
kasiṇasarīrasamubmūyabhūripahābhariyagayaṇēhiṁ // SurSuCa.235

nimmalamaṇivalayasamucchalantakantīē payaḍavayaṇēhiṁ
gururōsavasaviyambhiyaphāraphaṇāghōrabhuyagēhiṁ // SurSuCa.236

dīharalalantajīhāsahassavipphuraṇabhīijaṇagēhiṁ
asarisaamarisavasavippamukkaphuṅkārasaddēhiṁ // SurSuCa.237


[p. 84]
aïgaruyapannagēhiṁ samantaō vẹ̄dhiyō aṇēgēhiṁ
ēgō divvāgārō purisō diṭṭhō ahē tassa // SurSuCa.238

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
aïdūsahaviyaṇāvasavimukkapuṇaruttamandahuṅkāraṁ
ākaṇṭhavẹ̄dhiyaṁ taṁ daṭṭhuṁ purisaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.239

dhī! dhī! hayavihiṇō vilasiyassa asamikkhiyassa ēyassa
ēyārisēvi purisē ērisadukkhaṁ karēntassa // SurSuCa.240

ēmāi maē paridēviyammi bhaṇiyaṁ imaṁ taō tēṇaṁ
alamimiṇā tē paridēviēṇa suṇa tāva maha vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.241

ciṭṭhaï cūḍāē mahaṁ majjhē baddhō phurantakiraṇillō
divvō maṇīṇa pavarō maṇī bhuyaṅgōhaviddavaṇō // SurSuCa.242

jassa pabhāvēṇa imē ḍasiumaṇāvi hu cayanti nō ḍasiuṁ
ghōravisāvi hu sappā sappanti na baddhavayaṇavva // SurSuCa.243


[p. 85]
taṁ ghēttūṇaṁ varamaṇiṁ siñcasu salilēṇa tēṇa tō pacchā
acchōḍēsu bhuyaṅgē aṅgavilaggē mahamaṇēgē // SurSuCa.244

āmanti bhaṇantēṇaṁ tavvayaṇaṁ sāyaraṁ kayaṁ savvaṁ
acchōḍiyā jalēṇaṁ jhatti vilīṇā aha bhuyaṅgā // SurSuCa.245

aviya maṇisalilēṇaṁ sittā khaṇēṇa savvēvi pāviyā vilayaṁ
kharajālāvalijalaṇōvatāviyā mayaṇapiṇḍavva // SurSuCa.246

aha sō paṇaṭṭhaviyaṇō sīyalataruchāhiyāē uvaviṭṭhō
mahapurisakayasukōmalakisalayasañchaṇṇasantharaē // SurSuCa.247

ābhaṭṭhō paḍhamaṁ ca tēṇa ahayaṁ kattō tumaṁ āgatō,
kiṁvā nāma kahiṁ kulammi vimalē jāō si, kō tē piyā?

ēvaṁ bhō dhaṇadēva! tēṇa taïyā puṭṭhē maē sāhiyā
puvvuttā sayalāvi tujjha kahiyā jā sā paüttī tahiṁ // SurSuCa.248


[p. 86]
sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsō ēttha samappaï vijjāharamōyaṇotti nāmēṇa
surasundarināmāē kahāē bīō paricchēō // SurSuCa.500

aha sōvi maē puṭṭhō kēṇa tumaṁ ērisāē ghōrāē
khittō si āvayāē kēṇa va kajjēṇa bhadda! muhā // SurSuCa.1

ēvaṁ ca pucchiō sō sadukkhamaïdīharaṁ ca nīsasiuṁ

aha sō bhaṇaï subhaṇiō saṁsārē rōgamōhiyamaṇāṇaṁ

na hu cōjjamāvayāhiṁ anijantiyakaraṇavaggāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.4


[p. 87]

aha bhaṇaï bhō sundara! jaï ēvaṁ suṭṭhu tumha nibbandhō

siddhāyayaṇapariṭṭhiyajiṇabimbaccaṇanimittamintīhiṁ

aïmahurabhāraīē ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇammi cāraṇamuṇīhiṁ

puvvāvarasāgarapāviēṇa hōūṇa majjhadēsammi

[p. 90]
suvisāladakkhiṇuttaravibhattasẹ̄dhīdugēṇa sōhillō

[navabhiḥ kulakam]
tatthatthi dakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē khayaralōyapaḍipunnaṁ

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]

[p. 91]

jammadiṇe cciya puranaracittacamukkārakārayaṁ majjha

kamasō ya bārasāhē vōlīṇē majjha jaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ
guratuṭṭhīē païṭṭhiyamahihāṇaṁ cittavēgotti // SurSuCa.25

vōlīṇēsu ya kaïvayavarisēsu ahaṁ mahantabuddhissa

[p. 92]

aha kamasō sampattō ahayaṁ navajōvvaṇārambhaṁ // SurSuCa.29

pasarantapavararayaṇōrudittivicchuriyanahayalā ' 'bhōyā

[yugmam]

[p. 9५]
annaṁ ca pañcasaralōddhaēṇaṁ mahumāsabiijjaēṇa dayarahiyaṁ

[p. 96]

jiṇabimbāṇaṁ bhattīē tēṇa ēē samāgayā dēvā

[yugmam]
aha savvēhivi bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti suṭṭhu tē bhaṇiyaṁ

[p. 99]

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
