[yuggam]
pūiya jiṇindabimbē kāuṁ cīivandaṇaṁ jahāvihiṇā
bāhiṁ nīhariō haṁ uvaviṭṭhō khayaramajjhammi // SurSuCa.75

vattē jiṇamajjaṇaē iō taō tattha sañcarantō haṁ
avarōpparadaṁsiyakōugēhiṁ sahiō vayaṁsēhiṁ // SurSuCa.76


[p. 100]
katthaï vilāsiṇijaṇaṁ pēcchantō naccamāṇayaṁ vivihaṁ
katthaï kavivaranivahaṁ jiṇacariyaṁ ahiṇavēmāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.77

vīṇāravasaṁvaliyaṁ katthavi gīyajjhuṇiṁ nisāmēntō
viraïyavivihāyāraṁ katthavi ya baliṁ palōēntō // SurSuCa.78

katthaï taruṇanarēhiṁ dijjantaṁ rāsayaṁ suṇēmāṇō
surasundarīhiṁ katthaï gijjantaṁ dhavalasaṅghāyaṁ // SurSuCa.79

ēvaṁ ca jāva kōūhalēṇa avarāvarēsu ṭhāṇēsu
hiṇḍāmi tattha bhavaṇē līlāē samaṁ vayaṁsēhiṁ // SurSuCa.80

tāva maha māulasuō saharisamāgamma sāiyaṁ dāuṁ
vajjaraï bhāṇuvēgō pabhūyakālāō diṭṭhō si // SurSuCa.81

[yugmam]
kusalaṁ ca pavaṇagaïṇō piubhagiṇīē ya baülavaïyāē?
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kusalaṁ savvēsi, annaṁ ca // SurSuCa.82


[p. 101]
ētthēva āgayāi imāiṁ ciṭṭhanti bhadda! jiṇabhavaṇē
ammāpiūṇa mūlaṁ samāgaō tēṇa sahiō haṁ // SurSuCa.83

sāyaramavagụ̄dhō sō tēhiṁ paüttiṁ ca pucchiō bhaṇaï
kusalaṁ maha jaṇagāṇaṁ nāgamaṇaṁ kāraṇāvēkkhaṁ // SurSuCa.84

aha sō maē pabhaṇiō vittappāyā imā hu jiṇajattā
sampaï puṇa amhāṇaṁ āgacchasu pāhuṇō tāva // SurSuCa.85

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu nisuṇēsu
maha cittabhāṇupiuṇā lahumāgacchējja iti bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.86

tā cittavēga! sampaï taṁ ciya nagarammi ēhi mahataṇaē
ukkaṇṭhiō pagāmaṁ jaṁ acchaï tumha māulaō // SurSuCa.87

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō ammāpīīhiṁ abbhaṇunnāō
bhāusamēō pattō nagaramahaṁ kuñjarāvattaṁ // SurSuCa.88


[p. 102]
tahiṁya ca cittabhāṇū maṁ daṭṭhūṁ suṭṭhu harisiō bhaṇaï
sundaramāyariyaṁ tē jamāgaō amha pāhuṇaō // SurSuCa.89

niyayapaüttiṁ savvaṁ kahiuṁ kayabhōyaṇāivāvārō
pattāē rayaṇīē pāsuttō pavarasayaṇīē // SurSuCa.90

tattha ya pabhāyasamaē lavamāṇē tambacūlaniurambē
diṭṭhō adiṭṭhapuvvō ēsō sumiṇō maē taïyā // SurSuCa.91

kila dhavalaphullamālaṁ maṇōharaṁ daṭṭhu taggahaṭṭhāē
caliō haṁ na ya sakkēmi gēṇhiuṁ taṁ jayā kahavi // SurSuCa.92

kēṇavi mittēṇa taō samappiyā āyarēṇa mē gahiyā
ōlambissaṁ galaē kila niyaē tāva sā jhatti // SurSuCa.93

paḍiyā maha hatthāō katthavi ya gayatti nēya jāṇāmi
tāhē mahantadukkhaṁ tavvirahē majjha sañjāyaṁ // SurSuCa.94

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]

[p. 103]
sukkāvi maē ēsā puṇōvi amilāṇakusumiyā vihiyā
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ kēṇavi kaṇṭhē viṇivēsiyā majjha // SurSuCa.95

tāva paḍupaṭahajhallarikāhalabhambhāmaündasaddālaṁ
sōuṁ tūrassa ravaṁ jhatti paṇaṭṭhā mahaṁ niddā // SurSuCa.96

tō harisavisāyaḍḍhaṁ daṭṭhuṁ sumiṇaṁ vicintiyaṁ hiyaē
kiṁ nāma majjha sūyaï adiṭṭhapuvvaṁ imaṁ sumiṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.97

kā handi! imā mālā vijjā va sampayā va maha hōjjā
dinnā kēṇavi naṭṭhā puṇaravi laddhā, na yāṇāmi // SurSuCa.98

ēvaṁ aṇicchiyatthō suviṇasarūvassa uṭṭhiō ahayaṁ
kāuṁ pabhāyakiccaṁ aha sahiō bhāṇuvēgēṇa // SurSuCa.99

ārụ̄dhō pāsāē uvarimabhūmīē cittasālāē
maṇirayaṇakōṭṭimammī uvaviṭṭhō mattavāraṇaē // SurSuCa.100

[yugmam]

[p. 104]
aha taṁ pabhāyadiṭṭhaṁ siṭṭhaṁ suviṇaṁ tu bhāṇuvēgassa
nicchaïuṁ nō sakkaï sōvi hu suviṇassa sabbhāvaṁ // SurSuCa.101

cintittā suviṇaphalaṁ vigappasaṅkappakhittaniyacittā
jā ciṭṭhāmō amhē khaṇantaraṁ tattha ṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.102

tāva ya varanēvatthō mahagghaābharamabhūsiyasarīrō
savvō vi nayaralōō gantuṁ katthavi payaṭṭōti // SurSuCa.103

[yugmam]
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ sabālavuḍ̣dhō imō jaṇō kattha
kayaüvasōhō vaccaï sāhasu bhō bhāṇuvēgamha? // SurSuCa.104

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa nisuṇasu ajjaṁ jaṁ mayaṇatērasī bhadda!
mayarandujjāṇaṭhiyassa tēṇa jattāē mayaṇassa // SurSuCa.105

ēsō naranārigaṇō pūyatthaṁ tassa vaccaï pamōyā
amhēvi hu gacchāmō pēcchāmō kusumasarajattaṁ // SurSuCa.106

[yugmam]

[p. 105]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti dōvi sañcaliyā
kayasiṅgārā payaō pattā ya kamēṇa ujjāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.107

kīlantakāmiṇīyaṇaraṇantanēuraravēṇa taruniyarō
mayaṇamahūsavatuṭṭhō gāyaï iva caccariṁ jattha // SurSuCa.108

malayānilahallāviyasāhāhiṁ vighummamāṇayā dhaṇiyaṁ
kōilakayakalakōlāhalēhiṁ aphuḍakravārālāvā // SurSuCa.109

āyambiranavakisilayaāyambamuhā mahīruhā jattha
āsāiyamahumāsā mattā iva saccavijjanti // SurSuCa.110

[yugmam]
suvisaṭṭakusumasōhantamañjarīpuñjaraïyasēharayā
jōhārēntativa pavaṇōṇayāhiṁ sāhāhiṁ paürajaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.111

tammi ya pavarujjāṇē ghaṇataruvaramaṇḍiē suramaṇīē
daṁsaṇamēttupāiyamayaṇē mayarandanāmammi // SurSuCa.112


[p. 106]
nāṇānēvatthēṇaṁ nāyaralōēṇa parigayā jāva
pavisāmō tā diṭṭhaṁ dūrāō mayaṇadēvaharaṁ // SurSuCa.113

[yugmam]
raïjuttamayaṇapūyaṇanimittamittēṇa paüralōēṇa
paḍipunnaṁ suvilāsaṁ uttuṅgaṁ tuṅgapāgāraṁ // SurSuCa.114

uddāmavajjantaaccantavaramaddalaṁ mattavarakāmiṇīsaṅghakayagundalaṁ
caccarīsaddaakkhittakāmuyajaṇaṁ paḍahiyāsaddanaccantabahuvāmaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.115

piyayamāsattanararuddhakayalīharaṁ dōliyārūḍhapurabāliyāsundaraṁ
saviḍavēsājaṇāraddhajalakīḍayaṁ salilasampāyakayakaddamuppīlayaṁ // SurSuCa.116

taṁ majjhē pavisittā daṭṭhūṇa raīē sañjuyaṁ mayaṇaṁ
niggantūṇaṁ dōṇṇivi uvaviṭṭhā bāravēīē // SurSuCa.117

nāṇavihakīlāhiṁ kīlantaṁ purajaṇaṁ pulōēntō
jāva khaṇantaramēgaṁ kumara! ahaṁ tattha acchāmi // SurSuCa.118


[p. 107]
tāvāsannammi dumē andōlintī sahīṇa majjhagayā
diṭṭhā aüvvarūvā juvaī navajōvvaṇārambhā // SurSuCa.119

pīṇunnayaghaṇasihiṇucchalantahārāvalīē kayasōhā
uttattakaṇayavannā maṇikuḍaṁlamaṇḍiyakavōlā // SurSuCa.120

amayamaïyavva vihiṇā vihiyā kayalōyalōyaṇāṇandā
daṁsaṇamēttēṇaṁ ciya palhāyantī jaṇamaṇāiṁ // SurSuCa.121

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ cintiyaṁ mē kā ēsā handi! maṇaharasaruvā
kiṁ nāgakannagēsā avaïnnā, ahava vaṇalacchī? // SurSuCa.122

kiṁvā suralōgāō pabbhaṭṭhā tiyasasundarī ēsā
kiṁvā mayaṇaviutta hōjja raī gahiyadēhatti? // SurSuCa.123

ēvaṁ vigappamāṇō aṇamisanayaṇēhiṁ taṁ pulōēntō
tīēvi pulōiō haṁ sasiṇiddhaavaṅgadiṭṭhīē // SurSuCa.124


[p. 108]
puṭṭhō ya bhāṇuvēgō kā ēsā kassa vāvi mahilatti?
īsīsivihasiuṇaṁ aha bhaṇiyaṁ bhāṇuvēgēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.125

ēīē saṅkahāē na hu kajjaṁ kiñci uṭṭhimō tāva
ēsā huṁ vaṅkavaṅkaṁ jōyaï tuha saṁmuhaṁ jēṇa // SurSuCa.126

aṅgēsu nivaḍamāṇā diṭṭhī ēvaṁvihāṇa mahilāṇa
dēhaṁ kuṇaï asatthaṁ avassa hiyayaṁ avaharējjā // SurSuCa.127

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ parihāsaparō si amhē ēmēva
pucchāmō kōugēṇaṁ taṁ puṇa annaṁ viappēsi // SurSuCa.128

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō imammi nayarammi atthi payaḍajasō
khayarō amiyagaī tassa bhāriyā cittamālatti // SurSuCa.129

ēsā ēgā dhūyā tāṇaṁ jāyā aṇōvamaguṇaḍ̣dhā
nāmēṇa kaṇagamālā vinnāṇasamanniyā kannā // SurSuCa.130


[p. 109]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kā ēsā mayaṇapūyaṇaṁ kuṇaï?
ēsāvi kā sahīē puraō vattaṁ kahēmāṇī? // SurSuCa.131

kō va imō avalambaï galaē vēsāē taruṇaō purisō?
ēmāi maē puṭṭhō hasiūṇa taō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.132

ēvaṁvihapucchāhiṁ kīsa tuma suyaṇu! maṁ payārēsa?
kō junnamajjariṁ kañjiēṇa paviyāriuṁ taraï? // SurSuCa.133

na hu suyaṇu! paḍhamapucchaṁ ērisapucchāhiṁ chāiüṁ tarasi
kiḍaēhiṁ payattēṇavi chāijjaï kaha ṇu paccūsō? // SurSuCa.134

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō lajjāē ahōmuhō ṭhiō ahayaṁ
taṁ daṭṭhu bhāṇuvēgō ṭhiō alakkhōvva hōūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.135

lajjāē tassamaē vālijjantīvi annaōhuttaṁ
maḍḍāē tahavi nivaḍaï maha diṭṭhī tīē muhakamalē // SurSuCa.136


[p. 110]
aṇurāyatantibaddhā diṭṭhī jaṇasaṅkulēvi maggami
sariūṇa saṇiya-saṇiyaṁ jattha piyaṁ tattha alliyaï // SurSuCa.137

sahijaṇapacchannēhiṁ puṇō puṇō taraladiṭṭhipāēhiṁ
bhaddavayamēhavijjūē vilasiyaṁ tīē vijiyanti // SurSuCa.138

tō tīē taralapamhaladiṭṭhībāṇēhiṁ jajjarē hiyaē
majjha paviṭṭhā pañcavi kusumasarā mayaṇapavimukkā // SurSuCa.139

ētthantarammitīē sahinivahō niyagihēsu sañcaliō
sāvi hu bālā caliyā puṇō puṇō maṁ pulōēntī // SurSuCa.140

valiyaggīvaṁ tīē sasiṇiddhaavaṅgadiṭṭhidōrēṇa
āyaḍ̣dhiya pacchannaṁ maha hiyayaṁ jhatti avahariyaṁ // SurSuCa.141

nāuṁvaharijjantaṁ maha hiyayaṁ tīē payavilaggāiṁ
kūyanti nēūrāiṁ puṇō puṇō kụdhiyapurisōvva // SurSuCa.142


[p. 111]
mayaṇattā sā jantī aṇamisanayaṇēhiṁ pulaïyā tāva
jāvujjāṇatarūhiṁ antariyā diṭṭhimaggāō // SurSuCa.143

vōlīṇadaṁsaṇāē tīē maha māṇasammi santāvō
duvvisahō sañjāō samayaṁ aïdīhasāsēhiṁ // SurSuCa.144

aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō gacchāmō niyagihammi amhēvi
ēvanti maē bhaṇiē samāgayā dōvi gēhammi // SurSuCa.145

tattō ahamārụ̄dhō uvarimabhūmīē tattha sayaṇīē
pāsuttō uvaviṭṭhō maha pāsē bhāṇuvēgōvi // SurSuCa.146

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō kīsa tumaṁ dummaṇōvva sañjāō?
muñcasi visāyagabbhē sudīharē kīsa nīsāsē? // SurSuCa.147

kiṁ kuṇasi aṅgabhaṅgaṁ dīhaṁ nīsasiya mukkahuṅkārō
bhaṭhṭhaṭṭiyacaṇagō viva sayaṇīē kīsa taḍaphaḍasi? // SurSuCa.148


[p. 112]
kiṅkimpi cintiūṇaṁ aṇimittaṁ cēva kīsa taṁ hasasi?
niyayavigappavasēṇaṁ kīsa puṇō dummaṇō hōsi? // SurSuCa.149

nāṇārasasaṅkinnaṁ nāḍayakavvaṁ ahiṇavēmāṇō
kiṁ ciṭṭhasi na ya sāhasi sabbhāvaṁ kiñci amhāṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.150

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bahusō pucchijjantēṇa kumara! mē bhaṇiyaṁ
jāṇāmi nēva kiṁ puṇa maha dēhaṁ gāḍhamassatthaṁ? // SurSuCa.151

hasiūṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ puvvaṁ ciya sāhiyaṁ maē tujjha
ēvaṁvihamahilāṇaṁ na sundaraṁ daṁsaṇaṁ hōi // SurSuCa.152

tā tīē cakkhudōsā ēsō savvōvi tujjha santāvō
dāvijjaï sā hatthaṁ paṭṭhīē jēṇa hōi suhaṁ // SurSuCa.153

nīsasiya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sandēhō jīviyassavi ya amhaṁ
taṁ puṇa suhiō bhāō ya parihāsaṁ kīsa nō kuṇasi? // SurSuCa.154


[p. 113]
tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō sabbhāvavivajjiyassa purisassa
annāyammi sarūvē kiṁ kāuṁ sakkimō amhē? // SurSuCa.155

tāhi maē vajjariyaṁ sāhijjaï tassa jō na yāṇāi
taṁ puṇa jāṇantōvi hu aliyaṁ ciya pucchisi mamanti // SurSuCa.156

ēmāivayaṇavittharavajjaraṇaparāyaṇāṇa amhāṇaṁ
cūyalayā gihadāsī āgantūṇaṁ imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.157

acchaï duvāradēsē samāgayā tumha daṁsaṇanimittaṁ
sōmalayā nāmēṇaṁ varadhāī kaṇagamālāē // SurSuCa.158

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō lahuṁ pavēsēha ēva bhaṇiyammi
aha sacciya sōmalayā samāgayā amha pāsammi // SurSuCa.159

kayaüvayārā tāhē uvaviṭṭhā bhaṇaï sāyaraṁ vayaṇaṁ
ēgantaṁ kuṇaha taō cūyalayā pēsiyā tattō // SurSuCa.160


[p. 114]
bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē saraṇāgayavacchalā jaō suyaṇā
paritāyaha paritāyaha mamaṁ taō bhīmavasaṇāō // SurSuCa.161

harisāūriyahiyaēṇa tāhē ēvaṁvihaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ
kattō bhaddē! vasaṇaṁ, sā bhaṇaī kusumabāṇāō // SurSuCa.162

īsīsi vihasiūṇaṁ vajjariyaṁ tāhi bhāṇuvēgēṇa
kaḍakaḍiyasavvasandhiṁ gayalāyannaṁ tuha śarīraṁ // SurSuCa.163

ninnaṭṭhadantapantiṁ siyakēsahasantasīsasōhillaṁ
dūrapalambiravalivalayasahiyasihiṇēhiṁ bībhacchaṁ // SurSuCa.164

daṭṭhūṇa bhīyabhīō dūraṁ dūrēṇa vaccaï aṇaṅgō
tattō kaha tujjha bhayaṁ jarāē jajjariyadēhāē? // SurSuCa.165

sōmalayāē bhaṇiyaṁ mā maṁ uvahasasu suṇasu vattantaṁ
jaha kusumabāṇavihiyaṁ paramparāē maha bhayanti // SurSuCa.166


[p. 115]
ujjāṇāu kīliya samāgayā niyagihē kaṇagamālā
vicchāyavayaṇasōhā viḍappagahiyā sasikalavva // SurSuCa.167

tattō ya maē puṭhṭhā kīsa tumaṁ putti! vimaṇadummaṇiyā?
na ya tīē kiñci siṭṭhaṁ sudīharaṁ navari nīsasiuṁ // SurSuCa.168

aṁsujalapūriyāiṁ nayaṇāiṁ kayāiṁ dīṇavayaṇāē
tattō ya maē puṭṭhā tīē sahī haṁsiyā nāma // SurSuCa.169

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ambē! ujjāṇa ajja pāviyā amhē
pūiya mayaṇaṁ bāhiṁ nīsariyā jāva tā diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.170

kōugavakkhittamaṇō uvaviṭṭhō bhāṇuvēgapāsammi
paccakkhōvva aṇaṅgō ēgō taruṇō mahābhāgō // SurSuCa.171

[yugmam]
taṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ ēsā jāyā nipphandalōyaṇā sahasā
āsattā tavvayaṇē ālēkkhagayavva niccēṭṭhā // SurSuCa.172


[p. 116]
savvaṅgiō imīē aṇimisadiṭṭhīē jōiō sa yuvā
na ya tēṇa imā diṭṭhā kōugavakkhittacittēṇa // SurSuCa.173

tō tassa nayaṇagōyaramapāvamāṇā salajjamuhakamalā
dōhaggadūsiyaṁ piva attāṇaṁ mannamāṇavva // SurSuCa.174

kiṅkimpi cintiūṇaṁ bhaṇaï sahīō! imammi cūyadumē
kīlāmō tāva khaṇaṁ bandhiya andōlayaṁ amhē // SurSuCa.175

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ tāhiṁ bhaṇiē tahēva sampāḍiyammi ēsāvi
gurusaddēṇa sahīō āsannāōvi vāharaï // SurSuCa.176

jaï ēsō maha saddaṁ sōūṇaṁ saṁmuhaṁ palōējjā
hōjjāmi tā kayatthā ii āsāē taḍijjantī // SurSuCa.177

taṁ pēkkhiūṇa ya maē parihāsavasēṇa jampiyaṁ ēyaṁ
āsannampi sahijaṇaṁ uccuccaṁ kīsa vāharasi? // SurSuCa.178


[p. 117]
kōugavakkhittamaṇō ēsō tuha dēi nēya paḍivayaṇaṁ
taṁ vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ savilakkhā kiñci sañjāyā // SurSuCa.179

ētthantarammi diṭṭhā tēṇa juvāṇēṇa 'ṇaṅgarūvēṇa
sajjhasaharisēhiṁ imā tāhi aüvvaṁ rasaṁ pattā // SurSuCa.180

tēṇālōiyamēttā sōhaggasamanniyaṁ ca appāṇaṁ
jīviyamavi sakayatthaṁ mannantā pulaïyasarīrā // SurSuCa.181

avaruṇḍaï sahinivahaṁ uccaṁ saṁlavaï hasaï animittaṁ
pāyaṅguṭṭhēṇa mahiṁ vilihaï kēsē ya sañjamaï // SurSuCa.182

ēmāiṁ saviyāraṁ cēṭṭhantā kīliūṇa khaṇamēgaṁ
mayaṇasaravihuriyaṅgī ihāgayā ērisā jāyā // SurSuCa.183

ēvaṁ ca haṁsiyāē bhaṇiyammi puṇōvi sā maē puṭṭhā
kō sō purisō haṁsiṇi!, kahiyaṁ savvampi maha tīē // SurSuCa.184


[p. 118]
sōhaṇaṭhāṇē rāgō puttīē, cintiuṁ gayā pāsē
tīē diṭṭhā ya maē sayaṇīyagayā kaṇagamālā // SurSuCa.185

āpaṇḍuramuhakamalā sudīhasāsēhiṁ sōsiyasarīrā
kahakahavi hu niyajīyaṁ mahayā kicchēṇa dhārantī // SurSuCa.186

piyavirahajalaṇajālāvalīhiṁ santāviyāē varaīē
hārō candaṇapaṅkō mummurasarisōvva paḍihāi // SurSuCa.187

cīyavva muṇālāiṁ naliṇīdalāimpi jālatullāiṁ
aṅgārarāsisarisā paḍihāsaï haṁsatūlīvi // SurSuCa.188

puṭṭhā na dēi vayaṇaṁ ālavaï na sahijaṇaṁ siṇiddhampi
jhāṇōvagayā varajōgiṇivva jāyā vigayacēṭṭhā // SurSuCa.189

piyavirahapisāēṇaṁ gahiya gayacēyaṇāvi hu sahīhiṁ
āsāsijjaü varaī sundara! tuha nāmamantēhiṁ // SurSuCa.190


[p. 119]
piyavirahapīḍiyaṁ taṁ tuḍigayaniyajīviyaṁ muṇēūṇaṁ
taddukkhadukkhiyā haṁ samāgayā tumha pāsammi // SurSuCa.191

ēvaṁ kusumasarāō aïgaruyaṁ āgayaṁ mahaṁ vasaṇaṁ
jaṁ tīē dukkhiyāē ahampi aïdukkhiyā cēva // SurSuCa.192

tā suyaṇu! kaṇagamālā jā sā nīsāsasōsiyasarīrā
āsāsijjaü varaī jāva na sāsā samappanti // SurSuCa.193

lahu kuṇasu kiñcuvāyaṁ jāva na nīsaraï jīviyaṁ tīē
gayajīviyāē pacchā kiṅkāhī lāvayarasēṇa? // SurSuCa.194

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ taïyā aha rāyaütta! mē bhaṇiyaṁ
ēyampi na jāṇāmō kā ēsā kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.195

tā puccha bhāṇuvēgaṁ patthuyavatthummi gahiyaparamatthaṁ
amhē puṇa pāhuṇayā ayāṇuyā ēttha vatthumi // SurSuCa.196


[p. 120]
aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō amhēvi hu nēva jāṇimō kiñci
tō bhaṇaï sōmalayā sāsūyaṁ ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.197

hariūṇa tīē hiyayaṁ diṭṭhibāṇēhiṁ pahariyaṁ aṅgē
tuḍigayajīyaṁ kāuṁ taṁ sampaï ayāṇuō jāō // SurSuCa.198

kaṇṭhagayajīviyāsā tuha virahē maraï natthi sandēhō
ayaṇattaṁ avalambiyaṁ taṁ ciṭṭhasi niddaō bhadda! // SurSuCa.199

annaṁ ca. 

jō jattha jaṇō nivasaï rakkhaï sō āyarēṇa taṁ gēhaṁ
tīē maṇammi vasantō kiṁ niddaya! taṁ maṇaṁ dahasi? // SurSuCa.200

hariūṇa tīē hiyayaṁ sampaï cōrōvva ninhavēmāṇō
na hu chuṭṭasi suyaṇu! tumaṁ kiñci uvāyaṁ vicintēsu // SurSuCa.201

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ amma! taṁ cēva sāhasu uvāyaṁ
ēvaṁ cavatthiyammi jaṁ juttaṁ amha kāuṁ jē // SurSuCa.202


[p. 121]
bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē cittaṁ pattaṁ va paccayanimittaṁ
paṭṭhavasu jēṇa cittaṁ sandhīraï sā tayaṁ daṭṭhuṁ // SurSuCa.203

tattō ya maē lihiyā pattē naliṇīō tīē paümammi
mōttūṇa sēsakusumē nilīyamāṇō alī lihiō // SurSuCa.204

hiṭṭhē ya tassa lihiyā ēsā gāhā uvvunnayarasēṇa
niyabhāvasūyaṇaparā pacchannatthā tayā kumara! // SurSuCa.205

taha kahavi pariṭṭhaviyaṁ aliṇō naliṇīē parimalaṁ hiyaē
lōyaṇuppayaṇaṁ jaha tassa kēvalaṁ saṁsakusumēsu // SurSuCa.206

taṁ ca bahu pattamajjhē kāuṁ tō pēsiō satambōlō
cūyalayāē hatthē dōvi gayā tīē pāsammi // SurSuCa.207

tattō khaṇantarāō cūyalayā āgayā imaṁ bhaṇaï
ēttō viṇiggayā haṁ pattā ya kamēṇa taggēhē // SurSuCa.208


[p. 122]
mattavva mucchiyā iva giliyā iva suyaṇu! gurupisāēṇa
diṭṭhā u kaṇagamālā visamamavatthantaraṁ pattā // SurSuCa.209

tīē sahīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ samāgayā cittavēgadūitti
aha sā tuha nāmakkharaāyannaṇaladdhabuddhiyā // SurSuCa.210

jhatti niviṭṭhā tattō pāsiya maṁ lajjiyāva maṇayanti
tāhē samappiō sē tambōlō saharisaṁ gahiō // SurSuCa.211

gahiyatthāē bhaṇiyaṁ kēṇēsō pēsiō mha tambōlō?
mē bhaṇiyaṁ taha sundari! maṇōharēṇaṁ piyayamēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.212

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ kannā ahanti kaha majjha piyayamō bhaddē!?
mē bhaṇiyaṁ naṇu hōhī aha sā aphuḍakkharaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.213

kaha māmi! aünnāē ēttiyamēttāṇi majjha punnāṇi
jaṁ sō bhattā hōhī daṁsaṇamittampi aïdulahaṁ // SurSuCa.214


[p. 123]
ēttiyamēttaṁ bhaṇiuṁ aṁsujalupphuṇṇalōyaṇā jhatti
nīsāsamōttūṇaṁ gayacēṭṭhā sā puṇō jāyā // SurSuCa.215

tattō sahīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sāhējjasu tassa nigghiṇamaṇassa
jahadiṭṭhaṁ hi sarūvaṁ imīē aïgaruyapēmmāē // SurSuCa.216

annaṁ ca jaha kahavi tāva vōlaï rayaṇī kusalēṇa tā pabhāyammi
ujjāṇammi gayāē dāyavvaṁ daṁsaṇamimīē // SurSuCa.217

taddaṁsaṇēṇa jīvaï na annahā ēsa nicchaō amha
ēvaṁ bahuhā bhaṇiyā samāgayā tumha pāsammi // SurSuCa.218

ēvaṁ cūyalayāē bhaṇiyaṁ sōūṇa tīē vuttantaṁ
duguṇatarō mē jāō tavvirahē garuyayasantāvō // SurSuCa.219

jaï marihī sā bālā kahavi hu guruvirahatāviyā handi!
ēēṇa nimittēṇaṁ tā majjhavi āgayaṁ maraṇaṁ // SurSuCa.220


[p. 124]
ahavā siṇēhajuttā jaï sā tā kīsa majjha paḍivayaṇaṁ
navi dinnaṁ tā mannē mandasiṇēhā u maha uvariṁ // SurSuCa.221

jaïvi hu sā ninnēhā tahavi maṇaṁ majjha tīē virahammi
pajaliyajalaṇasamujjalajālāliddhaṁva paḍihāi // SurSuCa.222

nayaṇēhiṁ pulaïyā sā tāiṁ ciya dahaü ēsa piyavirahō
hiyaēṇa kimavaraddhaṁ jēṇa tayaṁ niddayaṁ dahaï? // SurSuCa.223

annēṇa kayaṁ annō na bhuñjaē aliyamērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ
sā diṭṭhā nayaṇēhiṁ jāō hiyayassa santāvō // SurSuCa.224

rōvantu nāma taṁ jaṇamapēcchamāṇāṇi daḍḍhanayaṇāṇi
taṁ hiyaya! kiṁ vimūrasi sāhīṇē cintiyavvammi? // SurSuCa.225

nayaṇēhiṁ jōiyā sā hiyaēṇa kaō ya gurayapaḍibandhō
sarisēvi hu avarāhē virahō hiyayaṁ daḍhaṁ dahaï // SurSuCa.226


[p. 125]
ētthantarammi sūrō bhamiūṇaṁ bhuvaṇamaṇḍalamasēsaṁ
atthagirimatthayatthō jāō addhāṇakhinnōvva // SurSuCa.227

niṭṭhurakarēhiṁ bhuvaṇaṁ imēṇa santāviyanti rōsēṇa
najjaïva atthagiriṇā sīsāō ̣dhāliō sūrō // SurSuCa.228

nāūṇa sūrapaḍaṇaṁ aṇulaggā uvari atthasēlassa
rōsēṇa rattamuhā samāgayā jhatti aha sañjhā // SurSuCa.229

tayaṇantaramandhāriyadisivalayā navari āgayā rayaṇī
payaḍiyatārayanivahā kōsiyahuṅkārabhīsaṇayā // SurSuCa.230

tāva ya khaṇantarāō ninnāsiyabahalatimirasaṅghāō
māṇiṇimāṇummahaṇō vitthariō sasikaranihāō // SurSuCa.231

mayalañchaṇapavaṇēṇaṁ gāḍhaṁ sandhukkiō viōyaggī
santāviuṁ payattō maha hiyayaṁ tāhē sayaguṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.232


[p. 126]
aha cintiuṁ payattō amayamaō summaī imō candō
navaraṁ tavvirahē ajja vijjupuñjōvamō jāō // SurSuCa.233

hē hiyaya! kīsa ujjhasi uvvēyaṁ kīsa kuṇasi accatthaṁ?
dullahajaṇammi rāgaṁ paḍhamaṁ ciya kīsa taṁ kuṇasi? // SurSuCa.234

annaṁ ca jō kira karēi nēhaṁ tassēva ya hiyaya! racciuṁ juttaṁ
dūraṭṭhiōvi jō dahaï māṇasaṁ tammi kō rāgō? // SurSuCa.235

so cciya vubbhaï hiyaē so cciya aïniṭṭhurō dahaï dēhaṁ
kassa kahijjaï vattā saraṇāō bhayammi ubbhūē? // SurSuCa.236

kiṁ mannē hōjja diyahaṁ jammī laggējja majjha hatthammi
maṇanivvavaṇō tīē kamalōyarakōmalō hatthō // SurSuCa.237

acchaü tā dūre cciya pāṇiggahaṇāiyaṁ tu saha tīē
amhāṇa maṇōdaïyaṁ daṁsaṇamavi dullahaṁ mannē // SurSuCa.238


[p. 127]
kiṁ majjha jīviēṇaṁ kiṁvā maha handi! maṇuyajammēṇa
jō virahadukkhasamaṇaṁ tīē vayaṇaṁ na pēcchāmi? // SurSuCa.239

ahavā cūyalayāē bhaṇiēṇaṁ bhavissaī pabhāyammi
tīē saha daṁsaṇayaṁ aṇukūlō jaï vihī hōhī // SurSuCa.240

guruvirahajalaṇajālāvalīhiṁ santāviyassa hiyayassa
annō natthi uvāō piyadaṁsaṇaōsahaṁ mōttuṁ // SurSuCa.241

ēmāivigappēhiṁ paṇaṭṭhaṇiddassa majjha sā rayaṇī
caüjāmāvi hu taïyā jāmasahassōvamā jāyā // SurSuCa.242

asarisadūsahasantāvatāviyaṁ kahavi māṇasaṁ majjha
phuḍamāṇampi na phuṭṭaṁ mannē taddaṁsaṇāsāē // SurSuCa.243

sīyalakaraniyarēṇavi santāvaṁ phēḍiuṁ maha asattō
aha lajjiuvva candō atthagiriṁ pāviō tattō // SurSuCa.244


[p. 128]
paccūsagayavarummūliyāē uḍḍīṇasasivihaṅgāē
rayaṇilayāē galantiva kusumāiṁ tārayanihēṇa? // SurSuCa.245

aha indadisā sahasā kēsuyasuyatuṇḍasacchahā jāyā
āsannasūramaṇḍalavajjaraṇatthaṁva lōyassa // SurSuCa.246

paḍibōhiyakamalavaṇō pasariyakharakiraṇapūriyadiyantō
mēliyarahaṅgajuyalō tadaṇantaramuggaō sūrō // SurSuCa.247

ētthantarammi ahayampi samuṭṭhiūṇa kiccaṁ pabhāyataṇayaṁ kariuṁ payattō
bhō suppaïṭṭha! taïyā daïyāi hōhī sandaṁsaṇamha ii pahiṭṭhamaṇō pagāmaṁ // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï virahē sūruggamotti supasiddhō
surasundarināmāē kahāē taïō paricchēō 950 // SurSuCa.950



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 129]
[caturthaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha bhāō bhāṇuvēgō samāgaō pahasiō mamaṁ bhaṇaï
gammaü ujjāṇammi cūyalayāvayaṇamaṇusariuṁ // SurSuCa.1

harisāūriyahiyaēṇa tāhi ēvanti japamāṇēṇaṁ
takkāluciyaṁ jāva ya kāyavvaṁ kāumāradvaṁ // SurSuCa.2

ētthantarammi nisuō maṅgalatūrassa gahiranigghōsō
puṭṭhō ya maē bhāyā kattha imaṁ vajjaē tūraṁ? // SurSuCa.3

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō sammaṁ jāṇē na kāraṇaṁ ēttha
navaraṁ amiyagaïgihē bhāvijjaï ēsa tūraravō // SurSuCa.4

aha cintiyaṁ maē kiṁ āsannapiyāsamāgamassāvi
abbhahiō santāvō phuraï ya vāmaṁ tahā nayaṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.5


[p. 130]
tā bhaviyavvaṁ kēṇavi ēttha naṇu kāraṇēṇa tāhē maē
cūyalayā vāhariyā samāgayā aha imaṁ bhaṇiyā // SurSuCa.6

kattha imō tūraravō kēṇava kajjēṇa sammamuvalabbha
āgantūṇaṁ bhaddē! sigghaṁ ciya kahasu amhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.7

gantūṇaṁ cūyalayā khaṇantarāō samāgayā dhaṇiyaṁ
vicchāyavayaṇakamalā puṭṭhā ya maē imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.8

ēttō viṇiggayāē amiyagaïgihassa dāradēsammi
bhūrijaṇasaṅkulammī maē na laddhō pavēsōvi // SurSuCa.9

tattō ya bandhudattō patthuyavatthummi pucchiyā bhaṇaï
varaṇammi ēsa bhaddē! mahōcchavō kaṇagamālāē // SurSuCa.10

sirigandhavāhaṇasuō gaṅgāvattammi khayaranayarammi
nahavāhaṇotti summaï tassa viinnā kaṇayamālā // SurSuCa.11


[p. 131]
ēvaṁ viyāṇiūṇaṁ samāgayā ēttha tumha pāsammi
kannakaḍuyampi tumhaṁ sāhijjaï mandābhāgāē // SurSuCa.12

tīē vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ dhasatti gurumōggarēṇa pahaō haṁ
mucchānimīliyacchō paḍiō bhūmiē gayacēṭhṭhō // SurSuCa.13

ghaṇasārasāragōsīsamīsasalilēṇa tāhi saṁsittō
sukumālatālaviṇṭayasīyalapavaṇēṇa gayamucchō // SurSuCa.14

paricintiuṁ payattō pēcchaha duvvihiyavilāsiyaṁ vihiṇō
piyasaṅgamaṇōrahabhaṁsaṇammi ujjuttacittassa // SurSuCa.15

ahavā annaha paricintijjaï saharisakaṇḍujjaēṇa hiyaēṇa
pariṇamaï annahacciya kajjārambhō vihivasēṇa // SurSuCa.16

kattha imā kattha ahaṁ annōnnaṁ kattha garuyaaṇurāgō
navaraṁ hayāsavihiṇā savvaṁ ciya annahā vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.17


[p. 132]
puvvampi hu jaï buddhī ērisayā āsi tujjha rē divva!
tā kaha maha paḍhamaṁ ciya tīē saha daṁsaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ? // SurSuCa.18

kāūma daṁsaṇaṁ garūyarāyasahiyaṁ hayāsa! rē! divva!
annattha taṁ mayacchiṁ jōḍēntō ki naṁ lajjihisi? // SurSuCa.19

aviya nayaṇāṇa paḍaü vajjaṁ ahavā vajjassa vaḍḍilaṁ kimpi
amuṇiyajaṇēvi diṭṭhē aṇubandhaṁ jāṇi kuvvanti // SurSuCa.20

khaṇapariciyadullahalōyakāraṇē kīsa! taṁ mihasi?
muñcasu garuyavisāyaṁ vivarīō hayavihī jēṇa // SurSuCa.21

ērisaduvissahēvi hu sañjāē hiyayaṁ garuyadukkhammi
vajjaghaḍiyaṁva mannē jaṁ navi sayasikkaraṁ jāsi // SurSuCa.22

ēmāibahuvigappaṁ cintēmāṇassa garuyasōgassa
tavvirahadūmiyamāṇasassa taïyā mahaṁ kumara! // SurSuCa.23


[p. 133]
puṇaravi sā sōmalayā samāgayā kiñci harisiyāva maṇē
uvaviṭṭhā maṁ daṭṭhuṁ suṭṭhuṁ visāyāuraṁ taïyā // SurSuCa.24

[yugmam]
tā bhaṇaï kīsa sundara! dīsasi taṁ dummaṇōvva accatthaṁ
suṇiuṁ varaṇayavattaṁ, tāva nisāmēsu maha vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.25

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē ajjavi kiṁ āsā kāvi atthi amhāṇa
vajjarasi jēṇa ēvaṁ sōmalaē!, tāhi sā bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.26

tuha virahē gayacēṭṭhaṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ tāva kaṇagamālaṁ tu
cūyalayā kallammi paṭṭhaviyā tumha pāsammi // SurSuCa.27

sāvi hu sahīhiṁ kahavi tuha saṅgamasūyagēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ
āsāsiyāvi varaī tuha saṅgamapāvamāṇā u // SurSuCa.28

khaṇamēttaṁ mucchijjaï uṭhṭhiyaï puṇōvi muyaï huṅkārē
gāyaï hasaï ya vēvaïrōvaï ya khaṇēṇa uttasaï // SurSuCa.29


[p. 134]
gahagahiyā iva bālā asamañjasacēṭṭhiyāi kuṇamāṇā
hasiyāvi sahijaṇēṇaṁ navi jāṇaï kiñci hayahiyayā // SurSuCa.30

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
taṁ pēkkhiūṇa ya maē vicintiyaṁ jāva muyaï nō pāṇē
guruaṇurāgā ēsā tāva uvāyaṁ vicintēmi // SurSuCa.31

tattō tavvuttantō kahiō gantūṇa cittamālāē
tajjaṇaṇīē u maē ēgantagayāē savvōvi // SurSuCa.32

vinnāyasarūvatthā pāsē āgamma kaṇagamālāē
vajjaraï cittamālā kīsa tumaṁ putti! uvviggā? // SurSuCa.33

acchasi ōsannamuhī bhaṇiyāvi hu kīsa dēsi nālāvaṁ?
suhasajjhaṁ cēva imaṁ mā putti! visāyamuvvahasu // SurSuCa.34

amhāṇa cittabhāṇū āyattō taṁ ca putti! kannā si
uciō ya cittavēgō rūvēṇaṁ kalāhiṁ jaṁ tujjha // SurSuCa.35


[p. 135]
tassa ya uvariṁ jāō aṇurāgō tujjha tēṇa savvampi
amukūlamiṇaṁ jāyaṁ mā cintasu annahā vacchē! // SurSuCa.36

kintu tuha putti! jaṇaō gaṅgāvattammi khayaranayarammi
pāsammi gandhavāhaṇavijjāhararāiṇō hu gaō // SurSuCa.37

āgacchaü sō sigghaṁ kusalēṇaṁ tāhē tujjha vīvāhaṁ
mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ kārissaï cittavēgēṇa // SurSuCa.38

ēsōvi cittamāsō vittappāutti labbhihī laggaṁ
sigghaṁ ciya putti! tumaṁ mā kāhisi kiñci uvvēvaṁ // SurSuCa.39

ēvaṁ niyajaṇaṇīē bhaṇiyā sā vigayavirahasantāvā
jāyā maṇayaṁ satthā samuṭṭhiyā tāhē sē jaṇaṇī // SurSuCa.40

ētthantarammi sahasā samāgaō tāō khayaranayarāō
amiyagaī sē jaṇaō kayaviṇaō pariyaṇēṇēsō // SurSuCa.41


[p. 136]
ṇhāya vilittō bhuttō uvaviṭhṭhō uvarimāē bhūmīē
ahayampi cittamālāsahiyā tatthēva sampattā // SurSuCa.42

kusalapaütiṁ pucchiya niyadaïyaṁ tāhē cittamālāē
niyadhūyāē paüttī savvāvi hu tassa akkhāyā // SurSuCa.43

taṁ sōuṁ amiyagaī sāmamuhō takkhaṇēṇa sañjāō
bhaṇaï ahō! aïgarūyaṁ samāgayaṁ amha vasaṇanti // SurSuCa.44

tō bhaṇaï cittamālā piyayama! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ nu vasaṇassa?
tattō ya amiyagaïṇā vajjariyaṁ piyayamē! suṇasu // SurSuCa.45

naravaïkajjēṇēttō gaṅgāvattammi tammi nayarammi
sirigandhavāhaṇassa ō pāsammi gaō ahaṁ taïyā // SurSuCa.46

kayaviṇaō uvaviṭṭhō atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō pāsē
sambhāsiēṇa ya taō nivēiyaṁ rāyakajjaṁ sē // SurSuCa.47


[p. 137]
ētthantarammi sundari! paḍihāranivēiō aṇunnāō
atthāṇammi paviṭṭhō ēgō vijjāharakumārō // SurSuCa.48

vihiyapaṇāmō rannō pāraddhō ērisaṁ sa vajjariuṁ
vijjāharāṇa rāyā vēyaḍ̣dhē āsi jō dēva! // SurSuCa.49

saṁsiddhasayalavijjō sasurāsuramaṇuyalōyavikkhāō
suravāhaṇotti nāmaṁ vijjāharacakkavaṭṭitti // SurSuCa.50

avamāṇavajjiyaṁ jō vijjāhararāyalacchimaṇuhaviuṁ
vikkhāyajasaṁ puttaṁ niyayapaē ṭhāviūṇa tumaṁ // SurSuCa.51

saṁsāravāsabhīō nāūṇa asārayaṁ vibhūīē
rajjasiriṁ avaüjjhiya paḍaggalaggaṁ jarataṇaṁva // SurSuCa.52

siriusahanāhajiṇavaravajjariyaṁ savvaviraïrūvaṁ jō
cāritaṁ paḍivannō cittaṅgayamuṇivarasamīvē // SurSuCa.53


[p. 138]
gahaṇā ' 'sēvaṇarūvaṁ sikkhaṁ abbhasiya gurūsamīvammi
ahiyasuō paḍivajjiya ēgallavihārapaḍimaṁ sō // SurSuCa.54

chaṭṭha 'ṭṭhamadasamaduvālasāināṇāvihē tavōkammē
ujjuttō viharantō gāmāgaramaṇḍiyaṁ vasuhaṁ // SurSuCa.55

sampattō ētthēva ya vēyaḍ̣dhē cittakūḍasiharammi
tumha piyā suravāhaṇavijjāharamuṇivarō ajja // SurSuCa.56

paḍimāpaḍivannassiha sukkajjhāṇēṇa khaviyamōhassa
lōyālōyapayāsaṁ uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ tassa // SurSuCa.57

[navabhiḥ kulakam]
tattō ya tassa vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ gandhavāhaṇō rāyā
harisavasaviyasiyacchō bhaṇaï tayaṁ sāyaraṁ ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.58

bhō āgacchasu saṅgaya! āsannō, ajja tāyavattāē
sahalīkayaṁ mha jīyaṁ kēvalaüppattigabmāē // SurSuCa.59


[p. 139]
sasarīraparihiyaṁ sō savvaṁ ābharaṇavatthamāīyaṁ
vilaïya tassa sarīrē tattō bhaṇḍāriyaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.60

addhattērasakōḍī pavarasuvannassa dēsu ēyassa
pīīdāṇaṁ tattō tahatti sampāḍiyaṁ tēṇa // SurSuCa.61

tayaṇantaraṁ ca rāyā vijjāharaniyaraparigaō caliō
jaṇayassa cittakūḍē bhattīē vandaṇanimittaṁ // SurSuCa.62

vijjāviraïyavaravimāṇaārūḍhapariyaṇāṇugaō
suhanēvatthavirāiyanāyarajaṇaparigaō sahasā // SurSuCa.63

[yugmam]
tēṇa sahiō ahampi hu caliō muṇipāyavandaṇanimittaṁ
aha savvē sampattā āsannē cittakūḍassa // SurSuCa.64

caüvihadēvanikāyaṁ nivayantaṁ daṭṭhuṁ cittakūḍammi
savisēsaharisiyamaṇō viyasiyamuhapaṅkaō rāyā // SurSuCa.65


[p. 140]
sigghataraṁ gantūṇaṁ bahujaṇaparivāriō payattēṇa
surakayakēvalimahimaṁ thuvvantaṁ divvanārīhiṁ // SurSuCa.66

daṭṭhūṇa muṇivaraṁ taṁ kāūṇa payāhiṇaṁ ca tikkhuttō
bahumāṇavasasamuṭṭhiyarōmañcayañciyasarīrō // SurSuCa.67

bhūmitalaluliyamaüḍaṁ pañcaṅgaṁ kariya tāhē paṇivāyaṁ
paharisagalantanayaṇō aha ēvaṁ thuṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.68

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
jaya jaya jīvadayāvara! sukkajjhāṇēṇadaḍḍhakammavaṇa!
vōcchinnabhavanibandhaṇa! jāijarāmaraṇadukkhahara! // SurSuCa.69

uppannavimalakēvalaüvaladdhasamatthaṇēyasabbhāva!
sāsayasivasuhasāhaṇa! pattaahakkhāyacāritta! // SurSuCa.70

bhayavaṁ aṇāinihaṇē paribbhamantāṇa bhavasamuddammi
dāuṁ hatthālambaṁ amha samuttāraṇaṁ kuṇasu 71|| // SurSuCa.71


[p. 141]
ēvaṁ thuṇiūṇa muṇiṁ muṇimuhakamalanihiyamaṇanayaṇō
uvaviṭṭhō dharaṇīē nāsannē nāidūrammi // SurSuCa.72

ētthantarammi muṇiṇā paratthasampāyaṇēkkarasiēṇa
gambhīrabhāraīē pāraddhā dēsaṇā ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.73

aïdulahaṁ maṇuyattaṁ asāsaṁsārasāgaragayāṇaṁ
kugaīṇa paürabhāvā sakammavasagāṇa jīvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.74

tampi hu jarābhibhūyaṁ āvāsō rōgasōgavāhīṇaṁ
sārīramāṇasāṇēyadukkhasampāyakaliyanti // SurSuCa.75

pavaṇāhayadhayavaḍacañcalāō lacchīō tahaya maṇuyāṇaṁ
aṇavaṭṭhiyā ya nēhā suhisayamapiyāijaṇavisayā // SurSuCa.76

visayasuhampi hu pariṇāmadārūṇaṁ nārayāiduhahēū
ārambhapariggahasañciyassa pāvassa pariṇāmō // SurSuCa.77


[p. 142]
aïbhīsaṇēṇa bandhēṇa garūyapīḍāvahō khu jīvāṇaṁ
micchāviyappavasaō savvampi hu sōkkhamābhāi // SurSuCa.78

aṇavarayasampayaṭṭō maccū avaharaï jīvasaṅghāyaṁ
ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē bhō bhō bhaddā! sammaṁ vicintēha // SurSuCa.79

kēvalibhaṇiyaṁ dhammaṁ mōttūṇaṁ natthi kiñci annanti
saraṇaṁ bhavabhīyāṇaṁ bhaviyāṇaṁ bhavanibuḍḍāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.80

tamhā kuṇaha payattaṁ dulahaṁ laddhūṇa māṇusaṁ jammaṁ
jiṇaïndabhaṇiyadhammē sāsayasivasōkkhahēummi // SurSuCa.81

sāvajjakajjavajjaṇarūvaṁ parigēṇhiūṇa pavvajjaṁ
khaviūṇa kammasattuṁ sāsayasōkkhaṁ vayaha mōkkhaṁ // SurSuCa.82

iya kēvaliṇā bhaṇiē viṇivēsiya karayalañjaliṁ sīsē
vajjaraï gandhavāhaṇarāyā u tahatti jaṁ bhaṇaha // SurSuCa.83


[p. 143]
dāuṁ vijjāniyaraṁ rajjēṇa samaṁ tu niyayaputtassa
nahavāṇassa tattō karōmi gihavāsacāyanti // SurSuCa.84

ētthantarammi sundari! patthāvaṁ jāṇiūṇa pucchāē
vihiyapaṇāmēṇa maē puṭṭhō muṇikēvalī ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.85

lōyālōyavilōyaṇakēvalanāṇēṇa nāyabhāvassa
paccakkhaṁ hi bhayavaō ēyaṁ jamahaṁ tu pucchissaṁ // SurSuCa.86

ēkkacciya maha dhūyā jāyā vinnāṇarūvasampunnā
pāṇāṇavi vallahiyā nāmēṇaṁ kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.87

dhūyāē kō bhattā hōhī maṇavallahotti ēyāē
cintāē maha hiyayaṁ bhayavaṁ! niccapi akkhaliyaṁ // SurSuCa.88

tā maṇanivvuihēuṁ sāhijjaü ēsa amha vuttantō
pāṇiggahaṇaṁ tīē kō kira vijjāharō kāhī? // SurSuCa.89


[p. 144]
ēvaṁ ca pucchiēṇaṁ kēvaliṇā suyaṇu! ērisaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
mā bhadda! kuṇa visāyaṁ thōva ciya ēttha vatthummi // SurSuCa.90

tuha dhūyāē bhattā sō hōhī jō imammi vēyaḍ̣dhē
guṇakaliyaṁ pālissaï vijjāharacakkavaṭṭittaṁ // SurSuCa.91

puvvabhavanēhabaddhā tuha dhūyā tassa pāṇavallahiyā
hōhī sayalantēuralalāmabhūyā mahādēvī // SurSuCa.92

kēvalivayaṇaṁ sōuṁ sañjāō majjha garūyaāṇandō
ētthantarammi rāyā samuṭṭhiō vandiūṇa muṇiṁ // SurSuCa.93

tattō rannā sahiō samāgaō tammi cēva nayarammi
aha rannā haṁ bhaṇiō bahumāṇajuyaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.94

aïvallahāvi dhūyā dāyavvā tāva kassaï narassa
jaṁ ēsā lōgaṭṭhiī tēṇamhē ērisaṁ bhaṇimō // SurSuCa.95


[p. 145]
nahavāhaṇassa dijjaü sā kannā jēṇa vittavīvāhaṁ
niyayapaē ṭhaviuṇaṁ sēvāmō tāyapayajuyalaṁ // SurSuCa.96

tattō maēvi bhaṇiyaṁ ētthatthē natthi kiñci vattavvaṁ
dhūyā kittiyamēttaṁ pāṇāvi hu tumha āyattā // SurSuCa.97

sacciya dhūyā dhannā suṇhā jā hōi dēvapāyāṇaṁ
kēvaligirāvi saccā jaṁ kijjaï ērisē vihiē // SurSuCa.98

tumha suyaṁ mōttūṇaṁ vēyaḍḍhagirimmi hōjja kō annō
vijjāṇa cakkavaṭṭī jassa piyā hōjja maha dhūyā? // SurSuCa.99

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiē viyasiyavayaṇēṇa rāiṇāṇattō
sōmajasō jōisiō vivāhalaggaṁ nirūvēsu // SurSuCa.100

tattō jōisiēṇaṁ sammaṁ ālōciūṇa āiṭṭhaṁ
vaïsāhasuddhapañcamirattīē sōhaṇaṁ laggaṁ // SurSuCa.101


[p. 146]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ āēsaṁ dēha jēṇa gantūṇa
niyanayarēsañjuttiṁ vivāhakajjassa kārēmi // SurSuCa.102

tēṇāṇunnāō haṁ sigghaṁ ciya āgaō ihaṁ suyaṇu!
rāyāmaccēhiṁ samaṁ candajasā ' 'iccanāmēhiṁ // SurSuCa.103

ēēvi kaṇagamālāvaraṇatthaṁ āgayā maē samayaṁ
kallē pabhāyasamaē kila hōi varaṇayaṁ tīē // SurSuCa.104

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē ēsā ēkkā dhūyā suṭṭhu piyā tāva kaṇagamālamha

tā jaï maṇō 'ṇukūlaṁ sampāḍissaṁ na ēkkadhūyāē

uvayārēṇaṁ mahayā vimaggiyā rāiṇā suyanimittaṁ

[p. 147]
taṁ ca iyāṇiṁ annahakāuṁ cāijjaē na jaṁ suyaṇu!
ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ mē bhaṇiyaṁ āgayaṁ vasaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.108

ēvaṁ piyayamavayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ cittavēga! sañjāyā

tattō tīē bhaṇiyaṁ maha cittē phuraï ērisaṁ tāva
paricayaï kaṇagamālā tavvirahē jīviyamavassaṁ // SurSuCa.110

kahakahavi maē jaṁ sā tappāvaṇasuyagēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ
puvviṁ sadhīraviyā ēyaṁ puṇa annahā jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.111

bhaṇiyaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā ēvaṁ hi ṭhiē karēmi kiṁ suyaṇu!
jaï tāva na dēmi imaṁ tō rāyā rūsaï avassaṁ // SurSuCa.112

kēvalivayaṇā rannō aïgaruō ēttha āyarō jāō
tēṇa imāi adāṇē aïgaruyaṁ hōi maha khūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.113


[p. 148]
ruṭṭhēṇa tēṇa vēyaḍḍhanagavarē jaṁ na hōi āvāsō

annaṁ ca giṇhissaï maḍḍāivi rāyā ēyaṁ na ēttha sandēhō

jaï puṇa dijjaï ēsā rāyasuyaṁ mōttu cittavēgassa
tā tassāvi amhāṇavi pāṇāṇavi saṁsaō hōi // SurSuCa.116

tā sundari! na hu kajjaṁ annēhiṁ ēttha bahuvigappēhiṁ
taha bhaṇasu kaṇagamālaṁ jaha ujjhaï tammi aṇurāyaṁ // SurSuCa.117

kiñca uttamakulappasūō piyaṁvaō sayalajaṇamaṇāṇandō

[p. 149]
tattō sa ēva bhattā kamāgaō hōu kaṇagamālāē
na hu kajjaṁ annēṇa avāyabahulēṇa purisēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.120

ēvaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā bhaṇiyāē tāhi cittamālāē
bhaṇiyā haṁ sōmalaē! kiṁ juttaṁ sampayaṁ kāuṁ? // SurSuCa.121

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ cēva ya ittha gahiyaparamatthā
niyadhūyāē saruvassa ēttha kimahaṁ bhaṇāmitti? // SurSuCa.122

tō bhaṇaï cittamālā tīē gantūṇa bhāvamulabhasu
icchaï va navā annaṁ purisaṁ guṇadōsakahaṇēṇa? // SurSuCa.123

nahavāhaṇaṁ pasaṁsiya abbhahiyaguṇaṁhiṁ, nindiūṇannaṁ
taha kuṇasu jahā icchaï vīvāhaṁ ēyataṇaēṇa // SurSuCa.124

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sāmiṇi! kiṁ taṁ na yāṇasi sabhāvaṁ
niyadhūyāē jēṇaṁ āēsaṁ dēsi maha ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.125


[p. 150]
mannissaï vīvāhaṁ jaṁ sā aṇṇassa, acchaü sudūraṁ
sōuṁ paüttimēyaṁ mannē jīyaṁ pariccayaï // SurSuCa.126

maha vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ gurudukkhasamāhayā bhaṇaï tattō
viyalantasakajjalanayaṇasalilasāmaliyagaṇḍayalā // SurSuCa.127

jaṁ bhaṇasi tumaṁ bhaddē! majjhavi hiyayammi phuraï taṁ saccaṁ
navaraṁ hayāsavihiṇō vasēṇa aïdukkaraṁ jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.128

[yugmam]
tattō aïgurusōgaṁ ruyamāṇiṁ picchiūṇa niyadaïyaṁ
vajjariyamamiyagaïṇā sundari! kiṁ ēttha runnēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.129

kiṁ maha thōvaṁ dukkhaṁ navaraṁ na caēmi annahākāuṁ
suirampi cintiūṇavi labhāmi nannaṁ uvāyanti // SurSuCa.130

rāyasuyassa adāṇē dōsē ya guṇē vicintēsu // SurSuCa.131


[p. 151]
anna caṁ, kaṇagamālā bahumāṇaparā hu jaṇaṇijaṇagāṇaṁ
paḍikūlissaï vayaṇaṁ na amha guṇadōsakahaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.132

annañca, kannagāē bhattā kila hōi guruaṇunnāō
tadaṇunnāē ya jaō sayaṁvarāīvi kīranti // SurSuCa.133

kicca nahavāhaṇarāyasuō jāva na diṭṭhīi gōyarē paḍaï
tāvacciya aṇurāō imīē annammi purisammi // SurSuCa.134

nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvē diṭhṭhē uṇa tammi hōhihī rāgō
tā kiṁ sundarī! bahuṇā vigappasaṅkappajālēṇa // SurSuCa.135

gantūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ suniuṇavayaṇēhiṁ bhaṇasu taṁ suyaṇu!
ēyammi vaïyarammi jaha amhaṁ hōi na hu vasaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.136

ēvaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā bhaṇiyāē tāhi cittamālāē
bhaṇiyā haṁ sōmalaē! piyayamavayaṇaṁ lahuṁ kuṇasu // SurSuCa.137


[p. 152]
tattō tahatti bhaṇiu samuṭṭhiyā jāva tāhi mē puṭṭhā
candaṇanāmā cēḍī katthacchaï kaṇagamālatti? // SurSuCa.138

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēsā uvarimabhūmīō uttirēūṇa
gihaüjjāṇābhimuhā gacchaï vicchāyamuhakamalā // SurSuCa.139

taṁ sōūṇa vigappō uppannō maha maṇammi ērisaō

tēṇēva imā mannē jāyā vicchāvayaṇiyā bālā

tā sigdhaṁ ciya gantu nivāraṇē tīē ujjamāmitti
ēvaṁ vicintayantī aṇumaggēṇēva caliyā haṁ // SurSuCa.142

[yugmam]
pattā ya gharujjāṇē iō taō taggēvasaṇanimittaṁ
jā pariyaḍāmi ahayaṁ ghaṇataruyarasaṅkaḍillammi // SurSuCa.143


[p. 153]
ghaṇapattalakayalīharamaṇōharē tattha ēgadēsammi
pattalatamālatarutalahēṭṭhaniviṭṭhā maē diṭṭhā // SurSuCa.144

kiṅkimpi cintayantī galantathūlaṁsusittagaṇḍayalā
aṇahuntamaṇasamīhiyagurudukkhā kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.145

tattō vicintiyaṁ mē kiṁ mannē niyagihaṁ pamōttūṇa

[yugmam]
tā ēīi adiṭṭhā pacchannaṭhiyā niēmi jaṁ kuṇati

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tuṇhikkā kayalithambhaantariyā
khaṇamēgaṁ jā ciṭṭhāmi tattha tā suṇasu jaṁ jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.148

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tu kaṇagamālāē

[p. 154]
suciraṁ vicintiūṇavi tēṇa jaṇēṇaṁ na saṅgamō tāva
punnarahiyāē majjhaṁ hayavihiṇō vilasiyavasēṇa // SurSuCa.150

acchaü saṅgamasōkkhaṁ daṁsaṇaāsāvi dullahā jāyā
jāē tassa viōgē phuṭṭantaṁ dhāriyaṁ hiyayaṁ // SurSuCa.151

tā kā ajjavi āsā jēṇa tumaṁ hiyaya! phuṭṭasi na jhatti

na ya piuvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ icchiyajaṇavirahakārayaṁ hiyaṁ
vajjaghaḍiyaṁva mannē jaṁ navi sayasikkaraṁ jāsi // SurSuCa.153

ammāē tāyassavi vallahiyā haṁ ti iya maraṭṭō jō
hiyayammi āsi majjhaṁ sōvi hu iṇhiṁ palīṇotti // SurSuCa.154

suhasajjhaṁ ciya ēyaṁ kajjaṁ mā putti! kuṇa visāyanti
ēvaṁvihavayaṇēhiṁ payāriyā jēṇa ambāē // SurSuCa.155


[p. 155]
jassuvari tujjha icchā dāyavvā tassa taṁ maē putti!
iyaniyavayaṇaṁ tāēṇa sampayaṁ annahā vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.156

vinnāyamahasarūvō ō annahā jaï karēi tāōvi
maha vañchiyasampattīē sambhavō tā kahaṁ hōu? // SurSuCa.157

ēvaṁ viyāṇiūṇavi hiyaya! tumaṁ kīsa muñcasi na āsaṁ
tajjaṇasaṅgamavisayaṁ jēṇajjavi jīviyaṁ dharasi? // SurSuCa.158

ahavā na kōvi dōsō pahuparavasaciṭṭhiyassa tāyassa
summaï jaṇammi payaḍaṁ kaṭṭhō khalu bhiccabhāvotti // SurSuCa.159

jaïvi hu vijiyāṇaṅgō ruvēṇaṁ jaïvi sampayākaliō
jaïvi hu uttamavaṁsō sakkhā sakkandaṇō jaïvi // SurSuCa.160

tahavi na bhāvaï annō purisō taṁ hiyayavallahaṁ mōttuṁ
jaï ēsa nicchaō hiyaya! tujjha tā kiṁ vilambēṇa? // SurSuCa.161

[yugmam]

[p. 156]
ēsō sō patthāvō aïdulahō pāviotti kaliūṇaṁ
ujjama vicintiyatthē hōu avigdhēṇa sampattī // SurSuCa.162

ēvaṁ hi kaē tāyasya dēi dōsaṁ na kimpi rāyāvi
dūsahaviōyadukkhassa hōi ēvaṁ ca vōcchēō // SurSuCa.163

ēmāibahuvigappā bhaṇiūṇaṁ cittavēga! sā bālā
kayamaraṇajjhavasāyā ārụdhā aha tamālammi // SurSuCa.164

daṭṭhūṇa sāhasantīē navari dēhaṁ pakampiyaṁ majjhaṁ
na vahaï vāyā kahavi hu thakkāō savvasandhīō // SurSuCa.165

tattō ya kaṇagamālā āruhiūṇaṁ tamālasāhāē
bandhiya niuttarīyaṁ bandhaï niyakandharābhōē // SurSuCa.166

aha pabhaṇiuṁ payattā ammē! jaṁ kiñci bālabhāvāō
pabhiiṁ kilēsiyā taṁ taṁ khamiyavvaṁ mahaṁ saṁvvaṁ // SurSuCa.167


[p. 157]
tāya! tumampi hu maha khamasu sampayaṁ paṇayaparavasāi maē
puvviṁ kilēsiō jaṁ paralōyaṁ patthiyā ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.168

jaṇaṇīsamahiyanēhē! sōmalaē! khama kilēsiyā jaṁ si
susiṇiddhasahīsandōha! khamasu jaṁ kiñci avaraddhaṁ // SurSuCa.169

khaṇamittadiṭṭha! vallaha! hiyayabbhantarapaviṭṭha! nisuṇēsu
patthēmi kiñci sāmiya! pāṇaccāyaṁ karēmāṇī // SurSuCa.170

tuha saṅgamarahiyāē ēsō jammō hu tāva vōlīṇō
annabhavē puṇa sāmiya! taṁ ciya maha vallahō hujjā // SurSuCa.171

annaṁ bhaṇāmi sāmiya! jaïvi hu aïniṭṭhuraṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ
tahavi hu tuha āvayāvāraṇatthamēsō mha nibbandhō // SurSuCa.172

nīsara maha hiyayāō ruddhē kaṇṭhammi pāsaēṇahavā
sakkēsi na nīsariu sāmiya! maha pāṇavallahaya! // SurSuCa.173


[p. 158]
mannē ca kiñci laddhaṁ hayavihiṇā maraṇakāraṇaṁ annaṁ
maha tēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ tumaē saha daṁsaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.174

vaṇadēvayāō! nisuṇaha tumha pasāyāō annajammēvi
sō khaṇadiṭṭhō lōgō daïō maha hōjja, nannotti // SurSuCa.175

ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ tīē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhatti
ētthantarammi gayaṇē samuṭṭhiyā ērisā vāyā // SurSuCa.176

mā mā sāhasamēyaṁ āyara bhaddē! samucchugā hōuṁ
sō cēva tujjha bhattā hōhī naṇu cittavēgotti // SurSuCa.177

tatthēva laggadivasē pāṇiggahaṇaṁ bhavissaī tēṇaṁ
aha sundari! ētthatthē mā kiñcivi kuṇa visāyanti // SurSuCa.178

[yugmam]
vayaṇāṇantaramēva hi tuṭṭō sē pāsaō, taō ahayaṁ
tavvayaṇagaliyasajjhasasatthasarīrā gayā pāsē // SurSuCa.179


[p. 159]
tattō salajjavayaṇā bhaṇiyā ya maē na putti! tuha juttaṁ
ērisamāyariuṁ jaṇaṇijaṇagamāīṇaduhajaṇayaṁ // SurSuCa.180

tattō ya tīi bhaṇiyaṁ ambē! amhārisāṇa kiṁ anna
ēvaṁ hi gaē kāuṁ juttaṁ maraṇaṁ pamōttūṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.181

jaō vari maraṇaṁ mā virahō virahō aïdūsahō 'mha paḍihāi
vari ēkkaṁ ciya maraṇaṁ jēṇa samappanti dukkhāiṁ // SurSuCa.182

tattō ya maē tīsē kahiō savvōvi puvvavuttantō
bhaṇiyā ya putti! sampaï kiṁ tuha paḍihāsaē kāuṁ? // SurSuCa.183

aha tīē vajjariyaṁ lajjaṁ mōttuṁ bhaṇāmi ēyaṁ tu
navi majjha karē laggaï annō purisō ihaṁ jammē // SurSuCa.184

hasiūṇa maē bhaṇiyaṁ dēvayavayaṇāu siddhamēyanti
kintu kaha tujjha jaṇaō chuṭṭissaï gandhavāhaṇaō? // SurSuCa.185


[p. 160]
ētthantarammi puṇaravi gayaṇē vāyā samuṭṭhiyā ēsā
mā! kuṇaha bahuvigappē maha vayaṇaṁ tāva nisuṇēha // SurSuCa.186

gantūṇaṁ sōmalayā sāhaü jaṇayassa ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ
bhaṇiyā bahuppagāraṁ bhaṇaï taō kaṇagamālēvaṁ // SurSuCa.187

jaṁ cēva kuṇaï tāō taṁ cēva majjha bahumayaṁ savvaṁ
jaï hōi sundaraṁ iha tāyassavi kīraï tayanti // SurSuCa.188

tattō avigappaṁ sē varaṇāiṁ paḍicchiyavvanti
ēvaṁ hi kaē kamasō hōhī iṭṭhatthasampattī // SurSuCa.189

iya dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ cittavēga! amhāṇaṁ
sañjātō gurutōsō tatō ya maē imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.190

maṇavañchiyavatthummī mā kīraü putti! kāvi āsaṅkā
kavaḍēṇavi tēṇa tumaṁ mannasu niyajaṇayavayaṇanti // SurSuCa.191


[p. 161]
ēvaṁ ca dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ annassa nēva kahiyavvaṁ
mā vinnāyasarūvō virūvamāyaraï sō rāya // SurSuCa.192

ēyammi kaē payaḍē lōyapavāyāu nāyaparamatthō
rāyā 'vassaṁ tuha vallahassa āyaraï asuhanti // SurSuCa.193

tō bhaṇaï kaṇagamālā ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō
tā ambē! patthuyatthē ujjama kiṁ ēttha bahuēṇa? // SurSuCa.194

tattō ya maē gantuṁ siṭṭhaṁ ēyaṁ tu cittamālāē
bhaṇiyā bahuppagāraṁ tuha dhūyā bhaṇaï ēvaṁ tu // SurSuCa.195

jaṁ kiñci bhaṇaï tāō jaṁ ciya iha bahumayaṁ tu ambāē
jaṁ cēva ya saguṇataraṁ maēvi taṁ cēva kāyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.196

jaha abbhudaō tāyassa hōi, jaha hōi nāvayā kayāvi
taha cēva ya kāyavvaṁ maēvi, kiṁ ēttha annēṇa? // SurSuCa.197


[p. 162]
tattō ya cittamālā tavvayaṇaṁ kahaï niyayadaïyassa
taṁ sōuṁ amiyagaī harisiyavayaṇō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.198

sundaramaṇuṭṭhiyaṁ handi! majjha dhūyāē jaṇayabhattāē
dakkhinnavayaṇavinnāmapagarisō daṁsiō ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.199

tattō pabhāyasamaē rāyāmaccēhiṁ varaṇayaṁ tīsē
mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ vihiyaṁ kayajaṇayaāṇandaṁ // SurSuCa.200

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē tuha maṇanivvuihēuṁ tīē vayaṇēṇa āgayā ahayaṁ
kahaṇatthaṁ patthuyavatthuvittharassēttha tuha pāsē // SurSuCa.201

tā mā sundara! varaṇayasavaṇāō dummaṇō tumaṁ hōsu
jaṁ dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ aliyaṁ na ya havaï ēyaṁ tu // SurSuCa.202

ēvaṁ ca kaṇagamālābhāṇaï na nāha! taṁ pamōttūṇa
annassa karō laggaï maha hatthē ittha jammammi // SurSuCa.203


[p. 163]
dēvayavayaṇaṁ jaï saccayaṁ tā dharēmi niyapāṇā
tadabhāvē puṇa saraṇaṁ maraṇaṁ maha nicchaō ēsō // SurSuCa.204

bhō suppaïṭhṭha! ēvaṁ sōmalayāvayaṇasavaṇaō taïyā
jāyaṁ maṇayaṁ maha māṇasassa satthattaṇaṁ tattō // SurSuCa.205

ēvaṁ vicintiyaṁ mē kēvaliṇā jēṇa ērisaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
puvvabhavanēhabaddhā hōhī bhajjatti, tā ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.206

sambhavaï nūṇa amhaṁ avarōppadaṁsaṇāō aïgaruō
aṇurāō jāō jaṁ summaï lōyappavāō ya // SurSuCa.207

jāisarāiṁ mannē imāiṁ nayaṇāiṁ sayalalōyassa
viyasanti piyē diṭṭhē avvō! maülinti vēsammi // SurSuCa.208

tā bhaviyavvaṁ imiṇā navaraṁ aïdugghaḍamha paḍihāi
jaṁ sā rāyasuēṇaṁ variyā kaha majja hōhitti? // SurSuCa.209


[p. 164]
ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tambōlapayāṇapuvvayaṁ bhaṇiyā
jaṁ kiñci ēttha hōhī dīsissaï taṁ sayaṁ ambē! // SurSuCa.210

bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō
tattō vihiyapaṇāmā uṭṭhiyasaṭṭhāṇamaṇupattā // SurSuCa.211

aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō puvviṁ diṭṭhassa tassa sumiṇassa
lēsēṇa kōvi atthō 'vadhāriō tāva taṁ suṇasu // SurSuCa.212

ēsā hu kaṇagamālā mālā hōhitti, tīē jō rāgō
taggahaṇaṁ taṁ jāṇasu varaṇaṁ puṇa tīē apattī // SurSuCa.213

ēttiyamēttō atthō paripphuḍō tāva jāṇiō hu maē
sēsampi hu avvattaṁ viyāṇiyaṁ kiñci taṁ suṇasu // SurSuCa.214

kōvi uvāēṇa imaṁ appissaï tujjha sā puṇō kahavi
bhaṭṭhā tuha hatthāō pāvissaï āvaï garuiṁ // SurSuCa.215


[p. 165]
tattō rakkhiya kōvi hu ̣dhōissaï tujjha tēṇa pajjantō
suviṇassa sundarō iya viṇicchiō suviṇasabbhāvō // SurSuCa.216

taṁ sōuṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumē suyaṇu!
ghaḍaï jaō ēsatthō navaraṁ aïdugghaḍō lāhō // SurSuCa.217

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō vatthuṁ na taṁ atthi ēttha lōgammi
aṇukūlassa u vihiṇō jaṁ mannē dugghaḍaṁ hōi // SurSuCa.218

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ païdiyahaṁ takkahāviṇōēṇa
tappāvaṇaāsāē vōlīṇā vāsarā kaïvi // SurSuCa.219

āsannamāgayaṁ aha laggadiṇaṁ tāhi khayarapariyariō
mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ bandhujaṇasamanniō tattha // SurSuCa.220

vīvāhatthaṁ tīē nahavāhaṇakhayararāyaaṅgaruhō
sampattō aha pattā kamēṇa sā pañcamitihīvi // SurSuCa.221


[p. 166]
tattō 'varaṇhasamaē majjha vigappō maṇammi uppannō
avvō! kiṁ taṁ aliyaṁ hōhī iha dēvayāvayaṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.222

ahava na dīsaï kiñcivi aṇurūvaṁ tassa tēṇa mannāmi
sōmalayāvajjariyaṁ savvamalīgaṁ hi sañjāyaṁ // SurSuCa.223

ēmāibahuvigappaṁ cintēntō raṇaraṇēṇa gahiō haṁ
katthavi dhiimalahantō nīhariō tāō nayarāō // SurSuCa.224

pattō ya tamujjāṇaṁ saccaviyā jattha sā maē puvviṁ
andōlaṇataruhiṭṭhē gantumahaṁ tāhi uvaviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.225

aha cintiuṁ payattō iṇhiṁ kiṁ majjha kāumuciyaṁ tu
parahatthaṁ sampattā tāva piyā maha niyantassa // SurSuCa.226

dēvayavayaṇāsāē nēva uvāōvi cintiō kōvi
iṇhiṁ puṇa nō sakkaṁ kimpi uvāyantaraṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.227


[p. 167]
ēsōvi hu aṇurāgō ēvampi gaē na tuṭṭaē kahavi
païsamayaṁ ca pavaḍḍhaï santāvō virahasañjaṇiō // SurSuCa.228

aviya dullahalambhammi jaṇē jassiha purisassa hōi aṇurāgō
chillarayapāṇiēṇava aṇudiyahaṁ tēṇa susiyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.229

garuyapiyasaṅgamāsābhaṁsasamucchaliyaraṇaraṇāinnaṁ
na ya jāṇē kahava imaṁ niyahiyayaṁ saṇṭhavāmitti? // SurSuCa.230

tā kiṁ karēmiṁ iṇhiṁ ahavā kiṁ ēttha bahuvigappēhiṁ
guruvirahadukkhasamaṇō pāṇaccāō paraṁ juttō // SurSuCa.231

jaïvi na jujjaï ēsō vivēyajuttāṇa uttamanarāṇa
tīē virahē tahavi hu sakkēmi na jīviyaṁ dhariuṁ // SurSuCa.232

tā ētthēva taruvarē tīē andōlaṇēṇa supavittē
ubandhiya appāṇaṁ pāṇaccāyaṁ karēmitti // SurSuCa.233


[p. 168]
ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ ārụdhō tammi taruvarē ahayaṁ
dāuṁ galaē pāsaṁ aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.234

rē divva! annajanmē dullahalambhammi māṇasē nēhaṁ
mā maha karijja ēsā hu patthaṇā tuha maē vihiyā // SurSuCa.235

annaṁ ca kēvaliṇō taṁ vayaṇaṁ, sā vāyā dēviyāvi, taṁ suviṇaṁ
āsānibandhaṇaṁ majjha divva! savvaṁ kayaṁ aliyaṁ // SurSuCa.236

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa maē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhati
tāhē gạ̄dhībhūē pāsammi sarīrabhārēṇa // SurSuCa.237

rūddhaṁ galayaṁ ākuñciyāō dhamaṇīō pasariyā viyaṇā
bhaggaṁ lōyaṇajuyalaṁ ruddhō pavaṇassa sañcārō // SurSuCa.238

uvvēlliyamaṅgēhiṁ jāyaṁ udaraṁ ca pavaṇapaḍihatthaṁ
karaṇāiṁ ghāiyāiṁ jāyā aha vēyaṇā mandā // SurSuCa.239


[p. 169]
bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ viyaṇāparimandaïndiēṇa maē
ētthantarammi nisuō saddō apaṇaṭṭhacittēṇa // SurSuCa.240

mā sāhasa mā sāhasamēyaṁ kāurisajaṇasamāiṇṇaṁ
āyariya dēvadullahaniyaruvaṁ bhadda! nāsēsu // SurSuCa.241

ētthantarammi kēṇavi lambantaṁ ukkhivittu maha dēhaṁ
lahu cchindiūṇa pāsaṁ vihiō miusīyalō pavaṇō // SurSuCa.242

tattō tusārasīyalasāraminīracchaḍāhiṁ saṁsittō
ulhāsiūṇa hiyayaṁ aṅgaṁ saṁvāhiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.243

mucchānimīliyacchō savvaṁ suviṇaṁva taṁ vimannantō
kōmalakisalayaraïē sattharaē sōviō tēṇa // SurSuCa.244

puṇaruttapavaṇakaraṇāiyāhiṁ nāṇāvihāhiṁ ciṭṭhāhiṁ
gayavēyaṇēṇa tattō khaṇantarā cēyaṇā laddhā // SurSuCa.245


[p. 170]
ummīliyalōyaṇajuyalaēṇa diṭhṭhō visiṭṭhasaṇṭhāṇō
navajōvvaṇō juvāṇō paccakkhaṁ pañcabāṇōvva // SurSuCa.246

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa kiṁ bhadda! bāhaē, daṁsiyaṁ maē galayaṁ
aha saṁvāhaṇavihiṇā tampi hu satthaṁ kayaṁ tēṇa // SurSuCa.247

vigayasayalapīḍō satthadēhō tayā haṁ, kisalayaraïyammī sattharē saṁniviṭṭhō
virahavihuriyaṅgō dīhanīsāsakhinnō ahilasiyapaya-tthā 'sāhaṇuvvinnacittō // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï pāsagaparimōyaṇotti nāmēṇa
surasundarināmāē kahāē turiō paricchēō 1000 // SurSuCa.1000



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 171]
[pañcamaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha sō daṭhṭhūṇa mamaṁ viddāṇamuhaṁ galantanayaṇillaṁ
karayalanimiyakavōlaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō // SurSuCa.1

sundara! tuha sarisāṇaṁ uttamapurisāṇa jujjaï na kāuṁ
ahamajaṇasamāinnō appavahō kugaïsañjaṇaṇō // SurSuCa.2

annaṁ ca kō si tumaṁ kassa kaō kēṇa va kajjēṇa ēyamāyariyaṁ?
kīsa sasōgō sundara! aviralathūlaṁsuai muyasi? // SurSuCa.3

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ tattō ya maē tayā imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
kiṁ kahiyāē imāē vihalāē suyaṇu! vattāē? // SurSuCa.4

kahiēṇa jēṇa labbhaï kōvi guṇō, tamiha sāhiuṁ juttaṁ
annaha puṇa tusakhaṇḍaṇasarisēṇaṁ kiṁ nu kahiēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.5


[p. 172]
aviya vōlīṇapāyakajjē sāhārō kōvi natthi kahiēṇa
gayapāṇiyammi pālīi bandhaṇaṁ kaṁ guṇaṁ lahaü? // SurSuCa.6

dussahadukkhasamucchēyaṇammi ujjuttamāṇasassa tumē
kīsa kayaṁ maha vigdhaṁ pāṇaccāyaṁ karēntassa? // SurSuCa.7

tā mā kāhisi iṇhimpi majjha vigghanti, tāhi sō bhaṇaï
mā bhadda! kuṇasu ēvaṁ sāhasu maha kāraṇa tāva // SurSuCa.8

vinnāyammi sarūvē jēṇa uvāōvi labbhaē kōvi
tattō ya maē kahiyā nīsēsā puvvavattā sē // SurSuCa.9

ullambaṇaavasāṇā taṁ sōuṁ suppaïṭṭha! tēṇāhaṁ
bhaṇiō juvaīē kaē na hu juttaṁ uttamanarāṇa // SurSuCa.10

ērisamāyariuṁ bhō! visēsaō tumha nīikusalāṇa
jīvantā jēṇa narā kallāṇaparaṁ paramuvinti // SurSuCa.11


[p. 173]
kiñca dhannō si tumaṁ jassatthi tāva annōnnavayaṇasañcārō
taha dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ āsāē nibandhaṇaṁ atthi // SurSuCa.12

taha ēganagaravāsō avarōpparabhāvajaṇaṇasaṅgabbhō
tā kīsa kuṇasi sōyaṁ, dhannō taṁ punnavantō ya // SurSuCa.13

maha puṇa punnavihūṇassa kahavi taddaṁsaṇammi jā āsā
tīēvi hu dāliddaṁ tahavi hu dhārēmi niyapāṇē // SurSuCa.14

kittiyamittaṁ dukkhaṁ hontē vayaṇakkamammi tuha bhadda!?
jaṁ maha maṇadaïyāē ṭhāṇāiṁ ayāṇamāṇassa // SurSuCa.15

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sāhasu maha tāva niyayavuttantaṁ
ṭhāṇampi nēya jāṇasi kaha ṇu tumaṁ niyadaïyāē? // SurSuCa.16

kammi purē tuha vāsō kēṇava kajjēṇa āgaō ēttha?
tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēgamaṇō bhō! nisāmēhi // SurSuCa.17


[p. 174]
ētthēva atthi sēlē bahuvijjāharapurōhaparikaliē
suvibhattatiyacaükkaṁ nāṇāujjāṇaramaṇīyaṁ // SurSuCa.18

suvisālasālakaliyaṁ sakkandaṇapuravarassa sāricchaṁ
uttarasẹ̄dhīē puraṁ pavaraṁ suranandaṇaṁ nāma // SurSuCa.19

[yugmam]
sāhīṇasayalavijjō vijjāharaniyarapaṇayapayakamalō
kamaladalatullanayaṇō nayaṇamaṇāṇandaṇō sūrō // SurSuCa.20

sūrōvva nihayatēyassitēyanivahō akhaṇḍiyapayāvō
dappiṭṭhavaïrivāraṇanivāraṇē sīhapōyasamō // SurSuCa.21

vijjāharāṇa rāyā supasiddhō cēva savvakhayarāṇa
pasarantavimalakittī āsī haricandanāmotti // SurSuCa.22

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
sarasiruhasarisavayaṇā nīluppaladalavisālavaranayaṇā
kamalōyararuidēhā rayaṇavaī nāma sē mahilā // SurSuCa.23


[p. 175]
sayalōrōhapahāṇāē tīē pāṇappiyāē dēvīē
samayaṁ tivaggasāraṁ visayasuhaṁ aṇuhavantassa // SurSuCa.24

dēvakumārasaricchō aha tīē dāraō samuppannō
uciyasamaē ya tēhiṁ pahañjaṇō nāma sē vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.25

dhūyā ya bandhusundarināmā asamāṇaruvalāvannā
dōnnivi tāiṁ kamasō pattāiṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ // SurSuCa.26

aha annayā kayāivi avarōpparanēhagaruyabhāvāṇaṁ
ēgantammi ṭhiyāṇaṁ ullāvō tēsiṁ sañjāō // SurSuCa.27

bhaṇiyaṁ pahañjaṇēṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ tuha hōi kiñcijamavaccaṁ
dhūyā vā taṇaō vā taṁ maha taṇayassa dāyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.28

aviya tujjha mahaṁ vā jaṁ hōjja kimpi iha paḍhamagaṁ tu ḍimbharuyaṁ
avarōpparasambandhō tāṇaṁ amhēhiṁ kāyavvō // SurSuCa.29


[p. 176]
tā bandhusundarīē tahatti bahu manniyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ
garuyasahōyarasabbhāvanēhaakkhittacittāē // SurSuCa.30

ēttō ya atthinayaraṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarāē sẹ̄dhīē
savvōuyataruvaṇasaṇḍamaṇḍiyaṁ camaracañcanti // SurSuCa.31

tattha ya khayaranarīsō bhāṇugaï nāma atullasāmatthō
nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvō kāmiṇijaṇamāṇasāṇandō // SurSuCa.32

haricandakhayarapavarēṇa niyasuyā bandhusundarī tassa
dinnā varapīīē vivāhiā sāyaraṁ tēṇa // SurSuCa.33

tīi sutaṇūi samayaṁ aṇuhavamāṇō u garuyapīīē
pañcapayārē visaē bhāṇugaī bhuñjaï rajjaṁ // SurSuCa.34

vaccantēsu diṇēsuṁ tīē dēvīē dāriyā jāyā
ujjōiyadisivalayā u cittalēhatti nāmēṇa // SurSuCa.35


[p. 177]
tayaṇantaraṁ ca dēvī sundarasuviṇēhiṁ sūiya taṇayaṁ
sūyā suhatihirikkhē cittagaï nāma sē vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.36

haricandōvi hu rāyā cāraṇasamaṇassa sumuhanāmassa
payamūlē sōūṇaṁ jiṇadhammaṁ siddhisuhahēuṁ // SurSuCa.37

niyayapaē ṭhaviūṇaṁ pahañjaṇaṁ niyasuyaṁ viṇikkhantō
saṁsāravāsabhīō nivvinnō kāmabhōgāṇa // SurSuCa.38

[yūgmam]
sāmannaṁ kāūṇaṁ payamūlē cāraṇassa sumuhassa
niṭṭhaviyakammajālō, antagaḍō kēvalī jāō // SurSuCa.39

jō pahañjaṇōvi hu vijjāharanaravaī payāvillō
bhuñjaï jaṇayaviiṇṇaṁ rajjaṁ gayasayalaāsaṅkō // SurSuCa.40

tassaya sayalantēurapavarāō dunni aggamahisīō
kalahaṁsī mañjūsā uttamavaṁsappasūyāō // SurSuCa.41


[p. 178]
kalahaṁsīē jāō puttō jalaṇappahotti nāmēṇa
mañjūsāē lahuō puttō kaṇagappahō nāmō // SurSuCa.42

niyayasahōyaravayaṇaṁ sumarantī bandhusundarī dēvī
nāūṇa cittalēhaṁ niyadhūyaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ pattaṁ // SurSuCa.43

aha taṁ bhāuyavayaṇaṁ sāhaï daïyassa bhāṇugaïṇō sā
tattō ya bhāṇugaïṇā niyadhūyā cittalēhā sā // SurSuCa.44

dinnā khayarapahañjaṇasuyassa jēṭṭhassa rūvajutassa
jalaṇapahassa, tēṇavi pariṇīyā paramapīīē // SurSuCa.45

[yugmam]
suranandaṇammi nayarē nīyā aha tīē nēhasahiyāē
saha visaē bhuñjantō ciṭṭhaï dēvōvva diyalōē // SurSuCa.46

aha annayā kayāivi khayarāhivaī pahañjaṇō daṭṭhuṁ
gayaṇē sasaṅkadhavalaṁ dēvaülagōrayaṁ gēhaṁ // SurSuCa.47


[p. 179]
aha cintiuṁ payattō maṇōharō handi! ēsa āgārō
ēyāgiīē tā haṁ kārēmi jiṇālayaṁ rammaṁ // SurSuCa.48

maṇikuṭṭimammi tattō ālihiuṁ ujjaō jayā rāyā
tāva ya jhatti vilīṇō pavaṇahaō jalaharō savvō // SurSuCa.49

daṭhṭhūṇaṁ taṁ vilīṇaṁ khaṇēṇa rāyā vicintaē ēvaṁ
ēvaṁvihā narāṇaṁ lacchīō cavalarūvāō // SurSuCa.50

jaha ēsō abbhalavō khaṇēṇa diṭṭhō puṇō paṇaṭṭhotti
taha savvēvi payatthā khaṇamittāṇandasañjaṇaṇā // SurSuCa.51

rūvaṁ ca jīviyaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ ca savvēvi bandhusambandhā
ēvamaṇiccā avvō! dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa // SurSuCa.52

paccakkhaṁ hi aṇiccaṁ nāūṇavi jaṁ thiraṁva mannanti
visayā ' 'sattā sattā, ēyaṁ avivēyasāmatthaṁ // SurSuCa.53


[p. 180]
nāūṇavi jiṇavayaṇaṁ ārambhapariggahēsu vaṭṭanti
kāmāsattā jaṁ puṇa ahō! mahāmōhamāhappaṁ // SurSuCa.54

tā 'laṁ mama rajjēṇaṁ saṁsāranivāsahēubhūēṇa
jāṇiyajiṇindavayaṇassa handi! gurudukkhamūlēṇa // SurSuCa.55

tā sāvajjaṁ vajjiya pavvajjāujjamaṁ karēmi lahuṁ
kiṁ maha imiṇā duggaïnibandhaṇāsārarajjēṇa? // SurSuCa.56

annaṁ ca majjha vaṁsē rajjaṁ dāūṇa niyayaputtāṇa
bahavē kayasāmannā rāyāṇō pāviyā sugaïṁ // SurSuCa.57

tavvaṁsapasūēṇa maēvi kāyavvayaṁ imaṁ tamhā
iya cintiūṇa rāyā saṁsaï saṁnihiyakhayarāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.58

ētthantarē sughōsō caünāṇī cāraṇō muṇī tattha
virahantō sampattō bhaviyāṇa vibōhaṇaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.59


[p. 181]
rāyā pahañjaṇō aha suyassa jalaṇappahassa aha rajjaṁ
dāūṇa tahā kaṇagappahassa pannattivaravijjaṁ // SurSuCa.60

tattō ya viṇikkhantō sughōsasāhussa pāyamūlammi
avahāya rāyalacchiṁ pahañjaṇō khayararāyatti // SurSuCa.61

jalaṇappahōvi bhuñjaï rāyasiriṁ khayaraniyaraparikinnō
sayalōrōhapahāṇāi cittalēhāi samayanti // SurSuCa.62

kaṇagappahōvi sāhiya vijjaṁ pannattināmiyaṁ vihiṇā
vijjāpabhāvasañjāyagaruyasāmatthavitthārō // SurSuCa.63

ujjhiya niyavaṁsakamaṁ aṇavikkhiya ayasapaḍahayaṁ lōē
bahumanniya avivēyaṁ aviyāriya dōggaïgamaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.64

aṇavēkkhiya gurubhāvaṁ aṅgīkāūṇa taha adakkhinnaṁ
rāyasirilōluēṇaṁ vijjābaladappabhariēṇa // SurSuCa.65


[p. 182]
jalaṇappahassa jiṭṭhassa bhāuṇō piuvidinnarajjapayaṁ
uddāliyaṁ tu kaṇagappahēṇa vijjāpabhāvāō // SurSuCa.66

[catasr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
tattō ahiṭṭhiyaṁ taṁ rajjaṁ savvampi uggatēēṇa
sāmāiṇā savvō vasīkaō khayaraniurambō // SurSuCa.67

nīsāriō sabhūmīō tāhi jalaṇappahō kaṇiṭṭhēṇa
nayarammi camaracañcē samāgaō sasurapāsammi // SurSuCa.68

bahumāṇapuvvayaṁ sō pavēsiō niyapurammi sasurēṇa
bhāṇugaïrāiṇā aha samayaṁ ciya cittalēhāē // SurSuCa.69

aha paramapamōēṇaṁ tahiṁ vasantassa suranayarammi
bhō cittavēga! tassa u vōlīṇā vāsarā kaïvi // SurSuCa.70

aha annayā kayāivi jalaṇapahō sālaēṇa sañjuttō
cittagaïnāmaēṇaṁ nīhariō tāō nayarāō // SurSuCa.71


[p. 183]
pēcchantō bahuvihaüvavaṇāṁi ramaṇīyatarusaṇāhāiṁ
bhāraṇḍacakkamaṇḍiyapasannajaladīhiyānivahaṁ // SurSuCa.72

pasariyasiyabhāsāiṁ pēcchantō girivarassa siharāiṁ
kinnaramihuṇasusaṅgakayalīharavihiyasōhammi // SurSuCa.73

aïkalakūiyakalayaṇṭhilaṭṭhakōlāhalābhiramaṇīē
paribhamirabhamaraniurambagaruyajhaṅkāramahurammi // SurSuCa.74

ēgammi vaṇaniguñjē phalabharaviṇamantadumasayāinnē
pattō sakōugēṇaṁ samayaṁ ciya cittagaïṇā u // SurSuCa.75

[catusr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
vāyantamaüyamāruyahallantasupallavōhasōhillaṁ
pēcchaï rattāsōyaṁ mahuyarigaṇavihiyahalabōlaṁ // SurSuCa.76

tassa ya ahē niviṭṭhō kañcaṇapaümammi muṇivarō diṭṭhō
vijjāharanarakinnarasuravisarēṇaṁ namijjantō // SurSuCa.77


[p. 184]
uppannavimalakēvalanāṇō aha suravarēhiṁ thuvvantō
āsannē uṇa jalaṇappahēṇa sō paccabhinnāō // SurSuCa.78

sō ēsō majjha piyā pahañjaṇō nāma muṇivarō ēvaṁ
siṭṭhammi cittagaïṇō tattō tē dōvi harisēṇa // SurSuCa.79

ti païkkhiṇiuṁ sammaṁ harisavasuṭṭhantabahalarōmañcā
paṇamiyakēvalicalaṇā viṇiviṭṭhā dharaṇivaṭṭhammi // SurSuCa.80

[yugmam]
nijjiyasanīrajīmūyaghōsagambhīrabhāraīē taō
tīi parisāi bhayavaṁ pāraddhō dēsaṇaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.81

aviya gayakalahakannacavalā lacchī maṇuyāṇamāumaṇiccaṁ
jōvvaṇamavi maṇuyāṇaṁ sahasatti jarā abhiddavaï // SurSuCa.82

rōgasayapīḍiyaṁ tampi jōvvaṇaṁ jāi jīvalōgammi
iṭṭhaviyōgā 'ṇiṭṭhappaōgadukkhēhiṁ kēsiñci // SurSuCa.83


[p. 185]
aïparimiyammi cavalē rōgajarāsōgavāhipaürammi
jīvāṇa jōvvaṇē ērisammi kō nāma paḍibandhō? // SurSuCa.84

visayā kugaïnimittaṁ uvabhuttā tucchagā tahā tēvi
virasā saï avasāṇē tēsu taō kō va paḍibandhō? // SurSuCa.85

iya saṁsārē sāraṁ jaṁ kira paḍihāsaē vivajjāsā
tampi hu duhasayahēutti jāṇiuṁ kuṇaha jiṇadhammaṁ // SurSuCa.86

jaṁ dulahā sāmaggī ēsā tubbhēhiṁ bhavasamuddammi
pattā apattapuvvā tā mā taṁ nipphalaṁ nēha // SurSuCa.87

ēsā hu puṇō dulahā jāīlakkhōhasaṅkulabhavammi
hiṇḍantāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ na ya annaṁ jiṇamayaṁ mōttuṁ // SurSuCa.88

tamhā jiṇēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ dikkhaṁ ghēttūṇa sañjamaṁ kāuṁ
ujjhiya tō saṁsāra pāvaha siddhīē pavarasuhaṁ // SurSuCa.89


[p. 186]
ēvaṁ muṇiṇā dhammammi sāhiē kēvi tattha pavvaïyā
jāyā uvāsayā taha annē sammaṁ pavannatti // SurSuCa.90

ētthantarammi paṇamiya jalaṇapahō vinnavēi niyapiyaraṁ
bhayavaṁ! puṇaravi rajjaṁ kiṁ taṁ maha hōjja nō ahavā? // SurSuCa.91

aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ hōhī, taṁ kaïya, pucchiyamaṇēṇa
tō bhaṇaï muṇivarindō kēvalavinnāyaparamatthō // SurSuCa.92

bhāṇugaïdinnarōhiṇivijjāē sāhiyāē tē bhadda!
hōhī puṇaravi khayarāhivattaṇaṁ natthi sandēhō // SurSuCa.93

ēvaṁ muṇiṇā bhaṇiē pahasiyavayaṇēhiṁ vandiō bhayavaṁ
ētthantarammi parisā jahāgayaṁ paḍigayā savvā // SurSuCa.94

tattō tē dōvi jaṇā samāgayā jhatti niyayanayarammi
cittagaïṇā ya kahiyaṁ kēvalivayaṇaṁ tu niyapiuṇō // SurSuCa.95


[p. 187]
tattō ya bhāṇugaïṇā sōhaṇarikkhammi rōhiṇī vijjā
jāmāuyataṇayāṇaṁ dōṇhavi samayaṁ vidinnati // SurSuCa.96

bhaṇiyā ya puvvasēvaṁ karajāvavihāṇaō kuṇaha sammaṁ
vasimammi ṭhiyā samayaṁ chammāsaṁ jāva tō pacchā // SurSuCa.97

uttarasēvā uggā kāyavvā ēgagēhiṁ aḍavīē
bīēṇa puṇō uttarasāhagarūvēṇa hōyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.98

annaṁ ca bhīsaṇāsuvi vibhīsiyāsuṁ maṇaṁ na dāyavvaṁ
punnē sattamamāsē dēssaï aha daṁsaṇaṁ vijjā // SurSuCa.99

ēvaṁ rannā bhaṇiyā dōnnivi paṇamittu tassa payakamalaṁ
pāraddhā taṁ kāuṁ chammāsā jāva punnatti // SurSuCa.100

aha sattammi māsē gantuṁ aḍavīē tavvihī savvō
jalaṇappahēṇa puvviṁ pāraddhō jāvahōmāī // SurSuCa.101


[p. 188]
vasunandayakhaggakarō cittagaī tassa rakkhaō jāō
sōvi hu aṇannacittō pāraddhō taṁ vihiṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.102

annadivasammi turiyaṁ āgacchantī pakampamāṇataṇū
diṭṭhā u cittalēhā bhayabhīyā tammi ṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.103

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ niyabhagiṇiṁ cittagaī bhaṇaï kattha taṁ bhaddē!
āyā subhīsaṇāē ēkkallā ēttha aḍavīē? // SurSuCa.104

kassa va bhaēṇa gāḍhaṁ kampasi taṁ bhagiṇi! tāhi sā bhaṇaï
nayarāu niggayā haṁ pariyariyā dāsacēḍīhiṁ // SurSuCa.105

pattā ujjāṇammī tattha maē pūiō kusumabāṇō
niyagihamāgacchantī vimōhiyā jhatti kēṇāvi // SurSuCa.106

mōttūṇaṁ pariyaṇaṁ taṁ palāyamāṇī samāgayā ēttha
aḍavīē tāva maē diṭṭhō kaṇagappahō sahasā // SurSuCa.107


[p. 189]
pāvēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ iccha mamaṁ tāhi gāḍhakuddhāē
akkōsiō sa bahuhā niṭṭhuravayaṇēhiṁ mē tāhē // SurSuCa.108

uggīriūṇa khaggaṁ bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa icchasu mamanti
aha navi, tō tē sīsaṁ chindāmi imēṇa khaggēṇa // SurSuCa.109

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiyā palāyamāṇī bhaēṇa kampantī
pattā tumha samīvē rakkha mamaṁ tāō pāvāō // SurSuCa.110

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇiṁ taṁ sahasā āgamma giṇhiuṁ hatthē
uppaïō kaṇagapahō tamāladalasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.111

hā! rakkha rakkha bhāuya! hā vallaha! kuṇasu maha parittattiṁ
ēmāi vilavamāṇiṁ hīrantiṁ daṭṭhu niyabhagiṇiṁ // SurSuCa.112

niyakulakalaṅkakāraya! kattha mamaṁ jīsi diṭṭhipahapaḍiō?
purisō bhava ēsa tuhaṁ sīsacchēyaṁ karēmitti // SurSuCa.113


[p. 190]
ēmāi vāharantō cittagaī gahiyanisiyakaravālō
aṇumaggēṇuppaïō bhagiṇiē vimōyaṇaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.114

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
aha taṁ vimōhayantō kaṇagapahō āgaō niyanayarē
cittagaīvi khayarō aṇumaggaṁ tassa sampattō // SurSuCa.114

tattō vimōhaṇīē vijjāē mōhiūṇa cinttagaïṁ
suranandaṇē paviṭṭhō kaṇagapahō niyayanayarammi // SurSuCa.116

aha sō mōhiyacittō cittagaī tattha vāhirujjāṇē
vīsariyabhagiṇiharaṇō avayariō kōuhallēṇa // SurSuCa.117

daṭṭhuṁ jaṇasandōhaṁ usabhajiṇindassa pavarabhavaṇammi
jattāsamaē miliyaṁ vicittanēvatthasacchāyaṁ // SurSuCa.118

pavisiya jiṇindabhavaṇaṁ vandiya bhattīi paḍhamajiṇanāhaṁ
uvaviṭṭhō cittagaī vijjāharaniyaramajjhammi // SurSuCa.119


[p. 191]
pattō khaṇantarāō jalaṇappahapēsiō narō ēgō
pucchantō cittagaïṁ damaghōsō nāma jiṇabhavaṇē // SurSuCa.120

daṭṭhūṇa ya cittagaïṁ paṇamiya nēūṇa tāhi ēgantē
damaghōsō bhaṇaï taō bhagiṇīē vimōyaṇaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.121

uppaïō tāva tumaṁ, jalaṇapahō picchiumpi taṁ savvaṁ
akkhuhiyamaṇō sammaṁ navi caliō niyayakiriyāō // SurSuCa.122

[yugmam]
niccalacittaṁ daṭṭhuṁ jalaṇapahaṁ mantajāvavāvāraṁ
aha sā rōhiṇivijjā paccakkhā jhatti sañjāyā // SurSuCa.123

bhaṇiyaṁ tīē puttaya! aṇannasarisaṁ hi suṭṭhu dhīrattaṁ
tā siddhā tujjha ahaṁ bhaṇasu ya jaṁ majjha kāyavvaṁ? // SurSuCa.124

bhaṇiyaṁ jalappahēṇaṁ avahariyā majjha bhāriyā jā sā
kaṇagappahēṇaṁ, taṁ tāva sigghamāṇēha maha pāsaṁ // SurSuCa.125


[p. 192]
bhaṇiyaṁ vijjāi taō suṇasu imaṁ tāva vaïyaraṁ putta!
kēvalivayaṇāīō savvōvi hu vaïyarō tassa // SurSuCa.126

pannattīē kahiō tattō sō āgaō tuha samīvē
khōhaṇahēuṁ savvaṁ māyāē kayaṁ imaṁ tēṇa // SurSuCa.127

[yugmam]
tuha mahilā niyagēhē acchaï niruvaddavā suhēṇaṁ tu
cittagaī puṇa tēṇaṁ vimōhiō mōhaṇipabhāvā // SurSuCa.128

suranandaṇammi nayarē jiṇindabhavaṇammi acchaï niviṭṭhō
tā mā kāhisi kiñcivi ētthatthē putta! uvvēvaṁ // SurSuCa.129

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ vijjā adaṁsaṇaṁ jhatti uvagayā tāhē
ahayaṁ jalaṇapahēṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō tumha pāsammi // SurSuCa.130

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō damaghōsēṇaṁ amūḍhacittō sō
cittagaī sañjāō caliō saha tēṇa niyaṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.131


[p. 193]
ētthantarammi nhavaṇē vittappāyammi jiṇavarindassa
pavisaï nayarē lōgō nāṇāvihavāhaṇārụ̄dhō // SurSuCa.132

aviya kōvi hu sibiyārụ̄dhō ārụ̄dhō rahavarēsu cittēsu
hayagayaassatarēsuṁ ḍōliyajugēsu vivihēsu // SurSuCa.133

ētthantarammi hatthī kaṇagappahasantiō mahākāō
mayamattō ummiṭṭhō nīhariō tāō nayarāō // SurSuCa.134

bhañjantō gihadārē uḍ̣dhōsēntō varaṇḍaē bahusō
mārintō jaṇaniyaraṁ acchōlintō rahē vivihē // SurSuCa.135

aha taṁ kayantasarisaṁ uḍ̣dhīkayagurukaraṁ sughōramuhaṁ
daṭṭhuṁ naṭṭhō lōō disō disiṁ maraṇabhayabhīō // SurSuCa.136

sōvi hu pavahaṇanivahaṁ bhañjantō dantapāyaghāēhiṁ
ucchōlintō suṇḍāi hiṇḍaē savvaō tattha // SurSuCa.137


[p. 194]
kōūhalēṇa gayaṇē pariṭṭhiō pulōiüṁ payattō sō
cittagaī mattakariṁ kayantavayaṇaṁva duppicchaṁ // SurSuCa.138

ētthantarammi ēgammi rahavarē paḍhamajōvvaṇārambhā
juvaī aṇannarūvā bahuvihavarabhūsaṇāinnā // SurSuCa.139

ummaggapayaṭṭēhiṁ jaccaturaṅgēhiṁ hatthitaṭṭhēhiṁ
bhaggammi rahē bhūmīi nivaḍiyā vigayajīyavva // SurSuCa.140

[yugmam]
navanīluppalasacchahavisālalōlantalōyaṇā varaī
sambhaggakannakuṇḍalaviluliyavarakuntalakalāvā // SurSuCa.141

vicchinnakaṇayakhiṅkhiṇiniyarapalambantamēhalādāmā
īsīsihārapacchannathaṇaharā galiyasirakusumā // SurSuCa.142

vihaḍiyaaṅgayajuyalā nivaḍiyakaḍayā paṇaṭṭhagēvijjā
tuṭṭaguṇahāraviyaliyamuttāhalasōhiyasarīrā // SurSuCa.143


[p. 195]
sambhagganēurajuyā musumūriyarayaṇamāliyāniyarā
bhūmitalaluliyadēhā aha diṭṭhā tēṇa sā kariṇā // SurSuCa.144

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
tattō ujjhiyahatthō tīi vahaṭṭhāi karivarō caliō
taṁ daṭṭhu pariyarēṇa garuō hāhāravō vihiō // SurSuCa.145

susiliṭṭhaaṅguvaṅgaṁ aha taṁ paḍipunnacandasamavayaṇaṁ
karagijjhamajjhabhāgaṁ viyaḍaniyambatthaliṁ juvaïṁ // SurSuCa.146

daṭṭhumpi samāsannaṁ nāgaṁ, gantuṁ acāyamāṇiṁ tu
maraṇabhayāō gāḍhaṁ vēvantasarīrayaṁ khuddhaṁ // SurSuCa.147

tāyāramapikkhantiṁ sataralatāraṁ disō niyacchantiṁ
daṭṭhūṇaṁ citagaī gayaṇatthō cintaē ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.148

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
hā! hā! kāmanihāṇaṁ mahilārayaṇaṁ viṇassaï laggaṁ
ōyariūṇaṁ gayaṇāu tāhi aṅkammi sā gahiā // SurSuCa.149


[p. 196]
ghittūṇa sayaṁ sahasā ṭhāṇē niruvaddavammi nēūṇa
sīyalataruchāyāē nivēsiyā kuṭṭimucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.150

tattō ya uttarīyamiupavaṇā ' 'sāsiyāē sō tīē
lajjāsajjhasamaüliyanayaṇēhiṁ pulōiō tattō // SurSuCa.151

ciyapariciyaṁva daṭṭhuṁ taṁ taruṇaṁ garuyanēhasabbhāvā
amaēṇava saṁsittā jāyā aha viyasiyakavōlā // SurSuCa.152

cittagaīvi ya tīē daṭhṭhūṇa aṇōvamaṁ tayaṁ rūvaṁ
tavvayaṇanisiyanipphandalōyaṇō ciṭṭhaī jāva // SurSuCa.153

tāva ya tīē dhāī kaïvayajuvaīhiṁ parigayā jhatti
āgantuṁ uvaviṭṭhā bhaṇaï tayaṁ mahuravāṇīē // SurSuCa.154

[yugmam]
parakajjakaraṇanirayā havanti kira sajjaṇatti saccaviyaṁ
kannagamēyaṁ mōyantaēṇa tumaē gaïndāō // SurSuCa.155


[p. 197]
tā nikkāraṇavacchala! tujjha pabhāvāō jīviyā ēsā
ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ abhinandiya sā puṇō bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.156

gacchāmi amha gēhaṁ ussūraṁ vaṭṭaē jaō iṇhiṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ ca cittagaïṇā ēvaṁ kuṇahatti tattō ya // SurSuCa.157

niyanayarābhimuhāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ caliyāṇa tīē kannāē
cittagaïkarayalaō muddārayaṇaṁ lahuṁ gahiyaṁ // SurSuCa.158

niyayakarasaṇṭhiyaṁ puṇa samappiyaṁ tassa tāṇa pacchannaṁ
aha sā sajjhasavēviradēhā gantuṁ payaṭṭatti // SurSuCa.159

valiyaggīvaṁ tīē aïguruaṇurāyapisuṇadiṭṭīē
nijjhāiō tahāsō jaha jāō kusumasaravisaō // SurSuCa.160

aha sā sahiyaṇasahiyā kamēṇa niyapuravaraṁ paviṭṭhatti
cittagaīvi ya tīē jōvvaṇarūvēhiṁ hayahiyaō // SurSuCa.161


[p. 198]
cittalihiuvva jāō khaṇantaraṁ vigayaannavāvārō
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ damaghōsō saviṇayamēvaṁ samullavaï // SurSuCa.162

[yugmam]
attha girisiharamaṇusaraï diṇayarō ēsa viyaliyapayāvō
tā gammaü niyaṭhāṇē kumāra! kimiṇā vilambēṇa? // SurSuCa.163

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ kāuṁ āgārasaṁvaraṁ bhaṇaï
ēvaṁ karēmu navaraṁ kāraṇamēyaṁ vilambassa // SurSuCa.164

maha hatthāō paḍiyaṁ muddārayaṇaṁ tu ēttha katthavi ya
taṁ gavisiuṁ pabhāē jhaḍatti ahamāgamissāmi // SurSuCa.165

taṁ puṇa gacchasu sigdhaṁ kahējja jalaṇappahassa vuttantaṁ
īsi hasiūṇa taō damaghōsō ēvamullavaï 166 // SurSuCa.166

paccakkhammivi diṭṭhē kumāra! kiṁ ēttha vaṅkabhaṇiēēhiṁ?
kiṁ navi diṭṭhā kannā tuha hatthā taṁ pagiṇhantī // SurSuCa.167


[p. 199]
tā kavaḍaṁ mōttūṇaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva sāhiuṁ juttaṁ
kannāē mūlasuddhiṁ uvalabhiuṁ āgamissāmi // SurSuCa.168

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō cittagaī vihasiūṇa vajjaraï
sammaṁ viyāṇiyaṁ tē maṇōgayaṁ majjha damaghōsa! // SurSuCa.169

aha sō kayappaṇāmō uppaïō pāviō niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ
cittagaīvi paviṭṭhō jugāijiṇamandirē rammē // SurSuCa.170

vandiyajiṇindabimbō jiṇaüggahavajjiyammi ēgantē
gantūṇaṁ uvaviṭṭhō samāgayā tāva rayaṇīvi // SurSuCa.171

aha cintiuṁ payattō kiṁ mannē tīi majjha hatthāō
gahiuṁ muddārayaṇaṁ kiṁvā maha ̣dhōiyaṁ niyayaṁ? // SurSuCa.172

kaṇa ṇu maē nāyavvaṁ tīē kulaṁ kahava sā varēyavvā
jaï sā havijja mahilā havijja tō jīviyaṁ sahalaṁ // SurSuCa.173


[p. 200]
tārisarūvajuyāē samayaṁ iha visayasēvaṇaṁ juttaṁ
tadabhāvē visayāsā viḍambaṇā majjha pajihāi // SurSuCa.174

sō ya kayatthō purisō laggijjā jassa karayalē bālā
rambhāgabbhasukōmalabāhulayā haṁsagaïgamaṇā // SurSuCa.175

dhannō hamittiēṇaṁ gahiyā aṅkammi sā maē sutaṇū
avagūhiyā ya gāḍhaṁ jaṁ na maē vañciō taṁ tu // SurSuCa.176

puṇaravi havijja jattā hatthibhaē bhūminivaḍiyā taha sā
ghittūṇa jēṇa sahasā avayāsējjā tayaṁ gāḍhaṁ // SurSuCa.177

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ vicitayantassa taggayamaṇassa
niddāē samaṁ rāī khayaṁ gayā, uggaō sūrō // SurSuCa.178

aha sō pahāyasamaē vihiṇā vandittu jiṇavaraṁ paḍhamaṁ
caliō kannā kulaharaviyāṇaṇatthaṁ purābhimuhō // SurSuCa.179


[p. 201]
pattō ya puraṁ picchaï jaṇarahiyaṁ sunnasayaladhavalaharaṁ
puralacchivippamukkaṁ uvvasiyaṁ aḍavipaḍiruvaṁ // SurSuCa.180

aha picchiūṇa taṁ sō vimhiyahiyaō maṇēṇa cintēi
kattō hanta! akaṇḍē puramēyaṁ uvvasaṁ jāyaṁ? // SurSuCa.181

kiṁ hōjja indayālaṁ ahavā saccaṁ hi uvvasaṁ ēyaṁ
kiṁ kuviēṇa surēṇaṁ avahariyamimāō ṭhāṇāō // SurSuCa.182

ahavā bhayāō kassavi naṭṭhō lōgō imāō nayarāō
ēvaṁ vicintayantō cittagaī pavisaī jāva // SurSuCa.183

tāvaya samuhamintō ēgō purisō pulōiō tēṇa
uvayārapuvvayaṁ sō mahuragirāē imaṁ bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.184

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
bhaddamuha! kiṁnimittaṁ uvvasiyaṁ puravaraṁ imaṁ sahasā
tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi // SurSuCa.185


[p. 202]
tāva supasiddhamēyaṁ vijjāpannattigavviō sūrō
pālaï puravaramēyaṁ kaṇagapahō khayararāyatti // SurSuCa.186

jalaṇappahassa jēṭṭhassa bhāuṇō piuvidinnarajjapayaṁ
uddāliūṇa jēṇiha ahiṭṭhiyaṁ appaṇā cēva // SurSuCa.187

nīsāriō ya bhāyā jiṭṭhō sasurassa sō gaō nayarē
ēsōvi imammi purē acchaï rajjaṁ aṇuhavantō // SurSuCa.188

sasurēṇa bhāṇugaïṇā kila vijjā rōhiṇī u sē dinnā
sō sāhiuṁ payattō siṭṭhaṁ ca imassa vijjāē // SurSuCa.189

tattō tavvigghaṭṭhā rāyā kaṇagappahō gaō tattha
na ya khōbhiō sa tēṇaṁ maṇēṇa bhīō taō ēsō // SurSuCa.190

niyanayarābhimuhēṇaṁ āgacchantēṇa annacittēṇa
kahavi hu pamāyavasaō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ laṅghiyamaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.191


[p. 203]
puvvaṁ dharaṇindēṇaṁ ēsō samaō kaō nahayarāṇa
jiṇabhavaṇasāhupaḍimāṇaṁ laṅghaṇaṁ ēttha jō kāhī // SurSuCa.192

tassa khayarāhamassa ō vijjācchēō bhavissaī sahasā
ēvaṁ vēyaḍḍhanagē aïvidiyaṁ sayalakhayarāṇa // SurSuCa.193

[yugmam]
tattō imassa rannō jinabhavaṇaṁ laṅghiyanti ruṭṭhēṇa
dharaṇēṇa takkhaṇicciya vijjācchēō kaō bhadda! // SurSuCa.194

jalaṇappahassa vijjā siddhatti viyāṇiūṇa kaṇagapahō
vijjārahiō ihayaṁ ṭhāumasattōti aha naṭṭhō // SurSuCa.195

gaṅgāvattammi gaō bhayabhīō dakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē
sirigandhavāhaṇassa ō saraṇaṁ saha nāivaggēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.196

nāūṇa vaïyaramiṇaṁ khuhiō savvōvi nāyarō lōgō
pahurahiō bhayabhīō avarōpparamēvamullavaï // SurSuCa.197


[p. 204]
amhāṇa pahū naṭṭhō na ya sakkaï vāsiuṁ puraṁ ēyaṁ
tēṇa viṇā tā amhaṁ na juttamiha acchiuṁ iṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.198

kō kuṇaï amha rakkhaṁ ēttha vasantāṇa nāharahiyāṇa
savvēsiṁ tēṇa uciyaṁ puramēyaṁ ujjhiuṁ sigghaṁ // SurSuCa.199

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyammī nayaramahantēhiṁ mantakusalēhiṁ
savvōvi jaṇō naṭṭhō jāyaṁ aha sunnayaṁ nayaraṁ // SurSuCa.200

āsajja kāraṇamiṇaṁ uvvasiyaṁ tēṇa puravaraṁ ēyaṁ
cittagaī bhaṇaï taō kattha gaō sō jaṇa bhadda!? // SurSuCa.201

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kōvi jaṇō gayaṇavallahē nayarē
kōvi gaō vijayapurē kōvi hu iha vējayantammi // SurSuCa.202

sattuñjayammi kōvi hu ariñjaē kōvi taha gaō lōō
annō nandaṇanayarē avarō vimalammi nayarammi // SurSuCa.203


[p. 205]
rahanēurammi kōvi hu āṇandapurammi arijaē kōvi
sagaḍāmuhammi kōvi hu purīē taha vējayantīē // SurSuCa.204

kōvi hu rayaṇapurammi sirinayarē rayaṇasañcayaṁ kōvi
nayarammi jalāvattē kōvi gaō saṅkhanābhammi // SurSuCa.205

avarāvaranayarēsuṁ paḍivakkhasamāsaēṇa puralōō
savvōvi hu vikkhiriō sattuyapuñjōvva vāyahaō // SurSuCa.206

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa narō vihiyapaṇāmō sa gantumāraddhō
cittagaīvi ya tāhē sōccā tavvayaṇaṁ sahasā // SurSuCa.207

pahaüvva mōggarēṇaṁ giliō iva rakkhasēṇa khuhiēṇa
vajjēṇa tāḍiō iva dukkhaṁ aïdūsahaṁ pattō // SurSuCa.208

[yugmam]
aha cintiuṁ payattō daṭṭhavvā kattha sā maē bālā
maha hiyayakayāṇandā ēvaṁ vihiyammi hayavihiṇā? // SurSuCa.209


[p. 206]
itthavi nayarē tīē kulakōḍisamāulammi viulammi
daṁsaṇamavi aïdulahaṁ aviyāṇiyakulaharāē u // SurSuCa.210

iṇhiṁ puṇa nāṇāvihanayarēsuṁ pavasiyammi lōyammi
daïyāē paüttīyavi viyāṇaṇē sambhavō natthi // SurSuCa.211

tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ hayavihiṇā vihaḍiyammi ēyammi
labbhijja kaha paüttī kahavā maha daṁsaṇaṁ hōjjā? // SurSuCa.212

kō pucchijjaü nāmaṁ kō maha sāhijja kulaharaṁ tīē?
jattha gayā mama daïyā akkhijjā puravaraṁ kō taṁ? // SurSuCa.213

kahava tuḍijōgaō sā diṭṭhā amhēhiṁ hayavihiniōgā
iṇhiṁ puṇa daṭṭhavvā kō jāṇaï katthava navatti? // SurSuCa.214

tīē nāmakkharāiṁ virahapisāyassa mantabhūyāiṁ
suigōyaraṁ gayāiṁ na majjha hā! kattha vaccāmi? // SurSuCa.215


[p. 207]
hā! hiyaya! kāsa jhūrasi nibbandhaṁ muñca tammi lōyammi
ajjavi kā tuha āsā ṭhāṇampi ayāṇamāṇassa // SurSuCa.216

aviya jaï ḍajjhasi tā ḍajjhasu kuṭṭasi hē hiyaya! na hu nivārēmi
daïyāē jaṁ paüttīvi dullahā sampayaṁ jāyā // SurSuCa.217

ahavā kiṁ imiṇā cintiēṇa aïgaruyavisāyagabbhēṇa
avalambiya dhīrattaṁ kiñci uvāyaṁ vicintēmi // SurSuCa.218

jēṇa uvāyapayaṭṭā purisā pāvinti icchiyaṁ atthaṁ
summaï lōyammi jaō labbhaï suviṇaṁ suyantēhiṁ // SurSuCa.219

ēsō ya iha uvāō bhamāmi savvēsu khayaranayarēsu
mā kahaya kōvi katthavi tīē paüttimpi sāhijjā // SurSuCa.220

dāsijja ahava sakkhā paribbhamantēhi kammivi purammi
candamuhī sā bālā, tahā ya aïsundaraṁ cēva // SurSuCa.221


[p. 208]
ēvaṁ viṇicchiyatthō sō haṁ bhō cittavēga! cittagaī
daïyāviōyagurudukkhavajjaniddaliyamaṇasēlō // SurSuCa.222

paricattabandhuvaggō aha guruaṇurāyaparavasō tattō
ēgāgī vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarasẹ̄dhīē nayarēsu // SurSuCa.223

savvēsuvi paribhamiō na ya laddhā tīē katthavi paüttī
tattō ya dakkhiṇāē sēṇīē āgaō ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.224

tatthavi purēsu kēsuvi āhiṇḍiya icchiyaṁ apāvintō
ajja puṇō iha pattō tuha nayaraṁ kuñjarāvattē // SurSuCa.225

ēyammi ya ujjāṇē maha pavissantassa sōhaṇō saüṇō
sañjāō taha phuriyā dāhiṇabāhū tahā nayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.226

tattō viyappiyaṁ mē avassamajjēva hōhiī tīē
daïyāē daṁsaṇaṁ, ahava kiñci aïsōhaṇaṁ annaṁ // SurSuCa.227


[p. 209]
ēvaṁ vicintayantō pattō haṁ ēttha kayaligēhammi
kāūṇa pāyasōyaṁ uvaviṭṭhō kuṭṭimucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.228

tāva ya khaṇantarāō samāgayā suyaṇu! majjha niddatti
sōūṇa tujjha saddaṁ jhatti pabuddhō ahaṁ tattō // SurSuCa.229

kēṇa imaṁ ullaviyanti cintiuṁ jā disāō pulaēmi
tāva ya tumaṁ hi diṭṭhō palambamāṇō tarulayāē // SurSuCa.230

hā! hā! aṇaṅgarūvō kaha ṇu juvāṇō viṇassaē laggō?
ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ hāhāsaddaṁ karēmāṇō // SurSuCa.231

pattō tujjha samīvē chinnō aha pāsaō maē sahasā
bhō cittavēga! sēsaṁ paccakkhaṁ cēva tuha savvaṁ // SurSuCa.232

[yugmam]
taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ kaha ṇu tumaṁ bhadda! niyayadaïyāē
ṭhāṇampi nēya jāṇasi taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.233


[p. 210]
tō dulahaṁ maṇuyattaṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ rūvajōvvaṇasamēyaṁ
mahilāmittassa kaē na hu maraṇaṁ hōi kāyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.234

bhō cittavēga! jaïvi hu piyavirahē dūsahaṁ havaï dukkhaṁ
uttamakulappasūyāṇa tahavi ēyaṁ na juttanti // SurSuCa.235

jāṇāmi ahampi imaṁ maṇavallahamāṇusassa virahammi
naraē nēraïyassava uppajjaï dāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ // SurSuCa.236

tahavi hu na hōi juttō appavahō kintu kōvi hu uvāō
cintēyavvō jaha sā pāvijjaï hiyayavallahiyā // SurSuCa.237

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ vajjariē tēṇa cittagaïṇā ō
dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ hi maē samullaviyaṁ // SurSuCa.238

vōlīṇā tīi kahā na hu iṇhiṁ atthi kōvi uvāō
ajjēva ya rayaṇīē jaṁ hōhī tīi vivāhō // SurSuCa.239


[p. 211]
cittagaī bhaṇaï taō ēkkōvi ya tīē pāvaṇōvāō
maha phuraï māṇasammī jaï tuha paḍihāsaē suyaṇu! // SurSuCa.240

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē kō sō tattō sō bhaṇaï bhadda! nisuṇēsu
kila ēsō kulāyārō dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīē khayarāṇa // SurSuCa.241

kannāvivāhasamaē ēkallā pūyaē kusumabāṇaṁ
niyakulakamāgayaṁ aha pariṇijjaï sā taō pacchā // SurSuCa.242

taṁ kamamaṇupālintī sā ēhī mayaṇapūyaṇanimittaṁ
amhē puṇa dōvi jaṇā puvvaṁ ciya ittha pavisāmō // SurSuCa.243

aha tīē āgayāē nēvatthaṁ tīē santayaṁ ahayaṁ
ghittūṇa itthirūvō gacchissaṁ varayapāsammi // SurSuCa.244

ghitūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ taṁ puṇa nāsijja takkhaṇā cēva
ahayampi uvāēṇaṁ nāsissaṁ laddhapatthāvō // SurSuCa.245


[p. 212]
ēvaṁ hi kaē tīē sampattī atthi, nannahā bhadda!
taha dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ hōjjā ēvaṁ ca saccanti // SurSuCa.246

kiñca purisēṇa purisayārō kāyavvō tāva icchiyatthammi
vihiṇō niōgaō puṇa havaï hu kajjassa nipphattī // SurSuCa.247

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa kahiē uciē uvāē āgāmiyaṁ garuyadukkhamacintiūṇa
bhō suppaïṭṭha! vayaṇaṁ paḍivannayaṁ sē tivvāṇurāgaparimōhiyamāṇasēṇa // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi kaṇagamālāpāvaṇaüvaēsasūyagō bhaṇiō
surasundarīkahāē pañcamaō varaṁ paricchēō 1250 // SurSuCa.1250

itthantarammi sūrō bhamiūṇaṁ gayaṇamaṇḍalamasēsaṁ
avarasamuddaṁ pattō pahakhinnō majjaṁṇatthavaṁ // SurSuCa.1

bhaṇiyaṁ ca cittagaïṇā annāyā ēva ēttha pavisāmō
mayaṇassa gihē sampaï patthuaatthassa hēummi // SurSuCa.2

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti uṭṭhiyā dōvi
ucciṇiya kaïvayāiṁ pupphāiṁ tattha ujjāṇē // SurSuCa.3

pavisiya mayaṇassa gihē pūiya mayaṇaṁ ca ēvamullaviyaṁ
bhayavaṁ! tuha ppasāyā sampajjaō icchiyaṁ amha // SurSuCa.4

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa taō dōvi nilukkā aṇaṅgapaṭṭhīē
rayaṇīē jāmamittē bōlīṇē, kiñciahiyammi // SurSuCa.5


[p. 214]
bahupariyaṇapariyariyā gijjantā pavaramaṅgalasaēhiṁ
vajjantēṇa ya vivihaṁ nāṇāvihatūranivahēṇa // SurSuCa.6

niyasahiyaṇēṇa sahiyā ārụ̄dhā uttimāē sibiyāē
kayamaṅgalōvayārā siyabhūsaṇabhūsiyasarīrā // SurSuCa.7

siyavasaṇapāuyaṅgī ābaddhasugandhakusumaāmēlā
pattā ō kaṇagamālā dārē aha kāmagēhassa // SurSuCa.8

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
uttinnā siviyāō pūyaṇaüvagaraṇayaṁ gahēūṇa
dhariūṇa dāradēsē sayalaṁ niyapariyaṇaṁ tāhē // SurSuCa.9

ēgāgiṇī paviṭṭhā mayaraddhayabimbapūyaṇanimittaṁ
pavisittu bhavaṇadāraṁ aggaliyaṁ tāē bālāē // SurSuCa.10

[yugmam]
sampūiūṇa kāmaṁ aha sā nivaḍēvi tassa calaṇēsu
dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ galantathūlaṁsunayaṇillā // SurSuCa.11


[p. 215]
lahusaddēṇaṁ ēyaṁ sōvālambhaṁ sagaggaraṁ bhaṇaï
nijjiyasuramaṇuōvi hu paharasi itthīṇa kiṁ bhayavaṁ!? // SurSuCa.12

[yugmam]
jaï majjha tammi lōē bhayavaṁ! garuō kaō hu aṇurāō
tā kīsa taṁ pamōttuṁ ghaḍasi mamaṁ annalōēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.13

annaṁ ca summanti ittha lōē pañcēva silīmuhā ō kila tujjha
navaraṁ mamaṁ paḍuccā sahassabāṇōvva taṁ jāō // SurSuCa.14

jaï jāva majjha paharasi paharasu kō taṁ nivārēi bhayavaṁ!
navaraṁ taha maha paharasu kayantabhavaṇē jaha vayāmi // SurSuCa.15

tumaē puṇa taha pahayā jaha na mayā nēya jīviyā ahayaṁ
tā kiṁ bhaṇāmi iṇhiṁ saraṇammi samāgayā tujjha? // SurSuCa.16

daḍḍhassa huyavahēṇaṁ sō cēva jahōsahaṁ tu lōyassa
tumaē pīḍiyadēhā taha saraṇaṁ tujjha allīṇā // SurSuCa.17


[p. 216]
jaï majjha tumaṁ tuṭṭhō dēhi varaṁ patthiō maē ēyaṁ
mā maha havijja ērisaviḍambaṇā annajammēvi // SurSuCa.18

tāva imō maha jammō piyajaṇaāsāē vōliō ahalō
taṁ ciya daïyaṁ dijjasu bhayavaṁ! maha annajammēvi // SurSuCa.19

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ tāhi kaṇagamālāē
vialantathūlaaṁsuyapavāhasaṁsittasihiṇāē // SurSuCa.20

nāṇāviharayaṇaviṇimmiyammi pasarantavimalakiraṇammi
gabbhaharadāranihiē rammē aha tōraṇē tīē // SurSuCa.21

baddhō niuttarīēṇa pāsaō tāhi sā puṇō bhaṇaï
ēsā marāmi sampaï kusumāuha! tujjha puraō haṁ // SurSuCa.22

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
mā maha bhaṇijja kōvi hu vihiyamajuttanti kaṇagamālāē
ēttiyamittaṁ kālaṁ vimāliyaṁ jēṇa āsāē // SurSuCa.23


[p. 217]
iṇhiṁ puṇa na hu sakkā kāuṁ bhaṅgaṁ tu niyapaïnnāē
taṁ mōttuṁ hiyayadaïyaṁ na laggaē maha karē annō // SurSuCa.24

annaṁ ca dēvayāō! aliyaṁ jampanti nēya kaïyāvi
tampi hu annaha jāyaṁ majjha aünnēhiṁ pāvāē // SurSuCa.25

ahava kavaḍēṇa kēṇavi pisāyarūvēṇa vañciyā taïyā
nahavāhaṇabhattēṇaṁ ahavā khayarēṇa kēṇāvi // SurSuCa.26

tā sampayaṁmi mā hōjja majjha abhivañchiyatthavāghāō
bhayavaṁ! tuha ppasāyā sijjhaü maraṇaṁ avigghēṇa // SurSuCa.27

piyavirahagaruyamōggarajajjariyamaṇāē majjha pāvāē
maraṇaṁ hōjja na hōjja va ajjavi āsaṅkaē hiyayaṁ? // SurSuCa.28

piyavirahadukkhasamaṇaṁ labbhaï maraṇampi garuyapunnēhiṁ
taṁ jaï havijja iṇhiṁ sukayatthā hōjja tā ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.29


[p. 218]
ēvaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tīē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhatti
turiyaṁ gantūṇa maē chinnō aha pāsaō tīē // SurSuCa.30

gahiūṇa tayaṁ aṅkē tāhē saṇiyaṁ maē imaṁ bhaṇiyā
nijjiyasurāsurindō tuṭṭhō tuha suyaṇu! raïnāhō // SurSuCa.31

asarisasāhasaāvajjiēṇa mayaraddhaēṇa tuha suyaṇu!
ēyammi cēva jammē uvaṇīō sō jaṇō ēsō // SurSuCa.32

kijjaü kaṇṭhaggahaṇaṁ gāḍhaṁ ukkaṇṭhiō jaṇō tujjha
ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā bālā lajjāē ahōmuhī jāyā // SurSuCa.33

cittagaīvi ya tāhē samāgaō tammi cēva ṭhāṇammi
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ varamittō ēsa maha suyaṇu! // SurSuCa.34

tujjha viōē sundari! appavahē ujjaō ahamimēṇa
viṇivāriō akāraṇavacchallajuēṇa dhīrēṇa // SurSuCa.35


[p. 219]
tuha pāvaṇē uvāō ēsō maha sāhiō imēṇēva
ēēṇa sahāēṇaṁ sijjhissaï icchiyaṁ amha // SurSuCa.36

kannāsahāvasulahaṁ ujjhittā sajjhasaṁ suyaṇu! tamhā
niyanēvatthaṁ savvaṁ jhatti samuppēsu ēyassa // SurSuCa.37

kāūṇa tujjha rūvaṁ jēṇa imō suyaṇu! vaccaē bāhiṁ
pariyaṇavimōhaṇaṭṭhā parakajjasamujjaō dhīrō // SurSuCa.38

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiyā saharisahiyayā karēi taṁ savvaṁ
aha dōvi nilukkāiṁ puṇaravi mayaṇassa paṭṭhīē // SurSuCa.39

cittagaīvi ya tīē nīsēsaṁ nivisiūṇa nēvatthaṁ
ugdhāḍiuṁ duvāraṁ ārụ̄dhō jhatti siviyāē // SurSuCa.40

aha tammi gaï lōē nīsaddaṁ jāṇiūṇa taṁ bhavaṇaṁ
bhaṇiyā ya maē ēsā sundari! kiṁ iṇhi kāyavvaṁ? // SurSuCa.41


[p. 220]
ōṇayaṁmuhīē tīē sajjhasavasakampamāṇagattāē
kahakahavi hu ullaviō khalantaavvattavāṇīē // SurSuCa.42

guruvirahapīḍiyāē piyayama! taṁ pāviō tuḍivasēṇa
