taïyā ya maṇī divvō samappiō jīvarakkhaṭṭhā // SurSuCa.9

tattō ya gaō turiyaṁ ghaṇavāhaṇamuṇivarassa pāsammi
diṭṭhō ya maē dēvō uvasaggaṁ tassa kuṇamāṇō // SurSuCa.10

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē rē! rē! tiyasāhama! kattha vaccasē iṇhiṁ
dēvidavandiyāṇaṁ muṇīṇa ēvaṁ karēmāṇō? // SurSuCa.11


[p. 341]
uppāyantō pīḍaṁ muṇīṇa samasattumittavaggāṇaṁ
pāviṭṭha! kattha vaccasi diṭṭhīmaggammi maha paḍiō? // SurSuCa.12

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiē bhavaṇavaī sō surō sasambhantō
naṭṭhō sahasā tāva ya sukkajjhāṇē paviṭṭhassa // SurSuCa.13

muṇiṇō mōhāvagamā uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ varaṁ nāṇaṁ
kēvalimahimā vihiyā taō maē paramaviṇaēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.14

[yugmam]
sōuṁ dunduhisaddaṁ dēvā maṇuyā ya āgayā bahavē
kahiō tēsiṁ dhammō kēvaliṇā mōkkhasuhahēū // SurSuCa.15

patthāvaṁ lahiūṇaṁ puṭṭhō sō kēvalī maē ēvaṁ
bhayavaṁ! kiṁ avaraddhaṁ imassa dēvassa tumhēhiṁ // SurSuCa.16

jēṇēsō pāvamaī jīviyavavarōvaṇammi ujjuttō?
tō bhaṇaï muṇī nisuṇasu jaha vēraṁ āsi anna bhavē // SurSuCa.17


[p. 342]
dhāyaïsaṇḍavidēhē campānāmēṇa āsi varanayarī
tīē paümō rāyā juvarāyā samarakēutti // SurSuCa.18

jiṇavayaṇabhāviyappā sahōyarā dōvi nēhasañjuttā
pālēnti dēsaviraïṁ rajjadhuraṁ taha ya nīīē // SurSuCa.19

atthāṇamuvagayāṇaṁ nāhiyavāī samāgaō kavilō
vajjaraï natthi jīvō na ya savvannū na nēvvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.20

jiṇamayasatthatthaviyāṇaēṇa juvarāiṇā jiō vāē
diṭṭhantahēukāraṇanāṇāvihajuttinivahēṇa // SurSuCa.21

juvarannō paḍivayaṇaṁ jāhē na caēi kimpi sō dāuṁ
tāhē mantimahattamasāmantāīhiṁ uvahasiō // SurSuCa.22

jāō ya vilakkhō sō daḍhaṁ paüṭṭhō ya samarakēussa
kaha ṇu mahāyaṇamajjhē ēēṇaṁ dharisiō ahayaṁ? // SurSuCa.23


[p. 343]
ēvaṁ vicintayantō aïgururōsēṇa dhamadhamantō sō
atthāṇamaṇḍavāō nīhariō cintaē ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.24

na ya kēṇaï puvvamahaṁ parāiō vāiṇā ihaṁ lōē
pāvēṇa imēṇa puṇō sabhāē majjhammi kaha vijiō? // SurSuCa.25

tā rayaṇīē bhavaṇē imassa gantūṇa gahiyakaravālō
chindāmi uttimaṅgaṁ jēṇa maṇaṁ nivvuiṁ lahaï // SurSuCa.26

rōddajjhāṇōvagaō ēvaṁ sō cintiūṇa rayaṇīē
gahiyāuhō paviṭṭhō vāsaharē samarakēussa // SurSuCa.27

vaccōharabhitīē pacchannō acchaē palīṇō sō
kāūṇa gōsakiccaṁ samāgaō tattha juvarāyā // SurSuCa.28

dīvayavaggakarēhiṁ narēhiṁ ujjhōiēṇa maggēṇaṁ
vaccōharagamaṇicchā aha jāyā rāyaüttasya // SurSuCa.29


[p. 344]
purisēhiṁ tattha diṭṭhō vaccōharasaṇṭhiō sa duṭṭhamaī
āyaḍḍhantō khaggaṁ gahiō baddhō ya sahasatti // SurSuCa.30

juvarannā nāō sō nāhiyavāī sa ēsa kavilotti
nūṇaṁ vāyammi jiō majjha vahaṭṭhā iha paviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.31

daṭhṭhūṇa dīṇavayaṇaṁ vēvantasarīrayaṁ tayaṁ kavilaṁ
paricattajīviyāsaṁ jāyā karuṇā kumārassa // SurSuCa.32

bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa taō jīvantō tāva iṇhi mukkō si
mōttūṇa majjha dēsaṁ ṭhāēyavvaṁ tumē pāva! // SurSuCa.33

iya bhaṇiō sō naṭṭhō gantūṇaṁ tāhi dūradēsammi
bhillajaṇāinnāē avaṭṭhiōbhillapallīē // SurSuCa.34

aha annayā ya paümō puttaṁ ahisiñciūṇa rajjammi
juvarāiṇā samēō pavvaïō gurusamīvammi // SurSuCa.35


[p. 345]
dōnnivi guruṇā sahiyā viharantā bahuvihēsu dēsēsu
satthēṇa samaṁ caliyā rayaṇapuraṁ nāma varanayaraṁ // SurSuCa.36

satthāō kahavi bhaṭṭhā dōnnivi aḍavīē mōhiyā muṇiṇō
sampattā pallīē pāṇayaaṭṭhā paviṭṭhā tē // SurSuCa.37

diṭṭhā ya pariyaḍantā kavilēṇaṁ kahavi paccabhinnāyā
kuddhō ya daḍhaṁ ēsō daṭṭhūṇa muṇiṁ samarakēuṁ // SurSuCa.38

cintēi tāhē kavilō imēṇa vāēvi nijjiō ahayaṁ
nivvisaō āṇattō taïyā ya imēṇa pāvēṇa // SurSuCa.39

tā kavaḍēṇaṁ kēṇavi vaïrassantaṁ karēmi iṇhimpi
iya cintiūṇa vandaï tē muṇiṇō paramaviṇaēṇa // SurSuCa.40

nīyā ya nijē gēhē visamīsaṁ bhattapāṇayaṁ dinnaṁ
bhaṇiyā ya viṇayapuvvaṁ bhayavaṁ! ētthēva bhuñjēha // SurSuCa.41


[p. 346]
addhāṇagamaṇakhinnā nivviyaṇē ēttha ēgadēsammi
bhuñjiya vīsamiuṁ tō pabhāyakālē vaējjāha // SurSuCa.42

ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā tēṇaṁ suhabhāvā vīsamittu khaṇamēgaṁ
sajjhāyaṁ kāūṇaṁ pāraddhā bhōyaṇaṁ kāūṁ // SurSuCa.43

saṁnihiyadēvayāē muṇiaṇukampāē tayaṁ visaṁ hariyaṁ
bhōttūṇa taō dōnnivi sajjhāyaṁ kāumāraddhā // SurSuCa.44

cintēi taō kavilō hanta visēṇaṁ na kiṁ mayā ēē
nūṇaṁ mantabalēṇaṁ avahariyā hōjja visasattī // SurSuCa.45

tā rayaṇīi avassaṁ mārēyavvō maē imō muṇḍō
jīvantammi imammi natthi mamaṁ jēṇa santōsō // SurSuCa.46

pattāē rayaṇīē sajjhāyaṁ kaṭṭu sāhuṇō suttā
kavilōvi addharattē samāgaō sāhuvahaṇaṭṭhā // SurSuCa.47


[p. 347]
āyaḍ̣dhiūṇaṁ khaggaṁ jāva pahāraṁ karēi sāhussa
ruṭṭhāē dēvayāē pahaō sō tēṇa khaggēṇa // SurSuCa.48

rōddajjhāṇōvagaō mariūṇa gaō biijjapuḍhavīē
muṇiṇōvi niraïyāraṁ sāmannaṁ kāuṁ bahukālaṁ // SurSuCa.49

kālaṁ kāuṁ vihiṇā dōnnivi sōhammanāmakappammi
uppannā suhappunnā accharagaṇasaṅkulavimāṇē // SurSuCa.50

[yugmam]
tattō ya paümajīvō sāgaramēgaṁ tu āuyaṁ tattha
aṇuhaviūṇiha dīvē ēravaē vijayanayarīē // SurSuCa.51

dhaṇabhūināmagassa ō jāō taṇaō sudhammanāmotti
kāūṇa ya sāmannaṁ uppannō bīyakappammi // SurSuCa.52

[yugmam]
candajjuṇē vimāṇē sasippahō nāma sō surō jāō
dō cēva sāgarāiṁ sampunnaṁ āuyaṁ tassa // SurSuCa.53


[p. 348]
bhadda! vihuppaha! sampaï vimāṇasāmī u sō surō tumha
jassāēsēṇa tumaṁ samāgaō maha samīvammi // SurSuCa.54

sō samarakēujīvō sāgaramēgaṁ tu aṭṭhapaliēhiṁ
abbhahiyaṁ aṇubhaviuṁ dēvabhavē aha cuō tattō // SurSuCa.55

ētthēva bharahakhēttē kusagganayarammi bhaddakittissa
rannō piyamahilāē subandhudattāē kucchīē // SurSuCa.56

uppannō sō dēvō jāō ya kamēṇa dāraō tattō
ghaṇavāhaṇotti nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ sē uciyasamayammi // SurSuCa.57

vaḍḍhantō ya kamēṇaṁ pattō aha jōvvaṇaṁ jaṇāṇandaṁ
ahisiñciya taṁ rajjē jāō samaṇō piyā tassa // SurSuCa.58

[yugmam]
sōvi bahupuvvalakkhē rajjaṁ parivāliūṇa sambuddhō
naravāhaṇaṁ tu puttaṁ rajjē ṭhaviūṇa pavvaïō // SurSuCa.59


[p. 349]
bhadda! vihuppaha! sō haṁ viharantō ajja iha purē pattō
aha ēgarāiyāē ṭhiō ya paḍimāē aha ēttha // SurSuCa.60

sōvi hu kavilō naraē aṇuhaviuṁ dāruṇaṁ mahaṁ dukkhaṁ
sāgaramēgaṁ ahiyaṁ āuṁ bhōttūṇa uvvaṭṭō // SurSuCa.61

jāō magahāvisaē ābhīrō sābhaḍotti nāmēṇa
kāūṇa ya bālatavaṁ bhavaṇavaī sō surō jāō // SurSuCa.62

paramāhammiyadēvō uvaruddō nāma sō tahiṁ jāō
daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ ihaïṁ samāgaō āsuruttotti // SurSuCa.63

sumarantō taṁ vaïraṁ samāgaō tēṇa maha vahaṭhṭhāē
ēyaṁ vaïranimittaṁ samāsaō tuha maē siṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.64

bhō cittavēga! tattō puṇaravi sō kēvalī maē puṭṭhō
bhayavaṁ! kēttiyamāuṁ katthaṁ va maha hōjja uppattī? // SurSuCa.65


[p. 350]
kō va piyā maha hōhī bōhissaï kō jiṇindadhammammi?
ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiṁō bhayavaṁ! sō bhaṇiuṁmāḍhattō // SurSuCa.66

ciṭṭhaï āugasēsaṁ ēgavīsaṁ vāsakōḍikōḍīō
tattō caïūṇa tumaṁ āukkhaē hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.67

siriamarakēurannō dēvīkamalāvaīē kucchimmi
bahuuvayāiyaladdhō uvavajjisi puttabhāvēṇa // SurSuCa.68

[yugmam]
jaṇaṇīi samaṁ tattha ya avahariō puvvavēriyasurēṇa
bhō cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi // SurSuCa.69

ēntēṇa maha samīvē divvamaṇī jassa ̣dhōiō tumaē
so cciya paramatthapiyā bhavissaï tammi jammammi // SurSuCa.70

pāsammi suppaïṭṭhassa sūriṇō pāviūṇa gihidhammaṁ
aha laddhuṁ samaṇattaṁ kāhisi saṁsāravōcchēyaṁ // SurSuCa.71


[p. 351]
iya kēvaliṇā bhaṇiē tahatti bahu manniūṇa tavvayaṇaṁ
ti payakkhiṇiūṇa puṇō 'bhivandiō sō maē bhayavaṁ // SurSuCa.72

tattō uppaïūṇaṁ samāgaō ēttha tuha samīvammi
jaṁ taṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.73

bhō cittavēga! sampaï kāyavvaṁ jaṁ maē tamāisasu
tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō suravara! nisuṇēsu maha vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.74

nahavāhaṇēṇa nīyā jā sā maha bhāriyā sudukkhattā
tayavatthaṁ maṁ daṭṭhuṁ vilavantī kaluṇasaddēṇa // SurSuCa.75

bhuyagōhavẹ̄dhiyassavi na tārisaṁ āsi majjha maṇadukkhaṁ
jaha tīē kaluṇarōvaṇavilāvasaddaṁ suṇantassa // SurSuCa.76

sā kaha ciṭṭhaï sampaï na navatti majjha sāhēsu?
ōhinnāṇēṇa tumaṁ jāṇasi paccakkhamiva savvaṁ // SurSuCa.77


[p. 352]
īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō dēvō vajjaraï bhadda! nisuṇēsu
sā tuha bhajjā nīyā gaṅgāvattammi ruyamāṇī // SurSuCa.78

nahavāhaṇēṇa tattō chụ̄dhā antēurammi niyayammi
gurusōyapīḍiyāē kila ēvaṁ cintayantīē // SurSuCa.79

sō maha daïō tāvaya bhīsaṇabhuyagēhiṁ gahiyasavvaṅgō
guruvēyaṇāē mannē hōhī pāṇēṇa paricattō // SurSuCa.80

aha kahamavi jaï jīvaï tahavi hu maha tēṇa natthisañjōgō
vijjābalaahiēṇaṁ pāvēṇa imēṇa hariyāē // SurSuCa.81

tā sampaï maha juttaṁ mariuṁ gurusōyadukkhataviyāē
suviṇēvi nēva annō purisō maha laggaē aṅgē // SurSuCa.82

iya mantiūṇa tīē aïuggavisaṁ tu bhakkhiyaṁ sahasā
bhañjiya lōyaṇajuyalaṁ mahīyalē nivaḍiyā tattō // SurSuCa.83


[p. 353]
tadavatthaṁ taṁ daṭṭhuṁ hāhāsaddō samuṭṭhiō tattha
taṁ sōuṁ nahavāhaṇakhayarōvi samāgaō tattha // SurSuCa.84

nāūṇa visaviyāraṁ mantē tantē paüñjaī vivihē
visanimmahaṇē maṇiṇō ābandhaī tīē aṅgammi // SurSuCa.85

na ya tīē kōvi guṇō jāō visaghāriyāē bālāē
āhūyā aha bahavē visamantaviyāṇayā khayarā // SurSuCa.86

savvāyaralaggēhivi tēhivi paüṇā na sakkiyā kāuṁ
tāhē mayatti kāuṁ mayakiccaṁ tīē kāūṇa // SurSuCa.87

nīyā pēyavaṇammī nahavāhaṇapariyaṇēṇa sā bālā
cīyāē pakkhiviuṁ tattō uddīviō jalaṇō // SurSuCa.88

[yugmam]
ēttiyamēttaṁ sāhaï sō dēvō jāva cittavēgassa
dhaṇadēva! tāva nisuṇasu jaṁ saṁvittaṁ tahiṁ taïyā // SurSuCa.89


[p. 354]
sōuṁ daïyāmaraṇaṁ dūsahagurudukkhadaliyasavvaṅgō
vajjāsaṇibhinnō iva uggabhuyaṅgēṇa gasiuvva // SurSuCa.90

gahiuvva rakkhasēṇaṁ pahaō iva mōggarēṇa garuēṇa
nīsasiya dīhadīhaṁ gurusōyāuriō khayarō // SurSuCa.91

mucchānimīliyacchō dhasatti dharaṇīyalammi sō paḍiō
ninnaṭṭhasayalacēṭṭhō sañjāō vigayajīuvva // SurSuCa.92

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
daṭhṭhūṇa cittavēgaṁ tadavatthaṁ tāhē tēṇa dēvēṇa
sīyalajalamāṇēttā sittō sō savvaaṅgēsu // SurSuCa.93

vihiō ya maē pavaṇō sukōmalō niyayaüttarīēṇa
tattō khaṇantarāō laddhūṇavi cēyaṇaṁ kahavi // SurSuCa.94

puṇaruttaṁ mucchijjaï aïguruaṇurāyamōhiō khayarō
aïvallahamahilāē maraṇaṁ sariūṇa dukkhattō // SurSuCa.95


[p. 355]
kahakahavi samāsatthō vihiō gurusōyapīḍiō tahavi
thūlaṁsuē muyantō ahōmuhō ciṭṭhaī jāva // SurSuCa.96

tāva ya surēṇa bhaṇiō mahilāmēttasya kāraṇē kīsa
āyasijjaï appā ēvaṁvihasōyakaraṇēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.97

[yugmam]
vibuhajaṇanindaṇijjaṁ asamañjasacēṭṭhiyaṁ pamōttūṇa
vatthusarūvaṁ sundara! bhāvēyavvaṁ payattēṇa // SurSuCa.98

saṁsārammi aṇantē paribbhamantāṇa honti jīvāṇa
saṁyōgavippaōgā iṭṭhāṇiṭṭhēhiṁ sayahuttaṁ // SurSuCa.99

nahu harisō sañjōgē nēvaṁ visāōvi iṭṭhavirahammi
kāyavvō buddhimayā saṁsārarūvayaṁ nāuṁ // SurSuCa.100

kiñca puvvabhavē jō tumaē aṇurāgō nēva ujjhiō taïyā
samaṇattaṇēvi pattē tasya pabhāvāu saggēvi // SurSuCa.101


[p. 356]
riddhibalatēyahīṇō āsi tumaṁ taha ya ēttha jammammi
ēvaṁ viōyadukkhaṁ pattaṁ takkammadōsēṇa // SurSuCa.102

[yugmam]
tahavi hu ajjavi rāgaṁ tīē uvariṁ na muñcasē kīsa?
ēvaṁvihadukkhāṇaṁ ēso cciya kāraṇaṁ paramaṁ // SurSuCa.103

aha bhaṇaï cittavēgō suravara! maha phuraï dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ
pahasiyamuhō ya dīsasi tumanti tā kahasu paramarttha // SurSuCa.104

kiṁ jīvaï sā bālā saccaṁ ciya ahava sā mayā varaī?
jaï tāva tumaṁ mittō āsi mahaṁ annajammammi // SurSuCa.105

daṁsijjaü sā sigghaṁ aha navi tā majjha jīviyaṁ natthi
lajjāmi bahu bhaṇantō ēsō ciya nicchaō majjha // SurSuCa.106

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō dēvō vajjaraï bhadda! jaï ēvaṁ
tā piṭṭhaō nirūvasu jēṇa tayaṁ pēcchasē daïyaṁ // SurSuCa.107


[p. 357]
ēvaṁ surēṇa bhaṇiō valiyaggīvaṁ nirūvaī jāva
tāva ya vihūsiyaṅgī pēcchaï niyabhāriyaṁ sahasā // SurSuCa.108

taṁ daṭṭhu cittavēgō sasaṅkiō niyamaṇammi vajjaraï
suravara! sāhasu saccaṁ hāsaṁ mōttūṇa maha iṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.109

kiṁvā sacciya ēsā nahavāhaṇaavahiyā mahaṁ daïyā
maha āsāsaṇahēuṁ suramāyā aha tumē vihiyā? // SurSuCa.110

jaï tāva visaṁ bhakkhiya maha virahē sā mayā sudukkhattā
tā kaha iha jīvantī sampattā akkhayasarīrī? // SurSuCa.111

tattō ya bhaṇaï dēvō sacciya ēsā, na hōi suramāyā
avahariya sā maē ihāṇiyā tahaya nisuṇēsu // SurSuCa.112

kēvalimahimaṁ kāuṁ āgacchantēṇa tuha samīvammi
ōhinnāṇēṇa maē diṭṭhā tuha bhāriyā ēsā // SurSuCa.113


[p. 358]
kayamaraṇajjhavasāṇā tattō ya maē vicintiyaṁ ēyaṁ
gahiūṇa imaṁ pacchā gacchissaṁ mittapāsammi // SurSuCa.114

iya cintiya pattō haṁ gaṅgāvattammi tammi nayarammi
visavēyavihuriyaṅgī diṭṭhā ya maē imā tattha // SurSuCa.115

hantūṇa mantasattiṁ savvēsiṁ thambhiyaṁ maē u visaṁ
tattō mayatti kaliuṁ mayakiccaṁ tīē kāūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.116

nīyā pēyavaṇammī nahavāhaṇapariyaṇēṇa sā bālā
cīyāē pakkhiviuṁ jāhē ujjāliō jalaṇō // SurSuCa.117

tāhē avahariya visaṁ dhēttūṇa imaṁ samāgaō ihaï
tujjha samīvē tāva ya ēsa vigappō mahaṁ jāō // SurSuCa.118

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
sōuṁ imīi maraṇaṁ kiṁ mannē ēsa kuṇaï maha mittō
kiṁ daḍharāgō ajjavi ahavāvi hu payaṇurāgotti // SurSuCa.119


[p. 359]
iya cintiūṇa ēsā addissā suyaṇu! tuha maē vihiyā
nāūṇa nicchayaṁ tē iṇhiṁ puṇa payaḍiyā bhadda! // SurSuCa.120

tā mā kuṇa āsaṅkaṁ sacciya ēsā u kaṇagamālatti
iya bhaṇiē sō khayarō pahasiyavayaṇō daḍhaṁ jāō // SurSuCa.121

aha paṇamiya taṁ dēvaṁ kayañjalī bhaṇaï cittavēgō sō
aïnēhō dakkhinnaṁ ahō ṇu tē mittavacchallaṁ // SurSuCa.122

paraüvayārarayā iha mahānubhāvā bhavanti payaīē
aṇuvakayāvi parēṇaṁ vaṭṭanti sayāvi uvayārē // SurSuCa.123

tumaē dinnaṁ jīyaṁ maṇasantāvō tumē ya nivvaviō
aṇahasarīsā ēsā tumaē majjha uvaṇīyā // SurSuCa.124

āulamaṇassa puvviṁ tumaē jaṁ kiñci majjha uvaïṭṭhaṁ
savvaṁ bhariyaghaḍassava taṁ maha pāsēṇa bōlīṇaṁ // SurSuCa.125


[p. 360]
tujjha pabhāvā suravara! jāō haṁ satthamāṇasō iṇhiṁ
kāyavvaṁ jaṁ kiñcivi sampaï āisasu taṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.126

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō havaï hu dēvāṇa daṁsaṇamamōhaṁ
tō bhaṇasu bhadda! kiñciṁvi jēṇa tayaṁ tuha payacchāmi // SurSuCa.127

tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō jaï ēvaṁ dēsu majjha taṁ kiñci
nahavāhaṇakhayarō jaha na sakkaē maṁ parābhaviuṁ // SurSuCa.128

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō mahilāsahiyassa pahariō jaṁ sō
vijjāharakayamēraṁ viṁladhiuṁ dappavāmụ̄dhō // SurSuCa.129

tēṇēva kāraṇēṇaṁ vijjācchēō imassa sañjāō
tā sampaï asamatthō bhadda! tumaṁ sō parābhaviṁu // SurSuCa.130

annaṁ ca. 

kila puvvavēriēṇaṁ avahariō jāyagaruyarōsēṇa
tō cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi // SurSuCa.131


[p. 361]
iya taïyā kēvaliṇā bhāvibhavaṁ majjha sāhayantēṇa
āiṭṭhaṁ tā tumaē hōyavvaṁ khayaranāhēṇa // SurSuCa.132

[yugmam]
vēyaḍḍhadakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē sayalakhayaranāhāṇaṁ
sāmiṁ karēmi sampaï tumanti, kiṁ ēttha annēṇa? // SurSuCa.133

majjha pabhāvāō tuha savvāō cēva khayaravijjāō
hōhinti pạdhiyasiddhā ahiyāō annakhayarēhiṁ // SurSuCa.134

paravijjāṇaṁ chēyaṁ mantāṇa ōsahīṇa ahalattaṁ
kāhisi icchāē tumaṁ khayarāṇaṁ vayaṇamattēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.135

aïdappiyāvi khayarā āṇāniddēsakāriṇō savvē
hōhinti viṇayapaṇayā majjha pabhāvāō tuha bhadda! // SurSuCa.136

tā iṇhiṁ gantūṇaṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē siddhakūḍasiharammi
sāsayajiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ mahimaṁ aṭṭhāhiaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.137


[p. 362]
abbhatthiya dharaṇinda savvāō tujjha khayaravijjhāō
dāuṇa jahāvihiṇā gacchissaṁ tāhi saṭṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.138

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ surēṇa bhaṇiō payajuyalaṁ paṇamiūṇa sē khayarō
suravara! mahāpasāō ēvaṁ hōutti vajjaraï // SurSuCa.139

bahumāṇajuyaṁ tattō ābhāsittā mamaṁ tu sō khayarō
dhaṇadēva! maha samappiya maṇimēyaṁ gurupamōēṇa // SurSuCa.140

dēvēṇa tēṇa sahiō saha mahilāē nahammi uppaïō
ahayampi taō tattō samāgaō niyayaṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.141

[yugmam]
tā bhō dhaṇadēva! maē ēēṇa kamēṇa pāviō ēsa
bahupunnapāvaṇijjō maṇī maṇāṇandasañjaṇaṇō // SurSuCa.142

diyalōyasamuppannō pavarō ēsō maṇī mahābhāga!
nissēsadōsasamaṇō visēsaō visasamūhassa // SurSuCa.143


[p. 363]
tā dhaṇadēva! mahāyasa! gēṇhasu ēyaṁ tumaṁ maṇiṁ divvaṁ
sayalaguṇēganihāṇaṁ maha aṇurōhēṇa, kiṁ bahuṇā // SurSuCa.144

ēyaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ kusalō bhaṇiīsu bhaṇaï dhaṇadēvō
bhō rāyasuya! jamēyaṁ tumaē saha daṁsaṇaṁ majjha // SurSuCa.145

jaṁ ca imaṁ accataṁ vayaṇaṁ sabbhāvagabbhiṇaṁ bhadda!
taṁ cēva majjha maṇisayasahassalakkhāṇa abbhahiyaṁ // SurSuCa.146

aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō nisamma dhaṇadēvabhāsiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ
atthi ya ēyaṁ dhaṇadēva! kintu ahayampi ēyammi // SurSuCa.147

gahiē divvamaṇimmī tumaē mannē kayatthamappāṇaṁ
tā bhō maha dhiihēuṁ kijjaü maṇigahaṇamaviyappaṁ // SurSuCa.148

[yugmam]
nāuṁ aïnibandhaṁ gahiō viṇiēṇa sō maṇī pavarō
aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō puṇaravi dhaṇadēvamāsajja // SurSuCa.149


[p. 364]
gantūṇa kusaggapurē niyattamāṇēṇa niyapurābhimuhaṁ
āgantavvaṁ ihaïṁ amhāṇa aṇuggahaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.150

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ hōu avigdhēṇa tāva samaō sō
jaṁ ēsō ciya maggō niyattamāṇāṇamamhāṇa // SurSuCa.151

ēvaṁ kayasambhāsō rayaṇiṁ gamiūṇa tassa gēhammi
pattē pabhāyasamaē saṁvụ̄dhē sayalasatthammi // SurSuCa.152

tavvēlasamuciyaṁ sō kāyavvaṁ kāuṁ niggaō tattō
niyapariyaṇasahiēṇaṁ pallīvaïṇā 'ṇugammantō // SurSuCa.153

[yugmam]
kahakahavi niyattēuṁ sasōyavayaṇaṁ tu pallīnāṁhaṁ taṁ
satthēṇa samaṁ caliō dhaṇadēvō vēsarārụ̄dhō // SurSuCa.154

kālēṇa ya sampattō kusagganayarammi vaṇiyasañjuttō
ghēttuṁ mahagdhamullaṁ darisaṇayaṁ naravaïsamīvē // SurSuCa.155


[p. 365]
sampattō naravāhaṇarannā bahu manniō taō tēṇa
suṅkavaï sayalabhaṇḍaṁ pañcaülaṁ sakkhiṇaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.156

[yugmam]
sāgarasēṭṭhissa taō bhavaṇēsu bhāḍaēṇa gahiēsu
uttāriyaṁ tu bhaṇḍaṁ savvampi niuttapurisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.157

uttaraï ya païdiyahaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ taha ghēppaē ya paḍibhaṇḍaṁ
ēvaṁ ca kaïvi māsā vōlīṇā tattha nayarammi // SurSuCa.158

sāgarasēṭṭhisuēṇaṁ siridattēṇa samaṁ tu ēyassa
sañjāyā gurupīī sambavahāraṁ karēntassa // SurSuCa.159

aha annayā ya nīō niyayagihē bhōyaṇassa kajjēṇa
mahayā uvarōhēṇaṁ siridattēṇaṁ tu dhaṇadēvō // SurSuCa.160

tattha ya gaēṇa diṭṭhā sirikantā pavararūvasampannā
bhagiṇī siridattassa u kannā navajōvvaṇārambhā // SurSuCa.161


[p. 366]
sā tāliyaṇṭahatthā vīēntī bhōyaṇaṁ karēntēṇa
saccaviyā paccaṅgaṁ abbhuvavannō taō ēsō // SurSuCa.162

tīēva sasiṇēhaṁ avaṅgadiṭṭhīē pulaïō ēsō
aha cintaï dhaṇadēvō tīē rūvēṇa akkhittō // SurSuCa.163

jaï tāva imā kannā, dēnti ya jaï mē vimaggiyā ēē
tā hōjja maha kayatthō daïyāē imāē maṇuyabhavō // SurSuCa.164

kaha hōjja majjha ēsā maggāmi sayampi ahava annēṇa
jaï dāhinti na majjhaṁ vimaggiyā, hōjja lahuyattaṁ // SurSuCa.165

ahavā samāṇajāī dhaṇavantō vasaṇavajjiō taha ya
ēsāvi jōvvaṇatthā tamhā dāhinti maha ēē // SurSuCa.166

ēvaṁ vicintayantō kāūṇaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ tu dhaṇadēvō
siridattēṇa viinnē tambōlavilēvaṇāimmi // SurSuCa.167


[p. 367]
gēhāō nīhariō gantūṇaṁ niyayavāsaṭhāṇammi
sirikantāhayahiyaō pāsuttō pavarasayaṇīē // SurSuCa.168

[yugmam]
ēttō ya mayaṇavasagā sirikantā raṇaraṇēṇa abhibhūyā
gantūṇa gihujjāṇē pāsuttā kayaligēhammi // SurSuCa.169

tatthayavakkhittamaṇā kasiṇabhuyaṅgēṇa bāhumūlammi
daṭṭhā dṭhṭhūṇa ahiṁ aīvabhayavēvirasarīrā // SurSuCa.170

āgamma māumūlē ruyamāṇī bhaṇaï vēyaṇaparaṭṭhā
ammō! khaddhā khaddhā ahayaṁ gurukasiṇasappēṇa // SurSuCa.171

[yugmam]
pēlavasattattaṇaō ukkaḍayāē ya visaviyārassa
vēyaṇāē pabhūyattā sabhayattā itthibhāvassa // SurSuCa.172

mīliyalōyalajuyalaṁ nīsāhārā dhasatti dharaṇīē
vihalandhalā nivaḍiyā jaṇaṇīē pēcchamāṇīē // SurSuCa.173


[p. 368]
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ sirimaïṇā sāgarasēṭṭhī tahēva siridattō
taha sayalapariyaṇō sō sahasati samāulībhūō // SurSuCa.174

tāhē bahugāruḍiyā hakkārijjanti mantatantaviū
kīranti mantajāvā taha vaṭṭijjantī mūlīō // SurSuCa.175

dhārēnti dhāraṇāō kēvi hu kannammi dinti sē jāvaṁ
kaluṇaṁ vilavaï jaṇaṇī sandhīraï sē piyā ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.176

sundari! mā kuṇa sōyaṁ ēyaṁ nēmittiyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ
sampaï payaḍīhōhī daïē! jāmāuō tujjha // SurSuCa.177

avisaṁvāī jaṁ sō sumaī nēmittiō tahā suyaṇu!
kamalāvaīē savvaṁ nivvaḍiyaṁ tēṇa āiṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.178

ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇē jāhē na caïnti tattha gāruḍiyā
savvāyaralaggāvi hu visaviyaṇaṁ sē niyattēuṁ // SurSuCa.179


[p. 369]
tattō tīē visannō savvōvi hu pariyaṇō piyā bhāyā
cintēnti ya kiṁ hōhī aliyaṁ nēmittiyāiṭṭhaṁ? // SurSuCa.180

puṇaravi ya tammi nayarē ḍiṇḍimasaddēṇa savvagāruḍiyā
vāhariyā na ya kēṇavi uṭṭhaviyā sappadaṭṭhā sā // SurSuCa.181

ētthantarammi kēṇavi paōyaṇēṇaṁ samāgaō tattha
dhaṇadēvō aha pēcchaï samāulaṁ pariyaṇaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.182

aha daṭṭhuṁ siridattaṁ pucchaï kiṁ mitta! āulā tubbhē?
dīsaha viddāṇamuhā, aha siridattō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.183

sirikantā maha bhagiṇī kannā sappēṇa ajja daṭṭhatti
na u jīvāvaï kōvi hu tēṇamhē āulā mitta! // SurSuCa.184

annaṁ ca. 

nēmittiēṇa puvvaṁ āiṭṭhaṁ āsi sappaḍasiyaṁ jō
ujjīvissaï ēyaṁ hōhī ēyāē sō bhattā // SurSuCa.185


[p. 370]
ēyaṁ ca tassa vayaṇaṁ aliyappāyaṁ tu sampaïṁ jāyaṁ
jaṁ sā ahiṇā ḍakkā na ya kōvi hu taṁ samuṭṭhavaï // SurSuCa.186

dhaṇadēva! taō amhaṁ sampaï tuṭṭā ō jīviyavvāsā
aïvallahabhagiṇīē tēṇamha sōgāulā dhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.187

iya sōuṁ dhaṇadēvō saharisacittō samullavaï ēvaṁ
mā kuṇa sōyaṁ sundara! na hōi aliyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.188

dē! picchāmō tāva ya tuha bhagiṇiṁ, tēṇa ēvamullaviē
nīō tīē samīvē dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï niyapurisaṁ // SurSuCa.189

taṁ supaïṭṭhadinnaṁ āṇēsu maṇinti tāhē sō purisō
ghittuṁ lahu divvamaṇiṁ samāgaō tassa pāsammi // SurSuCa.190

vimalasalilēṇa sittō divvamaṇī tāhē tēṇa nīrēṇa
abbhōkkhiyā salīlaṁ samuṭṭhiā suhapasuttavva // SurSuCa.191

aviya. 


[p. 371]
tīē taṁ dēhagayaṁ sappavisaṁ maṇijalēṇa saṁsittaṁ
sukkajjhāṇābhihayaṁ naṭṭhaṁ kammaṁva mōhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.192

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ siridattō sāgarasiṭṭhī ya harisiyā dōvi
pisuṇanti tujjha ēsā dinnā dhaṇadēva! sirikantā // SurSuCa.193

tattō sōhaṇalaggē pariṇīyā ucchavēṇa mahayā u
tīē sō aṇurattō visayasuhaṁ bhuñjaē tattha // SurSuCa.194

jā tattha kaïvi māsē ciṭṭhaï sō tīē jōvvaṇāsattō
tāva ya savvaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ vikkīyaṁ tassa purisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.195

paḍibhaṇḍaṁ pihu gahiyaṁ saṁvụ̄dhā sayalasatthiyā tāhē
dhaṇadēvō āpucchaï gamaṇatthaṁ sasuravaggaṁ taṁ // SurSuCa.196

aha bhūridaviṇajuttā dāsīdāsāipariyaṇasamaggā
sirikantā niyapiuṇā paṭṭhaviyā bhattuṇā samayaṁ // SurSuCa.197


[p. 372]
puvvuddiṭṭhakamēṇaṁ dhaṇadēvō garuyasatthapariyariō
caliō niyanayarammi kusagganayarāu suhadivasē // SurSuCa.198

aha kamasō sampattō sīhaguhāsannabhūpaēsammi
āvāsiyammi satthē dhaṇadēvō cintaē ēvaṁ // SurSuCa.199

taïyā pallīvaïṇā bhaṇiō u ahaṁ avassamēntēṇa
āgantavvaṁ tumaē maha dhiihēunti tā iṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.200

āsannā sā vaṭṭaï pallī tā sigghamēva gacchāmi
daṭhṭhūṇa suppaïṭṭhaṁ puṇaravi ihamāgamissāmi // SurSuCa.201

iya cintiūṇa kaïvayapurisajuō vēsarīē ārụ̄dhō
sampattō aha pēcchaï sīhaguhaṁ savvaō daḍḍhaṁ // SurSuCa.202

aviya. 

jālāluṅkhiyanivaḍiyagōmahisakaraṅkakaliyapērantaṁ
pērantasatthaviṇihayahayaruhirapavāhaduggandhaṁ // SurSuCa.203


[p. 373]
duggandhadharaṇinivaḍiyabhaḍamaṁsavasāpasattabahusuṇahaṁ
suṇahabhayaṁmukkamāṇusakaraṅkasivamukkaphēkkāraṁ // SurSuCa.204

phēkkārasavaṇasantaṭṭhabhīruuḍḍīṇagiddhasisunivahaṁ
sisunivahahatthasandaḍḍhabhillajuvaīhiṁ duppicchaṁ // SurSuCa.205

duppicchajalaṇajālāpaluṭṭhabhillōhabhavaṇabībhacchaṁ
bībhacchajalaṇakavaliyamayamāṇusasayasamāinnaṁ // SurSuCa.206

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ dhaṇadēvō ēvaṁ vajjaraï hā! kimēyanti
aïvisamāvi hu pallī kēṇa imā handi! daḍḍhatti? // SurSuCa.207

ētthantarammi kēṇavi karaṅkamajjhaṭṭhiēṇa vajjariyaṁ
dhaṇadēva! ēhī ēttō ahayaṁ sō dēvasammotti // SurSuCa.208

palicchinnacalaṇajuyalō gurupaharaṇaghāyajajjariyadēhō
gāḍhaṁ tisābhibhūō ajjavi ciṭṭhāmi jīvantō // SurSuCa.209


[p. 374]
taṁ sōuṁ dhaṇadēvō purisaṁ paṭṭhaviya pāṇiyanimittaṁ
aïguruvisāyajuttō pattō aha tasya pāsammi // SurSuCa.210

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sāhasu bhō! kēṇa vilasiyaṁ ēyaṁ
sō kattha suppaïṭṭhō aha sō saṇiyaṁ samullavaï // SurSuCa.211

ēttō taïyammi diṇē siddhapurāō samāgaō purisō
ēgantammi ya siṭṭhaṁ tēṇa imaṁ pallināhassa // SurSuCa.212

kumara! ahaṁ paṭṭhaviō tuhapiuvaramantisumaïnāmēṇa
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa, ēyaṁ sāhējjasu suppaïṭṭhassa // SurSuCa.213

suggīvassiha rannō atisurayapasaṅgadōsaō jāō
khayavāhī tēṇa imō cēṭṭhaï khaṇajīviyavvotti // SurSuCa.214

ēsōvi surahakumarō santāvaï sayalapayaïvaggaṁ tu
dussīlō ulluṇṭhō asabbhabhāsī akajjaraō // SurSuCa.215


[p. 375]
taha ēyassa virattā sāmantamahantamāiyā savvē
rajjasirīē ajōgō, taṁ cēva ya kumara! jōgō si // SurSuCa.216

tujjha puṇa vahaṭṭhāē kaṇagavaīē pabhūyavikkhēvō
paṭṭhaviō tā tumaē rakkhēyavvaṁ niyasarīraṁ // SurSuCa.217

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï sō purisō bhadda! pallināhassa
tāva ya sō vikkhēvō pabhūyarahaturayapāikkō // SurSuCa.218

sahasacciya sampattō samantaō vẹ̄dhiyā imā pallī
aha bhillanivahasahiō nīhariō suppaïṭṭhōvi // SurSuCa.219

[yugmam]
bahujaṇasaṁhārakaraṁ laggaṁ āōhaṇaṁ mahāghōraṁ
nihayā bahavō bhillā vijiyā amhē parabalēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.220

gahiūṇa taō sāraṁ savvaṁ ḍahiūṇa sīhaguhamēyaṁ
kāuṁ hayavippahayaṁ viṇiggayaṁ parabalaṁ tattō // SurSuCa.221


[p. 376]
ahayampi hu jujjhantō ēyamavatthantaraṁ ihaṁ pattō
dhaṇadēva! nēva jāṇē kiṁ jāyaṁ suppaïṭṭhassa // SurSuCa.222

pañcanamōkārō aha dinnō sammattavayasamēō sē
tēṇavi ya bhāvasāraṁ puṇaruttaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.223

ētthantarammi purisō salilaṁ dhittūṇa āgaō tattha
dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï taō piyasu jalaṁ dēvasamma! imaṁ // SurSuCa.224

aha sō jalaṁ pibantō aïtaṇhāsusiyatāluyattaṇaō
guruvēyaṇāparigaō sahasā pāṇēhiṁ paricattō // SurSuCa.225

dhaṇadēvōvi hu aïgurusōgō ḍahiūṇa tassa taṁ dēhaṁ
savvampi samarabhūmiṁ jōyāvaï niyayapurisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.226

na ya katthaï uvaladdhaṁ karaṅkamēttampi pallināhassa
tattō cintaï ēsō hā! dhī! vihiṇō vilasiyassa // SurSuCa.227


[p. 377]
tārisaguṇajuttassavi saralasahāvassa suppaïṭṭhassa
nigghiṇakaṇagavaīē hā! hā! kaha dāruṇaṁ vihiyaṁ? // SurSuCa.228

māindajālasarisaṁ savvaṁ ēyammi handi! saṁsārē
khaṇadiṭṭhanaṭṭharūvaṁ dhaṇapariyaṇajīviyavvāiṁ // SurSuCa.229

na ya najjaï kiṁ jāyaṁ mahāṇubhāvassa suppaïṭṭhassa
kiṁ jīvaï ahava maō saṅgāmē ēttha jujjhantō? // SurSuCa.230

ēmāi cintayantō dhaṇadēvō āgaō nijē satthē
aha kamasō sampattō satthajuō hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.231

tuṭṭhāō jaṇaṇijaṇayā savvē āṇandiyā vayaṁsā sē
sōhaṇadivasē vahuyā pavēsiyā niyayagēhammi // SurSuCa.232

aha puvvasiṇēhēṇaṁ sirikantā sāsuyāiṇunnāyā
niyacēḍijuyā pattā kamalāvaïdēvigēhammi // SurSuCa.233


[p. 378]
daṭṭhuṁ puvvavayaṁsiṁ viyasiyamuhapaṅkayā mahādēvī
aïgaruyasiṇēhēṇaṁ uṭṭhiya āliṅgaē ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.234

bhaṇaï ya vayaṁsi! ukkaṇṭhiyāē diṭṭhā pabhūyakālāō
aïsōhaṇaṁ hi jāyaṁ jaṁ sāsurayampi tuhavi ēttha // SurSuCa.235

jaṁ tumaē diṭṭhāē diṭṭhaṁ mannāmi piiharaṁ savvaṁ
iya bhaṇiuṁ dēvīē uciyapavittī kayā tīē // SurSuCa.236

uvaviṭṭhāō dōnnivi kusalapavittī ya sāhiyā savvā
khaṇamēgaṁ sambhāsaṁ kāūṇa bhaṇaï sirikantā // SurSuCa.237

gacchāmi iṇhi gēhē tattō kamalāvaī imaṁ bhaṇaï
païdiyahaṁ aï! tumaē āgantavvaṁ maha samīvē // SurSuCa.238

bhaṇiyaṁ sirikantāē ēvaṁ kāhāmi ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ
dēvīē aṇunnāyā samāgayā niyayagēhammi // SurSuCa.239


[p. 379]
ēvaṁ sirikantāē sasurakulē tattha acchamāṇīē
kamalāvaīdēvīē samayaṁ gurupīijuttāē // SurSuCa.240

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ samayaṁ visayasuhaṁ sammamaṇuhavantīē
bahuyāō aïkkantā vāsāṇaṁ kōḍikōḍīō // SurSuCa.241

[yugmam]
aha annayā kayāivi riuṇhāyā bhattuṇā samaṁ suttā
rayaṇīcarimajāmē sumiṇaṁ pāsittu paḍibuddhā // SurSuCa.242

aha bhaṇaï maē piyayama! sumiṇē candō muhēṇa pavisantō
diṭṭhō, taṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ sahasā buddhā taō ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.243

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sundari! puttō bhavissaē tujjha
sayalavaṇivaggapavarō iya ēvaṁ sūyaē sumiṇaṁ // SurSuCa.244

bhaṇiyaṁ sirikantāē ēvaṁ piya! hōu vayaṇayaṁ saccaṁ
sāsamadēvīpabhāvā baddhō ēsō maē gaṇṭhī // SurSuCa.245


[p. 380]
tīē ciya rayaṇīē tīē kucchiṁsi gabbhasambhūī
jātā kamēṇa jāva ya bōlīṇā dōnni māsā sē // SurSuCa.246

taïyammi puṇō māsē dōhalaō tīē abhayadāṇammi
jāō dhaṇadēvēṇavi siṭṭhē sō pūriō tīē // SurSuCa.247

aha uvaciyagabbhā pūriē dōhalammī pasavaṇasamayammī āgayammī suhēṇa
suhagahanivahammī uccaṭhāṇaṭṭhiyammī suhakaraṇamuhuttē dārayaṁ sā pasūyā // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï sirikantātaṇayapasavaṇō nāma
surasundarināmāē kahāē navamō paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 381]
[daśamaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

takkammakusalavilayāsamūhavihiyammi sūikammammi
halluttāvaligihadāsivihiyatakkālakaraṇijjē // SurSuCa.1

saharisapariyaṇavajjariyavajjasuyajammaharisiyamaṇēṇa
dhaṇadhammasēṭṭhiṇā aha vaddhāvaṇayaṁ samāḍhattaṁ // SurSuCa.2

[yugmam]
aviya. 

gahiyakkhavattapavisantanayaranārījaṇōharamaṇīyaṁ
ramaṇīyaṇamuhamaṇḍaṇa- vāvaḍaniyabandhuvaradāraṁ // SurSuCa.3

varadāragganivēsiyavandaṇamālāsaṇāhasiyakalasaṁ
siyakalasahatthapavisantavaṭṭakijjantakalasaddaṁ // SurSuCa.4


[p. 382]
kalasaddapaürapāulamaṅgalasaṅgīyaparavapēkkhaṇayaṁ
pēkkhaṇayapikkhakkhittalōyadijjantatambōlaṁ // SurSuCa.5

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
aviya. 

ghōsiyajīvā 'ghāō mōyāviyaviulabandini urambō
dijjantavivihadāṇō dīṇāṇāhāisuhajaṇaō // SurSuCa.6

païjiṇamandirakijjantavajjavaramajjaṇāivāvārō
varavatthamāiēhiṁ saṁmāṇiyasāhusandōhō // SurSuCa.7

bhōjiyasayaṇasamūhō saṁmāṇiyavaṇiyanāyaramahalallō
jaṇajaṇiyacamakkārō suyajammamahūsavō vihiō // SurSuCa.8

ēvaṁ kayakāyavvō sampattē bārasammi diyahammi
gahiūṇa darisaṇīyaṁ sampattō rāiṇō mūlaṁ // SurSuCa.9

kayaviṇaō dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï mahārāya! sēṭṭhivayaṇēṇa
dēvīsahiēṇa tumē bhōttavvaṁ amha gēhammi // SurSuCa.10


[p. 383]
hasiūṁ rannā bhaṇiyaṁ na hōi kiṁ sēṭṭhiṇō imaṁ gēhaṁ?
piusarisō jaṁ sēṭṭhī vicintagō sayalarajjassa? // SurSuCa.11

tahavi hu sēṭṭhī jaṁ bhaṇaï kiñci taṁ cēva amha kāyavvaṁ
iya bhaṇiē dhaṇadēvō mahāpasāutti bhaṇiūṇa // SurSuCa.12

niyagēhē gantūṇaṁ takkāluciyaṁ samatthakaraṇīyaṁ
niyapariyaṇēṇa kāraï āṇandiyamāṇasō jāva // SurSuCa.13

dēvīsahiō rāyā karēṇuyāvisaraparigaō tāva
sampattō sēṭṭhigihē bandijaṇugghuṭṭhajayasaddō // SurSuCa.14

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
kayamaṅgalōvayārō uttariya karēṇuyāi dēvijuō
varamuttāhalaviraïyacaükkasīhāsaṇē pavarē // SurSuCa.15

uvaviṭṭhō dēvijuō tattō ya vilāsiṇīhiṁ pavarāhiṁ
ārattiyāvaraṇapamuhammi vihimmi vihiyammi // SurSuCa.16


[p. 384]
bhuttō divvāhāraṁ niyapariyaṇasañjuō jahāvihiṇā
gōsīsavilattaṅgō parihāviyadivvavaravatthō // SurSuCa.17

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
viṇaya naēṇaṁ tattō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ imaṁ tu vinnattō
dēvīē piyabhagiṇī vajjaraï imaṁ mahārāya! // SurSuCa.18

pasavanti piuharammī paḍhamaṁ kila sayalavaṇiyajāyāō
kāraṇavasēṇa kēṇavi sañjāyaṁ nēva taṁ majjha // SurSuCa.19

tā dēvidaṁsaṇēṇaṁ ihēva kila piuharanti mannāmi
tā jaï ittiyabhūmiṁ āgacchaï hōi tā laṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.20

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiē aha dēvī rāiṇā aṇuṇṇāyā
sirikantāē samīvē sampattā kañcuisamēyā // SurSuCa.21

tattha ya maṇōramāē vilēvaṇāharaṇavatthamāīhiṁ
pūiya bhaṇiyā dēvī suyassa nāmaṁ karēsutti // SurSuCa.22


[p. 385]
bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō siṭṭhiṇi! tuha cēva hōi uciyamiṇaṁ
tahavi tumaē bhaṇiyaṁ kāyavvamavassamamhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.23

gahiūṇa niucchaṅgē taṁ bālaṁ kamalakōmalakarēhiṁ
kamalāvaīē bhaṇiyaṁ sugandhagandhē khivantīē // SurSuCa.24

sirikantāē jaṇiō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ tu bālaō ēsō
māupiuaddhanāmō siridēvō nāmamēyassa // SurSuCa.25

aïsōhaṇaṁ hi nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ dēvīi iya bhaṇantēṇa
avihavanārigaṇēṇaṁ maṅgalasaddō samugghuṭṭhō // SurSuCa.26

aha taṁ maṇaharadēhaṁ muṭṭhīkayakarajuyaṁ visālacchaṁ
sukumālapāṇipāyaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa vicintaē dēvī // SurSuCa.27

dhannā majjha vayaṁsī jīē suō ērisō samuppannō
jaṇamaṇanayaṇāṇandō maha puṇa ēyampi na hu jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.28


[p. 386]
kiṁ majjha jīviēṇaṁ kiṁvā maha vihalagavvarajjēṇa
jā niyataṇayassa muhaṁ picchāmi na mandabhaggatti // SurSuCa.29

ēmāi cintayantī ābhāsittā vayaṁsiyaṁ niyayaṁ
rannā sahiyā dēvī sampattā niyayagēhammi // SurSuCa.30

tattha ya taṁ cintantī suyajammukkaṇṭhiyā sasōillā
paricattadēhaciṭhṭhā uvviggā sayalakajjēsu // SurSuCa.31

mattā va mucchiyā iva suttavva mayavva vigayasattavva
jhāṇagayajōgiṇi iva uvarayanīsēsavāvārā // SurSuCa.32

parihāyantasarīrā gurusōyāyāsa sāmamuhakamalā
rannā kayāi diṭṭhā puṭhṭhā kamalāvaī tāhē // SurSuCa.33

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
dēvi! tumaṁ kiṁ vimaṇā dubbaladēhā ya dīsasē iṇhiṁ
kiṁ vachiyaṁ na pujjaï sāhīṇē kiṅkarammi maē // SurSuCa.34


[p. 387]
bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō aṁsujalāsārāsittasihiṇāē
piyayama! tuha ppasāyā sampajjaï vañchiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.35

taṁ natthi kimpi sōkkhaṁ tuha ppasāyāu jaṁ na mē pattaṁ
navaraṁ puttapalōyaṇasōkkhaṁ suiṇēvi nō diṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.36

dhannāu tāu nārīō ittha jāō ahō nisiṁ nāha!
niyaya thaṇaṁ dhayantaṁ thaṇandhayaṁ handi! picchanti // SurSuCa.37

pacchā pariṇīyāivi sirikantāē suō samuppannō
tumaē mannāyāē na puṇō maha mandabhāgāē // SurSuCa.38

tā dēva! dēsu puttaṁ aha navi tā natthi jīviyaṁ majjha
tuṭṭaï thaṇōvi aha ēi khīramannā gaī natthi // SurSuCa.39

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ ētthatthē kuṇasu dēvi! mā sōgaṁ
ārāhittā tiyasaṁ pūrēmi maṇōrahē 'vassaṁ // SurSuCa.40


[p. 388]
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ rāyā kāuṁ pūyaṁ jiṇindapaḍimāṇaṁ
siyavasaṇadharō ummukkasayalamaṇikañcaṇāharaṇō // SurSuCa.41

pōsahasālaṁ gantuṁ aṭṭhamabhattaṁ pagiṇhiuṁ vihiṇā
kusasattharē nisannō ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō // SurSuCa.42

dēvō va dāṇavō vā jiṇasāsaṇabhattisañjuō kōvi
jaha saṁnihiō siggha āgacchaü vañchiyaṁ dēu // SurSuCa.43

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō ēgantē saṁniruddhajaṇapasarō
niccaladēhō ciṭṭhaï rāyā jā tinni diyahāiṁ // SurSuCa.44

tā rayaṇicarimajāmē viddhaṁsiyasayalatimirasaṅghāyaṁ
bhāsuradēhaṁ purisaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa vicintaē rāyā // SurSuCa.45

[yugmam]
nimisanti lōyaṇāiṁ tā kiṁ ēsō na hōi dēvotti
na ya maṇuyāṇa sarīrē jāyaï ēvaṁvihā dittī // SurSuCa.46


[p. 389]
tā hōjja imō kō puṇa caraṇāvi mahiṁ phusanti nēyassa
ēvaṁ vigappayantō rāyā ābhāsiō tēṇa // SurSuCa.47

bhō amarakēunaravara! uggatavēṇaṁ kilāmiō si na kiṁ?
ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇō sō abbhuṭṭhiya rāiṇā bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.48

kō si tumaṁ kattō vā samāgaō kahasu maha mahābhāga!?
bhaṇiyaṁ surēṇa naravara! kahēmi kōūhalaṁ jaï tē // SurSuCa.49

īsāṇakappavāsī vihuppahō nāma suravarō ahayaṁ
āsannacavaṇasamaō paralōyahiyaṁ samāyariuṁ // SurSuCa.50

titthayaravandaṇatthaṁ vidēhavāsammi āgaō āsi
tattha maē sō bhayavaṁ āpuṭṭhō niyayavuttantaṁ // SurSuCa.51

[yugmam]
uppattī kattha mahaṁ cuyassa ēttō bhavissaē bhayavaṁ!?
tattō jiṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bharahammi ya hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.52


[p. 390]
jō acchaï puttatthī pōsahasālāi pōsahammi ṭhiō
siriamarakēurāyā tassa tumaṁ hōsi puttotti // SurSuCa.53

[yugmam]
tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ samāgaō rāya! tuha samīvammi
tā mā kuṇasu kilēsaṁ ahayaṁ hōhāmi tuha puttō // SurSuCa.54

gēṇhasu kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ narinda! ēyaṁ taō u dēvīē
jīē icchasi puttaṁ dāyavvaṁ tīi ābharaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.55

iya bhaṇiuṁ kannāṇaṁ uttāriya kuṇḍalāiṁ divvāiṁ
rannō samappiūṇaṁ dēvō addaṁsaṇībhūō // SurSuCa.56

rannāvi rayaṇiviramē gantuṁ dēvīē viyasiyamuhēṇa
suradaṁsaṇāi savvō vuttantō sāhiō tattō // SurSuCa.57

kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ appiya pabhāyakiccaṁ karittu nīsēsaṁ
paḍilāhiya sāhujaṇaṁ sayaṁ pabhuttō varāhāraṁ // SurSuCa.58


[p. 391]
aha annayā ya dēvī riuṇhāyā rayaṇicarimajāmammi
daṭṭhuṁ sumiṇaṁ sahasā paḍibuddhā vēvirasarīrā // SurSuCa.59

bhaṇiyā rannā sundari! kīsa akamhāō kampiyā taṁ si
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama! sampaï sumiṇaṁ maē diṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.60

kila kaṇagamaō kalasō majjha muhē pavisiuṁ viṇikkhantō
kēṇāvi bhañjaṇatthaṁ nīō dūraṁ sa kuddhēṇa // SurSuCa.61

puṇaravi bahukālāō kahavi hu laddhō sa khīrapaḍipunnō
siyakusumamāliyāē maēvi sampūiō tattō // SurSuCa.62

ēyaṁ sumiṇaṁ daṭṭhuṁ muhakaḍuyaṁ pariṇaīi sundarayaṁ
jāō bhaēṇa kampō maha dēhē tēṇa naranāha! // SurSuCa.63

taṁ sōūṇa narindō jāō sōgāurō daḍhaṁ hiyaē
vajjaraï dēvi! suviṇaṁ lābhaṁ sūēi taṇayassa // SurSuCa.64


[p. 392]
sēsaṁ ca suviṇajāṇagapucchagavihiṇā viyāṇiuṁ tujjha
sāhissaṁ mā kāhisi uvvēgaṁ kiñci hiyayammi // SurSuCa.65

tattō pabhāyasamaē gantuṁ atthāṇamaṇḍavē rāyā
āṇavaï sumiṇasatthatthajāṇaē jhatti vāharaha // SurSuCa.66

tattha niuttanarēhiṁ tahēva sampāḍiyāē āṇāē
sāmantamantipuranāyagēhiṁ punnammi atthāṇē // SurSuCa.67

kayaviṇayā suviṇannū uvaviṭṭhā aha narindaāsannē
dhaṇadēvōvi hu rannō āsannō cēva uvaviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.68

[yugmam]
tattō rannā tēsiṁ siṭṭhō suradaṁsaṇāivuttantō
puvvuttō savvōvi hu suviṇagaüvalambhaavasāṇō // SurSuCa.69

sammaṁ viṇicchiūṇaṁ suviṇasarūvaṁ kahēha bhō! tattaṁ
iya bhaṇiyā tē rannā annōnnaṁ jāva cintinti // SurSuCa.70


[p. 393]
tāva ya dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ naranāha! dēsu avahāṇaṁ
suviṇaparamatthajāṇaṇahēuṁ nisuṇēsu vuttuntaṁ // SurSuCa.71

[yugmam]
taō aha aḍavīē diṭṭhō bhillavaī, tēṇa jaha ya sappēhiṁ
baddhō u cittavēgō vimōiō maṇipabhāvāō // SurSuCa.72

jaha tēṇa niyayacariē siṭṭhē dēvassa āgamō āsi
dēvēṇa kēvalī aha diṭṭhō ya kusagganayarammi // SurSuCa.73

jaha bhāvibhavaṁ puṭṭhō kēvaliṇā jaha ya tassa āiṭṭhaṁ
siriamarakēurannō hōhisi puttō tumaṁ bhadda! // SurSuCa.74

jaṇaṇīi samaṁ tattha ya avahariō puvvavēriyasurēṇa
tā cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi // SurSuCa.75

ēmāi puvvaüttaṁ savittharaṁ sāhiyaṁ naravaïssa
dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ jāva ya sampattō hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.76


[p. 394]
tā dēva! dēviudarē vihuppahō sō surō samuppannō
hōhī, jaō na kēvalivayaṇaṁ iha annahā hōi // SurSuCa.77

puvvaviruddhasurēṇaṁ hariō khayarassa vaḍ̣dhiō gēhē
sāhiyabahuvihavijjō milihī sō niyayajaṇaṇīē // SurSuCa.78

icchiyakannādāṇaṁ mālāē pūyaṇampi mannā si
ēsō naridaṁ! suviṇayaparamatthō phuraï maha hiyaē // SurSuCa.79

ēyaṁ dhaṇadēvassa ō vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa suviṇayannūhiṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ ahō! aüvvaṁ ēyassa u buddhikōsallaṁ // SurSuCa.80

sayayaṁ tallicchēhivi bahusatthaviyakkhaṇēhiṁ amhēhiṁ
tavvihabuddhiviuttēhiṁ sakkiyaṁ nō viṇicchēuṁ // SurSuCa.81

susiliṭṭhō naṇu atthō nirūviō rāya! vaṇiyaüttēṇa
savvēsiṁ amhāṇavi susaṁmaō cēva ēsotti // SurSuCa.82


[p. 395]
iya bhaṇiē tē rannā tambōlapayāṇapuvvayaṁ savvē
paṭṭhaviyā taha savvē sāmantamahantamāīyā // SurSuCa.83

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ iṇhiṁ dhaṇadēva! kimiha kāyavvaṁ
dēvīi samaṁ amhaṁ uvaṭṭhiē dusahavirahammi // SurSuCa.84

kiṁ ēttha atthi kōvi hu paḍighāyavihī suduṭṭhasuviṇassa
bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ na annahā kēvaligirā ō // SurSuCa.85

tahavi hu ēsa uvāō kīraï mā hōjja tēṇa paḍighāō
mañcayapaḍiyāṇa puṇō tahaṭṭhiyā cēva bhūmitti // SurSuCa.86

pallīvaïṇā taïyā divvamaṇī jō samappiō majjha
sō ēsa aṅgulīyaganivēsiō ciṭṭhaü karammi // SurSuCa.87

ēsō acintasattī aṇēyaṭhāṇēsu diṭṭha māhappō
tā ēyaṁ dēvīē karaṭṭhiyaṁ dēva! kārēha // SurSuCa.88

[yugmam]

[p. 396]
puvvaviruddhōvi surō haraṇē dēvīi hōjja asamatthō
ēyassa pabhāvāō, aha kahavi karijja avaharaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.89

tahavi hu avagārammī sakkissaï nēva vaṭṭiuṁ vaïrī
nāuṁ imaṁ narēsara! mā sōgaṁ kiñcivi karēha // SurSuCa.90

annaṁ ca. 

suviṇapaḍighāyaṇatthaṁ kārēsu jiṇālaēsu mahimāō
puēsu samaṇasaṅghaṁ taduciyavatthāsaṇāīhiṁ // SurSuCa.91

dāvēsu abhayadāṇaṁ vivihābhiggahatavēsu ujjamasu
ēvaṁ kayammi naravara! savvampi hu sundaraṁ hōhī // SurSuCa.92

iya bhaṇiuṁ dhaṇadēvō samappiuṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ niyayaṁ
paṇamittā rāyāṇaṁ viṇiggaō rāyabhavaṇāō // SurSuCa.93

rannāvi hu gantūṇaṁ dēvībhavaṇammi sayalavuttantō
siṭṭhō samappiyaṁ taha dēvīē aṅgulīyaṁ taṁ // SurSuCa.94


[p. 397]
bhaṇiyā ya dēvī! ēyaṁ khaṇampi hatthāō nēva mōttavvaṁ
ēyassa pabhāvāō pabhavanti na khuddasattāī // SurSuCa.95

jiṇamandirajattāiṁ kāraviyaṁ tāhi rāiṇā savvaṁ
kamalāvaīvi tattō jāyā āvannasattatti // SurSuCa.96

suhasampaḍantahiyaïṭṭhavatthusuviṇīyapariyaṇajuyāē
aha sattamammi māsē jāō dēvīē dōhalaō // SurSuCa.97

lajjāē taṁ kassavi jāhē na kahēi tāva kaïyāvi
parihāyantasarīrā diṭṭhā rannā imaṁ bhaṇiyā // SurSuCa.98

dēvi! tuha kiṁ na pujjaï dīsasi aïdubbalā jaō iṇhiṁ
dēvīē tō bhaṇiyaṁ dōhalaō ēsa mē nāha! // SurSuCa.99

varavāraṇamārụ̄dhā dāṇaṁ dintī ya atthilōyassa
tuhaücchaṅganiviṭṭhā tumaē chattaṁ dharantēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.100


[p. 398]
hiṇḍāmi rāya! nayarē pariyariyā sayalabhiccavaggēṇa
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! kīraï ahuṇā duyaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.101

[yugmam]
aha pavarapaṭṭahatthī siṅgāriya āṇiō niuttēhiṁ
tatthārụ̄dhō rāyā dēvī uṇa tassa ucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.102

uvari dhavalāyavattaṁ muttāhalarēhiraṁ sayaṁ rannā
dhariyaṁ tattō vivihaṁ paḍhantathuipāḍhanivahēṇa // SurSuCa.103

tūrēsu rasantēsuṁ vajjantēsu ya asaṅkhasaṅkhēsu
kalapāṇaēhiṁ vihiē viyambhamāṇē ya saṅgīē // SurSuCa.104

atthijaṇapūriyāsaṁ dāṇaṁ dēntā samatthanayarammi
āṇandanibbharāhiṁ thuvvantā nayaranārīhiṁ // SurSuCa.105

āhiṇḍiūṇa vivihaṁ caükkatiyacaccarēsu icchāē
aha puravarāu bāhiṁ nīhariō kuñjarō kamasō // SurSuCa.106

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]

[p. 399]
sahasacciya ummiṭṭhō vicchōlintō samatthajaṇaniyaraṁ
aïvēgēṇa payaṭṭō īsāṇadisāmuhō tāē // SurSuCa.107

rē! lēha lēha dhāvaha ēsa gaō ēsa jāi puraotti
ēmāi vāharantō bhiccajaṇō dhāi paṭṭhīē // SurSuCa.108

rāyāvi hu jāhi kahavi hu dhariuṁ na caēi karivaraṁ taṁ tu
tāhē bhaṇiyā dēvī ēsa gaō tāva ummiṭṭhō // SurSuCa.109

aïvēgaō payaṭṭō cāijjaï kahavi nō niyattēuṁ
tā uttarimō kahavi hu iyaraha aḍavīē pāḍēhī // SurSuCa.110

kamalāvaīē bhaṇiyaṁ ōyariyavvaṁ kahaṁ nu naranāha!
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu picchasi vaḍapāyavaṁ puraō // SurSuCa.111

ēyassa ya hēṭṭhēṇaṁ jāhī hatthī taō tumē dēvi!
sāhāē laggiavvaṁ sahasā hatthiṁ pamōttūṇa // SurSuCa.112


[p. 400]
ēvaṁ ca jāva rāyā dēviṁ ullavaï tāva sō hatthī
aïvēgēṇaṁ pattō vaḍavāyavahiṭṭhabhūbhāgē // SurSuCa.113

dakkhattaṇaō rāyā jhatti vilaggō ya tassa sāhāē
laggasu laggasu dēvi! jhatti ēyaṁ bhaṇēmāṇō // SurSuCa.114

aïvēgaō karissā ( ssa? ) adakkhayāē ya itthibhāvassa
gabbhassa ya garuyattā bhayavēviraō sarīrassa // SurSuCa.115

kayaajjhavasāyāvi hu na sakkiyā jāhi tattha laggēuṁ
tāhē ya karivarō sō jhaḍatti tattō avakkantō // SurSuCa.116

[yugmam]
aha gurusōgō rāyā tahaṭṭhiō jā taō palōēi
tā picchaï gayaṇēṇaṁ jantaṁ vēgēṇa taṁ kariṇaṁ // SurSuCa.117

aha vimhiō maṇēṇaṁ cintaï rāyā ahō! mahacchariyaṁ
mōttuṁ bhūmipayāraṁ vaccaï hatthī nahayalēṇa // SurSuCa.118

ahavā. 


[p. 401]
puvvaviruddhasurō sō vilasaï nūṇaṁ imēṇa rūvēṇa
na hu kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyā bhāvā iha annahā honti // SurSuCa.119

ēvaṁ vicintayantassa tassa, hatthī adaṁsaṇībhūō
tāva aṇumaggalaggaṁ rannō sinnaṁ samaṇupattaṁ // SurSuCa.120

aha karivaramaggēṇaṁ samarappiyapamuhasuhaḍasayakaliyaṁ
dēvīgavēsaṇatthaṁ paṭṭhaviuṁ sāhaṇaṁ rāyā // SurSuCa.121

kahakahavi garuyasōō sāmantamahantagāṇa vayaṇēṇa
pattō niyanayarammī sunnō vunnō nirāṇandō // SurSuCa.122

[yugmam]
paricattarajjacittō ciṭṭhaï jā kaïvi tattha divasāṇi
kamalāvaïsampāvaṇaāsāē dhariyaniyajīō // SurSuCa.123

tā annadiṇē sinnaṁ samarappiyapamuhamāgayaṁ sahasā
dīṇaṁ vimaṇaṁ khinnaṁ lajjāviṇamantamuhakamalaṁ // SurSuCa.124

[yugmam]

[p. 402]
aha rannā āpuṭṭhō samarappiō kahasu bhadda! vuttataṁ
kiṁ diṭṭhō duṭṭhakarī dēvīvi vimōiyā tattō? // SurSuCa.125

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ samarappiēṇa suṇa dēva!
karivaradisāpayaṭṭā pattā aḍavīi tā amhē // SurSuCa.126

tattha ya bahuppayāraṁ gavēsamāṇēhiṁ dēva! amhēhiṁ
diṭṭhō na sō karivarō nēva ya dēvī na ya paüttī // SurSuCa.127

avarāvarasavaragaṇaṁ pucchatāṇaṁ sudūrapattāṇaṁ
aha annadiṇē kahiyaṁ kappaḍiyanarēṇa ēkkēṇa // SurSuCa.128

tattō sattamadivasē paümōyaranāmaē saravarammi
gayaṇāu nivaḍamāṇō mahilāsahiō karī diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.129

tattō bhayabhīēṇaṁ dūraṭṭhiyaguvilatarupaviṭṭhēṇa
nārīrahiō puṇaravi palōiō tattha hatthitti // SurSuCa.130


[p. 403]
viyaratō saratīrē, iya tassa ō vayaṇayaṁ suṇēūṇa
bhaṇiyaṁ daṁsasu bhaddaya! taṁ sigghaṁ saravaraṁ amha // SurSuCa.131

[yugmam]
aha tēṇa daṁsiyaṁ taṁ palōiyaṁ saravaraṁ samaṁ tēṇa
na ya uvaladdhā dēvī niuṇampi gavēsamāṇēhiṁ // SurSuCa.132

saravarajōyaṇamittē viuttapurisēhiṁ pāviō hatthī
taṁ ghittuṁ nirāṇandā ihāgayā dēvamūlammi // SurSuCa.133

tā kiṁ tatthēva sarē gabhīranīrammi uvarayā dēvī
aha tattō uttariuṁ pattā u kahimpi vasimammi? // SurSuCa.134

ahavā sāvayapaürē vaṇammi kēṇavi viṇasiyā hōjja
na ya jāṇāmō kiñcivi narinda! dēvīē vuttantaṁ // SurSuCa.135

ēvaṁ ca jāva jampaï samarappiō patthivassa sē puraō
tāva ya dāraniuttō kayaviṇaō ēvamullavaï // SurSuCa.136


[p. 404]
dārammi sumaïnāmō nēmittī ciṭṭhaïti suṇiūṇa
bhaṇiyaṁ rannā kiṁ bhō! sō ēsō sumaïnēmittī? // SurSuCa.137

jassāēsāu tayā dinnā naravāhaṇēṇa maha dēvī?
pāsaṭṭhiēhiṁ siṭṭhaṁ, narinda! ēvanti, aha rannā // SurSuCa.138

bhaṇiyaṁ pavisaü sigdhaṁ pucchāmō jēṇa dēvivuttantaṁ
vayaṇāṇantaramēsō pavēsiō dāravālēṇa // SurSuCa.139

kayaüvayārō rannā uvaviṭṭhō viṇayapuvvayaṁ sumaī
āpuṭṭhō, kiṁ dēvī jīvaï va navatti vajjarasu? // SurSuCa.140

uvaōgaṁ dāūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ aha sumaïṇā jiyaïti
akkhayadēhā sampaï miliyā iva bandhuvaggassa // SurSuCa.141

kaïyā samāgamō maha tīē, kiṁ vā havējja sē gabbhē?
iya puṭṭhō naravaïṇā kayaüvaōgō puṇō bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.142


[p. 405]
jaïyā narinda! suviṇē giṇhasi visamaṭṭhiyaṁ kusumamālaṁ
tattō ya māsamittē samāgamō tumha dēvīē // SurSuCa.143

hōhī taṇaō tīē vijujjihī kintu jāyamēttō sō
niyamāūē, naravara! ēvaṁ kila kahaï hu nimittaṁ // SurSuCa.144

puṭṭhō puṇaravi rannā jaṇaṇiviuttō sa jīvihī kiṁ nō?
katthavi vuḍ̣dhi jāhī, kaïyā va samāgamē tēṇa // SurSuCa.145

aha sumaī bhaṇaï puṇō bahukālaṁ jīvihī sa tē puttō
kattha ya vuḍ̣dhiṁ jāhī ēyaṁ puṇa nēva jāṇāmō // SurSuCa.146

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā gayaṇāō kannagā paḍihī
tattō ya sigghamēva hi samāgamō tumha taṇaēṇa // SurSuCa.147

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ gayasōgō pahasiō bhaṇaï rāyā
bhō! bhō! suvannalakkhaṁ sigghaṁ sumaïssa dēhasi // SurSuCa.148


[p. 406]
ēyavayaṇāō amhaṁ dēvīvirahammi garuyasōgaggī
pasarantō ōlhaviō samāgamāsājalōhēṇa // SurSuCa.149

aha niyayābharaṇēṇaṁ suvannalakkhēṇa pūiō sumaī
nīhariō rāyāvi hu maṇayaṁ jāō vigayasōgō // SurSuCa.150

aha annayā ya rāyā suttō rayaṇīi pēcchaē sumiṇaṁ
uttaradisāmuhēṇaṁ vayamāṇēṇaṁ maē kūvē // SurSuCa.151

paḍiyā addhamilāṇā dhavalā kusumāṇa māliyā diṭṭhā
gahiyā sahasā jāyā paccaggā surahigandhaḍ̣dhā // SurSuCa.152

[yugmam]
daṭhṭhūṇamiṇaṁ sumiṇaṁ paḍibuddhō cintaē imaṁ rāyā
ēyaṁ hi sumaïbhaṇiyaṁ diṭṭhaṁ sumiṇaṁ maē ajja // SurSuCa.153

tā hōhī lahu iṇhiṁ majjha vayantassa uttaradisāē
visamadasāpattāē dēvīē saṅgamō 'vassaṁ // SurSuCa.154


[p. 407]
iya cintiūṇa rāyā niyadēsapalōyaṇacchalēṇaṁ tu
gurusēṇāpariyariō nīhariō hatthiṇapurāō // SurSuCa.155

kaïvayapayāṇagāiṁ gantuṁ uttaṅgagirisamāinnē
aïguvilatarusaṇāhē aḍavipaēsammi ēgammi // SurSuCa.156

āvāsiō sasēnnō aha kūvē dīhataṇasamōcchaïē
kahavi hu pamāyavasaō paḍiyā rannō camarahārī // SurSuCa.157

[yugmam]
aha rannā āṇattō purisō rajjuppaōgaō tattha
ōinnō santamasē iō taō jāva gavisēi // SurSuCa.158

tā ēgatthaniluṅkkaṁ picchaï juvaïṁ taḍīi agaḍassa
bhayakampantasarīraṁ santamasē tattha accantaṁ // SurSuCa.159

kāsi tumaṁ iha sundari! ii puṭṭhā jā na dēi paḍivayaṇaṁ
tāva ya jalamajjhagayā vilāsiṇī kaṇṭhagayapāṇā // SurSuCa.160


[p. 408]
sampattā tēṇa taō ghittūṇaṁ tayaṁ kamēṇa nīhariō
vajjaraï rāya! ētthaṁ annāvi hu acchaē juvaī // SurSuCa.161

[yugmam]
ābhaṭṭhāvi na bhāsaï bhaēṇa kampantataṇulayā varaī
ēyaṁ nisamma rannō phuriyaṁ aha dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.162

aha vimhiēṇa rannō vicintiyaṁ kiṁ havijja sā dēvī
ahavā iha aḍavīē dēvīē sambhavō kattha? // SurSuCa.163

ahavā kammavasāṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ navari ēttha saṁsārē
bhaviyavvayāvasēṇaṁ natthi tayaṁ jaṁ na sambhavaī // SurSuCa.164

jaï sā havijja dēvī tā sundaramēva, kāvi aha annā
tahavi hu uttārijjaü karuṇāmūlō jaō dhammō // SurSuCa.165

iya cintiuṇa rannā bhaṇiō purisō tayampi kaḍ̣dhēhi
aha sō rajjūi puṇō purisō kūvammi ōinnō // SurSuCa.166


[p. 409]
bhaṇiyā ya suyaṇu! ahayaṁ rannō siriamarakēunāmassa
vayaṇēṇaṁ tuhuttāraṇakajjēṇaṁ puṇaravi paviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.167

tā āruha mañcīē naragāgārāō andhakūvāō
jēṇuttārēmi lahuṁ ēyaṁ ca nisamma sā vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.168

ārụ̄dhā mañcīē kamēṇa uttāriyā taō dēvī
dubbaladēhā rannā kahakahavi hu paccabhinnāyā // SurSuCa.169

[yugmam]
sāvi ya daṭṭhuṁ rāyaṁ rōvantī ghaggharēṇa saddēṇa
caraṇavilaggā rannā aṁsujalapphunnanayaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.170

nīyā niyayāvāsē dēviṁ daṭhṭhūṇa pariyaṇō savvō
aïgurusōgō rōvaī vivihapalāvēhiṁ dīṇamuhō // SurSuCa.171

[yugmam]
aha kayasarīraciṭhṭhā puṭṭhā kamalāvaī narindēṇa
taïyā kariṇā nīyāē kiṁ tumē dēvi! aṇubhūyaṁ? // SurSuCa.172


[p. 410]
kaïyā va kahava paḍiyā bhīsaṇakūvammi ēttha aḍavīē?
kamalāvaīi bhaṇiyaṁ suṇasu mahārāya! sāhēmi // SurSuCa.173

vaḍapāyavammi laggē dēvē taṁ vilaggiuṁ asattā haṁ
vēgapahāviyakariṇā hariyā ēgāgiṇī tāva // SurSuCa.174

aha sō girisariyāē visamataḍiṁ pāviūṇa sahasatti
aïvēgabhaṅgabhīuvva nahayalaṁ jhatti uppaïō // SurSuCa.175

tattō bhayabhīyāē vicintiyaṁ hanta! karivarapaviṭṭhō
avahaï kōvi dēvō na jēṇa kariṇō vayanti nahē // SurSuCa.176

iya vimhiyahiyayā haṁ puṇō puṇō jā mahiṁ palōēmi
picchāmi tāva giritarupamuhaṁ samagaṁva vaccantaṁ // SurSuCa.177

aviya. 

ēgāgiṇī araṇṇē mahilā bīhijja aḍavīmajjhammi
iya kaliuṁva sahāyā taruṇō vēgēṇa dhāvanti // SurSuCa.178


[p. 411]
kiḍiyanarasamāiṁ calantamaṇuyāiṁ gāmanayarāiṁ
jalabhariyasaravarāiṁvi ( pi? ) mahinivaḍiyachattasarisāiṁ // SurSuCa.179

dīharavaṇarāīō sappasaricchaō saccavijjanti
pālisāricchā giriō sāraṇisarisāō sariyāō // SurSuCa.180

aha dūramaïgayāē sambhariō aṅgulīyagamaṇī sō
avahatthiya tāhi bhayaṁ pahaō sō tēṇa kumbhayaḍē // SurSuCa.181

aviya maṇisañjuyakarapahaō vajjēṇiva tāḍiō gaïndō sō
mōttuṁ gurucīhāḍiṁ ahōmuhō jhati gayaṇāō // SurSuCa.182

jā nivaḍaï vēgēṇa tāva ya hiṭṭhāmuhaṁ niyantīē
diṭṭhaṁ mahantamēgaṁ sarōvaraṁ bhaṅgurataraṅgaṁ // SurSuCa.183

[yugmam]
parihatthamacchapucchacchaḍāhi ucchaliyasalilaüppīlaṁ
mahumattamahuyarīvisararuddhaṁviyasantatāmarasaṁ // SurSuCa.184


[p. 412]
aviya phurantamaṇijālayaṁ tarantaṭiṭṭibhālayaṁ
rahaṅgapantimaṇḍiyaṁ vihaṅgasatthavaḍḍayaṁ // SurSuCa.185

bhamantabhūrigōhiyaṁ sarōruhālisōhiyaṁ
aṇēgasāvayāulaṁ jhasōhaluddhasāulaṁ // SurSuCa.186

calantabhīmagāhayaṁ raḍatadadadūrōhayaṁ
marālapantisōhiyaṁ tamālatālarēhiyaṁ // SurSuCa.187

raṇantachappayāliṁyaṁ balāyapantimāliyaṁ
phurantasippisumpuḍaṁ bhamantabhīmadīvaḍaṁ // SurSuCa.188

aha tammi nīrapunnē aṇōrapārammi saravarē hatthī
gayaṇāō nīsahaṅgō paḍiō buḍḍō ya jalamajjhē // SurSuCa.189

aha nīsahē gaïndē buḍḍē gambhīranīramajjhammi
maṇiṇō māhappēṇaṁ jalaüvariṁ cēva thakkā haṁ // SurSuCa.190


[p. 413]
āsāiyaphalagāvi ya uttariuṁ saravarassa tīrammi
upaviṭṭhā bhayabhīyā gurusōgā iya vicintanttā // SurSuCa.191

tārisariddhijuyāvi hu khaṇēṇa ēgāgiṇī kahaṁ jāyā
dēsiyajuvaīva ahō! aïguvilō kammapariṇāmō // SurSuCa.192

sō kattha bhiccavaggō sā ya sirī sō viṇīyaparivārō
hōhāmi kahaṁ iṇhiṁ vihiyā ēgāgiṇī vihiṇā? // SurSuCa.193

ēmāi cintayantī uvarimavatthēṇa chāiüṁ vayaṇaṁ
saraṇavihuṇā sōēṇaṁ tattha ahaṁ rōviuṁ laggā // SurSuCa.194

ētthatarammi kēṇavi bhaṇiyā kiṁ suyaṇu! rōyasē karuṇaṁ?
tattō sasambhamāē palōiyaṁ mē taōhuttaṁ // SurSuCa.195

kaïvayapurisasahāō taruṇanarō vēsarīi ārụ̄dhō
kayamuhasandhī puraō diṭṭhō uddhadhūliyaṅgillō // SurSuCa.196


[p. 414]
aha sō daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ vimhiyahiyaüvva vēsarāhintō
uttariya majjha calaṇēsu nivaḍiō bhaṇaï ēvaṁ tu // SurSuCa.197

parijāṇasi bhagiṇi! mamaṁ siridattō haṁ kusagganayarāō
āsi gaō paravisaē vaṇijjabuddhīē satthajuō // SurSuCa.198

bārasamavaccharāō puṇaravi caliō purammi niyayammi
satthēṇa samaṁ iṇhiṁ sampattō iha paēsammi // SurSuCa.199

tā bhagiṇi! kēṇa vihiṇā jāyā ēgāgiṇī tumaṁ ēttha?
iya bhaṇiyā tēṇa ahaṁ vigayabhayā jhatti sañjāyā // SurSuCa.200

tattō ya maē siṭṭhō gayāvahāraïniyayavuttantō
aha dinnavayaṇasōyā bhaṇiyā vaṇiēṇa tēṇāhaṁ // SurSuCa.201

dūrammi hatthiṇapuraṁ sāvayacōrēhiṁ duggamō maggō
āsannaṁ khu kusaggaṁ kiṁ kāyavvaṁ tumē bhagiṇi!? // SurSuCa.202


[p. 415]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kusagganayarammi vaccimō tāva
pēcchāmi bandhuvaggaṁ pabhūyakālāō siridatta! // SurSuCa.203

aha tēṇa saharisēṇaṁ nīyā satthammi niyayaāvāsē
viṇaōvayārapuvvaṁ ca kāriyā sayaladēhaṭhiiṁ // SurSuCa.204

taṁ dēvadinnakuṇḍalapamuhaṁ savvampi niyayaābharaṇaṁ
mōttūṇa aṅgulīyaṁ samappiyaṁ tassa vaṇiyassa // SurSuCa.205

tattō satthēṇa samaṁ caliyā siridattapariyaṇasamēyā
kijjantavivihaviṇayā vaṇiēṇaṁ, ḍōliyārụ̄dhā // SurSuCa.206

sōvi hu satthō jāva ya lahuyapayāṇēhiṁ vayaï aṇudiyahaṁ
kaïvayapayāṇagāiṁ tā ēgadiṇammi aḍavīē // SurSuCa.207

avasaüṇēṇaṁ thakkō diyahē diyahē na jāyaē saüṇaṁ
jāva ya divaḍḍhamāsē vōlīṇē savvasatthillā // SurSuCa.208


[p. 416]
sambalarahiyā tahaïṁ ṭhāumasattā taō samuccaliyā
avaganniya avasaüṇaṁ niyapuragamaṇassa turamāṇā // SurSuCa.209

[yugmam]
tattō bīyapayāṇē pabhāyasamayammi tammi satthammi
sahasā annāucciya dinnō bhillēhiṁ ōkkhandō // SurSuCa.210

aha kalayalaṁ nisāmiya satthajaṇē tattha āulībhūē
bhillēhiṁ hammamāṇē lhasijjantē ya sayarāhaṁ // SurSuCa.211

sajjhasabhariyā ahamavi paḍiyā aḍavīi jāva ikkallā
ghēttūṇaṁ ēgadisaṁ naṭṭhā aïguvilatarugahaṇē // SurSuCa.212

khaṇamēgaṁ tatthacchiya vayāmi kila tammi satthaṭhāṇammi
puṇaravi milāmi jēṇaṁ satthassa ahanti cintantī // SurSuCa.213

jāva payaṭṭā gantuṁ tāva na jāṇāmi kattha gantavvaṁ
kattō samāgayā haṁ kāē va disāē sō satthō // SurSuCa.214

[yugmam]

[p. 417]
bhayakampantasarīrā tāhē ēyaṁ disaṁ gahēūṇa
sañjāyadisāmōhā caliyā tarugahaṇamajjhēṇa // SurSuCa.215

dūraṁ gantūṇa puṇō valiyā vaccāmi piṭṭhaōhuttaṁ
siridattajaṇagavēsaṇaparāyaṇā tattha vaṇagahaṇē // SurSuCa.216

aha bhayataralacchīē iō taō tattha paribhamantīē
ummaggagamaṇabhajjantakaṇṭayāinnacaraṇāē // SurSuCa.217

pahasamasụdhiyāi daḍhaṁ paē paē nīsahaṁ kaṇantīē
vasimannēsaṇahēuṁ caḍiūṇa thalammi ēgammi // SurSuCa.218

jā pulaïyaṁ samantā tāva na dīsaï kahampi vasimanti
viyaranta vālanivahā samantaō bhīsaṇā aḍavī // SurSuCa.219

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
aviya kattha ya karālakēsariguñjiyasavaṇuttasantasāraṅgā
katthaï mahantajujjhantamattavaṇamahisayāinnā // SurSuCa.220


[p. 418]
katthaï garuya pavaṅgamavimukkabōkkārabahiriyadiyantā
kattha ya vaṇadavaḍajjhantajantukayabhīsaṇārāvā // SurSuCa.221

katthaï payaṇḍagaṇḍayakhaṇḍiyaru ruvisararuhirabībhacchā
katthaï sarahapalōyaṇapalāyamāṇōrukarivisarā // SurSuCa.222

aviya viyarantamahādhaṇuhatthalōddhayā sukkamayasirasaṇāhā
jēṭṭhakkamūlakaliyā gurucitārōhiṇīsamēyā // SurSuCa.223

bhaddavayasamaṇasahiyā uṭṭhantavisāhapayaḍamandārā
viyarantabhūririkkhā rēhaï aḍavī nahasirivva // SurSuCa.224

aha taṁ aḍaviṁ suiraṁ palōyayantīi gāḍhatisiyāē
ēkkammi disābhāē diṭṭhaṁ jalabhariyasaramēgaṁ // SurSuCa.225


[p. 419]
tattō tattōhuttaṁ caliyā bhayalōlalōyaṇā ahayaṁ
kahakahavi hu sampattā tammi paēsammi kicchēṇa // SurSuCa.226

pīyaṁ ca tattha salilaṁ uvaviṭṭhā taruvarassa hiṭṭhammi
ētthantarammi taraṇī antariō pasariyā rayaṇī // SurSuCa.227

taō phēkkāranti sivāō jaha jaha guñjanti sāvayā vivihaṁ
taha taha bhaēṇa hiyayaṁ kampaē maha tattha rannammi // SurSuCa.228

aha aḍḍharattasamaē jāyā udarammi dūsahā viyaṇā
tavvasaō ya kaṇantī lulāmi bhūmīē jāva ahaṁ // SurSuCa.229

tāva ya migīva rannē aïguru viyaṇāhi pīḍiyasarīrā
sayamēva pasaviyā haṁ mahākilēsēṇa naranāha! // SurSuCa.230

[yugmam]
mucchāviramē ya taō lulamāṇaṁ mahiyalammi taṁ bālaṁ
ghittūṇa nijucchaṅgē garuyasiṇēhēṇa tattō ya // SurSuCa.231


[p. 420]
gantūṇa jalāsannē ṇhāvittā tāhi niyayavatthāiṁ
pakkhāliya ēgantē uvaviṭṭhā tarulayāgahaṇē // SurSuCa.232

[yugmam]
taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ uttariya aṅgulīyayaṁ hatthā
kaṇṭhammi maē baddhaṁ suyassa ēvaṁ bhaṇantīē // SurSuCa.233

ēyassa pabhāvāō mā maha taṇayassa kēvi aṅgammi
paharantu bhūyasāvayapisāyaduṭṭhaggahāīyā // SurSuCa.234

vaṇavāsiṇīō! nisuṇaha bhō bhō vaṇadēvayāō! maha vayaṇaṁ
taṇayasamēyā sampaï saraṇaṁ bhavaīṇamallīṇā // SurSuCa.235

kēsarivagghāiṇaṁ maṁsāhāraṇa kūrasattāṇaṁ
bhīsaṇaaḍavīpaḍiyā rakkhēyavvā payattēṇa // SurSuCa.236

jaï putta! imā rayaṇī hontā maha tammi hatthiṇapurammi
tā ēttiyavēlāē rāyā vaddhāviō hontō // SurSuCa.237


[p. 421]
sayalassa pariyaṇassa ya purassa sāmantantivaggassa
kassa va na hōjja tōsō puttaya! tuha jammasamayammi // SurSuCa.238

duvvihiyavihivihāṇā paḍiyāē bhīsaṇē ya rannammi
jāō si majjha puttaya! karēmi kiṁ mandabhaggā haṁ? // SurSuCa.239

jāyammi tumē puttaya! rannampi hu sampayaṁ imaṁ vasimaṁ
naṭṭhaṁ bhayaṁ asēsaṁ ucchaṅgagaē tumē vaccha // SurSuCa.240

tuha muhapalōyaṇēṇaṁ sampannamaṇōrahā bhavissāmi
ravikarapahayandhayārē jāyammi diṇammi sakayatthā // SurSuCa.241

ēmāi bhaṇantīē pahasamakhinnāē nīsahaṅgāē
viyaṇāvigamāō tahiṁ samāgayā mē tahiṁ niddā // SurSuCa.242

tattō khaṇantarāō paḍibuddhā jhatti mandabhaggā haṁ
kēṇāvi hu ullaviyaṁ ēyaṁ saddaṁ suṇēūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.243


[p. 422]
niuṇaṁ jōyantēṇavi pabhūyakālāō pāva! diṭṭhō si
kāhāmi vaïraantaṁ aṇuhava duvvihiyaphalamiṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.244

ēyaṁ saddaṁ sōccā bhīyā, kō ēsa ēvamullavaï?
iya cintiya jāva ahaṁ niyaücchaṅgaṁ palōēmi // SurSuCa.245

tā natthi tattha puttō vicintiyaṁ tāhi hā! kimēyanti
kiṁ kahavi hōjja paḍiō ahavā kēṇāvi avahariō? // SurSuCa.246

kiṁvā sumiṇaṁ ēyaṁ kiṁvā maïvibbhamō mahaṁ ēsō?
ēmāi cintayantī gavēsiṁu tāhi pāraddhā // SurSuCa.247

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
iō taō tattha gavēsayantī suyaṁ mahārāya! apāuṇantī
sirammi vajjēṇava tāḍiyā haṁ ghasatti mucchāi vasaṁ gayatti // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï kamalāvaïputtaharaṇanāmotti
surasundarināmāē kahāē dasamō paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 423]
[ēkādaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha laddhacēyaṇā haṁ mucchāvirahammi garuyasōgillā
niyahiyayaṁ kuṭṭintī palaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā // SurSuCa.1

hā! niddaēṇa kēṇavi aḍavīpaḍiyāē dukkhataviyāē
takkhamēttuppannō puttō hariō ahannāē // SurSuCa.2

kila puttayassa vayaṇaṁ picchissamahaṁ pabhāyasamayammi
navaraṁ hayāsavihiṇā ēyaṁ maha annahā vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.3

aḍavipavēsāīyaṁ dukkhaṁ dāūṇa dūsahaṁ dēva!
kiṁ ajjavi na hu tuṭṭhō avahariō jēṇa maha puttō? // SurSuCa.4

vaṇadēvayāō! tumhaṁ saraṇammi samāgayāē maha puttō
hariō, tā kiṁ jujjaï ētthavi vēhā karēuṁ jē? // SurSuCa.5


[p. 424]
hā putta! kahamaraṇṇē mukkā haṁ saraṇavajjiyā tumaē
hā! kahamucchaṅgagaō sahasā addaṁsaṇībhūō? // SurSuCa.6

nūṇaṁ niṭṭhurarūvaṁ saddaṁ sōūṇa jassa paḍibuddhā
tēṇaṁ ciya avahariō pisāyarūvēṇa kēṇāvi // SurSuCa.7

jassa pabhāvāō tayā sahasā gayaṇāō gayavarō paḍiō
sōvi maṇī akayatthō jāō maha mandabhāgāē // SurSuCa.8

jaṁ kaṇṭhanibaddhēvi hu tammī aṅkaṭṭhiōvi hā putta!
hariō nikkaruṇēṇaṁ kēṇāvi addissarūvēṇa // SurSuCa.9

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ palavantīē tahiṁ sudīṇāē
maddukkhadukkhiyā iva khīṇā rayaṇīvi sahasatti // SurSuCa.10

aïkaruṇaṁ kandantiṁ daṭṭhuṁva mamaṁ sasōyavayaṇillā
nivaḍantathūlatārayaaṁsūhiṁva ruyaï nahalacchī // SurSuCa.11


[p. 425]
ētthantarammi sūrō suyāvahārayanihālaṇatthaṁva
nāsiyaghaṇandhayārō ārụdhō udayagirisiharaṁ // SurSuCa.12

aha addhapaharamēttē diyahē aïdukkhiyā ahaṁ tattha
aïkaruṇaṁ kandantī iō taō jāva viyarāmi // SurSuCa.13

tāva kamaṇḍaluhatthā miuvakkalavasaṇadhāriṇī tattha
pariṇayavayā pasanna samāgayā tāvasī ēgā // SurSuCa.14

[yugmam]
daṭṭhuṁ mamaṁ ruyantiṁ vivihapalāvēhiṁ tattha vaṇagahaṇē
sañjāyagaruyakaruṇā samāgayā majjha pāsammi // SurSuCa.15

mahuravayaṇēṇa tīē āpuṭṭhā suyaṇu! kīsa taṁ ruyasi
kattō samāgayā iha bhīsaṇarannammi ikkallā? // SurSuCa.16

kāuṁ tīi paṇāmaṁ tattō viyalantaaṁsuyāē maē
kuñjaraharaṇāīō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō // SurSuCa.17


[p. 426]
aha tāvasīē bhaṇiyaṁ imassa jōgā na hōsi taṁ suyaṇu!
tahavi hu kimittha kīraï sakammavasagammi jiyalōē? // SurSuCa.18

sundari! kammavasāṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ iha bhavē vasantāṇaṁ
ēvaṁvihadukkhāiṁ havanti jaṁ ēttha na hu cōjjaṁ // SurSuCa.19

jaṁ kiñci asuhakammaṁ annabhavē sañciyaṁ tumē āsi
tassa vivāgāō imaṁ samāgayaṁ suyaṇu! guruvasaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.20

tā annabhavaviḍhattē dukkhammi samāgayammi kō sōgō?
kiṁ vāvi vilaviēṇaṁ sarīrāyāsabhūēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.21

ēttō u samāsannē acchaï amhāṇa āsamō rammō
āgaccha suyaṇu! aṇuciyamēyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ jaō tujjha // SurSuCa.22

vāyaï sīyalapavaṇō ēttha ō taṁ abhiṇavapasūyā si
sukumālasarīrāē mā hōjja virūvayaṁ kiñci // SurSuCa.23


[p. 427]
iya bhaṇiya tāvasīē nīyā haṁ āsamammi rammammi
paḍijaggiyā ya sammaṁ nikkāraṇavacchalattēṇa // SurSuCa.24

aha kaïvayadivasēhiṁ sañjāyā satthadēhiyā maṇayaṁ
annammi diṇē nīyā tīē haṁ kulavaïsamīvē // SurSuCa.25

tīēvi puvvabhaṇiō vuttantō sāhiō kulavaïssa
karuṇāparēṇa tēṇavi aṇusaṭṭhā mahuravayaṇēhiṁ // SurSuCa.26

vacchē! iha saṁsārē sulahāiṁ ērisāiṁ dukkhāiṁ
akayammi suhanimittē dhammē paralōyabandhummi // SurSuCa.27

jāyanti dūsahāiṁ jēṇaṁ ciya ēttha dusahadukkhāiṁ
tēṇēva cattarajjā vaṇavāsamuvāgayā dhīrā // SurSuCa.28

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇassa u kulavaïṇō tīi tāvasīi ahaṁ
kannē hōuṁ bhaṇiyā bhayavaṁ varanāṇajuttō 'yaṁ // SurSuCa.29


[p. 428]
tō puccha icchiyatthaṁ bhaṇiyāē tāhi viṇayapaṇayāē
puṭṭhō maē mahāyasa! kēṇa hiō nandaṇō majjha? // SurSuCa.30

kiṁ jīvaï ahava maō pikkhissamahaṁ kayāivi navatti?
aha bhaṇiyaṁ kulavaïṇā sammaṁ dāūṇa uvaōgaṁ // SurSuCa.31

vacchē! ucchaṅgatthō tuha taṇaō avahiō u dēvēṇa
pāṇaviōyaṇahēuṁ puvvaviruddhēṇa kuddhēṇa // SurSuCa.32

vēyaḍḍhagiriniuñjē nēūṇa silāyalammi viulammi
mukkō chuhābhibhūō kila kicchēṇēsa maraütti // SurSuCa.33

aha kahavi vihivasēṇaṁ samāgaō tattha nahayarō ēkkō
niyabhāriyāsamēṇō tēṇa ya puttotti sō gahiō // SurSuCa.34

khayarassa tassa gēhē vuḍḍiṁ jāhī suhēṇa, tattō ya
sampattajōvvaṇō sō milihī tuha hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.35


[p. 429]
ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiē paṇaṭṭhasōgā narinda! jāyā haṁ
phalamūlakayāhārā viṇayaparā tāvasijaṇassa // SurSuCa.36

piya! kaïvayadivasāiṁ acchāmi tahiṁ tu āsamē jāva
tā annadiṇē kulavaï mūlē dhammaṁ suṇintīē // SurSuCa.37

bahutāvasisahiyāē sahasā āsēṇa vēgajuttēṇa
avahariō sampattō rāyasuō tattha ēgāgī // SurSuCa.38

[yugmam]
aha atihivacchalēhiṁ tāvasakumarēhiṁ vihiyasaṁmāṇō
āgamma vihiyaviṇaō uvaviṭṭhō kulavaï samīvē // SurSuCa.39

kulavaïṇā sō puṭṭhō kō si tumaṁ āgaō kuō bhadda!?
tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kahēmi nisuṇēha bhayavaṁ! ti // SurSuCa.40

siddhatthapurē rāyā suggīvō nāma āsi vikkhāō
kaṇagavaī sē dēvī tīē suō surahanāmō haṁ // SurSuCa.41


[p. 430]
aïvallahotti piuṇā juvarāyapayammi bālabhāvēvi
ahisittō avamanniya puttaṁ jiṭṭhaṁ tu suppaïṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.42

aha annayā kayāivi khayavāhīē mayammi jaṇayammi
tassa paē haṁ rāyā ahisittō mantivaggēṇa // SurSuCa.43

jiṭṭhassa annajaṇaṇītaṇayassa u tassa suppaïṭṭhassa
vijjāharēṇa kēṇavi kayaüvayārēṇa dinnāō // SurSuCa.44

nahagāmiṇipamuhāō vijjāō tappabhāvaō tēṇa
kāūṇa ya saṅgāmaṁ ahiṭṭhiyaṁ appaṇā rajjaṁ // SurSuCa.45

[yugmam]
tassa bhaēṇa ahampi hu samāgaō puravarīē campāē
jaṇaṇisamēō pāsē māyāmahakittidhammassa // SurSuCa.46

tēṇavi niyadēsantē dinnaṁ gāmāṇa sahassayaṁ ēgaṁ
tattha ya jaṇaṇīsahiō bhayavaṁ! acchāmi ahayanti // SurSuCa.47


[p. 431]
kaïvayadiṇēhiṁ intō imāi aḍavīi vāṇiyagasatthō
maha purisēhiṁ viluttō pattaṁ vittaṁ tahiṁ paüraṁ // SurSuCa.48

annaṁ ca tattha pattā tukkhāraturaṅgamā bahuvihīyā
tāṇāvāhaṇahēuṁ ajjēva pabhāyasamayammi // SurSuCa.49

bāhiṁ nīhariō haṁ kamēṇa turagē ō jāva vāhēmi
tāvikkēṇaṁ sahasā hariō vivarīyasikkhēṇa // SurSuCa.50

[yugmam]
aviya jaha jaha ōkkhañcijjaï taha taha vēgaṁ pagiṇhamāṇēṇa
bhayavaṁ! turagaṁmēṇa ihāṇiō āsamē tumha // SurSuCa.51

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï sō surahō kulavaïssa vuttanta
turayamaṇumaggalaggaṁ tāva ya sinnapi sē pattaṁ // SurSuCa.52

aha bhaṇiyaṁ surahēṇaṁ bhayavaṁ! vaccāmi niyayaṭhāṇammi
jaṁ kiñci maē iṇhiṁ kāyavvaṁ taṁ ca āisasu // SurSuCa.53


[p. 432]
aha kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ gurujaṇapūyāidhammakaraṇammi
jahasattīi payaṭṭasu saraṇāgayavacchalattē ya // SurSuCa.54

annaṁ ca bhadda! nisuṇasu ēsā rannō ya amarakēussa
dēvī gayaavahariyā acchaī kamalāvaī nāma // SurSuCa.55

dūrē hatthiṇanayaraṁ sāvayapaürā ya duggamā aḍavī
halakiṭṭhamahīē tahā viyaranti na tāvasakumārā // SurSuCa.56

tēṇa na ēsā sakkaï parāṇiuṁ niyapurammi amhēhiṁ
na ya kōvi tahārūvō annō iha āgaō satthō // SurSuCa.57

ēsā sukumālataṇū acchaï kicchēṇa ittha vaṇavāsē
tā jaï tumaṁ parāṇasi saṭṭhāṇaṁ hōi tā laṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.58

aha surahēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! jaṁ bhaṇaha taṁ karēmitti
gantuṁ sayamēva ahaṁ appissaṁ amarakēussa // SurSuCa.59


[p. 433]
bhaṇiyāṁ haṁ kulavaïṇā vacchē! surahassa bhāsiyaṁ nisuyaṁ?
tā vaccasu saha imiyā annō puṇa dullahō satthō // SurSuCa.60

aha cintiyaṁ maē kiṁ imēṇa saha hōi gamaṇamamhāṇaṁ
juggaṁ, ahavā jāṇaï bhayavaṁ ciya ēttha jaṁ uciyaṁ // SurSuCa.61

iya cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! jaṁ bhaṇasi taṁ karēmitti
jaï ēvaṁ tā vacchē! payaṭṭa, iha tēṇa bhaṇiyā haṁ // SurSuCa.62

bahu manniya tavvayaṇaṁ tāhē caliyā narinda! tēṇa samaṁ
takkāluciyaṁ kāuṁ tāvasisambhāsaṇāīyaṁ // SurSuCa.63

jāva ya kamēṇa pattā ēttha paēsammi tāva surahō sō
kimpi misaṁ kāuṇaṁ thakkō ētthēṇa raṇṇammi // SurSuCa.64

āvāsiūṇa sinnaṁ diṇē diṇē ēi maha samīvammi
daṁsēi ya bahumāṇaṁ, aha annadiṇammi ēgantē // SurSuCa.65


[p. 434]
ghittuṁ āharaṇāiṁ maha pāsē āgaō bhaṇaï ēvaṁ
ēyāiṁ giṇha sundari! na sōhasē taṁ nirābharaṇā // SurSuCa.66

[yugmam]
taṁ dēvadinnakuṇḍalapamuhaṁ savvampi niyayaābharaṇaṁ
pariyāṇiūṇa vimhiyahiyāē maē imaṁ bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.67

ēyāiṁ kuō tumaē pattāiṁ suraha! majjha sāhēsu
sō bhaṇaï suṇasu sundari! puvvaṁ maha bhillapurisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.68

iha aḍavīi samiddhō kusaggapurapatthiō vaṇiyasatthō
gahiō tahiṁ ca pattaṁ ēyaṁ tuha jōggamābharaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.69

[yugmam]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ maha santiyamēvamābharaṇamēyaṁ
siridattanāmagassa ō vaṇiyassa samappiyaṁ āsi // SurSuCa.70

harisiyamuhēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaï ēvaṁ tarihi sundarataranti
tā gēṇha imaṁ sundari! imassa jōggā tumaṁ nannā // SurSuCa.71


[p. 435]
aha tassa duṭṭhabhāvaṁ annāūṇaṁ tayaṁ maē gahiyaṁ
tattō ya païdiṇaṁ sō uvayaraï mamaṁ asuhabhāvō // SurSuCa.72

āgacchaï ēgantē parihāsakahāō kahaï maha puraō
saviyāraṁ ca palōyaï daṁsaï aṇurattamappāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.73

aha annadiṇē piyayayama! pāvēṇaṁ tēṇa mayaṇamụ̄dhēṇa
agaṇiya kulamajjāyaṁ ujjhiya lajjaṁ sudūrēṇa // SurSuCa.74

bahu manniya avivēyaṁ bhaṇiyā ēgantasaṇṭhiyā ēvaṁ
vammahapīḍiyadēhō saraṇaṁ tuha suyaṇu! allīṇō // SurSuCa.75

niyaaṅgasaṅgamēṇaṁ sahalaṁ mama kuṇasu jīviyaṁ ajja
tuha āyattā pāṇā savvassavi sāmiṇī taṁ si // SurSuCa.76

tuha suyaṇu! kiṅkarō haṁ āṇākārī ya pariyaṇō savvō
gạ̄dhāṇurāgarattaṁ kiṁ bahuṇā icchasu mamanti // SurSuCa.77


[p. 436]
tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ sahasā vajjēṇa tāḍiyāva ahaṁ
uppannagaruyadukkhā piyayama! cintāurā jāyā // SurSuCa.78

[yugmam]
hā! pāviṭṭhō ēsō balāvi sīlakhaṇḍaṇaṁ kāhī
saraṇavihūṇāi mamaṁ, tā iṇhiṁ kiṁ karēmitti? // SurSuCa.79

nibbhatthāmi girāhiṁ sampaï aïniṭṭhurāhiṁ jaï ēyaṁ
tā ēsa amajjāyō iṇhimpi virūvayaṁ kujjā // SurSuCa.80

tā sampaï mūyattaṁ juttaṁ avalambiuṁ taō pacchā
patthāvaṁ lahiūṇaṁ nāsissamimāō pāvāō // SurSuCa.81

iya cintiya tuṇhikā ahōmuhaṁ kāuṁ tattha khakkā haṁ
sōvi ya daṭhṭhūṇa mamaṁ niruttaraṁ uṭṭhiō tattō // SurSuCa.82

pattāē rayaṇīē nibbharasuttē ya sayalasinnammi
gahiūṇa tamābharaṇaṁ pāsāiṁ palōyaṇamāṇā // SurSuCa.83


[p. 437]
nihuyagaīē caliyā bhaēṇa kampantataṇulayā gāḍhaṁ
vañciya pāhariē haṁ nīhariyā tāō sinnāō // SurSuCa.84

ghittūṇa ya ēgadisaṁ caliyā ghaṇataruvaṇassa majjhēṇaṁ
nisuṇantī bahusāvayabhīsaṇasaddē bahuvihī( ha? )ē // SurSuCa.85

[yugmam]
pavaṇākampiyapāyavacalantapattāṇa saṇasaṇārāvaṁ
sīhōrālisamāṇaṁ mannantī vēvirasarīrā // SurSuCa.86

vēgēṇa ya gacchantī ghaṇandhayārāē tīē rayaṇīē
dīharaghaṇataṇaōcchāiyāē visamāē bhūmīē // SurSuCa.87

aviyāṇiyaparamatthā jhaḍatti paḍiyā ya ēttha kūvammi
piyayama! kayabahupāvā jīvā iva ghōranarayammi // SurSuCa.88

[yugmam]
bhaviyavvayāvasēṇaṁ na mayā gambhīrajalanivuḍḍāvi
agaḍassa taḍiṁ pāviya tattha nilukkā ahaṁ rāya! // SurSuCa.89


[p. 438]
maraṇē uvaṭṭhiēvi hu sīlaṁ saṁrakkhiyanti tuṭṭhamaṇā
appāṇaṁ sakayatthaṁ mannantā surahabhayamukkā // SurSuCa.90

gāḍhaṁ chuhābhibhūyā cattāri diṇāṇi ēttha kūvammi
paricattajīviyāsā ṭhiyā ahaṁ saraṇaparihīṇā // SurSuCa.91

ajja puṇa kalayalēṇa sibiraṁ āvāsiyanti nāūṇa
surahāsaṅkāē puṇō samāulā nāha! sañjāyā // SurSuCa.92

tattō kūvapaviṭṭhaṁ tumha naraṁ pāsiūṇa suṭṭhuyaraṁ
bhīyāi pucchiyāivi na uttaraṁ kiñci mē dinnaṁ // SurSuCa.93

puṇaravi ya tumha nāmaṁ sōūṇaṁ vigayaannaāsaṅkā
harisabharanibbharaṅgī uttariyā dēva! kūvāō // SurSuCa.94

ēyaṁ maē 'ṇubhūyaṁ saraṇavihuṇāē tumha virahammi
nisuēṇa jēṇa jāyaï dukkhaṁ pāsaṭṭhiyāṇampi // SurSuCa.95


[p. 439]
iya kamalāvaïbhaṇiyaṁ āyanniya amarakēunaranāhō
bāhajalāvilanayaṇō gurusōgō bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.96

kiṁ dēva! ittha kīraï sakammavasayāṇa navari jīvāṇa
jāyanti dūsahāiṁ dukkhāiṁ ēttha saṁsārē // SurSuCa.97

sakayaṁ suhamasuhaṁ vā ikkō aṇuhavaï vivihajōṇīsu
māyā piyā ya bhattā bandhujaṇō vāvi na hu saraṇaṁ // SurSuCa.98

rāgaddōsavasāē asuhaphalaṁ āsi jaṁ kayaṁ kammaṁ
tassa vasāō sundari! sampattā vasaṇariñchōlī // SurSuCa.99

ēvaṁ gaēvi jaṁ dēvi! ēttha kūvammi nivaḍiyā ēvaṁ
sampattā taṁ mannē anannapuṇṇōdaō kōvi // SurSuCa.100

paḍikūḍakāriṇāvi hu vihiṇā vihiyaṁ tu ēttiyaṁ laṭṭhaṁ
jaṁ akkhayadēhāē tumaē saha saṅgamō vihiō // SurSuCa.101


[p. 440]
ēmāibahuvigappaṁ dēviṁ āsāsiūṇa sō rāyā
niyasinnēṇa samēō samāgaō gayapuraṁ kamasō // SurSuCa.102

kāriyagaruyapamōō thuvvantō nayaranārinivahēṇa
kamalāvaīsamēō dāṇaṁ dēntō amarakēū // SurSuCa.103

kayamaṅgalōvayārō nāyarajaṇajaṇiyahiyayaāṇandō
niyamandirē paviṭṭhō pakkalapāikkapariyariō // SurSuCa.104

[yugmam]
ēvaṁ ca tassa rannō adiṭṭhadukkhassa dēvisahiyassa
bōlīṇāiṁ kaïvi hu varisāṇaṁ sayasahassāiṁ // SurSuCa.105

aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō tassa
paḍihārāṇunnāō samantabhaddotti nāmēṇa // SurSuCa.106

ujjāṇammi niuttō pattō paṇamittu rāyapayakamalaṁ
sīsanivēsiyakarakamalasampuḍō harisiō bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.107

[yugmam]

[p. 441]
puvvaṁ dēvēṇaṁ ahaṁ nēmittiyasumaïvayaṇayaṁ sōccā
kusumāyaraüjjāṇassa pālagattē niuttō mhi // SurSuCa.108

taṁ ca tisañjhaṁ niccaṁ palōyamāṇassa ēttiō kālō
vōlīṇō na ya diṭṭhaṁ kiñcivi nēmittiyāiṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.109

ajja puṇa appabhāē gayaṇē ujjāṇamajjhayārammi
kusumiyasāhisamūhaṁ iō taō picchamāṇēṇa // SurSuCa.110

ēgammi disābhāē vallaravēllīsaṇāhadumagahaṇē
uttāsiyahaṁsaülō uṭṭhāviō saüṇasandōhō // SurSuCa.111

nisuō vimhayajaṇaō bahiriyaāsannasattasuivivarō
muhariyadisāvibhāgō garuyakhaḍakkārasaṁsaddō // SurSuCa.112

[tisr̥bhiḥ viśēṣakam]
sōūṇa ya taṁ saddaṁ vimhiyaütphullalōyaṇēṇa maē
pulaïya tattōhuttaṁ cintiyamavvō! kimēyanti // SurSuCa.113


[p. 442]
kassa puṇa ēsa saddō samuṭṭhiō ēttha vaṇaniguñjammi
iya cintantō kōūhalēṇa tattōmuhō caliō // SurSuCa.114

tāva ya diṭṭhā bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyā baülapāyavasamīvē
mucchānimīliyacchī adhariyasurasundarīrūvā // SurSuCa.115

ahiṇavajōvvaṇaübbhēyasundarā sayalamaṇaharāvayavā
paümacuyā iva lacchī naravara! varabāliyā ēkkā // SurSuCa.116

[yugmam]
nūṇaṁ nahatthalāō nivaḍantīē imīē bhūmīē
juvaīē paḍisaddō samuṭṭhiō ēsa sahasatti // SurSuCa.117

kaha mannē ērisassavi juvaīrayaṇassa ērisā 'vatthā
vibuhajaṇasōyaṇijjā dhī! vihiṇō vilasiyaṁ cittaṁ // SurSuCa.118

iya cintantēṇa maē sīyalajalasīyarēhiṁ saṁsittā
miupavaṇakaraṇavihiṇā aha vihiyā sā samāsatthā // SurSuCa.119


[p. 443]
hariṇivva jūhabhaṭṭhā sataralatāraṁ disāō pulayantī
bhaṇiyā maē sumahuraṁ kīsa tumaṁ suyaṇu! bīhēsi? // SurSuCa.120

mā bhaddē! kuṇasu bhayaṁ thēvampi, hu jaṇayanivisēsō haṁ
kā si tumaṁ kattō vā iha paḍiyā majjha sāhēsu? // SurSuCa.121

aviya saggāō nivaḍiyā kiṁ sāvappahayā suraṅgaṇā taṁ si
kiṁ vāvi bhaṭṭhavijjā vijjāharabāliyā suyaṇu!? // SurSuCa.122

tuharūvadaṁsaṇuppannaharaṇabuddhissa nahapayaṭṭassa
vijjāharassa kassavi kiṁvā hatthāō pabbhaṭṭhā? // SurSuCa.123

sāhēsu suyaṇu! ēyaṁ mahantakōūhalaṁ imaṁ majjha
nīsāhārā kaha nahayalāō paḍiyā ihujjāṇē? // SurSuCa.124

iya sā bhaṇiyā bhūnāha! majjha paḍiuttaraṁ adāūṇa
gurudukkhasūyaṇaparaṁ aṁsujalaṁ mōttumāraddhā // SurSuCa.125


[p. 444]
aha taṁ tahāvihaṁ pāsiūṇa paricintiyaṁ maē ēyaṁ
taṁ ēyaṁ sañjāyaṁ jaṁ puvvaṁ sumaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.126

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā gayaṇāō kannagā paḍihī
tattō ya sigghamēva hi puttēṇa samāgamō hōhī // SurSuCa.127

tā kiṁ iha puṭṭhāē imāē, tāva sāhēmi
gantuṁ vaïyaramēyaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva naravaïṇō // SurSuCa.128

iya cintiūṇa tattō āsāsittā sumahuravayaṇēhiṁ
āṇīyā niyagēhē samappiyā sā sabhajjāē // SurSuCa.129

niyapariyaṇaṁ ca savaṁ sarīrasaṁvāhaṇāivāvārē
tīē niuïūṇaṁ samāgaṁō dēvapāsammi // SurSuCa.130

ēvaṁ samantabhaddēṇa sāhiyaṁ vaïyaraṁ nisāmittā
vimhiyahiyaō rāyā aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.131


[p. 445]
avvō! hu avitahaṁ taṁ picchaha nēmittiyassa sumaïssa
tā puttēṇa samāṇaṁ āsannaṁ daṁsaṇaṁ iṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.132

tā bhō samantabhaddaya! sigghaṁ āṇēha bāliyaṁ tamiha
jīē pabhāvēṇa maē pikkhēyavvō saputtōti // SurSuCa.133

vayaṇāṇantaramēva hi samantabhaddēṇa gantumāṇīyā
sā bāliyā viṇijjiyasurajuvaīrūvasōhaggā // SurSuCa.134

tīē sarīrasōhaṁ picchiya rannā vicintiyaṁ avvō
āgārō ciya sūyaï imīē sukulammi sambhūiṁ // SurSuCa.135

uciyāsaṇōvaviṭṭhā sā kannā amarakēunaravaïṇā
bhaṇiyā hiyayabbhantaragurusōgu vvāyapaṇḍumuhā // SurSuCa.136

vacchē! ujjhasu sōyaṁ cayasu bhayaṁ jaṇayanivisēsassa
sāhijjaü maha ēyaṁ kammi purē taṁ samuppannā? // SurSuCa.137


[p. 446]
kassa va dhūyā kaha vā ihāgayā kaha va majjha ujjāṇē
paḍiyā si nahayalāō sāhēsu savittharaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.138

aha sā ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā gurusōyā sajjhasēṇa abhibhūyā
ummukkadīhasāsā na kiñci paḍiuttaraṁ dēi // SurSuCa.139

aha puṇaruttaṁ rannā puṭṭhāē tīē kahavi saṁlattaṁ
tāya! caēmi na vōttuṁ bahudukhaṁ niyayavuttantaṁ // SurSuCa.140

tahavi hu alandhaṇīyā āṇā tāyassa tēṇa sāhēmi
jambuddīvē bharahē kusagganayarammi nāmēṇa // SurSuCa.141

atthi puraṁ supasiddhaṁ tattha ya naravāhaṇō puhaïnāhō
rayaṇavaī sē dēvī tīē dhūyā ahaṁ tāya! // SurSuCa.142

[yugmam]
surasundarittināmā puvviṁ duvvihiyakammapariṇāmā
vēriyasamēṇa kēṇaï pisāyarūvēṇa avahariyā // SurSuCa.143


[p. 447]
ēttiyamittaṁ bhaṇiuṁ sōyasamubbhuyagarumannuvasā
thūlaṁsuē muyantī nihuyaṁ rōuṁ pavattā sā // SurSuCa.144

ētthantarammi rannō addhāsaṇasaṅgayāē dēvīē
kamalāvaīē gahiyā rōvantī sā nijucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.145

bhaṇiyā vacchē! mā ruya na hōi dīvantaraṁ imaṁ suyaṇu!
hatthiṇapuraṁ hi ēyaṁ ēsō rāyā amarakēū // SurSuCa.146

kamalāvaī ahampi hu, sahōyarō hōi tuha piyā majjha
vacchē! tumampi amhaṁ suyapuvvā nāmamēttēṇa // SurSuCa.147

bahuvihapaōyaṇēṇaṁ kusagganayarāō jō jaṇō ēntō
sō savvō surasundari! tuha guṇanivahaṁ maha kahintō // SurSuCa.148

ēvaṁ surūvakaliyā ēvaṁ piuṇō ya vacchalā bāḍhaṁ
ēvaṁ kalāsu kusalā ēvaṁ dakkhinnadayajuttā // SurSuCa.149


[p. 448]
tā mā kuṇasu visāyaṁ ēyampi ya piuharaṁ nijaṁ tujjha
acchasu vīsatthamaṇā kīḍantī vivihakīḍāhiṁ // SurSuCa.150

ēvavihavayaṇēhiṁ āsāsittā nijuttarīēṇa
aṁsuyadhōyakavōlaṁ tīē muhaṁ sampamajjittā // SurSuCa.151

muhasōyaṁ dāūṇaṁ nīyā dēvīē mandirē niyaē
tatthavi uvviggamaṇā acchaï gurusōyasantattā // SurSuCa.152

[yugmam]
nīsasaï dīhadīhaṁ khaṇēṇa thūlaṁsuyāiṁ millēi
mucchijjaī khaṇēṇaṁ khaṇēṇa saṁvaraï appāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.153

vilavaï khaṇēṇa vihasaï rōvaï khaṇēṇa mūyalliyā hōi
gurucintābharavihuriyahiyayā parihāi aṇudiyahaṁ // SurSuCa.154

aha taṁ vigatayāṇandaṁ picchiya kamalāvaī vicintēi
āṇākārī savvōvi pariyaṇō tāva ēīē // SurSuCa.155


[p. 449]
taha ya samāṇavayāō siṇēhasārāō rāyakannāō
nāṇāvihacēṭṭhāhiṁ aṇudiyahamimaṁ viṇōēnti // SurSuCa.156

tahavi hu raïṁ na pāvaï ēsā cintāē susaï aṇudiyahaṁ
tā mannē kā cintā jīē ēsā u parihāi // SurSuCa.157

jaï tā māupiūṇaṁ sumaraï tā kiṁ kahēi na hu majjha?
mayaṇaviyārasaricchā nēya viyārā tahiṁ hunti // SurSuCa.158

ēgantaṁ jaha sēvaï vihaḍiyacakkāiṁ jaha ya mēllēi
piyasaṅgamasārāō kahāō jaha suṇaï taccittā // SurSuCa.159

taha mannē pēmmagahō vilasaï ēvaṁvihāhiṁ ciṭṭhāhiṁ
tā jaha ēsā majjhaṁ tahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhaï sarūvaṁ // SurSuCa.160

tā tassa pāvaṇammivi kōvi uvāōvi labbhaē nūṇaṁ
na ya ēsā vajjarihī puṭṭhāvi jahaṭṭhiyaṁ majjha // SurSuCa.161

[yugmam]

[p. 450]
vāmasahāvō mayaṇō akkhijjantō na pāyaḍō hōi
najjaï āgārēhiṁ gōvijjantōvi chēēhiṁ // SurSuCa.162

tahavi hu lahāmi kēṇavi handi! uvāēṇa bhāvamēīē
iya cintiya āṇattā niyacēḍī haṁsiyā nāma // SurSuCa.163

surasundarīi uvvēvakāraṇaṁ lahasu haṁsiē! kahavi
tujjha samāṇavayāē sāhissaï hiyayasabbhāvaṁ // SurSuCa.164

jaṁ āṇavēsi sāmiṇi! iya bhaṇiuṁ haṁsiyā gayā jhatti
ēgantaṭṭhiyasurasundarīē pāsammi allīṇā // SurSuCa.165

sabbhāvanēhasūyagēvīsambhakahāhiṁ vivihabhaṇiīhiṁ
uppāiya vīsambhaṁ bhaṇiyā surasundarī tīē // SurSuCa.166

surasundari! tuha cariyassa nisuṇaṇē atthi kōugaṁ majjha
kaha kēṇa kiṁ nimittaṁ avahariyā kiñca aṇubhūyaṁ? // SurSuCa.167


[p. 451]
surasundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ tāēṇavi āsi pucchiyā ēva
kiṁ puṇa lajjāē maē na sakkiyaṁ tattha vajjariuṁ // SurSuCa.168

kiñca maha cariyaṁ summantaṁ jaṇēī pāsaṭṭhiyāṇavi dukkhaṁ
tēṇa na vōttuṁ majjhavi gurudukkhasañjaṇagaṁ // SurSuCa.169

tahavi hu tumaē puṭṭhā vayaṁsi! kōūhalēṇa garuēṇa
sāhēmi tēṇa nisuṇasu ēgamaṇā vajjarijjantaṁ // SurSuCa.170

atthi puhaīpayāsaṁ niraggalōdaggavaggiraturaṅgaṁ
vaggiraturaṅgakharakhurukkhayakhēhāinnarikkhapahaṁ // SurSuCa.171

rikkhapahapavaṇakampiradhayavaḍarēhantabhūrisāṇūraṁ
sāṇūragahiravajjiratūraravupphuṇṇādisicakkaṁ // SurSuCa.172

disiccakkagēyasatthāhasatthakijjantavajjavāṇijjaṁ
vāṇijjakalāpattaṭṭhalaṭṭhavāṇiyagaramaṇīyaṁ // SurSuCa.173


[p. 452]
ramaṇīyaṇavaravajjiranēurajhaṅkāraruddhasuivivaraṁ
vivarīyarayaviyakkhaṇavilāsiṇīlōyapaḍipunnaṁ // SurSuCa.174

punnukkaḍajaṇavāsaṁ ibbhasahassōvasōhiyaṁ viulaṁ
viularasāyalaparigayaparihāpāyārasōhillaṁ // SurSuCa.175

sōhillatiyacaükkaṁ ukkaḍadappiṭṭhajōhasayakaliyaṁ
nāmēṇa kusaggapuraṁ nayaraṁ diyalōyasāricchaṁ // SurSuCa.176

[ṣaṅbhiḥ kulakam]
akkantaguruparakkamaaccantukkaḍapayāvapaḍivakkhō
tatthatthi suvikkhāō rāyā naravāhaṇō nāma // SurSuCa.177

tassa ya rannō mittō kumārabhāvammi kahavi sañjāō
vēyaḍḍhakuñjarāvattacittabhāṇussa aṅgaruhō // SurSuCa.178

nāmēṇa bhāṇuvēgō tēṇa ya pīīthirattaṇanimittaṁ
dinnā niyayā bhagiṇī rayaṇavaī nāma ēyassa // SurSuCa.179


[p. 453]
sayalantēurapavarā jāyā sā tassa hiyayavallahiyā
tīi saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa kālēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.180

[yugmam]
ēkkacciya dhūyā haṁ jāyā jammammi majjha tāēṇa
suyajammaṇaabbhahiō nayarammi mahōcchavō vihiō // SurSuCa.181

surasundarisamarūvā ēsā iha cintiūṇa tāēṇa
surasundaritti nāmaṁ païṭṭhiyaṁ uciyasamayammi // SurSuCa.182

kamasō pavaḍḍhamāṇā kumārabhāvammi juvaïjōggāō
gāhāviyā kalāō jāyā ya kamēṇa takkusalā // SurSuCa.183

aviya vittē naṭṭē gīē pattacchējjē ya hatthakaṇḍēsu
vīṇāsaralakakhaṇavañjaṇēsu vāyaraṇatakkēsu // SurSuCa.184

jāyā viyakkhaṇā haṁ buddhīē suragurussa sāricchā
ēkkammi paē laddhē sēsaṁ ūhēmi laddhīē // SurSuCa.185


[p. 454]
ambāē tāyassa ya sayalassa ya pariyaṇassa āṇandaṁ
kuṇamāṇā sampattā kamasō haṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ // SurSuCa.186

daṭhṭhūṇa jōvvaṇaṁ maha tāō cintāurō daḍhaṁ jāō
kō aṇurūvō hōhī bhattā iha majjha dhūyāē? // SurSuCa.187

aha annayā ya sumaī nēmittī āgaō tahiṁ rannā
puṭṭhō maha dhūyāē kō hōhī bhadda! bhattārō? // SurSuCa.188

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa naravara! vijāharacakkavaṭṭiṇō ēsā
hōhī sayalantēurapavarā aïvallahā dēvī // SurSuCa.189

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ maṇammi āṇandaēṇa tāēṇa
dāūṇa bhūridavvaṁ paṭṭhaviō sumaïnēmittī // SurSuCa.190

aha annayā ya ahayaṁ pariyariyā bahuvihāhiṁ cēḍīhiṁ
niyasahiyaṇasañjuttā pattā purabāhirujjāṇē // SurSuCa.191


[p. 455]
tattha ya vivihapagāraṁ kīḍantīē tadēgadēsammi
diṭṭhā paḍhamavayatthā vijjāharabāliyā ēkkā // SurSuCa.192

parijaviya kiñci mantaṁ uppaïumaṇā pasāraï bhuyāō
ullalaï nahayalammi nivaḍaï dharaṇīi puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.193

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ vimhiyā haṁ sampattā tīi antiyaṁ turiyaṁ
bhaṇiyā ya maē sundari! kā si tumaṁ kiñca kuṇasi imaṁ? // SurSuCa.194

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddē! āyannasu, girivarammi vēyaḍ̣dhē
dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīē rayaṇasañcayaṁ atthi varanayaraṁ // SurSuCa.195

vijjāharavaracakkī rāyā tatthatthi cittavēgotti
rāyā ya bhāṇuvēgō atthi purē kuñjarāvattē // SurSuCa.196

tassa ya dō bhagiṇīō sahōyarāō ya aīva iṭṭhāō
paḍhamā ō bandhudattā rayaṇavaī nāma bīyā u // SurSuCa.197


[p. 456]
sā suyaṇu! bandhudattā pariṇīyā cittavēganaravaïṇā
tīē dhūyā ahayaṁ nāmaṁ ca piyaṁvayā majjha // SurSuCa.198

annāvi mahādēvī tāyassa u atthi kaṇagamālatti
tīē ya atthi puttō nāmēṇaṁ mayarakēutti // SurSuCa.199

sō maha aīva iṭṭhō virahaṁ na sahāmi tassa nimisampi
sampaï puṇa tāēṇaṁ dinnāō tassa vijjāō // SurSuCa.200

vijjāṇa sāhaṇatthaṁ pasattakhittammi sō gaō vijaṇē
jahabhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ sāhaï sō tattha vijjāō // SurSuCa.201

vaṭṭaï bīō māsō vijjāō tassa sāhayantassa
ahamavi tassa viōgē tarāmi nō jāva acchēuṁ // SurSuCa.202

tā pucchiūṇa jaṇagaṁ caliyā haṁ tassa darisaṇanimittaṁ
āgamaṇaparissantā ōinnā ittha ujjāṇē // SurSuCa.203


[p. 457]
ahiṇavapạdhiyattaṇaō vijjāē kahavi majjha payamēgaṁ
pamhuṭṭhamahannāē tēṇa ya na caēmi uppaïuṁ // SurSuCa.204

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ ēyaṁ sāhiyaṁ suyaṇu! tujjha
vijjāvayassa bhaṁsē saṭṭhāṇaṁ kahaṇu pāvissaṁ? // SurSuCa.205

puṇaruttampi hu pạdhiē sambharaï na majjha taṁ payaṁ kahavi
uttaṭṭhamayasilimbacchi! tēṇamahamāulājāyā // SurSuCa.206

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvaē! atthi tīi vijjāē
ēsō kappō jaṁ kila sāhijjaï handi! annassa! // SurSuCa.207

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē sāhijjaï natthi kōvi dōsotti
jaï ēvaṁ tā sāhasu mā (mē) kahavi payaṁ uvalabhijjā // SurSuCa.208

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiē samāṇasiddhitti tīi bhaṇiūṇa
ṭhāūṇa kannamūlē pạdhiyā saṇiyaṁ tu sā vijjā // SurSuCa.209


[p. 458]
tattō citantīē lahumēva maē tayaṁ payaṁ laddhaṁ
lahiūṇa tīē siṭṭhaṁ bhavaï imaṁ kiṁ nu ēvanti? // SurSuCa.210

viyasiyamuhakamalāē tīē bhaṇiyaṁ suṭṭhu uvaladdhaṁ
calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ maha hōsi taṁ guruṇī // SurSuCa.211

jīē vijjhā dinnā, tā maha sāhēsu tujjha kiṁ nāma?
ēttha purammī kassa va dhūyā taṁ sukayapunnassa? // SurSuCa.212

majjha sahīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddē! naravāhaṇassa naravaïṇō
rayavaṇaïdēvīē dhūyā surasundarī ēsā // SurSuCa.213

accabbhuyaguṇaniyarā kiṁ na suyā sayalalōyavikkhāyā
vijjāharadhūyāē dhūyā surasundarī bhaddē!? // SurSuCa.214

ēvaṁ tīē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisabāhapuṇṇacchī
gahiūṇa mama kaṇṭhē piyaṁvayā bhaṇiumāḍhattā // SurSuCa.215


[p. 459]
ambāē majjha puvviṁ vajjariyaṁ āsi, majjha lahubhagiṇī
bhūmicaramittassa u rannō maha bhāuṇā dinnā // SurSuCa.216

tā māusiyādhūyā bhagiṇī taṁ hōsi majjhaṁ candamuhi!
iya jampiūṇa dinnaṁ tīē maha sāiyaṁ garuyaṁ // SurSuCa.217

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ āgacchasu bhagiṇi! majjha gēhammi
bandhujaṇavacchalāē ambāē daṁsaṇaṁ kuṇasu // SurSuCa.218

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē pikkhissaṁ māusiṁ paḍiniyattā
kāraṇavasēṇa sampaï gacchissaṁ bhāuyasamīvaṁ // SurSuCa.219

itthatthē nibbandhaṁ mā kāhisi ucchugā ahaṁ iṇhiṁ
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvanti ya kintu pucchāmi // SurSuCa.220

kiñcivi, taṁ maha sāhasu, tīē bhaṇiyaṁ tu puccha, sāhēmi
bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē bhaddē! kakkhāē gōviē ēttha? // SurSuCa.221


[p. 460]
cittapaḍē kiṁ acchaï lihiyaṁ, cittammi kōugaṁ majjha
tā daṁsijjaü ēyaṁ jaï jōggaṁ daṁsiuṁ bhagiṇi! // SurSuCa.222

[yugmam]
