viyasiyamuhāi tīē pasāriuṁ daṁsiō paḍō amha
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīi isō maē sahatthēṇa lihiutti // SurSuCa.223

tattha ya paḍammi lihiyaṁ daṭhṭhūṇamaṇaṅgasaṁnibhaṁ taruṇaṁ
amaēṇava sittā haṁ jāō hiyayassa āṇandō // SurSuCa.224

cirapariciyavva diṭṭhō diṭṭhī āṇandabāhapaḍihatthā
jāyā savvasarīrē samuṭṭhiō bahalarōmañcō // SurSuCa.225

phuraphuriyaṁ aharēṇaṁ ullasiyaṁ bhuyalayāhiṁ sahasatti
ūsasiyaṁ ca thaṇēṇaṁ tharahariyaṁ ūrujuyalēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.226

suttāva mucchiyā iva mattā iva vigayacēyaṇā jāyā
sōhaggamandiraṁ taṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ cittalihiyampi // SurSuCa.227


[p. 461]
nāūṇa majjha bhāvaṁ vasantiyāē sahīi saṁlattaṁ
kō ēsa taē lihiō piyaṁvaē! lōyaṇāṇandō? // SurSuCa.228

bhaṇiyamaha kumuiṇīē vasantiē! kiṁ tuhittha pucchāē?
kāmiṇihiyayāṇandō lihiō raïvirahiō mayaṇō // SurSuCa.229

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō sirimaïyāē sahīē saṁlattaṁ
ēttiyakālaṁ raïvirahiō imō āsi pañcasarō // SurSuCa.230

sampaï raīē sahiō ēsō mayaṇotti kiṁ na pulaēsi?
payaḍā raīvi ēsā āsannā cēva ēyassa // SurSuCa.231

taṁ sōuṁ savvāhiṁ sahatthatālaṁ tu pahasiuṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
ēvaṁ ēyaṁ sirimaï! sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumaē // SurSuCa.232

aha laddhacēyaṇāē vinnāyā hanti jāyalajjāē
āgāraṁ viṇigūhiya sakōvamēvaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.233


[p. 462]
hambhō! aliyapalāviṇi! daṁsaṇamittampi natthi ēēṇa
kattō āsannattaṁ jēṇa kayā haṁ raī tumaē? // SurSuCa.234

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ mā sahi! rūsasu, diṭṭhammi jēṇa ēyammi
cittammi raī jāyā tēṇa raī taṁ maē bhaṇiyā // SurSuCa.235

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē kiṁvā asamañjasabhāsiṇīhiṁ ēyāhiṁ
tāva ya, piyaṁvaē! kahasu ēsa kō vā taē lihiō? // SurSuCa.236

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē bhāyā maha ēsa mayarakēutti
rūvēṇa jō aṇaṅgō sūrō cāī kalākusalō // SurSuCa.237

kaïyāvi cittaphalaē kaïyāvi paḍammi tassa paḍirūvaṁ
lihiūṇa maē appā viṇōiō ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ // SurSuCa.238

sampaï puṇa asamatthā sahiuṁ virahaṁ imassa caliyā haṁ
tā bhagiṇi! muñca vaccāmi jēṇa pāsammi tassēva // SurSuCa.239


[p. 463]
bhaṇiyaṁ ca sirimaīē ēvaṁ jō garuyaguṇagaṇāvāsō
sō tuha bhāyā // SurSuCa.240

cittagaēṇavi tāva ya āṇandō sahijaṇassa sañjaṇiō
iṇhiṁ paccakkhampi hu daṁsijjaō amayabhūō sō // SurSuCa.241

vihasiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē bhaṇiyaṁ mā sahi
 // SurSuCa.242

aviya jaï tāva kāvi hu ahaṁ tā 'vassaṁ tassa saṅgamēṇa suhaṁ
kāyavvaṁ bhagiṇīē aṇukūlō jaï vihī hōhī // SurSuCa.243

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē tāva ya ēyāō havantu aliyabhaṇirīō
piyasahi! tumampi sampaï asamañjasabhāsiṇī jāyā // SurSuCa.244

aïniuṇaṁ kilaṁ citta amhē kōūhalēṇa pulaēmō
tumhē saḍhahiyayāō annaha savvaṁ viyappēha // SurSuCa.245


[p. 464]
aha kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō
tā sahi! tumampi ēvaṁ cittaṁ lihiuṁ samabbhasasu // SurSuCa.246

appēsu paḍaṁ ēyaṁ piyaṁvaē! jēṇa cittamabbhasaï
tuha bhagiṇī, aha tīē samappiō kumuiṇīi paḍō // SurSuCa.247

sambhāsiuṁ tāhiṁ piyaṁvayā sā taō mamaṁ uppaïyā nahaggē
sahīhi juttā bahukēliyāhiṁ ahampi pattā niyamandirammi // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï piyaṁvayādaṁsaṇotti nāmēṇa
surasundarīkahāē ēkkārasamō paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 465]
[dvādaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha tattha suvitthinnē pasatthavatthōhavihiyaüllōcē
gantuṁ niyavāsagihē pāsuttā pavarasayaṇīē // SurSuCa.1

bhaṇiyāō ya sahīō vaccaha savvāō niyayagēhēsu
maha kuṇakuṇāi sīsaṁ sīyanti ya savvaaṅgāiṁ // SurSuCa.2

jaragahiṁyava sarīraṁ tā sōvissaṁ khaṇantaraṁ ēgaṁ
tattō ya kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ karēsutti // SurSuCa.3

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō vajjariyaṁ sirimaīē kiṁ bhagiṇi!
sahasā jāyamasatthaṁ tuha dēhaṁ, kāraṇaṁ bhaṇasu? // SurSuCa.4

bhaṇiyaṁ vasantiyāē sirimaï! taṁ cēva vēccayaṁ muṇasi
tā cintēsu sayaṁ ciya rōgassa nidāṇamēyassa // SurSuCa.5


[p. 466]
aha sirimaīi majjhaṁ saṁ dhāṇāiṁ niēva sāsūyaṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ na kimpi tāva ya lakkhijjaï bajjhavittīē // SurSuCa.6

aviya duvihā saṅkhēvēṇaṁ sārīrā ' 'gantuyā ya rōgatti
aha vāyapittasimbhubbhavā ya, iha ādimā nēyā // SurSuCa.7

tāṇaṁ maṅkhaṇalaṅghaṇanivāyasēvāiyā cigicchāō
vējjayasatthuddiṭṭhā purisaṁ kālaṁ na nāūṇa // SurSuCa.8

bhūyagahacakkhusāgiṇidōsā āgantuyā muṇēyavvā
balihōmamantatantāiyā hu vivihā cigicchā siṁ // SurSuCa.9

sārīriyarōgāṇaṁ na lakkhaṇaṁ kiñci dīsaï imīē
tā nūṇaṁ āgantuyadōsō takkijjaī nannō // SurSuCa.10

uttārijjaü lōṇaṁ hakkārijjantu vivihagāruḍiyā
sarisavaghāō dijjaü bajjaü taha rakkhapōṭṭaliyā // SurSuCa.11


[p. 467]
aha laliyāē bhaṇiyaṁ tā kiṁ sigghaṁ na kīraē ēyaṁ
vāhī uvikkhiō jaṁ na hōi iha sundarō bhaddē! // SurSuCa.12

tō sirimaïē bhaṇiyaṁ lakkhēmō amhi kēvalaṁ vāhiṁ
na uṇō paüṇīkāuṁ sattā aha māhavī bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.13

lakkhaï jō kira vāhiṁ paüṇampi hu sō karissaē pattaṁ
jēṇiha diṭṭhā cōrā paharayamavi dēha sō nūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.14

nihuyaṁ hasiūṇa taō savvāhivi saharisaṁ samullaviyaṁ
sirimaï! iṇhi na chuṭṭasi amha sahiṁ jaṇasu paüṇanti // SurSuCa.15

annaṁ, sa tujjha jaṇaō suprasiddhō mantajāṇaō suyaṇu!
tā vāhiūṇa mantaṁ paüṇaṁ surasundariṁ kuṇasu // SurSuCa.16

aha sirimaīi bhaṇiyaṁ jaï maha jaṇaō viyāṇaī mantē
tā kiṁ maha, jaï miṭṭhaṁ khīraṁ tā kiṁ nu chāṇassa? // SurSuCa.17


[p. 468]
kimpuṇa bhaṇāmi ikkaṁ jaï maha ēsā na rūsaē sahiyā
ēsa aüvvō vāhī na phiṭṭaē mantamēttēṇa // SurSuCa.18

aha kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ puṇa kōvassa kāraṇaṁ ēttha?
sāhēsu nivvisaṅkā vigamō vāhīē jaï hōi // SurSuCa.19

tō sirimaīē bhaṇiyaṁ jō sō cittammi vilihiō diṭṭhō
sō jaï navaraṁ vējjō vāhiṁ avaṇijja ēiē // SurSuCa.20

aha cittapaḍaṁ sahasā pasāriyaṁ pūiūṇa tō bhaṇaï
kumuiṇiyā! jaï ēvaṁ, tā ēyaṁ handi! vinnavaha // SurSuCa.21

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō savvahivi saharisaṁ samullaviyaṁ
ēvanti, pañjaliuḍā bhaṇiuṁ ēyaṁ samāḍhattā // SurSuCa.22

dakkhinnanihi! mahāyasa! cittaṭṭhiya! suṇasu amha viṇṇattiṁ
tuha daṁsaṇāō ēsā amha sahī āurā jāyā // SurSuCa.23


[p. 469]
tā taha karēsu sundara! jaha ēsā hōi vigayavāhīyā
guru mayaṇāmayasampīḍiyāṇa mahilāṇaṁ taṁ vijjō // SurSuCa.24

huṅkāraṁ mōttūṇaṁ tāhiṁ sakōvaṁ maē imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
māē! gahagahiyā iva kimasambaddhaṁ samullavaha? // SurSuCa.25

kiṁ vāvi acittēṇaṁ vinnaviēṇaṁ guṇō imēṇaṁ tu
cittagaō nahi katthavi kōvi hu uppāyaē vāhiṁ // SurSuCa.26

aha sirimaīē bhaṇiyaṁ tuha cittagaō imō hu jēṇēva
tēṇēva ya accittā vihiyā surasundari! tumanti // SurSuCa.27

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ tāhē saṇiyaṁ maē samullaviyaṁ
jaï ēyampi viyāṇasi tā kiṁ na sampāḍasi jhati? // SurSuCa.28

iya bhaṇiūya ahōmuhavayaṇā vilihāmi jāva mahivaṭṭhaṁ
tāva ya sahatthatālaṁ hasiuṁ tīē samullaviuṁ // SurSuCa.29


[p. 470]
sabbhāvasāhagēṇaṁ imēṇa vayaṇēṇaṁ rañjiyā suyaṇu!
tā taha karēmi sampaï jaha savvaṁ sōhaṇaṁ hōi // SurSuCa.30

iya bhaṇiuṁ cittapaḍaṁ gahiuṁ pāsammi sā gayā jhatti
maha jaṇaṇīē tattō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō // SurSuCa.31

cittapaḍavilihiō sō aṇaṅgarūvō payaṁsiō taruṇō
tīēvi gantuṁ rannō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō // SurSuCa.32

aha tāō taṁ cittaṁ palōiüṁ harisiō imaṁ bhaṇaï
sōhaṇaṭhāṇē rāgō sañjāō majjha dhūyāē // SurSuCa.33

ahavā na rāyahaṁsa mōttuṁ annattha ramaï varahaṁsī
tassēva varissāmō sāhiyavijjassa niyadhūyaṁ // SurSuCa.34

taha bhāṇuvēgakhayarō amha samīvammi ēi aṇavarayaṁ
tēṇēva varissāmō niyadhūyaṁ amarakēussa // SurSuCa.35


[p. 471]
iya naravaïṇā bhaṇiē pahasiyavayaṇāē majjha jaṇaṇīē
bhaṇiyā sirimaī gantuṁ sāhijjaü majjha dhūyāē // SurSuCa.36

mā surasundari! iṇhiṁ uvvēvaṁ kuṇasu niyayacittammi
siddhaṁ samīhiyaṁ tuha iya bhaṇiyā sirimaī tāhē // SurSuCa.37

majjha samīvē pattā siṭṭhō savvōvi puvvavuttantō
ahayampi harisiyamaṇā maṇayaṁ jāyā samāsatthā // SurSuCa.38

cintēmi kahaya hōhī taṁ diyahaṁ jattha sō maē sakkhā
daṭṭhavvō nayaṇucchavabhūō maṇavallahō lōō? // SurSuCa.39

tassaṅgamaāsāē sāhārantīē māṇasaṁ niyayaṁ
taṁ cēva cittakammaṁ ālihamāṇā ya aṇudiyahaṁ // SurSuCa.40

susiṇiddhasahijaṇēṇaṁ tappāvaṇasūyagēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ
jāva ya kaïvi diṇāī ṭhiyā ahaṁ saṇṭhavijjantā // SurSuCa.41


[p. 472]
tāvannammi diṇammī parihiyavaraṇāō camariyāhatthā
kayagōrōyaṇatilayā nāhiyasatthēsu nimmāyā // SurSuCa.42

parivāiyā u ēgā āsīvāyaṁ karēttu amhāṇaṁ
puraō uvavisiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiṁu samāḍhattā // SurSuCa.43

[yugmam]
jaharuiyaṁ uvabhujjaï iṭṭhaṁ rāmijjaē imaṁ sāraṁ
jamhā na kiñci vijjaï annaṁ ihalōgavaïrittaṁ // SurSuCa.44

siratuṇḍamuṇḍaṇāiṁ paralōgatthaṁ kuṇantu jē kēvi
tē varayā varadhuttēhi vañciyā visayasōkkhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.45

jamhā jīvapayatthō vijjaï annō na dēhavaïrittō
paccakkhapamāṇēṇaṁ aggahaṇā kharavisāṇaṁva // SurSuCa.46

paccakkhaṁ mōttūṇaṁ na ya annaṁ atthi iha pamāṇaṁ tu
santēvi pamāṇattē na sijjhaï tēṇa jīvotti // SurSuCa.47


[p. 473]
paccakkhapuvvagaṁ jaṁ aṇumāṇaṁ iha, na tēṇa taggahaṇaṁ
na ya vijjaï taggahaṇē liṅgampi aṇindiyattaṇaō // SurSuCa.48

lōyapavañcaṇahēuṁ dhuttēhiṁ kayāṇi vivihasatthāṇi
na pamāṇaṁ vibuhāṇaṁ kaha tēhiṁ bhavijja tassiddhī? // SurSuCa.49

tā pañcabhūyasamudayarūvō jīvō na tēsiṁ vigamammi
tassābhāvammi kuō paralōgō jēṇa ya tadatthaṁ // SurSuCa.50

kīraï aïduddharayaṁ bambhavvayasīlapālaṇāīyaṁ
mụ̄dhēhiṁ sayaṁ naṭṭhēhiṁ taha paraṁ nāsayantēhiṁ // SurSuCa.51

[yugmam]
gammāgammavibhāgaṁ mōttuṁ visayāṇa sēvaṇaṁ kuṇaha
bhakkhaha sarasaṁ maṁsaṁ piyaha suraṁ vigayaāsaṅkā // SurSuCa.52

iya tīē buddhilāē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa kugaïsañjaṇagaṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ maē ahammē! mā mā ēvaṁ samullavasu // SurSuCa.53


[p. 474]
vibuhajaṇanindaṇijjaṁ aviyāriyasundaraṁ ajuttīyaṁ
kō va sakannō ēyaṁ tuha bhaṇiyaṁ saddahējjāvi? // SurSuCa.54

jaṁ bhaṇasi natthi jīō annō dēhāō, aṇuvaṁlabhāō
tamasaṅgayamaccatthaṁ, jamhā jīvassa aggahaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.55

kiṁ tuha paccakkhēṇaṁ uyāhu nīsēsapurisavisaēṇaṁ?
na ya tāva paḍhamapakkhō vissābhāvappasaṅgāō // SurSuCa.56

jaṁ jaṁ tumaṁ na picchasi taṁ taṁ jaï natthi tā phuḍaṁ muddhē!
dēsantarakālantarabhāvāṇamabhāvayā pattā // SurSuCa.57

aha sayaladēsakālubbhavā narā nēya taṁ palōinti
ēyaṁ ca kaha ṇu najjaï durahigayā annacittā jaṁ? // SurSuCa.58

kiñca jo cciya imaṁ vigappaï tuha dēhē handi! natthi jīvotti
sōvi ya jīvō paralōgagāmiō nāṇaliṅgotti // SurSuCa.59


[p. 475]
paccakkhamēva ēgaṁ jaṁ ca pamāṇaṁ, na juttamēyampi
paccakkhaparōkkhāiṁ dunnēva jaō pamāṇāiṁ // SurSuCa.60

lōyapayāraṇahēuṁ iccāiṁ jamuttamahalamēyampi
rāgaddōsavimukkā savvannū savvalōgahiyā // SurSuCa.61

tēhi paṇīyaṁ satthaṁ tēsiṁ āṇāi jaṁ ca annēhiṁ
kaha taṁ dhuttapaṇīyattaṇēṇa hōjjāpamāṇanti? // SurSuCa.62

tammi ya bhaṇiō jīvō annabhavō tassa hōi paralōgō
tā pañcabhūyasamudayarūvō jīvō kahaṁ muddhē!? // SurSuCa.63

siddhammi ya paralōgō bambhavvayapālaṇāiṁ savvampi
tabbhaṇiyaṁ tā juttaṁ kāuṁ savvaṁ hiyatthīṇaṁ // SurSuCa.64

gammāgammavibhāgaṁ iccāiṁ jamuttamahalamēyampi
jiṇavayaṇanisiddhattā paralōē dukkhahēuttā // SurSuCa.65


[p. 476]
ēmāivivihajuttīhiṁ sā kayā takkhaṇaṁ niruttariyā
jāyā vilakkhavayaṇā asamatthā uttaraṁ dāuṁ // SurSuCa.66

aha pāsavattiṇīhiṁ avahasiyā sahīhiṁ sōluṇṭhaṁ
ṭakkaraṭumbayamuhamakkaḍāhiṁ bāḍhaṁ abhiddaviyā // SurSuCa.67

amha sahīē saddhiṁ ajjavi vāyaṁ karēsi dussīlē!
tā vaccasu saṭṭhāṇaṁ diṭṭhaṁ paṇḍiccayaṁ tujjha // SurSuCa.68

iya hasiyā sā ruṭṭhā phurantaaharā viṇiggayā tattō
ahamavi sahijaṇajuttā suhēṇa jā tattha acchēmi // SurSuCa.69

[yugmam]
tā annadiṇē rāyā samāgaō majjha māugēhammi
bhaṇiō ambāē kiṁ dīsaha cintāurā tubbhē? // SurSuCa.70

tāēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ sammaṁ hi viyāṇiyaṁ tumē dēvi!
nisuṇēsu kahijjantaṁ gurucintākāraṇaṁ jamiha // SurSuCa.71


[p. 477]
surasundarīē vuddhilanāmā parivāiyā jiyā vāē
jā puvvaṁ kila tīē paüṭṭhacitāē ālihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.72

surasundarīi rūvaṁ cittapaḍē tāhi taṁ gahēūṇaṁ
ujjēṇīē pattā sattuñjayanaravaïsamīvē // SurSuCa.73

[yugmam]
taṁ daṁsiya naravaïṇō vajjariya tīē duṭṭhahiyayāē
naravara! amhē puhaïṁ hiṇḍāmō tumha kajjēṇa // SurSuCa.74

jaṁ rayaṇaṁ puhaīē picchāmō taṁ ca tumha sāhēmō
kannārayaṇaṁ ēyaṁ kusagganayarē maē diṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.75

naravāhaṇassa rannā dhūyā surasundarī imā kannā
kō tīē niravasēsaṁ lihiuṁ sakkijja taṇurūvaṁ? // SurSuCa.76

aviya. 

savvaṁ ciya sō thērō jēṇēsā nimmiyā payāvaïṇā
kahamannahā na vihiyā suhakhāṇī attaṇō bhajjā? // SurSuCa.77


[p. 478]
ēyaṁ viṇimmiuṁ laḍaharūvatāruṇṇacārusōhaggaṁ
nūṇaṁ aïbahumāṇō viriciṇō āsi attāṇē // SurSuCa.78

dhaṇuhāyaḍḍhaṇakhinnaṁ mayaṇaṁ nāūṇa hiyayabhēyakarā
mannē vihiṇā vihiyā ēsā naṇu hatthabhallivva // SurSuCa.79

annaṁ ca jō imīē pāṇiggahaṇaṁ karissaī purisō
sō bharahaddhanarīsō hōhī purisō na sandēhō // SurSuCa.80

iya aïsayanāṇīhiṁ āiṭṭhaṁ tīi jammasamayammi
tā naravara! tuha jōggā sā kannā na uṇa annassa // SurSuCa.81

aha bahudaviṇaṁ dāuṁ pahaṭṭhavayaṇēṇa tēṇa sā rannā
bhaṇiyā bhayavaï! siṭṭhā jaṁ kannā sōhaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ // SurSuCa.82

ēyaṁ ca majjha sundari! siṭṭhaṁ savvampi cārapurisēhiṁ
aha tēṇa majjha pāsē paṭṭhaviō rayaṇacūḍotti // SurSuCa.83


[p. 479]
nāmēṇa niyayamantī tēṇa ya āgamma maggiō ahayaṁ
sattuñjayanaravaïṇō dijjaü surasundarī kannā // SurSuCa.84

[yugmam]
bhaṇiyō ya maē ēsō nēmittiyasumaïvayaṇaō bhadda!
hōhī khayarassa piyā tassēva ya tēṇa dāyavvā // SurSuCa.85

annaṁ, sō tuha sāmī thērō tā kintha tassa kannāē?
tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mā ēvaṁ bhaṇasu naranāha! // SurSuCa.86

guruāyarēṇa ahayaṁ paṭṭhaviō tēṇa dēsu niyadhūyaṁ
ēīē adāṇēṇaṁ picchāmi na sundaraṁ tumha // SurSuCa.87

tattō ya maē gāḍhaṁ kuddhēṇaṁ ērisaṁ samullaviyaṁ
tāva ya na dēmi dhūyaṁ jaṁ ruccaï taṁ kuṇējjāsu // SurSuCa.88

tā gacchasu niyapahuṇō sāhijja jahaṭṭhiyaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ
gihamāgayassa kō puṇa tuha daṇḍō kīraü iṇhiṁ? // SurSuCa.89


[p. 480]
aha tēṇa tattha gantuṁ kahiē sō niyabalēṇa gāraviō
ujjēṇīō caliō amhāṇaṁ uvari jattāē // SurSuCa.90

aviya. 

bahubhaḍanarindasandaṇapakkalapāikkacakkapariyariō
kharakhurakhayakhōṇīyalaasaṅkhatōkkhāralakkhajuō // SurSuCa.91

dappiyapayaṇḍaparahatthisatthavittāsaṇikkarasiēhiṁ
gurugirigaruyāgārēhiṁ saṅgaō bahugaïndēhiṁ // SurSuCa.92

sō sattuñjayarāyā gururōsō bhūrisinnasañjuttō
cārapurisēhiṁ siṭṭhaṁ sampattō amha dēsētti // SurSuCa.93

[tisr̥bhi - rviśēṣakam]
tā dēvi! nimittēṇaṁ imēṇa cintāurō ahaṁ jāō
ambāē taō bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama! kiṁ ēttha cintāē // SurSuCa.94

surasundariti bhaṇiuṁ dhūyā kaṇagāvalīē mayalēhā
dijjaü kayasaṁmāṇō saṭṭhāṇaṁ jēṇa sō jāi // SurSuCa.95


[p. 481]
iharā pabhūyasēnnō appabalāṇaṁ sa amha dēsassa
kāhī garuyamuvaddavamiya bhaṇiē rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.96

mantīhivi dēvī! imaṁ vimantiyaṁ āsi navari mantissa
maïsāgarassa ēsō na sundarō bhāviō mantō // SurSuCa.97

jaṁ tēṇa imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ āgacchaü tāva sō kusaggammi
iha āgayassa jamhā maraṇaṁ sē sumaïṇā siṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.98

annaṁ ca tassa rannō niggamaṇē āsi maṅgulā saüṇā
ajayāvahā ya savvē saṇiccharāī gahā dhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.99

iha āgayammi tammī vijaō amhaṁ parājaō tassa
tā dēva! nivvisaṅkā acchaha kiṁ annamantēṇa? // SurSuCa.100

rōhagasañjuttī uṇa kīraü gāmāvi tassa jē maggē
tē uvvasantu khippaṁ tiṇaghāsāī ya ujjhantu // SurSuCa.101


[p. 482]
ḍhakkijjaü kūvāī kujalāiṁ sarōvarāiṁ kīrantu
pasaranivāraṇahēuṁ sasāhaṇaṁ tattha vayaütti // SurSuCa.102

iya dēvi! mantivayaṇaṁ kāriya savvampi āgaō ēttha
pabalattaṇaō sattussa tahavi cintāurō jāō // SurSuCa.103

aha haṁsiṇi! jā kaïvi hu suhēṇa vaccati tattha divasāiṁ
tā annadiṇē nayaraṁ pavẹ̄dhiyaṁ sattusinnāē // SurSuCa.104

taō pihiāiṁ gōurāiṁ jalēṇa paripūriyāō parihāō
saṁnaddhabaddhakavayā païkavisīsaṁ ṭhiyā jōhā // SurSuCa.105

saṁvā(cā) rimajantāiṁ paüṇīkīranti, vivihasatthāiṁ
tikkhalijjanti tahā kīraï suhaḍāṇa sammāṇō // SurSuCa.106

padadiyahaṁ dijjanti ya ukkālā sattusinnamaïgamma
nivaḍanti suhaḍakarisurayanaravarā ubhayapakkhēvi // SurSuCa.107


[p. 483]
saṁsaïyā sāmantā nāyarayā āulā daḍhaṁ jāyā
kiṅkāyavvavimụ̄dhā jāyā taha mantiṇō amha // SurSuCa.108

bhīyā kāyarapurisā saṅgarakaraṇammiuddhurā suhaḍā
sāhasadhaṇō ya tāō sandhīraï sumaïvayaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.109

ēvaṁ haṁsiṇi! jāē samantaō āulammi nayarammi
aha annadiṇē ahayaṁ pāsuttā hammiyatalammi // SurSuCa.110

rayaṇīē kēṇāvi hu hīrantaṁ appayaṁ pulōittā
paḍibuddhā bhayabhīyā vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā // SurSuCa.111

hā ammi! tāya! kōvi hu dēvō vā nahayarō va maṁ haraï
dhāvaha dhāvaha suhaḍā! imāō mēllāvaha mamanti // SurSuCa.112

ēmāiṁ vilavamāṇā bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa suyaṇu! mā bhāhi
nō tujjha kiñci virūvaṁ karēmi pāṇappiyā taṁ si // SurSuCa.113


[p. 484]
tuha rūvadaṁsaṇuppannagaruyaaṇurāyaparavasēṇa maē
hariyā si kīsa sundari! bhayabhīyā ēvamullavasi? // SurSuCa.114

vēyaḍḍhanaganivāsī khayarō haṁ suyaṇu! mayarakēutti
bhuñjihisi maē saddhiṁ bhōē kiṁ ruyasi uvviggā? // SurSuCa.115

ēyaṁ ca tassa vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyā ahaṁ cittē
kiṁ nāma majjha daïō ēsō sō mayarakēutti? // SurSuCa.116

bhāyā piyaṁvayāē jassa tayā cittavilēhiyaṁ rūvaṁ
daṭhṭhūṇa mayaṇavasagā jāyā ummattiyā ahavā // SurSuCa.117

sō ajjavi vijjāō sāhaï tā āgamō kaha ṇu tassa?
kaha maha ittiyapunnā jaṁ sō dīsijja paccakkhaṁ? // SurSuCa.118

ēmāiṁ cintayantī nīyā haṁ tēṇa katthavi paēsē
ōinnā bhūmīē mukkā haṁ kayaligahaṇammi // SurSuCa.119


[p. 485]
ētthantarammi rayaṇī khayaṁ gayā sāhiuṁva paramatthaṁ
sammaṁ niyaccha vacchē! na hōi sō vallahō ēsa // SurSuCa.120

jāē pabhāyasamaē diṭṭhō sō sāmalēṇa dēhēṇa
tattō gurusōgāē vicintiyaṁ hā! na sō ēsō // SurSuCa.121

sō tattakañcaṇanibhō rūvēṇa aṇaṅgarūvasāricchō
cittagaēṇa imassa jō sāricchaṁ natthi thēvampi // SurSuCa.122

tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ saraṇavihūṇā paravvasā ahayaṁ
iya cintatīē tayā bhaēṇa kampō samuppannō // SurSuCa.123

aha sō daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ aṁsujalāsārasittagaṇḍayalaṁ
bhayabhīyaṁ kampantiṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō // SurSuCa.124

kiṁ suyaṇu! tumaṁ bīhasi bhūyapisāuttisaṅkirī majjha
nisuṇasu jō haṁ jēṇa va hariyā kajjēṇa ya mayacchi! // SurSuCa.125


[p. 486]
vēyaḍ̣dhē varanayaraṁ gaṅgāvattanti atthi suprasiddhaṁ
tattha ya rāyā sirigandhavāhaṇō āsi vikkhāō // SurSuCa.126

mayaṇāvalīdēvīē taṇaō nahavāhaṇotti sē āsi
bīō ya mayarakēū taïō puṇa mēhanāutti // SurSuCa.127

nahavāhaṇōvi sāhiyavijjō aha jōvvaṇaṁ tu sampattō
variyā ya tannimittaṁ varakannā kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.128

sā uṇa vivāhasamaē vijjāharacittavēganāmēṇa
avahariuṁ pariṇīyā ruṭṭhō ēsō taō tassa // SurSuCa.129

aṇumaggaṁ gantūṇaṁ baddhō sō nāgiṇīē vijjāē
gahiūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ samāgaō niyayanayarammi // SurSuCa.130

tattō vijjācchēō jāō nahavāhaṇassa jēṇēsō
mahilāsamēyavijjāharassa jāō 'vagāritti // SurSuCa.131


[p. 487]
cirapariciyadēvēṇaṁ dinnāō cittavēgakhayarassa
vijjāō tēṇa jāō vijjāharacakkavaṭṭī sē // SurSuCa.132

sayamēva nahayarindā savvēvi hu paṇaïmuvagayā tasya
iya muṇiuṁ maha jaṇaō saṁviggō bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.133

picchaha bhō! maṇuyāṇaṁ maṇōrahā annahā visaḍḍhanti
vihiṇō vasēṇa navaraṁ annaha kajjāṇa pariṇāmō // SurSuCa.134

kira niyataṇayaṁ kāuṁ vijjāharacakkavaṭṭiṇaṁ, karihī
kayakiccō pavvajjaṁ kēvalijaṇayassa pāsammi // SurSuCa.135

taṁ puṇa annaha jāyaṁ tā kiṁ kajjaṁ imēṇa rajjēṇaṁ
narayāinimittēṇaṁ, sēvāmō tāyapayajuyalaṁ // SurSuCa.136

jaō. 

saṁsārō hu asārō ghōrā aïdāruṇā ya narayammi!
dusahāō viyaṇāō cittō kammāṇa pariṇāmō // SurSuCa.137


[p. 488]
cavalō indiyagāmō rāgaddōsā ya dujjayā lōē
aṇavaṭṭhiyaṁ ca cittaṁ kimpāgaphalōvamā visayā // SurSuCa.138

aïdusahō piyavirahō bammahalaliyaṁ vivāyakaḍuyanti
narayapuravattiṇīō sēvijjantāō juvaīō // SurSuCa.139

kusasūivisamasaṇṭhiyapavaṇāhayasalilacañcalaṁ jīyaṁ
sāmannaṁ savvēsiṁ maraṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ saṁsārē // SurSuCa.140

vañcaṇaparā ya jīvā duṭṭhakasāēhiṁ tāviō lōō
asuhaphalō gharavāsō maṇuyattaṁ taha ya nō sulahaṁ // SurSuCa.141

dulahā dhammammi maī bahuvigghasamāulaṁ ahōrattaṁ
payaīē calā lacchī pēmmaṁ suviṇōvamaṁ lōē // SurSuCa.142

āriyakhēttāīyā aïdulahā sampayā ya jiyalōē
aïdāruṇamannāṇaṁ jīvā micchattavāmụ̄dhā // SurSuCa.143


[p. 489]
parihāyantā bhāvā dhammē aïnindiō pamāutti
khijjaï taṇusāmatthaṁ āuyamavi thōvayaṁ hōi // SurSuCa.144

kiṁ bahuṇā?

nārayatiriyanarā 'maragaīsu gurudusahadukkhataviyāṇa
mōttūṇaṁ jiṇadhammaṁ jiyāṇa saraṇaṁ jaō nannaṁ // SurSuCa.145

tamhā tāyasamīvaṁ gantuṁ sahalīkarēmi maṇuyattaṁ
nahavāhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ahamavi tāyamaṇugamissaṁ // SurSuCa.146

jaō. 

sāmittaṁ kāūṇaṁ āṇāniddēsakāragassāvi
kaha sēvaṁ kāhāmō sampaï bhiccassa niyayassa? // SurSuCa.147

bhaṇiyaṁ tāēṇa taō kāyavvamimaṁ vivēyajuttāṇaṁ
tattō niyasuyasahiō takkāluciyaṁ karēūṇa // SurSuCa.148

suravāhaṇakēvaliṇō mūlē kāūṇa nimmalacarittaṁ
niṭṭhaviyaaṭṭhakammō antagaḍō kēvalī jāō // SurSuCa.149

[yugmam]

[p. 490]
aha cittavēgakhayarāhivēṇa tatthēva niyayanayarammi
dāuṁ sadēsakhaṇḍaṁ ahisittō khayararāyā haṁ // SurSuCa.150

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē kāraṇavasēṇa kēṇaï pabhāyasamayammi
niyanayarā ēgāgī caliō haṁ rayaṇadīvammi // SurSuCa.151

nahapaṭṭhiēṇa diṭṭhā sundari! hammiyatalammi pāsuttā
taṁ si taō avahariyā mēttalasarasalliēṇa maē // SurSuCa.152

tā mā rōvasu sundari! pāṇāṇavi sāmiṇī tumaṁ majjha
bhuñjihisi maē saddhiṁ bhōē vēyaḍḍhasēlammi // SurSuCa.153

tavvayaṇaṁ sōuṇaṁ vajjēṇava tāḍiyā sudukkhattā
iya cintiuṁ payattā hāhā! maha pāvapasarassa // SurSuCa.154

majjha kaēṇaṁ tāō pāraddhō garuyasattuṇā tāva
ahamavi imēṇa hariyā annattha nibaddharāgāvi // SurSuCa.155


[p. 491]
dhā! maha! jīēṇaṁ na tāyaāsāsaṇaṁ na piyalābhō
sattuñjayadinnāē hōjja suhī tāva tāōvi // SurSuCa.156

maṇavallahassa tassa u lābhēṇa havijja ahava suhiyā haṁ
maha pāvapariṇaīē ēttō ēkkampi nō jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.157

ēvaṁ vicintayantī bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa tāva ētthēva
ciṭṭhaü tumaṁ jāva ahaṁ āsannē vaṁsigahaṇāmmi // SurSuCa.158

gantūṇaṁ vijjāē pannattīē lahuṁ payacchāmi
jāvasahassamēttaṁ pārambhiyapuvvasēvāē // SurSuCa.159

[yugmam]
iya bhaṇiūṇa gaō sō ahamavi gurusōyatāviyā tattha
kiṅkāyavvamụ̄dhā saraṇavihūṇā bhayuppitthā // SurSuCa.160

hariṇivva jūhabhaṭṭhā sataralatāraṁ disāō pulayantī
aṁsujalapunnanayaṇā ruyamāṇī jāva ciṭṭhāmi // SurSuCa.161


[p. 492]
tāva ya tatthāsannaṁ picchāmi visālasālasōhillaṁ
pavaṇākampiyaphalabharavinamiyaguñjōhasaṅkinnaṁ // SurSuCa.162

maṇahariphalaṁ pasarantaparimalaṁ bahalapattalacchāyaṁ
tapphalabhakkhaṇanivaḍantajantusantāṇakayasadda // SurSuCa.163

nivaḍantasasantataḍapphaḍantamayavihagakaliyabhūvīḍhaṁ
taruyaramuccaṁ maccuṁ jantusantāṇanāsayaraṁ // SurSuCa.164

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
taṁ daṭṭhuṁ visarukkhaṁ vicintiyaṁ garuyadukkhataviyāē
piyasahi! haṁsiṇi! taïyā maraṇammi nibaddhacittāē // SurSuCa.165

kiṁ kāhāmi ahannā rahiyā piyabandhujaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ
vihiṇā viḍambiyā haṁ jīvantī iya vicintēntī // SurSuCa.166

gantuṁ tassa samīvē gahiūṇa phalaṁ muhammi pakkhittaṁ
mā maha havijja ērisaviḍambaṇā annajammēvi // SurSuCa.167


[p. 493]
iya bhaṇiūṇa sasōyaṁ khaṇantaraṁ jāva tattha acchāmi
tāva ya guruvisaviyaṇāē vibbhalā mahiyalē paḍiyā // SurSuCa.168

[tisr̥bhiḥ kulakam]
taō bhamiyaṁva vaṇatarūhiṁ uvvattiyayaṁva sayalavasuhāē
sandhīhiṁ vihaḍiyaṁ piva visīiyaṁ savvaaṅgēhiṁ // SurSuCa.169

tattō ya akahaṇīyaṁ pāviyavatthantaraṁ tayā bhaddē!
jāṇāmi nēva kiñcivi taduttaraṁ jaṁ mahaṁ jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.170

kēvalamucchaṅgagayaṁ kassavi taruṇassa amayabhūyassa
visanivvavaṇasamatthaṁ maṇisalilaṁ pāyayantassa // SurSuCa.171

khaṇamēttaṁ tēna ciya majjha sarīraṁ pasiñcamāṇassa
sayamaṅgāiṁ kōmalakarēhiṁ parimaddayantassa // SurSuCa.172

jalasittatālavēṇṭayahatthāē vihiyasisiravāyāē
ciradiṭṭhaṁ piyasahīē piyaṁvayāē kahijjantaṁ // SurSuCa.173


[p. 494]
sayalaṁ maha vuttantaṁ cittapaḍālōyaṇāipajjantaṁ
harisabharapulaïyaṅgaṁ khaṇantaraṁ nisuṇamāṇassa // SurSuCa.174

appāṇaṁ pāsittā paṇaṭṭhavisavēyaṇā samāsatthā
sumiṇaṁva mannamāṇā paḍibuddhā haṁsiē! taïyā // SurSuCa.175

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
ummīliyanayaṇajuyā tāva ya pēcchāmi mayaṇapaḍirūvaṁ
mahahiyayaniggayaṁ piva taruṇanaraṁ cittasaṁvāiṁ // SurSuCa.176

taṁ daṭṭhu cintiyaṁ mē kiṁ mannē indajālamēyanti?
kiṁ vāvi annajammō uyāhu kiṁ suviṇayaṁ ēyaṁ? // SurSuCa.177

kiṁvā maïsaṁmōhō kiṁvāvi hu saccamēva ēyanti?
ahavā nahi nahi ēyaṁ kattō maha ittiyā punnā? // SurSuCa.178

jaṁ sō maṇavallahaō dīsijja jaṇō imēhiṁ nayaṇēhiṁ
jaṁ sē ucchaṅgagayā imassa puṇa sambhavō kattha? // SurSuCa.179


[p. 495]
ēvaṁ vicintayantī piyaṁvayāē imaṁ samullaviyā
surasundari! kiṁ ajjavi uvvuṇṇamuhivva pulaēsi? // SurSuCa.180

ēsō hu rayaṇadīvō bhagiṇī ya piyaṁvayā ahaṁ tujjha
sāhiyavijjō ēsō maha bhāyā mayarakēutti // SurSuCa.181

ēvaṁ ca tīē bhaṇiē ēsōcciya sotti harisiyā cittē
sajjhasavēviradēhā saṅkinnarasantaraṁ pattā // SurSuCa.182

uṭṭhēttu tadaṅkāō piyaṁvayāē samīvamallīṇā
addhacchipēcchiēhiṁ pēcchittā taṁ apēcchantaṁ // SurSuCa.183

ētthantarammi ēgō khayarō āgamma bhaṇaï kayaviṇaō
jiṇapūyāē vēlā samaïcchaï kumara! uṭṭhēha // SurSuCa.184

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ piyaṁvayaṁ ṭhāviuṇa maha pāsē
kaïvayapurisamēō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ pāviō ēsō // SurSuCa.185


[p. 496]
tāva ya piyaṁvayāē puṭṭhā kaha suyaṇu! ēttha taṁ pattā
bhūmīcaramaṇuyāṇaṁ suduggamē rayaṇadīvammi? // SurSuCa.186

kīsa va visamuvabhuñjiya appā vasaṇammi pāḍiō bhīmē?
tattō ya maē tīē puvvuttaṁ sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.187

aha sāvi maē puṭṭhā cittapaḍaṁ appiūṇamamhāṇaṁ
taïyā kattha gayā taṁ kiṁvā aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ tumaē? // SurSuCa.188

kaha vā uvabhuttavisā bhīmaarannammi pāviyā ahayaṁ?
kaha vā duṭṭhampi visaṁ khaṇēṇa dēhāō avaṇīyaṁ? // SurSuCa.189

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē cittapaḍaṁ appiūṇa tumhāṇa
vēgēṇa ahaṁ pattā imammi vararayaṇadīvammi // SurSuCa.190

diṭṭhō ya mayarakēū kaïvayaniyapariyaṇēṇa sañjuttō
bhāusiṇēhēṇa ṭhiyā kaïvayadivasāṇi ahamēttha // SurSuCa.191


[p. 497]
ētthāgayatāēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā haṁ putti! ciṭṭhasu ihēva
hōsu paḍicārigā iha tāva tumaṁ mayarakēussa // SurSuCa.192

jaṁ āṇavēi tāutti jampiyaṁ tāhē ēttha dīvammi
vijjapasāhaṇujjayabhāusamīvē ṭhiyā suyaṇu! // SurSuCa.193

nāuṁ vijjāsiddhiṁ bahuvihakhayarēhiṁ sañjuō tāō
aṭṭhāhiyānimittaṁ samāgaō ēttha dīvammi // SurSuCa.194

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ jiṇindamahimaṁ karēttu vijjāō
sampūiya jahavihiṇā saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.195

pūittu pūyaṇīē dāṇaṁ dāūṇa khayaralōyassa
varanaṭṭagīyavāiyakaliyaṁ aṭṭhāhiyaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.196

ajjēva nisāviramē sampattō rayaṇasañcayaṁ tāō
kāyavvasēsakiccō ṭhiō ihaṁ mayarakēūvi // SurSuCa.197

[tisr̥bhi - rviśēṣakam]

[p. 498]
kāuṁ pabhāyakiccaṁ sarīracintāē niggaō ajja
vaṁsikuḍaṅgāsannē diṭṭhaṁ ca pahāṇakaravālaṁ // SurSuCa.198

gahiūṇa kōugēṇaṁ jamajīhāsacchahaṁ tayaṁ khaggaṁ
taruṇatamāladalābhaṁ phurantadhārāsuduppicchaṁ // SurSuCa.199

āsannakuḍaṅgīē chēyaparicchākaēṇa sahasatti
dāuṁ ēgapahāraṁ chinnā sā vaṁsajālitti // SurSuCa.200

[yugmam]
aha thūlamuttiyāvalipariyattaṇakhaṇiyavāmahatthassa
vijjāparijavaṇaniruddhanāsiyānimiyanayaṇassa // SurSuCa.201

tammajjhadēsaparisaṇṭhiyassa vijjāpasāhaṇarayassa
vijjāharassa kassavi maṇikuṇḍalabhūsiyakavōlaṁ // SurSuCa.202

sahasatti uttimaṅgaṁ nivaḍantaṁ picchiūṇa mahivaḍ̣dhē
sañjāyasajjhasēṇaṁ nirūviyaṁ hā! kimēyanti? // SurSuCa.203

[tisr̥bhi-rviśēṣakam]

[p. 499]
pulayantēṇa ya nāyaṁ ēsō sō mayarakēunāmotti
sāmī gaṅgāvattassa gandhavāhaṇanarindasuō // SurSuCa.204

avvō! pamāyavasaō kaha varaō māriō niravarāhō?
dhī! dhī! annāṇassa u niratthayaṁ pāvamāyariyaṁ // SurSuCa.205

ēmāi cintayantō puṇō puṇō appayaṁ ca nindantō
jā vayaï thōvabhūmiṁ tā phuriyaṁ dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.206

kiṁ mannē maha sūyaï sunimittamimanti cintaï jāva
tāva visarukkhamūlē diṭṭhā taṁ nivaḍiyā suyaṇu! // SurSuCa.207

maṇaharasayalāvayavaṁ miyaṅkalēhavva jaṇamaṇāṇandaṁ
daṭhṭhūṇa tumaṁ sundari! sittō amaēṇava kumārō // SurSuCa.208

avvō! kaha ṇu mayāvi hu āṇandaṁ dēi majjha hiyayassa?
piyapaṇayiṇivva ēsā juvaī navajōvvaṇārambhā // SurSuCa.209


[p. 500]
tā kiṁ imā mayacciya kiṁvā sajiyatti jāva pulaēi
tāva ya tuhamuhasaṇṭhiyavisaphalakhaṇḍēṇa vinnāyaṁ // SurSuCa.210

aïtivvavisaviyārā jāyā ō acēyaṇā imā bālā
tō nēūṇa saṭṭhāṇaṁ karēmi ēīi tēgicchaṁ // SurSuCa.211

iya cintiya surasundari! gahiūṇa tumaṁ samāgaō ēttha
siṭṭhō puvvuddiṭṭhō vuttantō tēṇa maha savvō // SurSuCa.212

bhaṇiyā ya ahamimēṇaṁ ̣dhōēsuṁ tamaṅgulīyayaṁ sigghaṁ
vijjāpayāṇasamaē tāēṇa samappiyaṁ jaṁ tu // SurSuCa.213

taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasarassa
uvaladdhapaccayaṁ puṇa visēsaō visasamūhammi // SurSuCa.214

[yugmam]
bhaṇiyā khayarakumārā pūyāsāmaggiyaṁ lahuṁ kuṇaha
ēyaṁ paüṇīkāuṁ jiṇapūyaṁ tāhi kāūṇa // SurSuCa.215


[p. 501]
kāhāmi santikammaṁ vigdhajayaṭṭhā ya mantajāvaṁ ca
vijjāharavāyāyaṇapāvavisuddhiṁ samicchantō // SurSuCa.216

[yugmam]
ētthantarammi ya maē samappiyaṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ tassa
tassalilapāṇavihiṇā kayā pasatthā tumaṁ suyaṇu! // SurSuCa.217

jāva ya imassa puraō cittapaḍālōyaṇāivuttantaṁ
sāhēmi tāva sundari! uvaladdhā cēyaṇā tumaē // SurSuCa.218

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ maē ēyaṁ
tā surasundari! siddhaṁ samīhiyaṁ tujjha savvampi // SurSuCa.219

ahavā. 

dīvantaraṭhiyampi hu jalanihimajjhāō dūradēsāō
āṇittu ghaḍēi vihī aṇukūlō iṭṭhalōyanti // SurSuCa.220

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu nisuṇēsu
majjha kaēṇaṁ tāō acchaï gurusattupāraddhō // SurSuCa.221


[p. 502]
piyadaṁsaṇēvi jāē ajjavi sōgāuraṁ daḍhaṁ hiyayaṁ
piyasahi! maha santāvō tēṇajjavi bāhaē dēhaṁ // SurSuCa.222

sattuñjayapāraddhō vaṭṭaï pāṇāṇa saṁsaē tāō
tā kaha aṇukūlattaṁ vihiṇō maha mandabhāgāē? // SurSuCa.223

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ haṁsiṇi! sōgāvēgāō rōumāraddhā
tāva ya kayakāyavvō samāgaō tīē sō bhāyā // SurSuCa.224

bhaṇiyā ya tēṇa kimiyaṁ piyaṁvaē! ruyaï tujjha piyabhagiṇī
tīēvi savvaṁ sōyassa kāraṇaṁ tassa akkhāyaṁ // SurSuCa.225

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! mā rūya avassamajjēva
gantuṁ kayantavayaṇaṁ nayāmi tuha jaṇayapaḍivakkhaṁ // SurSuCa.226

jīvantē maï sundari! kō tuha jaṇayaṁ parābhavējjati?
tā gacchissaṁ sampaï bāhusahāō ahaṁ tattha // SurSuCa.227


[p. 503]
ētthēva paḍhamajinavarabhavaṇammi piyaṁvayāsamēyāē
acchēyavvaṁ tumaē jahāsuhaṁ sōyarahiyāē // SurSuCa.228

jāvāgacchāmi ahaṁ hantuṁ sattuñjayaṁ durāyāraṁ
iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō gayaṇaṁ vasunandakhaggakarō // SurSuCa.229

sahiyā piyaṁvayāē tatthēva ṭhiyā ahampi taddivasaṁ
cintēntī tassēva ya samāgamaṁ garuyaaṇurāyā // SurSuCa.230

kiṁ ajjavi maṇadaïō sahasā hantūṇa taṁ durāyāraṁ
vijjāpayāvakaliōvi āgaō nēya sō jhatti // SurSuCa.231

vōlīṇammi ya divasē rayaṇiṁ savvampi bhagiṇisahiyā haṁ
kiṁ puṇa na āgaō sotti jāva ciṭṭhāmi uvviggā // SurSuCa.232

tāva ya kharapharusagiraṁ tajjitō bhīsaṇō sarūvēṇa
niddhūmasihisihāvalipiṅgaladhammillavikarālō // SurSuCa.233


[p. 504]
jiyadasaṇacchayadasaṇō karagganarasirapaṇaccaṇikkaraō
marukūvavivarasarisā ' 'piṅgalalōyaṇasuduppicchō // SurSuCa.234

galatalavilaïyakhalakhalakhalintanaramuṇḍamāliyākaliō
taḍipuñjujjalacañcalanillāliyadīhajīhālō // SurSuCa.235

bhīmaṭṭahāsapaḍiravaüttāsiyasayalasattasaṅghāō
kasiṇō vigarālamuhō vēyālō āgaō tattha // SurSuCa.236

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
ā pāvē! jaṁ taïyā parapurisāsattamāṇasāē tumē
parajuvaïlōluēṇaṁ tēṇa ya pāviṭṭhapurisēṇa // SurSuCa.237

maha vihiyaṁ gurudukkhaṁ tassa phalaṁ tēṇa pāviyaṁ tāva
iṇhiṁ tumampi pāvasu niyaciṭṭhiyasacchahaṁ phalanti // SurSuCa.238

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇō sō haṁsiṇi! ghittuṁ mamaṁ bhayuppitthaṁ
uppaïō gayaṇēṇaṁ niṭṭharavayaṇēhiṁ tajjētō // SurSuCa.239

[tisr̥bhi kulakam]

[p. 505]
maha aṇumaggavilaggaṁ akkōsintiṁ piyaṁvayaṁ sahasā
kāuṁ gayajīviyaṁ piva bhīsaṇahuṅkārakaraṇēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.240

nēūṇa dūradēsaṁ mukkā gayaṇāō tēṇa pāvēṇa
sañcunniyaṅguvaṅgā nūṇaṁ maraütti buddhīē // SurSuCa.241

[yugmam]
daïvavasēṇa ya paḍiyā layāviyāṇammi tammi ujjāṇē
diṭṭhā samantabhaddēṇa tāhi puṭṭhā ya vuttantaṁ // SurSuCa.242

kiṁ indayālamēyaṁ kiṁvā sumiṇanti kattha vā pattā
kattha gaō vēyālō piyaṁvayāē ya kiṁ jāyaṁ? // SurSuCa.243

maṇavallahassa imiṇā havējja vihiyaṁ asōhaṇaṁ kiñci
mannē tēṇēva lahuṁ na āgaō tammi sō dīvē // SurSuCa.244

kiṁvā majjha nimittaṁ samāgaēṇaṁ havijja vihiyaṁ tu
sattuñjayanaravaïṇā thōvabalassēha tāyassa? // SurSuCa.245


[p. 506]
ēmāi cintayantīi tāhiṁ gurusōyatāviyāē maē
pucchantassavi siṭṭhaṁ samantabhaddassa nō kiñci // SurSuCa.246

tattō ya āṇiyā haṁ bhūvaïpuraō samantabhaddēṇa
sajjhasasōēhiṁ tahimpi tārisaṁ kiñci nō kahiyaṁ // SurSuCa.247

iya payaḍiyaṁ gujjhaṁ nēhasārāi tujjhaṁ niyacariyamēvaṁ haṁsiē! savvamēyaṁ
aïgaruyasiṇēhā sāhiyaṁ vittharēṇaṁ paṇayaparavasāē pucchiyaṁ jaṁ taïtti // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisahapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï surasundariharaṇavannaṇō nāma
surasundarīkahāē bārasamō varaparicchēō // SurSuCa.250
