[p. 507]
[trayōdaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha haṁsiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ avvō! aïdūsahaṁ samaṇubhūyaṁ
jaṁ kila nisuṇantāṇavi uppajjaï garuyaüvvēvō // SurSuCa.1

ēvaṁvihadukkhāṇaṁ na ya uciyā hōsi piyasahi! tumanti
kiṁ puṇa kīraï vihiṇō vicittacariyassa lōyammi? // SurSuCa.2

niccaṁ suhōciyampi hu bahuvihadukkhāṇa kuṇaï āvāsaṁ
addiṭṭhaïṭṭhavirahampi virahiyaṁ kuṇaï daïēṇa // SurSuCa.3

iya surasundari! vihiṇō vicittayaṁ jāṇiūṇa uvvēvaṁ
thēvampi hu mā kāhisi, kō ṇu guṇō tassa karaṇēvi // SurSuCa.4

annaṁ ca jārisāiṁ tuha dēhē lakkhaṇāiṁ dīsanti
taha hōyavvaṁ tumaē vijjāhararāyapattīē // SurSuCa.5


[p. 508]
annaṁ ca maēvi suyaṁ kusagganayarāō āgayanarēṇa
kamalāvaïdēvīē puraō ēvaṁ kahijjantaṁ // SurSuCa.6

sattuñjayanaravaïṇā ruddhē nayarammi āulē lōē
nahavāhaṇanaranāhē saṁsaïbhūē sasāmantē // SurSuCa.7

ghāsindhaṇahāṇīē kicchēṇacchantayammi puralōē
jantavimukkamahōvalanihāyanivaḍantapāyārē // SurSuCa.8

paṭaüḍivivarasaṇṭhiyakōddāligakhayapaḍantakhaṇḍīsu
dhaṇusu(mu)haviṇiggayāṇēyapattipacchāiyanahaggē // SurSuCa.9

iya nayarammi kusaggē nivaḍantabhaḍōharuhiracikkhallē
sahasā phurantakhaggō samāgaō khēyarō ēgō // SurSuCa.10

tēṇa ya gaïndaparisaṇṭhiyassa sattuñjayassa khaggēṇa
sahasā sīsaṁ chinnaṁ phurantarōsāruṇacchēṇa // SurSuCa.11


[p. 509]
hantūṇa ya taṁ sattuṁ rannō naravāhaṇassa pāsammi
āgamma tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nihaō sattū tuha narinda! // SurSuCa.12

vijjāharahariyāē rayaṇaddīvē ṭhiyāē dhūyāē
tujjha surasundarīē vayaṇāō āgaō ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.13

siricittavēgataṇaō khayarō haṁ mayarakēunāmotti
pāsē piyaṁvayāē tuha dhūyā acchaï suhēṇa // SurSuCa.14

iya bhaṇiūṇa gaō sō rannā uṇa harisiēṇa niggantuṁ
sabalēṇa sattusinnē palāyamāṇammi pahurahiē // SurSuCa.15

gayarahaturaṅgamāiṁ gahiyaṁ savvampi davvasāraṁ sē
tā surasundari! piyasahi! tatthatthē kuṇasu mā cintaṁ // SurSuCa.16

[yugmam]
jamhā sō tuha jaṇaō tujjha piēṇēva nibbhaō vihiō
ahiṇavasāhiyavijjassa tassa kiṁ kāhii pisāō? // SurSuCa.17


[p. 510]
jāyaṁ havijja aha kāraṇantaraṁ kimpi tujjha daïyassa
tavvasaō sō piyasahi! na āgaō jhatti taṁ dīvaṁ // SurSuCa.18

ēmāiniuṇavayaṇēhiṁ tīē āsāsiyā narindasuyā
jāyā vimukkagurusōgavēgiyā ' 'ṇandapaḍihatthā // SurSuCa.19

aha haṁsiyāē savvaṁ gantuṁ kamalāvaīē dēvīē
siṭṭhaṁ tīēvi rannō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.20

surasundarīē ēvaṁ piubhagiṇinikēyaṇē vasantīē
antēuravilayāṇaṁ alamāṇandaṁ jaṇantīē // SurSuCa.21

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ suhēṇa jā kaïvi, tāva annadiṇē
abbhintaraparisāē kaïvayaniyapurisasahiyassa // SurSuCa.22

surasundarisahiyāē dēvīē saṅgayassa naravaïṇō
paḍihāraaṇunnāō rannō aïvallahō vaṇiō // SurSuCa.23


[p. 511]
bhāsurarayaṇasupūriyathālakarō āgaō kayapaṇāmō
dhaṇadēvō nāmēṇaṁ uvaviṭṭhō rāiṇō puraō // SurSuCa.24

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
uvaṇīyadarisaṇīyō sasambhamēṇēva rāiṇā bhaṇiō
bhō bhō dhaṇadēva! tumaṁ āsi gaō siṁhaladdīvaṁ // SurSuCa.25

tā kaha ṇu lahu niyattō kusalaṁ pōyassa kiñci nō jāyaṁ
jāyaṁ vigghaṁ jēṇiha samāgaō māsamēttēṇa? // SurSuCa.26

bahudivasapāvaṇijjē tammi gaō siṁhalammi dīvammi
sigghaṁ jaṁ si niyattō mahantamacchērayaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.27

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ āyannasu naravarinda! vuttantaṁ
jaha tattha gaō sigghaṁ samāgaō ēttha nayarammi // SurSuCa.28

siṅghaladīvāgayavāṇiēhiṁ pōcchāhiō iō tāva
caliō taduciyabhaṇḍaṁ ghittūṇa bahuppagāramahaṁ // SurSuCa.29


[p. 512]
tumhāṇa pāyajuyalaṁ paṇamiya bahusayaḍasatthasañjuttō
gambhīranāmayaṁ taṁ pattō vēlāulaṁ viulaṁ // SurSuCa.30

[yugmam]
aviya nāviyajaṇapaḍipunnaṁ paüṇīkīrantajāṇavattō haṁ
pūgaphalanāliērāirāsirēhantarāyapahaṁ // SurSuCa.31

gayadantapālikaliyaṁ gayavaïvayaṇaṁva katthaï vibhāi
katthaï kappūrāgurucandaṇasahiyaṁ suragirivva // SurSuCa.32

muttāhāravirāiyamahīvīḍhaṁ puṇḍarīyasiharaṁva
katthaï jāiphalēlākaliyaṁ taṁ kāmuyamuhaṁva // SurSuCa.33

nāṇādēsasamāgayabhūrikaraniruddhasayaladisipakkhaṁ
pavisantabhūribhaṇḍaṁ naravaïbhavaṇaṁva taṁ diṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.34

dāuṁ taduciyasuṅkaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ nīyaṁ samuddatīrammi
naïnāhagamaṇadacchaṁ bōhitthaṁ bhāḍiyaṁ viyaḍaṁ // SurSuCa.35


[p. 513]
kamasō ya sayalabhaṇḍaṁ caḍāviyaṁ jāhi tattha bōhitthē
tāhē suhatihirikkhē naïnāhē pūiē vihiṇā // SurSuCa.36

kāuṁ jiṇindapūyaṁ dāṇaṁ dāūṇa samaṇasaṅghassa
āpucchiya suhinivahaṁ sambhāsiya sayalaparivāraṁ // SurSuCa.37

kīrantamaṅgalaravē samucchalantē ya tūranigghōsē
paḍumāgahasandōhē jayajayasaddaṁ paüñjantē // SurSuCa.38

pihupattāsayamayalaṁ guṇaniyaranibaddhaphalahasaṅghāyaṁ
sañjamiyasayajōgaṁ bōhitthaṁ muṇivarasaricchaṁ // SurSuCa.39

ārụ̄dhō haṁ tattō vēlāē samāgayāē gahirāē
pavaṇapaḍipunnasiyavaḍavasēṇaṁ gantuṁ payaṭṭaṁ taṁ // SurSuCa.40

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
parihatthamacchapuñchacchaḍaacchōḍaṇapōcchalantasalilōhaṁ
salilōhasamucchāiyaphurantagirigaḍayabhīsaṇayaṁ // SurSuCa.41


[p. 514]
bhīsaṇamagarōvaggiyabhuyagagasijjantagōhiyānivahaṁ
nivahaparisaṇṭhiyuṭṭhiyatimiṅgilāḍhattaāvattaṁ // SurSuCa.42

āvattasamuvvattiyasattasamāḍhattabhīsaṇārāvaṁ
ārāvavasavisaṇṭhulajalayaraparisaraṇaghōrajalaṁ // SurSuCa.43

ghōrajalaghaṇaghaṇāravamuhariyadisicakkamukkaḍataraṅgaṁ
raṅgantaviddumāsiyasappasamuppitthamīṇaülaṁ // SurSuCa.44

aviya. 

bahusattakayāhāraṁ nivaḍantamahanta āvayānivahaṁ
appattapayāvāsaṁ duggapurisaṁva naïnāiṁ // SurSuCa.45

calamāṇamīṇamayaraṁ phurantaghaṇatimiraruddhapēranta
kasiṇanisāgāsaṁ piva apattapērantasīmāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.46

ēvaṁvihaṁ samuddaṁ majjhaṁmajjhēṇa jāṇavattaṁ taṁ
jā vaccaï kaïvi hu jōyaṇāṇi vēgēṇa naranāha! // SurSuCa.47


[p. 515]
tāva ya annammi diṇē kūvayakhambhaggasaṁniviṭṭhēṇa
nijjāmaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ picchaha acchērayaṁ purisā! // SurSuCa.48

[yugmam]
kōvi hu mahāṇubhāvō adīṇavayaṇō surindasamarūvō
bāhāhiṁ kaha samuddaṁ aṇōrapāraṁ imaṁ taraī? // SurSuCa.49

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ paḍibēḍayasaṅgayā maē rāyā
tappāsē paṭṭhaviyā pattaṭṭhā kōliyakumārā // SurSuCa.50

gantūṇa tēhiṁ bhaṇiō sō purisō bhadda! ittha āruhasu
dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ vaṇiēṇaṁ tujjha pāsammi paṭṭhaviyā // SurSuCa.51

iya bhaṇiyō ārụ̄dhō samāgaō tāhi amha bōhitthē
diṭṭhō ya maē naravara! taruṇanarō sō mahābhāgō // SurSuCa.52

nijjiyaaṇaṅgarūvō punnimamayalañchaṇōvva aïsōmō
varakaṇayanihasagōrō ahiṇavaüṭṭhintamuharōmō // SurSuCa.53


[p. 516]
kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ aṇuharaē naravarinda! sō tumha
diṭṭhammi tammi diṭṭhī amhaṁ sittavva amaēṇa // SurSuCa.54

avvō! mahāṇubhāvō ēsō aṇuharaï mayarakēussa
tā hōjja kiṁ nu ēsō jō taïyā aḍavipaḍiyāē // SurSuCa.55

kamalāvaïdēvīē aṅkāō jāyamittaō hariō
puvvaviruddhasurēṇaṁ kēṇavi addiṭṭharūvēṇa? // SurSuCa.56

[yugmam]
ahavā kiṁ maha imiṇā vicintaēṇēha tāva pucchāmi
kō kattha kaha va ēsō paḍiō ya samuddamajjhammi? // SurSuCa.57

iya cintiūṇa ya maē abbhaṅguvvaṭṭaṇāiyaṁ tassa
paramāyarēṇa kāriya bhuñjāviya paramaviṇaēṇa // SurSuCa.58

[yugmam]
puṭṭhō suhāsaṇagaō kaha ṇu tumaṁ dhīra! ēttha bhīmammi
rayaṇāyarammi paḍiō kattha va tumhāṇa āvāsō? // SurSuCa.59


[p. 517]
tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu dhaṇadēva! vajjarijjantaṁ
ēgaggamaṇō hōuṁ ētthatthē kōugaṁ jaï tē // SurSuCa.60

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīyapurē vēyaḍ̣dhē rayaṇasañcaē atthi
pavaṇagaïkhayaraputtō baülavaī kucchisambhūō // SurSuCa.61

khayarindacakkavaṭṭī vikkhāō cittavēganāmotti
amiyagaïkhayaradhūyā bhajjā sē kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.62

[yugmam]
tīē ya ahaṁ puttō maṇadaïō mayarakēunāmotti
kamasō ya vaḍḍhamāṇō pattō haṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ // SurSuCa.63

ēttō ya atthi nayaraṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarāē sẹ̄dhīē
savvōuyataruvaṇasaṇḍamaṇḍiyaṁ camaracañcanti // SurSuCa.64

bhāṇugaïkhayaraputtō cittagaī tattha khayaravararāyā
sō maha piuṇō mittaṁ ahampi aïvallahō tassa // SurSuCa.65


[p. 518]
aha annayā kayāivi pattassa purammi camaracañcammi
pīīi cittagaïṇā dinnā maha rōhiṇī vijjā // SurSuCa.66

sā sattahiṁ māsēhiṁ tatthēṇa ṭhiēṇa sāhiyā vijjā
jahabhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ vihīsiyāṇaṁ abhīēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.67

tattō sāhiyavijjō sampattō niyapurē ahaṁ piuṇā
paramāṇandiyahiyaēṇa saṁsiō khayaramajjhammi // SurSuCa.68

picchaha kaha bālēṇavi raüddarūvāvi rōhiṇī vijjā
akkhuhiyamāṇasēṇaṁ sāhiyā majjha taṇaēṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.69

ajjavi vijjāō kila sāhiumasamatthaō imō bālō
iya cintāē na dinnā vijjāō imassa addēhiṁ // SurSuCa.70

tā jaï imēṇa paḍhamaṁ raüddaruvāvi sāhiyā ēsā
kā gaṇaṇā annāsimpi sāhaṇē hōjja ēyassa? // SurSuCa.71


[p. 519]
aha sōhaṇammi diyahē kāuṇaṭṭhāhiyaṁ mahāmahimaṁ
siddhāyayaṇaṭhiyāṇaṁ jiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ pamōēṇa // SurSuCa.72

bhaṇiuṁ samāṇasiddhiṁ dinnāō majjha sayalavijjāō
sōhaṇavihīvi savvō uvaïṭṭhō tāṇa tāēṇa // SurSuCa.73

[yugmam]
gantūṇa rayaṇadīvē phurantakiraṇōharayaṇavicchuriē
vijjāharavaranimmiyajugāijiṇamandirē rammē // SurSuCa.74

tattha ya pasatthakhittē viyaṇē vipphuriyakiraṇajālēsu
vijjāpasāhaṇujjayakhayarōciyavivihabhavaṇēsu // SurSuCa.75

sāhasu vijjāniyaraṁ parimiyapiyapariyaṇēṇa pariyariō
kayajiṇavandaṇapūō parihariyāsēsavāvārō // SurSuCa.76

jōyaṇamēttē khittē hiṁsā pañcindiyāṇa sattāṇa
appaparajōgajaṇiyā jattēṇa ya vajjaṇīyatti // SurSuCa.77


[p. 520]
jamhā pamāyaōvi hu jāyāi imāi jāyaē vigdhaṁ
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ piuṇā samappiyaṁ majjha aṅguliyaṁ // SurSuCa.78

ēyampi bandhasu karē nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasassa
puttaya! iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō pariyaṇasamēō // SurSuCa.79

[ṣaḍbhiḥ kulakam]
gantūṇa rayaṇadīvē pāraddhō sāhiuṁ jahāvihiṇā
bahurūviṇipamuhāō nāṇārūvāō vijjāō // SurSuCa.80

aviya. 

bahurūvā pannattī gōrīgandhārimōhaṇuppayaṇī
āgarisaṇi ummōyaṇi uccāḍaṇi taha vasīyaraṇī // SurSuCa.81

ēmāibahuvihāō sāhēmāṇassa majjha vijjāō
chammāsā vōlīṇā ūṇā divasēhiṁ thōvēhiṁ // SurSuCa.82

ētthantarammi rayaṇīi carimajāmammi jāvapajjantē
tharahariyaṁ dharaṇīē dhaṇiyaṁva disāgaïndēhiṁ // SurSuCa.83


[p. 521]
pajjaliyaṁ gayaṇēṇa hasiyaṁva pabhūyabhūyanivahēṇa
ḍhaṇiyaṁva pavvaēhiṁ varisiyamiva uvalavarisēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.84

tayaṇantaraṁ samīrō sugandhagandhō ya vāiō maüō
paviralaphusiyaṁ gandhōdagaṁ ca paḍiyaṁ tahiṁ divvaṁ // SurSuCa.85

divvā ya kusumavuṭṭhī dasaddhavannā samantaō paḍiyā
payaḍībhūyāō taō vivihālaṅkārakaliyāō // SurSuCa.86

niyaniyanāmaṅkēhiṁ kaliyāō vicittacindhanivahēhiṁ
cittavaravāhaṇāō nāṇānēvatthakaliyāō // SurSuCa.87

annōnnavannābhāsurasarūvarūvāō vivihavilayāō
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāhiṁ amhē vijjāō tujjha siddhāō // SurSuCa.88

[tisr̥bhiḥ viśēṣakam]
tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyacittēṇa pūyaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ
agghāīyaṁ tāsiṁ pattēyaṁ jīi jaṁ uciyaṁ // SurSuCa.89


[p. 522]
vijjāsiddhiṁ nāuṁ mahayā bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sañjutō
āujjagīyavāyaṇanaṭṭavihiṁ bahuvihaṁ ghēttuṁ // SurSuCa.90

aṭṭhāhiānimittaṁ pūyāuvagaraṇayaṁ gahēūṇa
vēyaḍ̣dhāō tāva ya tāōvi samāgaō tattha // SurSuCa.91

[yugmam]
kāūṇa mahāmahimaṁ jugāijiṇamandirammi bhattīē
sampūjiya jahavihiṇā vijjāniyaraṁ payattēṇa // SurSuCa.92

nimmalapavittatitthōdaēhiṁ paḍimāō jiṇavarindāṇaṁ
nhaviūṇa mahādāṇaṁ dāuṁ vijjāharōssa // SurSuCa.93

pūēttu pūyaṇijjē saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaniyaraṁ
varagīyanaṭṭavāiyasañjuyamaṭṭhāhiyaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.94

paḍupaḍahabhēribhambhādunduhisaddōhapūriyadiyantaṁ
sundaranahayarasundaripēkkhaṇayakkhittakhayarōhaṁ // SurSuCa.95


[p. 523]
nimmalajiṇaguṇakittaṇapaḍiṭṭhapaḍumāgahōhasaṅkinnaṁ
vajjantavaṁsavīṇākalasaddāṇandiyajaṇōhaṁ // SurSuCa.96

pēcchāgayasurakinnaracittacamukkārakārayaṁ rammaṁ
kāuṁ jiṇindabhavaṇē jāgaramurupāvaviddavaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.97

sayalaparivārasahiō pattō vēyaḍḍhapavvayaṁ tāō
kāyavvasēsakiccō tatthēva avaṭṭhiō ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.98

[saptabhiḥ kulakam]
kāuṁ jiṇassa pūyaṁ vihiṇā jiṇavandaṇaṁ ca kāūṇa
uiē ravimmi ahayaṁ sarīracintāē nīhariō // SurSuCa.99

kāuṁ sarīracintaṁ kayasōō dīhiyāi līlāi
vaccāmi jāva thōvaṁ bhūbhāgaṁ tāva picchāmi // SurSuCa.100

[yugmam]
vaṁsikuḍaṅgāsannē khaggaṁ bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyaṁ pavaraṁ
ghittūṇa cavalayāē jhaḍatti chinnā kuḍaṅgī sā // SurSuCa.101


[p. 524]
tattha ya puvvapaviṭṭhō āsī khayarō u mayarakēutti
sāmī gaṅgāvattassa gaṅghavāhaṇanarindasuō // SurSuCa.102

chinnāē kuḍaṅgīē chinnaṁ mahivaṭṭhasaṇṭhiyaṁ diṭṭhaṁ
sahasā sīsaṁ tassa ō jhaṁratayaṁ ruhirapabbhāraṁ // SurSuCa.103

taṁ daṭṭhūṇa sasambhamacalantapihulōlalōyaṇajuēṇa
hā hā! ahō! akajjaṁ kayanti paridēviyaṁ bahuhā // SurSuCa.104

avvō! pamāyavasaō vihiyā hiṁsā maē imā jāō
tattō ya kimpi hōhī viggha maha mandabhaggassa? // SurSuCa.105

ahavā saṁsiddhāō vijjāō vigghasambhavō natthi
tahavi hu vigghajayaṭhṭhā juttaṁ maha jāvapūyāiṁ // SurSuCa.106

iya cintiya caliō haṁ aha phuriyaṁ dāhiṇēṇa nayaṇēṇa
kiṁ mannē maha sūyaï sunimittamimanti cintintō // SurSuCa.107


[p. 525]
kaïvi hu payāṇi jāva ya vayāmi dhaṇadēva! tattha vaṇagahaṇē
picchāmiṁ tāva kimpāgasāhiṇō hiṭṭhabhūbhāgē // SurSuCa.108

suttaṁva mucchiyaṁ piva sarīrasōhāē sūiyaṁ tivvaṁ
niyakulalacchimaüvvaṁ amaēṇava nimmiyaṁ juvaïṁ // SurSuCa.109

[yugmam]
aviya dīharakasiṇasukōmalakuntalabhārēṇa sahaï akkantaṁ
āyaḍ̣dhiyabhamaraülaṁ tīē kamalaṁva varasīsaṁ // SurSuCa.110

kannantapattalōyaṇanāsāvaṁsōvasōhiō ruirō
uvahasaïva muhacandō tīi sasaṅkaṁ asampunnaṁ // SurSuCa.111

kambunnayasukumālā gīvā jaḍasaṅgavajjiyā tīē
kharakaṇṭayakaliyāiṁ uvahasaï muṇālanālāiṁ // SurSuCa.112

ghaṇavakkalapīṇunnayathaṇajuyalaṁ sayalalōyamaṇahāri
kaha uvamijjaü tīai surindagayakumbhajuyalēṇa? // SurSuCa.113


[p. 526]
tāva ya vivēyarahiyaṁ thaṇajuyalaṁ kāmuē daḍhaṁ dahaü
pattasavaṇāṇa tumhaṁ nayaṇāṇa na hōi juttamiṇaṁ // SurSuCa.114

iya bhaṇamāṇaṁ mannē jhīṇaṁ majjhaṁ tu tīi bālāē
ahavā aviṇīyajaṇē uvaēsō lahuyayaṁ kuṇaï // SurSuCa.115

garuō sihiṇāṇa bharō vōḍhavvō kaha maïtti cintāē
jhīṇaṁ tīē majjhaṁ dāliddiyadhūyajaṇaüvva // SurSuCa.116

maṇahārisugambhīrā payāhiṇāvattanābhiyā tīē
mayaraddhayamajjaṇakūviyavva vihiṇā viṇimmaviyā // SurSuCa.117

maṁsalasūmālēṇaṁ viyaḍaniyambacchalēṇa sā kuṇaï
ālōiyamittēṇavi samittalaṁ taruṇajaṇahiyayaṁ // SurSuCa.118

rambhāgabbhasukōmalamurujuyaṁ tīi rēhaē rammaṁ
mayaṇagharadāradēsē ujjhiyamiva tōraṇaṁ vihiṇā // SurSuCa.119


[p. 527]
kummunnayacalaṇajuyalaṁ saṁhayamiumaṁsalaṅgulisaṇāhaṁ
aṇurāillaṁ tīē bhaṇa kassa na cōraē cittaṁ? // SurSuCa.120

iya taṁ sahasā daṭṭhuṁ diṭṭhī āṇandiyā daḍhaṁ majjha
ciyapariciyaṁva daṭṭhuṁ jāō hiyayassa āṇandō // SurSuCa.121

piyapaṇaïṇivva tāhē nirūviyā sā maē vigayaciṭṭhā
muhanīharantaphēṇā sanīladēhacchavī bālā // SurSuCa.122

niyaaṅguliṁ khivittā tīē vayaṇaṁ nirūviyaṁ jāva
kimpāgaphalaṁ tāva ya uvaladdhaṁ addhacavviyayaṁ // SurSuCa.123

ēyaphalaviyārāō jāyā ō acēyaṇā imā nūṇaṁ
tā nēuṁ saṭṭhāṇaṁ karēmi ēīi parikammaṁ // SurSuCa.124

vijjāharassa kassavi dhūyā ēsā havijja iha pattā
nivvēēṇaṁ kēṇavi visaphalamasiyanti mannāmi // SurSuCa.125


[p. 528]
bhūmicaramaṇuyāṇaṁ suduggamō ēsa rayaṇadīvō jaṁ
tēṇēva bhūmīgōcara-dhūyā ēsā kahaṁ hōjjā? // SurSuCa.126

ērisanēvatthāō kannā ēsatti nicchaō ēsa
jaṁ puṇa acchipphuraṇaṁ maha hōhī bhāriyā tēṇa // SurSuCa.127

daṭṭhūṇaṁ vivihāō vijjāharabāliyāō aṇurāō
na ya āsi majjha puvviṁ daṭhṭhūṇa imaṁ jahā jāō // SurSuCa.128

tā nūṇaṁ bhaviyavvaṁ imāē sutaṇūē majjha daïyāē
ēmāiṁ vicintēntō gahiṁu niyabāhuucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.129

tīē sukōmalamaṇaharataṇuphāsasuhētinivvuyasarīrō
niyaṭhāṇaṁ sampattō jugāijiṇamandirāsannē // SurSuCa.130

[yugmam]
aha āsi tattha bhagiṇī piyaṁvayā aṇṇajaṇaṇī dhūyā mē
puvvuddiṭṭhaṁ kahiyaṁ vuttantaṁ tāhi sē bhaṇiyā // SurSuCa.131


[p. 529]
nimmalajalēṇa sahiyaṁ appēsu tamaṅgulīyagaṁ sigghaṁ
vijjāpayāṇasamaē tāēṇa samappiyaṁ jaṁ tu // SurSuCa.132

taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasarassa
uvaladdhapaccayaṁ puṇa visēsaō visasamūhammi // SurSuCa.133

tassalilaṁ pāintō tīē aṅgāiṁ tahaya siñcantō
bhaṇiō piyaṁvayāē ēsā maha hōi bhagiṇitti // SurSuCa.134

bhaṇiyaṁ maē kahaṁ puṇa katthavi diṭṭhā imā taē puvviṁ?
bhaṇiyaṁ piyavayāē māūē majjha lahubhagiṇī // SurSuCa.135

rayaṇavaī u kusaggē daïyā naravāhaṇassa naravaïṇō
tīē ēsā dhūyā kannā surasundarī nāma // SurSuCa.136

[yugmam]
vēyaḍ̣dhāō puvviṁ āgacchantī imammi dīvammi
khinnā avaïnnā haṁ kusaggapurabāhirujjāṇē // SurSuCa.137


[p. 530]
tattha ya diṭṭhā ēsā vijjāē payaṁ tahiṁ ca vīsariyaṁ
paḍupannāē imīē sāhiyamēttāē uvaladdhaṁ // SurSuCa.138

taha cittapaḍē lihiyaṁ rūvaṁ daṭṭhūṇa tumha ēyāē
āhūō aṇurāō garuō ummāyavaḍḍhaṇaō // SurSuCa.139

aviya aïsundarotti mudiyaṁ daïō hōjjatti khijjiyaṁ bahuhā
jaï tāva daṁsaṇampi hu hōjja kayatthatti nīsasiṁya // SurSuCa.140

jaï tāva kāvi hu ahaṁ tā 'vassaṁ tassa saṅgamēṇa suhaṁ
kāyavvaṁ bhagiṇīē iya bhaṇiyā ahaṁ ihaṁ pattā // SurSuCa.141

ēmāi jāva sāhaï piyaṁvayā tīi puvvavuttantō
tāva visavēgavigamāō cēyaṇā tīi uvaladdhā // SurSuCa.142

uvaladdhacēyaṇamahaṁ satthasarīraṁ piyaṁvayāpāsē
mōttūṇa gatō risahassa pūyaō vigghajayahēuṁ // SurSuCa.143


[p. 531]
kāuṁ jiṇindapūyaṁ vihiṇā jiṇavandaṇaṁ karēūṇa
taha santidēvayāē mantaṁ javiūṇa uvaüttō // SurSuCa.144

tīē thuiṁ pạdhittā ussaggaṁ kariya taha saüssāsaṁ
vijjāharavāvāyaṇavigghassa vighāyaṇaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.145

jāva ya samāgaō haṁ puṇaravi ya piyaṁvayā pāsammi
tāva ya sōyavasāgayavāhajalōhaliyagaṇḍayalā // SurSuCa.146

rūyamāṇī sā diṭṭhā puṭṭhā ya piyaṁvayā mayā tāhē
kīsa imā kamalacchī rōyaï gurusōgatattavva? // SurSuCa.147

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēīi kāraṇē garuyasattusaṁruddhō
acchaï imīi jaṇaō tēṇa imā ruyaï sōgēṇa // SurSuCa.148

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyā sāhīṇē kiṅkarammi ēyammi
kō tuha piyaraṁ sundari! sakkēi parābhavēuṁ jē? // SurSuCa.149

[yugmam]

[p. 532]
vasunandayakhaggakarō ēgāgī cēva taṁ durāyāraṁ
gantuṁ haṇāmi sattuñjayārimahamēva kiṁ bahuṇā? // SurSuCa.150

ētthēva paḍhamajiṇavarabhavaṇammi piyaṁvayāsamēyāē
acchēyavvaṁ tumaē jahāsuhaṁ sōyarahiyāē // SurSuCa.151

jāvā gacchāmi ahaṁ hantuṁ sattuñjayaṁ durācāraṁ
iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō tamāladalasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.152

pattō ya kusaggapuraṁ ubbhaḍabhaḍaruddhaviyaḍapāyāraṁ
antōvahantabahujantavattapāsāṇabhīsaṇayaṁ // SurSuCa.153

aṭṭālayaraïyadhayaṁ sayagghisaṅghāyaruddhakavisīsaṁ
vaḍḍhantabahalakalayalagajjantubbhaḍabhaḍāḍōvaṁ // SurSuCa.154

aha kōūhalavasaō gayaṇatthō pēcchiuṁ payattō haṁ
tāva purabhañjaṇatthaṁ samuṭṭhiyaṁ mālavāṇīyaṁ // SurSuCa.155


[p. 533]
aviya appēha majjha kasiyaṁ kavayaṁ maha dēha sundaraṁ vapharaṁ
iya sattuñjayasinnē summanti bhaḍāṇa ullāvā // SurSuCa.156

̣dhukkantu vaḍaïlāō jantāiṁ vahantu saraü paṭṭaüḍī
aha khuppaü nīsēṇīṁ pāyārē ghaḍaü sūyariyā // SurSuCa.157

dahaha tamaṅgāvaraṇaṁ chuhēha parihāsu pattharē paürē
aṭṭālayavikasiyāhiṁ khaṇaha sattuñjaī bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.158

musumūriūṇa gurupattharēhiṁ cuḍulīhiṁ sataṇanivahāhiṁ
ujjhanti tamaṅgantaraṭhiēhiṁ jōhēhiṁ sūyariyā // SurSuCa.159

pāyāranimiyanisēṇisaṇṭhiyāpuranarindajōhēhiṁ
kuntaggalacchijjantā paḍanti parihāsu aripurisā // SurSuCa.160

aṭṭālayajantāgayapattharaniyarēṇa vaḍaïlāniyarō
umacchijjaï kattalavihuriyabhaḍahatthadhariōvi // SurSuCa.161


[p. 534]
pakkhahatamaṅgasaṇṭhiyadhāṇukkavimukkabāṇanibbhinnā
kalayalacaḍulaniyattā kasiyāittā vivajjanti // SurSuCa.162

pāyālamūlaparisakkirāṇa khurudukkhiyāṇa jōhēhiṁ
sīsāiṁ dalasayāiṁ kīranti sayagdhipayarēhiṁ // SurSuCa.163

pāyāramapattāō paṭṭaüḍīōvi tillasittēhiṁ
ḍajjhanti sasaṅkajaliyarūvagurukaṭṭhanivahēhiṁ // SurSuCa.164

kavisīsantarasaṇṭhiyapakkaladhāṇukkabāṇasañchannaṁ
jāyaṁ siridhariyāraṇanipphandamarāiṇō sinnaṁ // SurSuCa.165

tāva ca rōsavasuṭṭhiyaaṇēyasāmantasuhaḍanivahēṇa
āsāsiya niyasinnaṁ ̣dhukkijjaï sālasaṁmuhayaṁ // SurSuCa.166

ubbhaḍapasaṇḍimaṇḍiyapayaṇḍakōdaṇḍakaṇḍanibbhinnō
pāyārō kayapurapakkhaṇōvva rōmañcamuvvahaï // SurSuCa.167


[p. 535]
tō pūriūṇa parihāō sattujōhēhiṁ dīhavaṁsēhiṁ
pajjāliya pērantaṁ palīviyaṁ sayalamāvaraṇaṁ // SurSuCa.168

laggantajantapattharapaḍantapāyārasiharaparituṭṭhaṁ
rahasavasuṭṭhiyahalabōlamuhuriyaṁ hōi sattubalaṁ // SurSuCa.169

aha paḍiyā kōṭṭaṭṭālayāvi gurupihulapattharasubaddhā
jantēhiṁ suraṅgāhi ya kasiyāhi ya viddavijjantā // SurSuCa.170

iya paribalēṇa sahasā parāiē picchiūṇa purasuhaḍē
rōsavasadaṭṭhaüṭṭhō uggīriya maṇḍalaggō haṁ // SurSuCa.171

pattō gaïndaparisaṇṭhiyassa sattuñjayassa āsannē
bhaṇiō ya imō rē! rē! diṭṭhō taṁ ajja kālēṇa // SurSuCa.172

jō maha daïyājaṇayassa paribhavaṁ kuṇasi akayavērassa
ahavā viṇāsasamaē hōi phalaṁ vaṁsaviḍavassa // SurSuCa.173

[yugmam]

[p. 536]
purisō bhavasu iyāṇiṁ jaï saccaṁ suhaḍavāyamuvvahasi
ghittūṇa tayaṁ kēsēsu jhatti aha matthayaṁ chinnaṁ // SurSuCa.174

aha luyasīsaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa sāmiyaṁ paribalaṁ sasambhantaṁ
valiūṇa bāṇaniyarēṇa ghāiüṁ maṁ samāḍhattaṁ // SurSuCa.175

aha taṁ sutikkhasaraniyara dhōraṇiṁ vañciuṁ payattēṇa
pattō sasōyanaravāhaṇassa atthāṇabhūmīē // SurSuCa.176

sattuñjayassa sīsaṁ puraō mōttūṇa kayapaṇāmēṇa
dhaṇadēva! puvvavuttō vuttantō sāhiō tassa // SurSuCa.177

tā accha niruvviggō ahayaṁ puṇa jāmi rayaṇadīvāō
āṇēttu tumha dhūyaṁ jēṇa samappēmi sigghanti // SurSuCa.178

iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō daïyāmuhadaṁsaṇussuō jāva
pattō imaṁ paēsaṁ tāva ya sahasā maē diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.179


[p. 537]
tālatarūdīhajandhō masimūsāmahisakālagasarīrō
asiliṭṭhalambabāhū niggayadasaṇō palambōṭṭhō // SurSuCa.180

khajjōyadittacakkhū nillaliyajamalajuyalajīhālō
aïvīṇaciviḍhanāsō vēyālō tāvasañjaṇaō // SurSuCa.181

apphōḍantō bahusō abhigajjantō tahaṭṭahāsēhiṁ
palayaghaṇanīsaṇēhiṁ kuṇamāṇō nahayalaṁ muhalaṁ // SurSuCa.182

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
rē! rē! taïyā jaṁ dinnamāsi daïyāvahāraō dukkhaṁ
vaïrassa tassa antaṁ karēmi, diṭṭhō kahiṁ jāsi? // SurSuCa.183

rē vaïriya! bālattē jīvantō tāva kahava chuṭṭō si?
iṇhi nō puṇa chuṭṭasi chụdhō bhīmammi jalahimmi // SurSuCa.184

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ sahasā pattō addaṁsaṇaṁ sa vēyālō
ahamavi gayaṇāhintō dhasatti paḍiō jalanihimmi // SurSuCa.185


[p. 538]
puṇaruttajavijjantī jāva na sā vahaï nahagamā vijjā
tāhē nāyaṁ nūṇaṁ hariyāō majjha vijjāō // SurSuCa.186

kōvi hu ēsa payaṇḍō vaïrī asurotti cintayantēṇa
dhaṇadēva! tāva bāhāhiṁ jalanihiṁ tariumāraddhō // SurSuCa.187

ēvaṁ narinda! sāhaï jāva ya sō majjha niyayavuttantaṁ
nijjāmaēṇa tāva ya sabhayaṁ ēvaṁ samullaviyaṁ // SurSuCa.188

bhō bhō nāviyapurisā! sakannadhārā samujjayā hōha
dīsaï kayantavayaṇaṁva bhīmamuppāiyaṁ jēṇa // SurSuCa.189

suppappamāṇamubbhūyamabbhavaddalayamuaha nahamaggē
khalasaṅgayaṁva jaṁ kuṇaï saṅkhayaṁ jhatti vaḍḍhantaṁ // SurSuCa.190

ērisaṭhāṇē jāyaṁ ēyaṁ uppāiyaṁ mahādhōraṁ
aïrā sabhaḍanāviyanāvāiviṇāsaṇaṁ kuṇaï // SurSuCa.191


[p. 539]
ēyaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ kūvayakhambhaggasaṇṭhiyanarassa
pavahaṇapurisasamūhō saṅkhuddhō vigayajīyāsō // SurSuCa.192

taō. 

muccaï naṅgaranivahō kūvayakhambhō tiricchaō vihiō
nāvāvi siyavaḍēṇaṁ ghaṇēṇa pacchāiyā savvā // SurSuCa.193

ētthantarammi pacchāiyaṁ nahaṁ kasiṇamēhanivahēṇa
saṅkhōhiyasalilanihī pavāiō māruō caṇḍō // SurSuCa.194

jamajīhavva camakkaï taḍicchaḍāsantataṁ samantēṇa
dhārāharāvi gajjanti bhīsaṇaṁ maccusuhaḍavva // SurSuCa.195

kharapavaṇuddhuyasāyarataraṅgavēgēhiṁ hīraē nāvā
gurukallōlavasuṭṭhiyanaṅgaraniyarēṇa dhariyāvi // SurSuCa.196

aṇavarayataraṅgēhiṁ uppayanivayaṁ kuṇantiyā vahaï
tandūsayassa līlaṁ kōṭṭimakarahammamāṇassa // SurSuCa.197


[p. 540]
tāva ya khaṇantarāō kharamāruyakhañcaṇēṇa jajjariyā
karakarakarassa tuṭṭanti naṅgarā vīivēgēhi // SurSuCa.198

pavaraturaṅgamataruṇivva tāhiṁ ummukkabandhaṇā nāvā
vīīnōlijjantā pahāviyā garuyavēgēṇa // SurSuCa.199

katthaï susiddhavijjā khayarivva nahaṅgaṇēṇa uppayaï
vijjāvigamē katthaï nivaḍaï khayarivva gayaṇāō // SurSuCa.200

ḍaṇḍāhayā bhuyaṅgivva jāi katthaï taraṅgaraṅgatā
mahajaṇasaduttatthavva dhāvaē katthaï aīva // SurSuCa.201

katthaï jhāṇōvagayā jhāyaï sā jōgiṇivva nikkampā
katthaï kantāragayā thērī iva mandayaṁ vayaï // SurSuCa.202

katthaï gurujaṇadiṭṭhā varāhakulabāliyavva lajjāē
ghummaï vēviradēhā sā nāvā jalahimajjhammi // SurSuCa.203


[p. 541]
kallōlajalapalāviyaphalayagalantōrubinduaṁsūhiṁ
ruyaïvva samassiyajaṇōhaparirakkhaṇā 'sattā // SurSuCa.204

vihaḍiyabandhaṇaphalahōhamukkagurusaddavippalāvēhiṁ
āsannabhaṅgabhīyavva vilavaī saraṇaparihīṇā // SurSuCa.205

ummattiyavva tattō iō taō sāyarammi bhamamāṇā
avavarayaṁ vidalantā jalagayamāmayasarāvuvva // SurSuCa.206

uvvunnakannadhārā āulavilavantakōliyakulōhā
uttatthavaṇiyasatthā uddhayakandantakammayarā // SurSuCa.207

kacchōṭṭantaragōviyasuvannakhaṇḍammi jaṇasamūhammi
niyataṇusandāmiyaphalayakhaṇḍadakkhammi vaṇiniyarē // SurSuCa.208

niyakuladēvayaniyaraṁ ōvāyatē samatthalōyammi
nāviyajaṇē ya bhaṇḍaṁ pavikkhirantē samuddammi // SurSuCa.209


[p. 542]
jalacchāiyapērantaṁ ēkkaṁ āsāiūṇa girigaḍayaṁ
vidalantaphalayaniyarā phuṭṭā sahasatti sā nāvā // SurSuCa.210

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]
ahamavi tattō naravara! āsāiyaphalahayammi saṁlaggō
antēṇṇivēllinōlijjamāṇalahumacchavicchuriō // SurSuCa.211

katthaï asaṅkhasaṅkhōhakhōhiō jalanihimmi buḍḍantō
katthaï gāhagasijjantagōhiyāmuhaviṇimmukkō // SurSuCa.212

katthaï nakkukkattiyasippipuḍupphiḍiyamottiyāinnō
katthaï taraṅgavēviraviddumagahaṇēṇa rujjhantō // SurSuCa.213

avarāvaragurulaharītaraṅgavēgēhiṁ hīramāṇō haṁ
diṇapañcagēṇa naranāha! pāviō nīrapērantaṁ // SurSuCa.214

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
ravikarasampāyapaṇaṭṭhapaürajaḍḍō taō samuttariuṁ
kāuṁ supakkakayalīphalāiṇā pāṇavittimahaṁ // SurSuCa.215


[p. 543]
parisusiyanāliēruggaēṇa tillēṇa kāumabbhaṅgaṁ
ṇhāūṇa sarōtīrē candaṇatarupallavarasēṇa // SurSuCa.216

kappūramīsiēṇaṁ kāūṇa vilēvaṇaṁ payattēṇa
jāiphalēlāsahiyaṁ samāṇiya pavaratambōlaṁ // SurSuCa.217

vararayaṇasilāvaṭṭhē uvaviṭṭhō cintiuṁ payattō haṁ
avvō! kaha ṇu akaṇḍē jāō dhaṇapariyaṇaviṇāsō? // SurSuCa.218

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
kaha sō mahāṇubhāvō hōhī bhaggammi jāṇavattammi?
āsāiyaphalaō jaï samuttarējjā bhavē laṭṭhaṁ // SurSuCa.219

ēmāi cintayantō kaïvi hu divasāṇi jāva acchāmi
tā annadiṇē kēṇavi ullaviyaṁ vayaṇamēyanti // SurSuCa.220

bhō dhaṇadēva! mahāyasa! uvviggō kīsa acchasē ēvaṁ?
tattō tattōhuttaṁ jāva palōēmi sambhantō // SurSuCa.221


[p. 544]
tāva ya diṭṭhō bhāsurasarīradhārī pahaṭṭhamuhakamalō
parihiyasakhiṅkhiṇīpañcavannavaravatthasōhillō // SurSuCa.222

uttaṁsaṭṭhiyabhāsurasappaphaṇāgāraciñcaïō
aïpicchaṇijjarūvō kōvi hu dēvō mahābhāgō // SurSuCa.223

[tisr̥bhiḥ viśēṣakam]
aha kayaabbhuṭṭhāṇō avagụ̄dhō tēṇa sāyaraṁ ahayaṁ
bhaṇiō ya mamaṁ parijāṇasīha kiṁvā na taṁ bhadda! // SurSuCa.224

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ajjavi sammaṁ na yāṇimō dēva!
tā sāhijjaü amhaṁ kō si tumaṁ kattha diṭṭhō vā? // SurSuCa.225

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō āsi taē hatthiṇāurē nayarē
diṭṭhō maṇōramujjāṇasaṇṭhiō dēvasammotti // SurSuCa.226

lakkhaṁ dāūṇa tayā jōgiyahatthāō supaïṭṭhasuō
jayasēṇō nāmēṇaṁ vimōiō jassa vayaṇēṇa // SurSuCa.227


[p. 545]
jō ya tayā aḍavīē satthavilōvammi suppaïṭṭhassa
pallīvaïṇō pāsē bālaggāhō taē diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.228

taha ya kusaggapurāō niyattamāṇēṇa daḍḍhapallīē
sīhaguhāē bāhiṁ karaṅkamajjhaṭṭhiō diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.229

palicchinnacalaṇajuyalō gurupaharaṇaghāyajajjariyadēhō
gāḍhaṁ tisābhibhūō jō taïyā kaṇṭhagayapāṇō // SurSuCa.230

parahiyaraēṇa tumaē arahaṁ dēvō susāhuṇō guruṇō
iya accantaṁ dāuṁ sammattaṁ niyamasañjuttaṁ // SurSuCa.231

tattō ya namōkkārō dinnō saṁsārasāgaruttārō
jassāsi taē taïyā sō haṁ bhō! dēvasammajiō // SurSuCa.232

[saptabhiḥ kulakam]
navakārapabhāvāō vēlandharanāgarāyamajjhammi
jāō sivaō nāmaṁ sāmāṇiyapaṇayapayakamalō // SurSuCa.233


[p. 546]
tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu pucchami
ṭhāṇammi kammi acchaï tumhē sāhēha maha ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.234

aha suravarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu mērussa dakkhiṇadisāē
bāyālīsasahassāhiṁ jōyaṇāṇaṁ aṇūṇāiṁ // SurSuCa.235

lavaṇasamuddaṁ ōgāhiūṇa atthittha pavvaō rammō
sattarasasaya ēgavīsē uḍḍhaṁ uccattaṇaṁ jassa // SurSuCa.236

addhaṭṭhajōyaṇāiṁ samantaō niyayakantipasarēṇa
lavaṇōhissa salilaṁ payāsaī aṅkarayaṇamaō // SurSuCa.237

nāmēṇa daübhāsō tassa ya siharammi atthi varabhavaṇaṁ
bāvaṭṭhijōyaṇuccaṁ rammaṁ vararayaṇaciñcaïyaṁ // SurSuCa.238

tattha ya vasāmi ahayaṁ sāmāṇiyadasasahassa pariyariō
paliōvamaṭṭhiīō sivaō vēlandharāhivaī // SurSuCa.239

[pañcabhiḥ kulakam]

[p. 547]
lavaṇasamuddē annāvi atthi sivayā ō rāyahāṇī mē
jōyaṇasahassabārasavitthiṇṇā sā samantēṇa // SurSuCa.240

sivayāi tīi bahusō acchāmi ahaṁ aṇēyadēvīhiṁ
pariyariō divvasuhaṁ bhuñjantō taha daübhāsē // SurSuCa.241

tā bhadda! tuha pasāyāō ērisī pāviyā maē riddhī
kallammi daübhāsammi āgaō pavvaē ahayaṁ // SurSuCa.242

ōhinnāṇēṇa tumaṁ pattaṁ daṭhṭhuṇa rayaṇadīvammi
āyāō tuhadaṁsaṇakaṅkhī, bhaṇa jaṁ maē kiccaṁ? // SurSuCa.243

avvō! jiṇindadhammassa ērisaṁ ēttiyassavi phalanti
tā kīsa na gēṇhāmō jiṇadikkhaṁ iya vicintēntō // SurSuCa.244

bhaṇiō puṇōvi dēvēṇa hōi dēvāṇa daṁsaṇamamōhaṁ
tō bhava paüṇō jēṇāhamajja bahurayaṇasañjuttaṁ // SurSuCa.245


[p. 548]
divvavimāṇārūḍhaṁ nēmi tumaṁ hatthiṇāurē nayarē
tattha ya gayassa hiyaïcchiyampi hōhī mahābhāga! // SurSuCa.246

[tisr̥bhiḥ rviśēṣakam]
ēvanti maē bhaṇiē divvavimāṇaṁ viuvviyaṁ sahasā
bhūrirayaṇōhasahiō caḍāviō tammi tēṇāhaṁ // SurSuCa.247

raṇayanivahaṁ taddīvatthaṁ aṇēyapayārayaṁ naravara! varaṁ ghēttuṁ majjhaṁ samappiya sāyaraṁ
sivagapahuṇā sammaṁ divvē vimāṇavarē ṭhiō gayapurapuraṁ tēṇāṇīō khaṇēṇa taō ahaṁ // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï gayapurapaccāgamotti nāmēṇa
surasundarīkahāē tērasamō iha paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 549]
[caturdaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï dhaṇadēvō naravaïssa vuttantaṁ
ētthantarammi surasundarīvi gurusōyasantattā // SurSuCa.1

hā! maha imassa dukkhāgarassa hiyayassa vajjaghaḍiyassa
assōyavvaṁ sōccāvi phuṭṭaē jaṁ na saïkhaṇḍaṁ // SurSuCa.2

kiṁ dhariēhiṁ iṇhiṁ imēhiṁ pāṇēhiṁ dukkhanilaēhiṁ?
maṇavallaïssa jāyammi maṅgulē jāṇabhaṅgammi // SurSuCa.3

saï daṁsaṇēvi nēhassa pagarisō daṁsiō taē nāha!
sattuñjaēṇa ruddhō vimōiō jēṇa tāotti // SurSuCa.4

avahariyā jēṇāhaṁ surēṇa tēṇēva chinnavaravijjō
kaha hōhisi nāha! tumaṁ jāṇavivattīē jalahimmi? // SurSuCa.5


[p. 550]
hā! kaha sasaṅkakaranimmalaṁ muhaṁ nāha! tuha palōissaṁ
ēvaṁvihammi vihiē vihiṇā hayabhāgadhēyā haṁ? // SurSuCa.6

calanēhāō mahilāō honti saccō jaṇappavāō 'yaṁ
jaṁ ērisēva nisuē ajjavi jīvāmi pāvā haṁ // SurSuCa.7

ēmāi vicintēntī sōgāvēgāō vigayacēyannā
pāsaṭṭhiyadēvīē paḍiyā mucchāē ucchaṅgē // SurSuCa.8

kamalāvaīvi dēvī sambhāviyasuyaviōgasōgattā
bāhajalāvilanayaṇā vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā // SurSuCa.9

hā! puttaya! aḍavīē taïyā maha jāyamittaō hariō
iṇhimpi akayadaṁsaṇa! kattha gaō maha aünnāē? // SurSuCa.10

dhannā ēsā jīē tāva ya tuha putta! pulaïyaṁ vayaṇaṁ
hā! hā! ahaṁ ahannā jāē jāōvi na hu diṭṭhō // SurSuCa.11


[p. 551]
jaṁ taïyā kulavaïṇā āiṭṭhaṁ, hōjja kiṁ nu taṁ aliyaṁ
sampattajōvvaṇō sō milihī kila hatthiṇapurammi? // SurSuCa.12

rāyāvi amarakēū karayalapalhatthavayaṇavicchāō
suyasōyavihuriyaṅgō bāhajalaṁ mōttumāraddhō // SurSuCa.13

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ ētthantarammi surasundariṁ pavīyantī
puṭṭhā vilāsiṇī haṁsiyā u sañjāyasaṅkēṇa // SurSuCa.14

mucchānimīliyacchī kā ēsā kannagā aüvvatti
ujjāṇanivaḍaṇāiṁ tīivi sē sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.15

sambhariyasumaïvayaṇō dhaṇadēvō tāhi ēvamullavaï
kīsa visannō naravara! vilavasi kiṁvā tumaṁ dēvi! // SurSuCa.16

kiṁ taṁ visumariyaṁ bhē nēmittiyasumaïṇā jamāiṭṭhaṁ
kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā kira kannagā paḍihī // SurSuCa.17


[p. 552]
tattō sigghaṁ hōhī samāgamō tumha niyayaputtēṇa
tā mā tūraha sampaï milihī sō natthi sandēhō // SurSuCa.18

[yugmam]
jaṁ sō jahatthavāī sumaī uvaladdhapaccaō bahusō
tā mā kuṇaha visāyaṁ jāēvi hu jāṇabhaṅgammi // SurSuCa.19

ēvaṁ ca samāsāsaï dhaṇadēvō jāva niuṇavayaṇēhiṁ
ētthantarammi sahasā dunduhisaddō samucchaliō // SurSuCa.20

gayaṇāō ōyarantā dēvā dīsanti nayarabāhimmi
summaï jayajayasaddō surakāmiṇigīyasaṁvaliō // SurSuCa.21

kiṁ kiṁ imanti jampanti jāva atthāṇasaṇṭhiyā lōyā
tāva ya samantabhaddō samāgatō harisapaḍihatthō // SurSuCa.22

bhaṇaï ya kayappaṇāmō purassa puvvuttarē disābhāē
kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïjaṇajōggammi bhūmīē // SurSuCa.23


[p. 553]
samaṇagaṇasamparivuḍō samatthasatthatthavittharavihinnū
paravāivāravāraṇanivāraṇē kēsarisaricchō // SurSuCa.24

vivihatavōvihiniraō visuddhacārittasañjamujjuttō
parahiyakaraṇēkkaraō sūrī supaïṭṭhanāmotti // SurSuCa.25

ajjēva samōsariō tassa ya niddaḍḍhaghāikammassa
sampaï appaḍivāī uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.26

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
kēvalimahimākaraṇatthamittha tiyasā samāgayā dēva!
taṁ sōūṇa narindō sāṇandō vandiuṁ caliō // SurSuCa.27

dēvi! tumampi hu paüṇā sahiyā surasundarīē hōhitti
vandittā bhagavantaṁ puccha tumaṁ puttavutantaṁ // SurSuCa.28

ṇhāyavilittō rāyā mahayā bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sañjuttō
pavaragaïndārụ̄dhō pattō kusumāyarujjāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.29


[p. 554]
sayalaparivārasahiō kāuṁ tipayakkhiṇaṁ muṇivarassa
payajuyalaṁ paṇamittā uvaviṭaṭhō uciyadēsammi // SurSuCa.30

aha kayakēvalimahimō sadēvamaṇuyāsurāiparisāē
gambhīrabhāraīē sūrī vajjariumāraddhō // SurSuCa.31

nārayatiriyanarāmaragaīsu sattēhiṁ dukkhataviēhiṁ
kahakahavi māṇusattaṁ pāvijjaï ēttha saṁsārē // SurSuCa.32

laddhūṇavi taṁ dulahaṁ micchattāīhiṁ mōhiyā bahavē
na kuṇanti parattha hiyaṁ visayāmisalōluyā jīvā // SurSuCa.33

jiṇavayaṇasuivihīṇā kajjākajjāiṁ nēva jāṇanti
bhakkhēyābhakkhēyaṁ pēyāpēyaṁ na lakkhēnti // SurSuCa.34

gammāgammavibhāgaṁ giddhā na gaṇanti vigayamajjāyā
dhammiyahiyalōēṇaṁ vārijjantā iya bhaṇanti // SurSuCa.35


[p. 555]
mụ̄dhā tumhē dhuttēhiṁ vañciyā natthi kōvi jaṁ jīvō
jō paralōyaṁ gacchaï suhaduhabhōttā amuttō vā // SurSuCa.36

tassābhāvē pāvaṁ hiṁsāikayaṁ havijja kassēha?
tā pañcabhūyasamudayamittaṁ nannaṁ jaē kiñci // SurSuCa.37

ēvaṁvihapariṇāmā nigghiṇahiyayā kuṇanti jiyaghāyaṁ
aliyaṁ vayanti, giṇhantadattayaṁ, jati paradāraṁ // SurSuCa.38

bhūripariggahanirayā rāgaddōsēhiṁ mōhiyamaīyā
nisibhōyaṇamaṁsāsī giddhā mahumajjapāṇammi // SurSuCa.39

kōhamayamāyalōbhēhiṁ vidduyā saṅkiliṭṭhapariṇāmā
avirayamicchaddiṭṭhī kiliṭṭhakammaṁ samajjanti // SurSuCa.40

tavvasagā puṇa kālaṁ kāuṁ nivaḍanti ghōranaraēsu
niccaṁ ghaṇandhayārēsu tivvasīuṇhakaliēsu // SurSuCa.41


[p. 556]
tattha ya tē uvavannā paramāhammiyasurēhiṁ virasantā
chijjanti nisiyakaravattadittaparasūhiṁ sayahūttaṁ // SurSuCa.42

gurutikkhakaṇṭayāinnasimbalīniviḍasāhamajjhammi
ārōviuṇa bahusō ākāḍ̣dhijjanti rajjūhiṁ // SurSuCa.43

kaḍhakaḍhakạdhēntakumbhīsu tēhiṁ paccanti niddayamaṇēhiṁ
pāījjanti jalantaṁ tambaṁ tisiyatti jampantā // SurSuCa.44

sasarīrasamukkattiyamaṁsaṁ chuhiyāṇa aggisaṅkāsaṁ
kāuṁ chubbhaï vayaṇē nēraïyāṇaṁ anāhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.45

pūivasaruhirapunnaṁ vēyaraṇiṁ nimmayaṁ viuvvittā
vōlijjanti rasantā hā! hā! māyatti jampantā // SurSuCa.46

chāyatthā sampattā asipattavaṇammi nisiyapattēhiṁ
chijjanti vilavamāṇā asitōmarakuntarūvēhiṁ // SurSuCa.47


[p. 557]
tattha kayacchijjantā rakkhaha saraṇāgayatti jampantā
sumarāviyapuvvabhavā gāḍhayaraṁ tēhiṁ hammanti // SurSuCa.48

kiṁ bahuṇā acchinimīliyamittaṁ natthi suhaṁ dukkhamēṁva santattaṁ
naraē nēraīyāṇaṁ ahōnisiṁ paccamāṇāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.49

ēvaṁ pabhūyakālaṁ aṇuhaviuṁ dāruṇāiṁ dukkhāiṁ
kahavi hu uvvaṭṭittā jāyanti tirikkhajōṇīsu // SurSuCa.50

tatthavi chuhāpivāsuṇhasīyavahabandharōyaviyaṇāhiṁ
bhārarōvaṇanatthaṇadamaṇaṅkusatōttayāīhiṁ // SurSuCa.51

avarōpparabhakkhaṇatāḍaṇāidukkhāiṁ viviharuvāiṁ
paccaṇubhavanti bahusō puṇō puṇō vivihajōṇīsu // SurSuCa.52

tattō lahanti jaï kahavi dullahaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ jīvā
tatthavi jāyaï dukkhaṁ sārīraṁ māṇasaṁ vivihaṁ // SurSuCa.53


[p. 558]
dāriddagaruyamōggaranivāyaduhiyā karēnti annēsiṁ
nīyāṇavi āṇattiṁ kadannalavapāvaṇicchāē // SurSuCa.54

na gaṇinti rāidiyahaṁ vaccanti sudūravisamadēsampi
pavisanti visamavivaraṁ laṅghati ya jalanihiṁ dīṇā // SurSuCa.55

dhaṇapāvaṇavañchāē dukkhaṁ na gaṇinti lōhagahagahiyā
dippantakuntapaürē pavisanti ya bhīmasaṅgāmē // SurSuCa.56

iṭṭhajaṇaviyōgāō aṇiṭhṭhasampāvaṇē ya jaṁ dukkhaṁ
vivihāvayāhi ya tahā kō puṇa taṁ vanniuṁ taraï? // SurSuCa.57

bahuviharōgāyaṅkēhi pīḍiyā nivvuiṁ na pāvinti
ghippanti jarāi taō marēnti tattō sunivvinnā // SurSuCa.58

jaï kaïvi hu dēvattaṁ pāvinti tahimpi jāyaē dukkhaṁ
īsāvisāyabhayasōyalōhasantattacittāṇa // SurSuCa.59


[p. 559]
parariddhiṁ pēcchantā bhiccā viva sāmiēṇa āṇattā
jāyanti cavaṇasamaē dēvāvi hu dukkhiyā dhaṇiyaṁ // SurSuCa.60

culasīijōṇilakkhēkkasaṅkulē iha bhavē bhamantēhiṁ
taṁ natthi kimpi ṭhāṇaṁ aṇantukhattō na jaṁ ēntaṁ // SurSuCa.61

savvatthavi dukkhattā jāyanti jiṇindadhammaparihīṇā
tā bhō dēvāṇupiyā! karēha jiṇadēsiyaṁ dhammaṁ // SurSuCa.62

sō duvigappō bhaṇiō jaïdhammō taha gihatthadhammō ya
duvihassavi vinnēyaṁ sammattaṁ guṇagaṇāvāsaṁ // SurSuCa.63

tattatthasaddahāṇaṁ suhāyapariṇāmarūvayaṁ taṁ tu
jīvāiṇō payatthā tattaṁ puṇa hōi vinnēyaṁ // SurSuCa.64

jīvā 'jīvāpunnaṁ pāvāsavasaṁvarā ya nijjaraṇā
bandhō mukkhō ya tahā tattāṇi imāṇi nava honti // SurSuCa.65


[p. 560]
suhumā bāyara bēindiyā ya tēindiyā ya caürindī
sannī assannī khalu cōddasa pajjatta 'pajjattā // SurSuCa.66

dhammā 'dhammā ' 'gāsā tiyatiyabhēyā ya tahēva kālō ya
khandhā dēsapaēsā paramāṇū ajīva cōddasahā // SurSuCa.67

sāyaṁ uccāgōyaṁ sattatīsaṁ ca nāmapagaīō
tiṇṇi ya āuṇi tahā bāyālaṁ punnapagaḍīō // SurSuCa.68

nāṇantarāyadasagaṁ daṁsaṇa nava mōhapagaïchavvīsaṁ
nāmassa caüttīsaṁ tiṇha ya ēkkikka pāvāu // SurSuCa.69

indiya kasāya avvaya kiriṇā paṇa caüra paṇa ya paṇavīsā
jōgā tinnēva bhavē bāyālaṁ āsavō bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.70

samiī guttī dhammō aṇuppēhaparīsahā carittaṁ ca
sattāvannaṁ bhēyā paṇatiyabhēyāi saṁvaraṇē // SurSuCa.71


[p. 561]
aṇasaṇabhēyāi tavō bārasahā tēṇa nijjarā bhaṇiyā
kaṇagāvalibhēyāō ahava tavō 'ṇēgahā hōi // SurSuCa.72

payaïṭhiīaṇubhāgapaēsabhēyā caüvvihō bandhō
aṭṭhavihakammavigamō mōkkhō puṇa sāsaō bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.73

ēēsiṁ saddahāṇē arihaṁ dēvō susāhuṇō guruṇō
iya paḍivattinimittaṁ sammattaṁ hōi vinnēyaṁ // SurSuCa.74

sāvajjajōgaparivajjaṇaṁ tu maṇavayaṇakāyajōgēhiṁ
ēsō jaīṇa dhammō duraṇucarō mandasattāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.75

kāyavvā jēṇa dayā chaṇhavi puḍhavāiyāṇa jīvāṇa
savvōvāhivisuddhaṁ bhaṇiyavvaṁ saccayaṁ vayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.76

tiṇamittampi adinnaṁ na ya ghittavvaṁ asuddhacittēṇa
dhārēyavvaṁ ca sayā nava guttisaṇāhabambhavayaṁ // SurSuCa.77


[p. 562]
dhammōvagaraṇavajjō thēvōvi pariggahō na kāyavvō
āhāracaükkampi hu rayaṇīē nēva bhōttavvaṁ // SurSuCa.78

samiīu pañca guttīu tinni niccaṁ ca sēviyavvāō
jēyavvā taha uiyā bābīsaparīsahā sammaṁ // SurSuCa.79

kāyavvaṁ sattīē vēyavaccaṁ ca sūripamuhāṇa
naratiridēvōhakayā uvasaggā taha ya sahiyavvā // SurSuCa.80

saddāisu visaēsuṁ rāgaddōsā na cēva kāyavvā
bāyāladōsasuddhō bhōttavvō kāraṇē piṇḍō // SurSuCa.81

vēyaṇavēyāvaccē īriyaṭṭhāē ya sañjamaṭṭhāē
taha pāvavattiyāē chaṭhṭhaṁ puṇa dhammacintāē // SurSuCa.82

kāyavvō sajjhāō parihariyavvāō savvavikahāō
ujjamiyavvaṁ sayayaṁ sabbhintarabāhiratavammi // SurSuCa.83


[p. 563]
mōttūṇa aṭṭaruddē jhāēyavvāṇi dhammasukkāṇi
bhavēyavvō ya aṇiccayāivarabhāvaṇānivahō // SurSuCa.84

abbhasiyavvō viṇaō pāvā sacchandayā na kāyavvā
niccampi aṇuṭṭhēō dasappayārōvi jaïdhammō // SurSuCa.85

khantī maddava ajjava muttī tavasañjamē ya bōddhabvē
saccaṁ sōyaṁ ākiñcaṇaṁ ca bambhaṁ jaïdhammō // SurSuCa.86

vasiyavvaṁ muṇimajjhē nō kāyavvā kusīlasaṁsaggī
pañcavihōvi pamāō parihariyavvō payattēṇa // SurSuCa.87

majjaṁ visayakasāyā niddā vigahā ya pañcamī bhaṇiyā
iyaṁ pañcavihapamāō jīvaṁ pāḍēi saṁsārē // SurSuCa.88

kiṁ bahuṇā dhīdubbalamaṇatāvakarō u jāvajīvāē
bōḍhavvō aṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassapabbhārō // SurSuCa.89


[p. 564]
kīrantō jaïdhammō khippaṁ mōkkhammi nēi naranāha!
dīharakālēṇaṁ puṇa sāvagadhammōvi taṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.90

pañca ya aṇuvvayāiṁ guṇavvayāiṁ ca honti tinnēva
sikkhāvayāiṁ caürō sāvagadhammō duvālasahā // SurSuCa.91

ēmāivittharēṇaṁ duvihēvi hu sāhiyammi dhammammi
patthāvaṁ nāūṇaṁ rannā sūrī imaṁ puṭṭhō // SurSuCa.92

kamalāvaīi puttō aḍavīē jayamēttaō kēṇa
avahariō, puvvakayaṁ kiṁvā vēraṁ sarantēṇa? // SurSuCa.93

vuḍ̣dhiṅgaō sa kattha va bhayavaṁ! kaïyā va amha sō milihī?
ēyaṁ savittharēṇaṁ sāhēha aṇuggahaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.94

nāūṇa ya uvagāraṁ kahijjamāṇē pabhūyalōyassa
aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kahimō āyannasu narinda! // SurSuCa.95


[p. 565]
dhāyaïsaṇḍē dīvē puracchimaddhammi bharahakhittammi
atthi purī pōrāṇā nāmēṇaṁ avarakaṅkatti // SurSuCa.96

tīē ambaḍavaṇiṇō mahilā nāmēṇa atthi acchuttā
tīē kamēṇa jāyā vararūvā tinni puttāō // SurSuCa.97

maṇḍaṇamalhaṇacandaṇanāmā, tēsiṁ ca tinni mahilāō
lacchisarassaïsampayanāmāō pavararūvāō // SurSuCa.98

payaīi taṇukasāyā annōnnaṁ pavarapīisañjuttā
dāṇarayā santuṭṭhā suhēṇa acchanti tē vaṇiṇō // SurSuCa.99

aha annayā kayāivi lacchī vaṇṭhēṇa ninnanāmēṇa
diṭṭhā, abbhuvavannō sō tīē ruvalāvannē // SurSuCa.100

patthēi ya taṁ bahusō sā puṇa taṁ nēcchaī maṇēṇāvi
aha annayā talāē tōyanimittaṁ gayā lacchī // SurSuCa.101


[p. 566]
turayārụdhō aha ninnaōvi pattō 'ṇumaggaō tīē
viyaṇē gahiyā maḍḍāi rōviyā turayapaṭṭhīē // SurSuCa.102

vilavantī vēgapahāviēṇa turaēṇa pāḍiyā aḍaviṁ
bhillēhiṁ samaṁ jujjhammi māriō ninnaō rannē // SurSuCa.103

gahiyābharaṇā lacchī mukkā bhillēhiṁ tattha aḍavīē
hiṇḍantī tattha mūḍhadisā asiyā sīhēṇa chuhiēṇa // SurSuCa.104

aha sā malhaṇapattī sarassatī mōhilēṇa vaṇiēṇa
patthijjantī païṇō sāhēi jahaṭṭhiyaṁ savvaṁ // SurSuCa.105

aha malhaṇēṇa rannō gantuṁ siṭṭhammi tammi vuttantē
uddāliyadaviṇō mōhilōvi nivvāsiō rannā // SurSuCa.106

puvvasayasahassāiṁ bahūṇi parivāliūṇa niyamāuṁ
tinnivi kālaṁ kāuṁ nibaddhamaṇuyāuyā tattō // SurSuCa.107


[p. 567]
jambuddīvē ētthaṁ atthi purī mēhalāvatī nāma
ēravaē varakhēttē āriyadēsammi vitthinnā // SurSuCa.108

bhīmarahō tatthāsī rāyā kusumāvalī u sē dēvī
tīē puttatāē uvavannō maṇḍaṇō tāva // SurSuCa.109

jāō ya uciyasamaē dēvakumārōvamō visālacchō
kaṇagarahō sē nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ uciyammi samayammi // SurSuCa.110

kamasō jōvvaṇapattō visuddhavaṁsāṇa rāyakannāṇa
rāyasirīpamuhāṇaṁ pavarāṇaṁ gāhiō pāṇiṁ // SurSuCa.111

juvarāya paē ṭhaviō bhujaï māṇussaē pavarabhōē
antēuramajjhagaō dēvō viva dēvalōgammi // SurSuCa.112

tīi nayarīi ibbhā sahōyara dōnni āsi satthāhā
sāgaradattō ya tahā samuddadattō ya supasiddhā // SurSuCa.113


[p. 568]
aha sō ninnayavaṇṭhō nihaō bhillēhiṁ tattha aḍavīē
kaïvayabhavagahaṇāiṁ hiṇḍittā tiriyajāīsu // SurSuCa.114

uvvaṭṭiūṇa puttō sāgaradattassa satthavāhassa
dhannāē bhāriyāē subandhunāmō samuppannō // SurSuCa.115

[yugmam]
sōvi hu malhaṇajīvō kālaṁ kāūṇa āupajjantē
jāō sudaṁsaṇāē bhajjāē samuddadattassa // SurSuCa.116

puttō dhaṇavaïnāmō suruvajuttō kalāsu pattaṭṭhō
ēttō ya atthi nayarī vijayā tatthēva ēravaē // SurSuCa.117

[yugmam]
tīē samiddhijuttō dhaṇabhūī nāma āsi satthāhō
mahilā sundarināmā puttō ya sudhammanāmotti // SurSuCa.118

aha candaṇōvi vaṇiō mariuṇa taō sudhammanāmassa
ēgōyarō kaṇiṭṭhō jāō dhaṇavāhaṇō nāma // SurSuCa.119


[p. 569]
tatthēva ya ēravaē supaïṭṭhapurammi āsi haridattō
ibbhō tassa ya mahilā viṇayavaī viṇayasañjuttā // SurSuCa.120

puttō uṇa vasudattō aha sā lacchī tayā ō aḍavīē
sīhahayā mariūṇaṁ bhabhiūṇa tirikkhajōṇīsu // SurSuCa.121

viṇayavaīē dhūyā jāyā ō sulōyaṇatti nāmēṇa
vasuddattassa kaṇiṭṭhā suruvaruvā suruvahuvva // SurSuCa.122

[yugmam]
sāvi hu candaṇabhajjā kālaṁ kāūṇa sampayā tattō
jāyā sulōyaṇāē kaṇiṭṭhabhagiṇī aṇaṅgavaī // SurSuCa.123

ētthantarammi malhāṇabhajjāvi sarassaī mayā santī
tāṇaṁ dōṇhavi lahuī vasumaïnāmā samuppannā // SurSuCa.124

ēvaṁ ca tāō tinnivi vasēṇa bhaviyavvāyāi ēgattha
jāyāō bhagiṇīō avarōpparanēhakaliyāō // SurSuCa.125


[p. 570]
jōvvaṇamaṇupattāō samāṇajāīṇa rūvajuttāṇa
aṇurūvāṇa varāṇaṁ māyāvittēhiṁ variyāō // SurSuCa.126

aviya jēṭṭhā sulōyaṇā sā pariṇīyā ninnavaṇṭhajīvēṇa
sāgaradattasuēṇaṁ subandhunāmēṇa vaṇiēṇa // SurSuCa.127

bīyā aṇaṅgavaïyā dhaṇabhūisuēṇa vijayanayarīē
dhaṇavāhaṇanāmēṇaṁ pariṇīyā puvvadaïēṇa // SurSuCa.128

taïyā vasumaïnāmā malhaṇajīvēṇa puvvadaïēṇa
dhaṇavaïṇā pariṇīyā taṇaēṇa samuddadattassa // SurSuCa.129

jiṭhṭhaṁ sulōyaṇaṁ vajjiūṇa bhaviyavvayāniōēṇa
puvvabhavavallahēhiṁ juttāō nēhakaliēhiṁ // SurSuCa.130

puvvabhavabbhāsāō sulōyaṇā vallahā subandhussa
tīē uṇa sō na tahā, ēvaṁ vaccanti divasāiṁ // SurSuCa.131


[p. 571]
aha annayā kayāivi kaṇayarahō turayavāhaṇanimittaṁ
bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sahiō niggacchaï rāyamaggēṇa // SurSuCa.132

tāva ya nāyariyāō niyaniyahammiyatalēsu caḍiūṇa
kumaraṁ niggacchantaṁ pulaïumēvaṁ payattāō // SurSuCa.133

ēkkā vilāsapaüraṁ kumaraṁ daṭṭhuṁ aṇaṅgapaḍirūvaṁ
kayaünnā sā jīē ēsō daïotti cintēi // SurSuCa.134

annā kumarapalōyaṇataggayacittā vimukkavāvārā
nipphandalōyaṇajuyā suravahūlīlaṁ samuvvahaï // SurSuCa.135

annā uṇa karasaṇṭhiyamuttāhalatārahāriyā sahaï
phalihakkhamālavāvaḍajhāṇaṭṭhiyajōgiṇisaricchā // SurSuCa.136

kōugarahasapayaṭṭā gurujaṇasaṅkāi taha nittantī
rēhaï dōlārūḍhavva kāvi kumarassa niggamaṇē // SurSuCa.137


[p. 572]
līlācalantalōyaṇakumarapalōyaṇavimukkanīsāsā
mayaṇasarasalliyaṅgivva najjaē caürasahiyāhiṁ // SurSuCa.138

kāvi hu cumbaï bālaṁ annā sahiyāi laggaē galaē
annā karēi gīyaṁ kāvi hu uccaṁ samullavaï // SurSuCa.139

līlācalantagīvō jattō jattō niyacchaï kumārō
sōhaggamahō vaḍḍhaï tahiṁ tahiṁ nayaranārīṇaṁ // SurSuCa.140

ēvaṁ ca samayaṇāhiṁ pulaïjjantō sa nayaranārīhiṁ
pattō kamēṇa sāgaradattagihāsannabhūbhāgē // SurSuCa.141

diṭṭhō sulōyaṇāē avalōyaṇasaṇṭhiyāi tēṇāvi
diṭṭhā imā sakajjalasiṇiddhapihunayaṇasōhillā // SurSuCa.142

puvvabhavabbhāsāō avarōpparadaṁsaṇāō sañjāō
aïguruō aṇurāō takkhaṇamēttēṇa dōṇhampi // SurSuCa.143


[p. 573]
aha niggaō turantō turaṅgamārūḍhaviggahō kumarō
dēhēṇa na cittēṇaṁ sulōyaṇārūvahayahiyaō // SurSuCa.144

puṭṭhō aṇēṇa sumaī bālavayaṁsō vayasaṁ! kassēsā
dappaṇavāvaḍahatthā avalōyaṇasaṇṭhiyā juvaī? // SurSuCa.145

ēsā kumara! sulōyaṇanāmā daïyā subandhuvaṇiyassa
sāgaradattasuyassa ō iya bhaṇiē sumaïṇā kamasō // SurSuCa.146

āvāhiūṇa turaē samāgaō niyagihammi kaṇagarahō
mayaṇasaravihuriyaṅgō cinttaï tappāvaṇōvāyaṁ // SurSuCa.147

kiṁ majjha vibhūīē kiṁvā antaürēṇa rajjēṇa?
jō tīē muhakamalē chappayalīlaṁ na pāvēmi // SurSuCa.148

jaïvi hu lōyaviruddhaṁ sukuluppannāṇa ērisaṁ kajjaṁ
tahavi hu tīē viuttō sattō dhariuṁ na jīyampi // SurSuCa.149


[p. 574]
nāūṇa tīē bhāvaṁ dūīsampēsaṇēṇa cittagayaṁ
jaï tāva sāvi icchaï khivāmi antēurē niyaē // SurSuCa.150

iya cintiūṇa tēṇaṁ paḍuyā pavvāiyā samāṇattā
taha kuṇasu tumaṁ bhayavaï! jaha sā maē paṇaïṇī hōi // SurSuCa.151

tīēvi gantu viyaṇē taha sā ābhāsiyā suniuṇāē
jaha payaḍiyasabbhāvā hiyayagayaṁ jhatti ullavaï // SurSuCa.152

uvviggā viva dīsasi kīsa tumaṁ putti! kēṇa bhē kajjaṁ?
āṇēmi jēṇa aïdullahampi niyamantasattīē // SurSuCa.153

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaï! maha hiyayaṁ dullahaṁ jaṇaṁ mahaï
nibbhaggarōrapurisōvva bhōyaṇaṁ cakkavaṭṭissa // SurSuCa.154

jaha kāvi sāramēī icchaï sīhēṇa saṅgamamalajjā
taha cēva ahaṁ bhayavaï! saṅgaṁ icchāmi kumarēṇa // SurSuCa.155


[p. 575]
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ idampi putti! āṇēmi mantasattīē
kittiyamēttaṁ ēyaṁ maha mantō jattha vipphuraï // SurSuCa.156

mā putti! kuṇa visāyaṁ jāvaṁ mantassa taha payacchissaṁ
ajjavi ya kumārēṇaṁ jaha saṅgō jāyaē tujjha // SurSuCa.157

taha kāyavvaṁ bhayavaï! na hōi jaha majjha lāghavaṁ lōē
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ tīē dinnā muttāvalī niyayā // SurSuCa.158

pavvāiyāē tattō gantuṁ kumarassa sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ
harisiyamaṇēṇa tēṇavi āṇāviya niyayapurisēhiṁ // SurSuCa.159

antēurammi khittā sulōyaṇā rāgamōhiyamaṇēṇa
agaṇiya jaṇāvavāyaṁ ullaṅghiyaniyayamajjāyaṁ // SurSuCa.160

[yugmam]
vinnāyavaïrēhiṁ ca sāhiyaṁ nāyarēhiṁ naravaïṇō
tēṇavi bahuppagāraṁ sikkhaviō mahuravayaṇēhiṁ // SurSuCa.161


[p. 576]
na ya icchaï taṁ mōttuṁ tāhē nāūṇa tassa nibbandhaṁ
rannā paürā bhaṇiyā asamatthā amhē kumarassa // SurSuCa.162

sāmēṇa tā na muñcaï daṇḍō kumarammi tīraï na kāuṁ
tā khamaha ēkkamēyaṁ avarāhaṁ amha kumarassa // SurSuCa.163

ēyaṁ naravaïvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ nāyarāvi dīṇamuhā
vicchāyanirāṇandā jahāgayaṁ paḍigayā savvē // SurSuCa.164

kaṇagarahōvi hu tīē surayasuhāsattamāṇasō niccaṁ
kamasō sēsantēuraparibhōgaparammuhō jāō // SurSuCa.165

cintēi na rajjaṭhiiṁ na nīi bāhiṁ na dēi atthāṇaṁ
sahiō sulōyaṇāē acchaï vivihāhiṁ kīlāhiṁ // SurSuCa.166

ēvaṁ pabhūyakālō vōlīṇō tassa rāyataṇayassa
tīē ahiṇavajōvvaṇasuhaphāsapasattacittassa // SurSuCa.167


[p. 577]
aha annayā kayāivi paribhūyā hanti jāyakōvāē
puvviṁ tassiṭṭhāē dēvīē rāyasiriyāē // SurSuCa.168

paricariyaparivvāiyavidinnaümmāyakāraō cunnō
ēgantapasuttāṇaṁ dōṇhavi sirammi pakkhittō // SurSuCa.169

[yugmam]
tassa ya vasēṇa dōnnivi sahasā ummattayāṇi jāyāṇi
gāyanti hasanti samullavanti asamañjasaṁ bahuhā // SurSuCa.170

bhīmarahēṇavi tattō vāhariyā mantatantiyā bahavē
tēvi hu karinti kiriyaṁ bhūyavigārotti mannantā // SurSuCa.171

aviya kāuṁ sarīrarakkhaṁ gāḍhaṁ gahiūṇa kēvi muddāsu
pahaṇanti gurucavēḍāghāēhiṁ kasappahārēhiṁ // SurSuCa.172

ālihiya mañja 'lēsuṁ kēvi hu viṇivēsiūṇa uvaüttā
ahimantiya siddhatthayaghāēhiṁ haṇanti puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.173


[p. 578]
kēvi hu virālatannayapurīsamīsēhiṁ guggulāīhiṁ
uvvariyammī khivittā uddhūvaṇiyaṁ payacchanti // SurSuCa.174

vāyassa vigārasaṅkirēhiṁ vējjēhiṁ vivihakiriyāō
pāraddhāō na uṇō kōvi guṇō tāṇa sañjāō // SurSuCa.175

ummattayarūvēṇaṁ paṇaṭṭhacittāṇa vaccaē kālō
aha annayā pasuttē pāhariyajaṇammi rayaṇīē // SurSuCa.176

bhañjittā niyalāiṁ nihuyaṁ ciya niggayāiṁ nayarīō
dōnnivi bhamanti sīuṇhavāyabahudukkhataviyāiṁ // SurSuCa.177

[yugmam]
iya naravara! saṁsārē suhiō hōūṇa jāyaē duhiō
rāyāvi bhamaï bhikkhaṁ suvaï mahīē nirāvaraṇō // SurSuCa.178

pavarāhāravilēvaṇaāharaṇavibhūsiyāiṁ hōūṇa
hiṇḍanti tāiṁ bhikkhaṁ gihē gihē dukkhataviyāiṁ // SurSuCa.179


[p. 579]
dhūlīdhūsariyāiṁ bālōhahasējjamāṇacēṭṭhāiṁ
hiṇḍanti sudīṇāiṁ nivasiyajaradaṇḍikhaṇḍāiṁ // SurSuCa.180

bālōhapēcchaṇijjaṁ buhajaṇasaṁsōyaṇijjamaccatthaṁ
picchasu naravara! jāyaṁ taṁ mihuṇaṁ kammadōsēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.181

ēyaṁ ca tāva ēvaṁ, ēttō u purīē vijayanāmāē
rattō 'ṇaṅgavaīē bhuñjaï ghaṇavāhaṇō bhōē // SurSuCa.182

paḍibōhiō suhammēṇa sūriṇā jiṭṭhabhāuṇā ēsō
sahiō 'ṇaṅgavaīē pavvaïō sūripāsammi // SurSuCa.183

ēttō ya dhaṇavaīvi hu vasumaïyāē siṇēhajuttāē
sahiō pañcapayārē bhuñjaï māṇussaē bhōē // SurSuCa.184

jaha sō mōhilavaṇiō rannā nivvāsiō sadēsāō
kāūṇa tahāruvaṁ suhaphalayaṁ kimpaṇuṭṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.185


[p. 580]
uvavannō vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarasẹ̄dhīē vējayantapurē
cittaṅgayassa puttō puhavīi sumaṅgalō nāma // SurSuCa.186

sāhiyabahuvihavijjō aha sō gayaṇaṅgaṇēṇa hiṇḍantō
kaïyāvi mēhalāvaïpurīē līlāē sampattō // SurSuCa.187

hammiyatalamārụdhā ṇhāyantī tēṇa vasumaī diṭṭhā
puvvabhavabbhāsāō rattō sō tīi ruvammi // SurSuCa.188

kāuṁ dhaṇavaïrūvaṁ uvabhuttā tēṇa vasumaī muddhā
tīē surayapasattō dhaṇavaïrūvī ṭhiō tattha // SurSuCa.189

sō puṇa dhaṇavaïvaṇiō puvvabhavōvattakammadōsēṇa
avahariya tēṇa mukkō ihēva bharahē viṇīyāē // SurSuCa.190

sō tattha risahajiṇavaravaṁsapasūyassa daṇḍavīriyassa
kēvaliṇō payamūlē pavvaïō jāyanivvēō // SurSuCa.191


[p. 581]
puvvasayasahassāiṁ tīsaṁ kāūṇa uggatavacaraṇaṁ
uvavaṇṇō īsāṇē dēvō candajjuṇō nāma // SurSuCa.192

paradārapasattō sō sumaṅgalō tēṇa chinnavaravijjō
mukkō paraō māṇūsanagassa dēvēṇa kuddhēṇa // SurSuCa.193

paḍibōhiyā u dēvēṇa vasumaī jāyativvasaṁvēgā
sūrisuhammapavattiṇipayamūlē ajjiyā jātā // SurSuCa.194

ēvaṁ ca aṇaṅgavaī vasumaïajjāi saṁyuyā tattha
mayaharicandajasāē payamūlē kuṇaï uggatavaṁ // SurSuCa.195

aha annayā kayāivi viyārabhūmiṁ gayāhiṁ ēyāhiṁ
diṭṭhaṁ taṁ ummattaṁ mihuṇaṁ bahuḍimbhapariyariyaṁ // SurSuCa.196

uggāyantaṁ bahuhā naccantaṁ dhūlidhūsarasarīraṁ
taṁ daṭṭhumaṇaṅgavaī savisāyā ēvamullavaï // SurSuCa.197


[p. 582]
ajjē! vasumaï! ēsā bhagiṇīi sulōyaṇāi aṇuharaï
jaradaṇḍikhaṇḍavasaṇā gahagahiyanarassa pāsatthā // SurSuCa.198

bhaṇiyaṁ ca vasumaīē suiraṁ nijjhāiūṇa savisāyaṁ
ēsō sō kaṇagarahō ēsāvi sulōyaṇā nūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.199

tattō gantuṁ dōhivi mahuraṁ ābhāsiyaṁ tayaṁ juyalaṁ
uggāyaï hasaï naccaï bōllaï asamañjasaṁ bahuyaṁ // SurSuCa.200

tāhē dōvi jaṇāiṁ suhammasūrissa pāyamūlammi
karuṇāparāhiṁ ajjāhiṁ tāhiṁ nīyāiṁ savisāyaṁ // SurSuCa.201

aïsayanāṇī ya guru puṭṭhō ummāyakāraṇaṁ tāhiṁ
guruṇāvi tāṇa siṭṭhō puvvuttō sayalavuttantō // SurSuCa.202

bhaṇiō ajjāhiṁ guru bhayavaṁ! jaï atthi kōvi paḍijōgō
tā ēyāṇa paüñjaha jaï picchaha kiñciṁ uvagāraṁ // SurSuCa.203


[p. 583]
tattō guruṇā tēsiṁ dinnō ummāyanāsaṇapaḍiṭṭhō
paḍijōgō jāyāiṁ dōnnivi aha satthacittāiṁ // SurSuCa.204

aha tāṇa vasumaīē siṭṭhō savvōvi puvvavuttantō
ēyassa gurupabhāvā naṭṭhō tumhāṇa ummāō // SurSuCa.205

iya sōūṇaṁ dōnnivi suhammasūrissa paramaviṇaēṇa
vandanti caraṇajuyalaṁ aha sūrī bhaṇiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.206

bhōgasuhalālasāṇaṁ paradārarayappiyāṇa purisāṇa
bahuvihaviḍambaṇāō iha paralōē ya jāyanti // SurSuCa.207

pāvanti visayatisiyā vahabandhaṇamāraṇāidukkhāiṁ
nāūṇa kumara! ēvaṁ bhōgapivāsaṁ pariccayasu // SurSuCa.208

paradārapasattēṇaṁ jaṁ pāvaṁ cikkaṇaṁ taē baddhaṁ
pupphasarisō vivāgō rajjabbhaṁsāiō tassa // SurSuCa.209


[p. 584]
ēttōvi aṇantaguṇaṁ kaḍuyavivāgaṁ phalaṁ tu paralōē
pāvijjaï duvvisahaṁ nārayatiriyāisaṁsaraṇē // SurSuCa.210

ēmāidēsaṇāē āvibbhūyammi caraṇapariṇāmē
pavvāviyaïṁ guruṇā dōnnivi nivvinnacittāiṁ // SurSuCa.211

mayahariyāē pāsē bhagiṇījuyalēṇa sañjuyā tattō
sammaṁ guruviṇayarayā sulōyaṇā kuṇaï vivihatavaṁ // SurSuCa.212

ēvaṁ candajasāē payamūlē tāṇa acchamāṇīṇaṁ
tiṇhampi hu bhagiṇīṇaṁ gayāṇi bahupuvvalakkhāṇi // SurSuCa.213

muṇiṇō kaṇagarahassavi ghaṇavāhaṇasāhuṇā samēyassa
vōlīṇāō bahuyā varisāṇaṁ kōḍikōḍīō // SurSuCa.214

aha aṇasaṇēṇa sūri kālaṁ kāūṇa bīyakappammi
jāō sasippahasurō vimāṇacandajjuṇāhivaī // SurSuCa.215


[p. 585]
ghaṇavāhaṇōvi mariuṁ jāō sāmāṇiō surō tassa
vijjuppahotti iyarā dēvī sē candarēhatti // SurSuCa.216

vasumaïajjāvi tahā puvvuvannassa tattha dēvassa
candajjuṇassa jāyā dēvī candappahā nāma // SurSuCa.217

ēttō ya sō subandhū daïyāi guruvirahasōyasaṁsattō
haṭṭagharakāṇaṇāīsu katthavi ya dhiiṁ apāvintō // SurSuCa.218

kaṇagarahassa paüṭṭhō cintēntō vivihamāraṇōvāyaṁ
rōddajjhāṇōvagaō vilavantō dīṇavayaṇillō // SurSuCa.219

rayaramiyahasiyajampiyasaharisaavaguhaṇāiṁ daïyāē
puṇaruttaṁ sumarantō jāō sō gahagahiuvva // SurSuCa.220

[tisr̥bhiḥ viśēṣakam]
taō niyayagharammi na ciṭṭhaï hiṇḍaï ujjāṇakāṇaṇaïsu
kattha gayā kēṇa hiyā kīsa nilukkā si jampantō // SurSuCa.221


[p. 586]
kaha ruṭṭhā maha sundari! jēṇa na daṁsēsi appayaṁ sigghaṁ
huṁ huṁ diṭṭhā diṭṭhā pasīya maha dēsu paḍivayaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.222

jaṁ jaṁ picchaï lōyaṁ taṁ taṁ pucchaï, taē piyā diṭṭhā?
ēmāiṁ vilavamāṇō nīhariō tāō nayarīō // SurSuCa.223

ummattayarūvēṇaṁ hiḍantō vivihagāmanayarēsu
duhiō dīṇō viyaṇō chuhāpivāsāhiṁ santattō // SurSuCa.224

kaïyāvi hu sampattō aṇēyatāvasajaṇāurē rammē
nāṇādumasayagahaṇāmmi āsamē vivihaphalapaürē // SurSuCa.225

tattha ya sē kulavaïṇā maṇayaṁ sañjāyasatthacittassa
niyadhammō parikahiō tassavi sō pariṇaō tāhē // SurSuCa.226

giṇhiya tāvasadikkhaṁ daïyāguruvirahajāyavēraggō
kayakandaphalāhārō ghōratavaṁ cariumāraddhō // SurSuCa.227


[p. 587]
dōmāsiyatēmāsiyacaümmāsāiyaṁ tavaṁ vivihaṁ
kāuṁ pabhūyakālaṁ atuṭṭavērāṇubandhō sō // SurSuCa.228

mariūṇa ya uvavannō paramāhammiyasurēsu ambarisī
uvavannamēttaō sō puvvabhavālōyaṇaṁ kuṇaï // SurSuCa.229

[yugmam]
nāūṇa puvvavaïraṁ vihaṅganāṇēṇa āsuruttō sō
cintēi kattha vaïrī sā vā maha duṭṭhamahilatti? // SurSuCa.230

dussīlā sā pāvā aṇurattaṁ taha mamaṁ pariccaïya
āsattā kaṇagarahē sacciya tā vaïriṇī paḍhamaṁ // SurSuCa.231

tārisadukkhaṁ dinnaṁ taïyā maha jēhiṁ duṭṭhasīlēhiṁ
iṇhiṁ gantuṁ dōnnivi hantavvāiṁ maē tāiṁ // SurSuCa.232

iya cintiūṇa vēgēṇa āgaō rōsaphuraphurantō sō
saṁlēhaṇasusiyaṅgō jatthacchaï kaṇagarahasāhū // SurSuCa.233


[p. 588]
dhammajjhāṇōvagayassa tassa paḍimāgayassa rayaṇīē
piuvaṇaṭhiyassa muṇiṇō ghōruvasaggē kuṇaï pāvō // SurSuCa.234

kāuṁ pisāyarūvaṁ ukkattaï nisiyakattiyāhatthō
maṁsāiṁ saruhirāiṁ sambhāriyapuvvakayavaïrō // SurSuCa.235

bhīmaṭṭahāsapuvvaṁ uḍḍhaṁ ukkhiviya khivaï khōṇīē
duvvisahagurukasāghāyatāḍaṇaṁ kuṇaï puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.236

muñcaï dhūlīvarisaṁ khaṇēṇa uvalōhapūriyaṁ kuṇaī
jalaṇavarisēṇa varisaï chindaï khaṇēṇa aṅgāiṁ // SurSuCa.237

kāūṇa hatthirūvaṁ sutikkhadantēhiṁ dēī vēhāiṁ
niyakāiyāē siñcaï lōlaï calaṇēhiṁ bhūmīē // SurSuCa.238

kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ nigghiṇahiyaēṇa tēṇa asurēṇa
muṇidēhē duvvisahā vihiyānaraōvamā viyaṇā // SurSuCa.239


[p. 589]
tīi viyaṇāi sāhū acaliyacittō pasatthasuhalēsō
dhammajjhāṇōvagaō nindantō niyayaduccariyaṁ // SurSuCa.240

kayaaṇasaṇō mahappā kālaṁ kāūṇa bīyakappammi
candajjuṇammi jāō vihuppahō nāma dēvotti // SurSuCa.241

ambarisī muṇidēhaṁ pāṇavimukkampi garuyarōsēṇaṁ
chindiya sayahā pattō sulōyaṇajjāsamīvammi // SurSuCa.242

sāvi hu pabhāyasamaē kāussaggē ṭhiyā suhajjhāṇē
sāhuṇimajjhōvagayā sumarāviyapuvvaduccariyā // SurSuCa.243

lōhamayapurisapaḍimaṁ phuliṅgajālāulaṁ viuvviya
pāvē! parapurisapiē! avagūhasu vallahaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.244

iya bhaṇiya tēṇa samayaṁ gāḍhaṁ bandhitu jaliyadaṇḍēhiṁ
haṇiūṇa takkhaṇēṇaṁ sāvi taō māriyā tēṇa // SurSuCa.245

[tisr̥bhi-rviśēṣakam]

[p. 590]
avicaliyasuddhabhāvā kālaṁ kāuṁ vihuppahasurassa
uppannā piyadēvī sayampabhā nāma tatthēva // SurSuCa.246

iya bhō naravara! daṭṭhuṁ rāgaddōsāṇa dāruṇavivāgaṁ
dūrēṇa cayasu saṅgaṁ rāgaddōsēhiṁ pāvēhiṁ // SurSuCa.247

vahaṁ vihāyā ' 'su pahiṭhṭhamāṇasō muṇīṇa sō ambarisī surāhamō
kayatthamappāṇa maṇē gaṇantō jahāgayaṁ tāhi gaō saṭhāṇayaṁ // SurSuCa.248

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē
rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi parisamappaï sulōyaṇākaṇagarahavahō nāma
surasundarīkahāē cōddasamō iha paricchēō // SurSuCa.250
