[p. 591]
[pañcadaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

aha sō kayasamaṇavahō aṁvarisī muiyamāṇasō tattha
niccaṁ nēraïyāṇaṁ kayatthaṇājāyagurutōsō // SurSuCa.1

bandhitu pāvakammaṁ taō cuō vihavapaṁsulīgabbhē
uvvannō sō tīē bahuvihakaḍukhārapāṇēhiṁ // SurSuCa.2

sāḍiyadēhō rōddaṁ jhāṇaṁ āūriūṇa narayammi
mariūṇa sattapaliō uvavannō paḍhamapuḍhavīē // SurSuCa.3

[tisr̥bhi-rviśēṣakam]
aṇuhaviya tivvadukkhaṁ niyaāukkhaē taōvi uvvaṭṭō
iha bharahē vippasuō uvavannō duggaō nāma // SurSuCa.4

dāriddadukkhataviō dikkhaṁ parivāyayāṇa ghittūṇa
kāuṁ annaṇatavaṁ ukkaḍarōsō maō tattō // SurSuCa.5


[p. 592]
dharaṇindassa u jāō sāhiyapaliyāuō mahārāō
nāmēṇa kālabāṇō divvamahāriddhisampannō // SurSuCa.6

tatthavi sumariyavaïrō uvaōgaṁ dēi tāṇa dōṇhampi
ṭhāṇaviyāṇaṇahēuṁ vibhaṅganāṇēṇa sakasāō // SurSuCa.7

tattiyanāṇābhāvāu bīyakappaṭṭhiyāṇi ēyāṇi
diṭṭhāṇi na tēṇa tahiṁ puṇaruttakaōvaōgēvi // SurSuCa.8

ēvaṁ vaccaï kālō narinda! sēsāuyassa aha tassa
bhuñjittu divvamōē thōvūṇayaaṭṭhapaliyāiṁ // SurSuCa.9

īsāṇakappavāsī vihuppahō sō surō taō caviuṁ
tuha puttō uvavannō kamalāvaïdēvikucchīē // SurSuCa.10

[yugmam]
dōhalapūraṇahēuṁ paribbhamantī purammi hatthigayā
sattamamāsē naravara! dēvī kamalāvaī ēsā // SurSuCa.11


[p. 593]
ētthantarammi diṭṭhā kaōvaōgēṇa kālabāṇēṇa
gavvaṭṭhiyaniyavaïriyadaṁsaṇasañjāyarōsēṇa // SurSuCa.12

āgamma taō turiyaṁ ahiṭṭhiō tēṇa kuñjarō sahasā
vicchōlintō lōyaṁ vēgēṇa pahāviō tēṇa // SurSuCa.13

vaḍapāyavasāhālaggaṇēṇa naravara! tumammi uttariē
gayaṇēṇa samuppaïō tēṇēva ahiṭṭhiō hatthī // SurSuCa.14

maṇisañjuyadēvikarapahāraparivihuriō gayaṁ mōttuṁ
jaṇaṇīsamayaṁ marihī gayaṇāō nivaḍiō vaïrī // SurSuCa.15

iya cintēntō naravara! kayakiccō sō surō gaō ṭhāṇaṁ
dēvīvi kuñjaragayā paḍiyā gayaṇāō saratīrē // SurSuCa.16

[yugmam]
uttariūṇa ya tattō miliyā siridattasatthavāhassa
caliyā satthēṇa samaṁ kusagganayarammi naranāha! // SurSuCa.17


[p. 594]
satthavilōvē jāē aḍavīpaḍiyāē tattha dēvīē
jāō puttō diṭṭhō kaōvaōgēṇa dēvēṇa // SurSuCa.18

aha puṇaravi sō dēvō vaïraṁ sariūṇa nigghiṇasahāvō
sampattō vēgēṇaṁ dēvīpāsammi gururōsō // SurSuCa.19

niuṇaṁ jōyantēṇavi pabhūyakālāō pāva! diṭṭhō si
kāhāmi vaïraantaṁ aṇuhava duvvihiyaphalamiṇhiṁ // SurSuCa.20

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇēṇaṁ pasuttakamalāvaīē aṅkāō
naravara! sō tuha puttō hariō surakālabāṇēṇa // SurSuCa.21

gahiūṇa ya taṁ bālaṁ cintēi surō kiliṭṭhapariṇāmō
mārēmi imaṁ sattuṁ iṇhiṁ maliūṇa hatthēhiṁ // SurSuCa.22

khaṇḍāṇi ahaṁ kāuṁ karēmi kiṁvā disābaliṁ ahavā
acchōḍēmi silāē tilaṁ tilaṁ kiṁ nu chindāmi? // SurSuCa.23


[p. 595]
ēvaṁ hi kaē ahavā na hōjja viyaṇā pabhūyakālīyā
maraṇāu takkhaṇēṇaṁ imassa avvattacittassa // SurSuCa.24

tā gantūṇaṁ katthavi muñcāmi amāṇūsammi ṭhāṇammi
taṇhāchuhābhibhūō marihī sayamēva dukkhēṇa // SurSuCa.25

iya cintiūṇa mukkō vēyaḍḍhasilāyalammi viyaṇammi
sō tuha puttō naravara! surōvi pattō niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.26

naravara! acchaü ēyaṁ kahēmi annaṁ kahantaraṁ tāva
īsāṇāō caviō vijjuppahō ēttha vēyaḍ̣dhē // SurSuCa.27

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīi purē ramaṇīē rayaṇasañcaē pavarē
pavaṇagaïkhayaraputtō uvavannō baülavaïyāē // SurSuCa.28

nāmēṇa cittavēgō ēttō dēvīvi candarēhā sā
caviūṇa ya uppannā nayarē sirikuñjarāvattē // SurSuCa.29


[p. 596]
khayarassa amiyagaïṇō piyāi bhajjāi cittamālāē
aïvallahā u dhūyā nāmēṇaṁ kaṇagamālatti // SurSuCa.30

[catasr̥bhiḥ kalāpakam]
ēttō ya puvvabhaṇiō sulōyaṇāiṇa āsi jō māyā
vasudattō nāmēṇaṁ sōvi hu bhamiūṇa saṁsārē // SurSuCa.31

uppannō vēyaḍ̣dhē gaṅgāvattammi khayararāyassa
sirigandhavāhaṇassa u puttō mayaṇāvalīē ō // SurSuCa.32

nahavāhaṇotti nāmaṁ variyā aha tassa kaṇagamālā sā
hariūṇa ya pariṇīyā chalēṇa sā cittavēgēṇa // SurSuCa.33

[tisr̥bhiḥ viśēṣakam]
nahavāhaṇēṇa baddhō sō khayarō nāgiṇīi vijjāē
āṇīyā niranayarē vilavantī kaṇagamālāvi // SurSuCa.34

pariyāyantarapattaṁ aṇicchamāṇimpi icchaē ramiuṁ
bhagiṇimpi piccha naravara! ēsō annāṇadōsēṇa // SurSuCa.35


[p. 597]
iya naravara! saṁsārē annāṇandhēhiṁ ēttha jīvēhiṁ
bhagiṇīvi ahilasijjaï dhūyā suṇhā va jaṇaṇī vā // SurSuCa.36

bhagiṇīvi hōi bhajjā, piyāvi puttō, suyāvi jaṇaṇitti
bhajjāvi jattha māyā dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa // SurSuCa.37

ēyaṁ ca tujjha naravara! dhaṇadēvēṇēva sāhiyaṁ puvvaṁ
sahasā surēṇaṁ puṇaravi uvaṇīyā cittavēgassa // SurSuCa.38

bahuvihavijjāhiṁ samaṁ jāō khayarāhivō taō ēsō
bhuñjaï daïyāē samaṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē tattha visayasuhaṁ // SurSuCa.39

candajjuṇōvi dēvō caïūṇaṁ uttarāē sẹ̄dhīē
nayarammi caramacañcē cittagaī nāma uvavannō // SurSuCa.40

candappahāvi dēvī jāyā ya piyaṅgumañjarī tassa
bhajjā sō tīi samaṁ bhuñjaï māṇussaē mōē // SurSuCa.41


[p. 598]
tassa ya uttarasẹ̄dhī samayaṁ vijjāhiṁ cittavēgēṇa
dinnā siṇēhasāraṁ iya tē acchanti vēyaḍ̣dhē // SurSuCa.42

puvvabhavabbhāsāō siṇēhasārāṇa tāṇa dōṇhampi
vōlīṇō bahukālō visayasuhaṁ aṇuhavantāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.43

aha annayā kayāī sahiō daïyāē kaṇagamālāē
khayarō sa cittavēgō aṭṭhāvayavandaō caliō // SurSuCa.44

bharahanarēsarakāriyajiṇindapaḍimāō tattha bhattīē
vandittu paḍiniyattō piccaï taṁ bālayaṁ tattha // SurSuCa.45

vēyaḍḍhavaṇaniuñjaṁ ujjōyantaṁ sadēhadittīē
galabaddhaaṅgulīyagavihūsiyaṁ lōyaṇāṇanda // SurSuCa.46

daṭṭhūṇa aṅgulīyaganivēsiyaṁ taṁ maṇiṁ sa vimhaïō
bhaṇaï ya piē! sa ēsō divvamaṇī suravaradinnō // SurSuCa.47


[p. 599]
jassa pabhāvāu tayā bhuyaṅgaparivẹ̄dhiōvi na maō haṁ
tā kēṇa ēsa baddhō imasma bālasma galayammi? // SurSuCa.48

ahavā rakkhāhēuṁ nūṇaṁ jaṇaṇīē jāyamittassa
baddhō havējja tattō kēṇavi hariūṇa iha mukkō // SurSuCa.49

tā gēṇha piē! ēyaṁ hōu aputtāē ēsa tuha puttō
sōcciya nūṇaṁ hōhī surajīvō ēsa uppannō // SurSuCa.50

gahiūṇa tayaṁ naranāha! dōvi pattāiṁ niyayanayarammi
kāuṁ vaddhāvaṇiyaṁ payāsiyaṁ sayalalōyassa // SurSuCa.51

jāō u kaṇagamālāi guttagabbhāi sampayaṁ puttō
uciyasamayammi vihiyaṁ nāmaṁ sē mayarakēutti // SurSuCa.52

vijjāharindabhavaṇē ēvaṁ vaḍḍhaï narinda! tuha puttō
ēttō ya tassa dēvī sayampabhā dēvalōgāō // SurSuCa.53


[p. 600]
caïūṇa samuppannā ēsā surasandarī mahārāya!
aha kamasō vaḍḍhantī ēsāvi hu jōvvaṇaṁ pattā // SurSuCa.54

[yugmam]
hariūṇa jēṇa nīyā taïyā khayarēṇa rayaṇadīvaṁmi
sō ya sulōyaṇajammē haridattō āsi sē jaṇaō // SurSuCa.55

iya piccha viruvattaṁ bhavassa dukkhāgarassa naranāha!
icchaï bhōē bhōttuṁ jaṇaō dhūyāē saha jattha // SurSuCa.56

kāuṁ pisāyarūvaṁ tēṇēva surēṇa kālabāṇēṇa
avahariuṁ vijjāō chụ̄dhō jalahimmi tuha puttō // SurSuCa.57

surasundarimpi tattō jāyapaōsō sa jāva gayaṇēṇa
avaharaï tāva naravara! sañjāō cavaṇasamaō sē // SurSuCa.58

tassa ya cuyassa ēsā paḍiyā gayaṇāō ēttha ujjāṇē
dhaṇadēvajāṇavattaṁ pattaṁ puṇa tujjha taṇaēṇa // SurSuCa.59


[p. 601]
jāyammi jāṇabhaṅgē pāviyaphalahō samuddamajjhammi
diṭṭhō piyaṁvayāē aha nīō tēṇa saṭṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.60

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ ēyaṁ sāhiyaṁ naravarinda!
milihī puṇa ajjēva ya viyālasamayammi sō tujjha // SurSuCa.61

sōūṇa sūrivayaṇaṁ rāyā surasundarī ya dēvī ya
pattā ya gurupamōyaṁ parisā savvāvi saṁviggā // SurSuCa.62

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ jāva ya puttēṇa saṅgamō tāva
kāhāmi taō sahalaṁ maṇuyattaṁ tuha pāsammi // SurSuCa.63

ētthantarammi paṇamiya dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhaguruṁ
taïyā pallībhaṅgē jāē ghōrammi saṅgāmē // SurSuCa.64

kaṇagavaīi balēṇaṁ haēsu naṭṭhēsu bhillasuhaḍēsu
kiṁ jāyaṁ tumhāṇaṁ kahavā samaṇattaṇaṁ pattaṁ? // SurSuCa.65


[p. 602]
bhaṇiyaṁ guruṇā nisuṇasu taïyā samaraṅgaṇammi jujjhantō
saraniyaravarisavihuriyadēhō paḍiō dharāvaṭṭhē // SurSuCa.66

diṭṭhō ya taṁ paēsaṁ samāgaēṇaṁ sucittavēgēṇaṁ
khayarēṇa tēṇa nīō siṇēhasārēṇa vēyaḍ̣dhē // SurSuCa.67

vihiō ya takkhaṇaṁ ciya ōsahisāmatthaō ahaṁ sattha
dinnā ya pavaravijjā puvvuvagāraṁ sarantēṇa // SurSuCa.68

pannattīnāmēṇaṁ vihiṇā sā sāhiyā maē tattha
tattō samāgaō haṁ siddhatthapurammi khayarajuō // SurSuCa.69

kaṇagavaīi samēyaṁ surahaṁ niddhāḍiūṇa dēsāō
siddhatthapurē jāō rāyā haṁ tāhi dhaṇadēva! // SurSuCa.70

parivāliūṇa rajjaṁ kaïvi hu varisāṇa kōḍikōḍīō
ahisiñciūṇa rajjē jayasēṇaṁ niyayaputtamahaṁ // SurSuCa.71


[p. 603]
dhaṇavāhaṇakēvaliṇō payamūlē jāyativvasaṁvēgō
pavvaïō saha pañcahiṁ saēhiṁ vararāyaüttāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.72

[yugmam]
abbhasiyasāhukiriō jāō kamasō ya bārasaṅgaviū
dhaṇavāhaṇakēvaliṇā ahisittō tāhi sūripaē // SurSuCa.73

kāūṇa ya sēlēsiṁ khaviuṁ cattāri sēsakammāiṁ
sō amha guru pattō nivvāṇaṁ bhadda! dhaṇadēva! // SurSuCa.74

iya supaïṭṭhasūrī jāva ya parikahaï niyayavuttantaṁ
tāvaya gayaṇāhintō ēgō khayarō samōinnō // SurSuCa.75

kayasūripaṇāmēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ aha tēṇa viṇayapaṇaēṇa
vēyaḍ̣dhāō vaddhāvaō ahaṁ āgaō tumha // SurSuCa.76

saṁsiddhasayalavijjō pavvaïumaṇēṇa cittavēgēṇa
ahisittō niyayapaē tumha suō mayarakēutti // SurSuCa.77


[p. 604]
sō khayaravindasahiō tumhāṇaṁ pāyavandaō ēhī
iya nayarē ajjēva ya iya tumha piyaṁ nivēēmi // SurSuCa.78

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisavasūsasiyarōmakūvēṇa
dinnaṁ aṅgavilaggaṁ pabhūyadavvaṁ ca sē rannā // SurSuCa.79

āṇandiyā dēvī ōyāraṇayaṁ karēi khayarassa
aṅgammi amāyantaṁ harisaṁ surasundarī pattā // SurSuCa.80

paṇamiya sūriṁ rāyā puraṁ paviṭṭhō sapariyaṇō tāhē
āṇavēi kuṭṭavālē sigghaṁ nayaraṁ visōhēha // SurSuCa.81

avaṇīya kayavarāō sigghaṁ sāravaha sayalasaraṇīō
mayaṇāhikuṅkumummīsiēṇaṁ nīrēṇa siñcēha // SurSuCa.82

viraēha sarasatāmarasamīsakusumōvayāramaṇavajjaṁ
pacchāiyagayaṇāō karēha varahaṭṭasōhāō // SurSuCa.83


[p. 605]
païmandiraṁ ca bandhaha vandaṇālāō viviharūvāō
dhavalaharamāliyāō vicittavannēhiṁ bhūsēha // SurSuCa.84

nimmalajalapaṇḍipunnē kañcaṇakalasē ṭhavēha dārēsu
ubbhēha vēñjayantīō bhavaṇadārēsu vivihāō // SurSuCa.85

varaphullatōraṇāiṁ mañcāiṁ karēha ēyamaggammi
gōrōyaṇasiddhatthayaduvvājuyasōtthiyālihaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.86

annaṁ ca ēvamāī karēha kārēha paüralōēṇa
iya tē rannā bhaṇiyā savisēsaṁ kariumāḍhattā // SurSuCa.87

halluttāvalapaürē iō taō sañcarantabhiccayaṇē
antēurammi rannō piyaṁvayā jhatti sampattā // SurSuCa.88

surasundarīi diṭṭhā uvagụ̄dhā harisanibbharaṅgīē
dinnāsaṇōvaviṭṭhā aha puṭṭhā puvvavuttanttaṁ // SurSuCa.89


[p. 606]
bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē atthi tumaṁ tāva tēṇa ukkhittā
vēyālēṇa ahaṁ puya paḍiyā mucchāi bhūmīē // SurSuCa.90

tattō khaṇantarāō mucchāviramammi sōgasantattā
hā! kattha gayā bhagiṇī kīsa na sō āgaō bhāyā? // SurSuCa.91

nūṇaṁ tēṇa pisāēṇa hōjja vihiyaṁ asōhaṇaṁ kimpi
ēmāi cintayantī gavēsiuṁ tāhi laggā haṁ // SurSuCa.92

aha tattha rayaṇadīvē samantaō hiṇḍiūṇa gayaṇatthā
bhamiyā lavaṇasuddē palōyayantī tumaṁ bahuhā // SurSuCa.93

phalayavilaggō diṭṭhō samuddamajjhammi vīinivahēṇa
tōlijjamāṇadēhō aha bhāyā mayarakēutti // SurSuCa.94

ukkhiviūṇa tattō nīō jiṇamandirammi aha tammi
puṭṭhō ya kaha ṇu paḍiō samuddamajjhammi, aha tēṇa // SurSuCa.95


[p. 607]
vēyāladaṁsaṇāī vijjācchēyāisayalavuttantō
kahiō aha maha tēṇavi bhaṇiyaṁ surasundarī kattha? // SurSuCa.96

bhaṇiyaṁ maēvi bhāōya pisāyarūvēṇa sāvi avahariyā
iya sōuṁ gurumōggarahaüvva sō mucchiō sahasā // SurSuCa.97

pāsaṭṭhiyakhayarēhiṁ sīyalapavaṇāikaraṇaō bahuhā
satthīkaōvi kumarō mucchijja jāhiṁ puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.98

tāhē gantuṁ tāyassa sāhiō nahayarēhiṁ vuttantō
taṁ sōuṁ gurusōgō tāōvi samāgaō tattha // SurSuCa.99

kahakahavi hu saṇṭhaviuṁ nīō vēyaḍḍhapavvaē kumarō
bahavē khayarakumārā āṇattā tāhi tāēṇa // SurSuCa.100

[yugmam]
chakkhaṇḍabharahamajjhē gāmāgarapaṭṭaṇēsu bhamiūṇaṁ
surasundarivuttantaṁ āṇēha jahaṭṭhiyaṁ sigghaṁ // SurSuCa.101


[p. 608]
iya bhaṇiuṁ paṭṭhaviyā bahavē vijjāharā ō tāēṇa
kumarōvi viṇōijjaï tāyādēsāu mittēhiṁ // SurSuCa.102

piyavirahasōyasampīḍiyassa kumarassa kaïvi divasāṇi
vaccanti jāva tāva ya annammi diṇammi tattha purē // SurSuCa.103

sampattō caünāṇī cāraṇasamaṇō duvālasaṅgaviū
damaghōsō nāmēṇaṁ sahasambavaṇē samōsariō // SurSuCa.104

[yugmam]
tassa ya vandaṇahēuṁ viṇiggaō kumarasañjuō tāō
vandittā uvaviṭṭhō mahivaṭṭhē pariyaṇasamēō // SurSuCa.105

saṁsārarunda sāyaruttāraṇajāṇavattasaṅkāsō
muṇiṇāvi tēsiṁ dhammō aṇavajjō kahiumāḍhattō // SurSuCa.106

sārīramāṇasāṇaṁ dukkhāṇaṁ khayaṁ samicchamāṇēhiṁ
jīvāṇa abhayadāṇaṁ maṇavaïkāēhiṁ kāyavvaṁ // SurSuCa.107


[p. 609]
jaramaraṇadukkhapaüraṁ saṁsāraṁ tē taranti līlāē
saccamaṇavajjavayaṇaṁ sayāvi bhāsanti jē jīvā // SurSuCa.108

dōgaccavāhijaramaraṇasōyapiyavippaōgavasaṇāiṁ
jāyanti na jīvāṇaṁ jē ō adinnaṁ na giṇhanti // SurSuCa.109

vajjanti jē abambhaṁ jīva maṇavayaṇakāyajōgēhiṁ
niddhūyasayalakammā vayanti tē sāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.110

dhammōvagaraṇavajjaṁ pariggahaṁ jē kayāi na dharēnti
tē bhavajalahiṁ tariūṇaṁ janti ayarāmaṇaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.111

ēmāisamaṇadhammē kahiē samaṇēṇa jiṇavaruddiṭṭhē
patthāvaṁ nāūṇaṁ kumarēṇa muṇī imaṁ puṭṭhō // SurSuCa.112

bhayavaṁ! vijjācchēō kīsa kaō majjha tēṇa dēvēṇa?
muṇiṇāvi vaïrakāraṇamakkhāyaṁ tassa nīsēsaṁ // SurSuCa.113


[p. 610]
taṁ muṇivayaṇaṁ sōuṁ uppannaṁ mayarakēukumarassa
jāīsaraṇaṁ sahasā īhāpōhaṁ karintassa // SurSuCa.114

sariūṇa ya puvvabhavaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa ēvamēyanti
hariūṇa kattha mukkā bhayavaṁ! surasundarī tēṇa? // SurSuCa.115

tattō muṇiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ cuyassa dēvassa tassa hatthāō
gayaṇāō nivaḍiyā sā paḍiyā kusumāyarujjāṇē // SurSuCa.116

hatthiṇapurammi acchaï sampaï sā tujjha kumara! jaṇaṇīē
kamalāvaīi pāsē tattō kumarēṇa vajjariyaṁ // SurSuCa.117

kiṁ maha na hōi jaṇaō ēsō jaṇaṇīva kaṇagamālatti
tattō muṇiṇā siṭṭhō surāvahārāivuttantō // SurSuCa.118

aha cittavēgarannā bhaṇiyaṁ muṇivayaṇabhāviyamaṇēṇa
kiṁ kumara! taṁ na sumarisi jaṁ taïyā dēvabhāvammi // SurSuCa.119


[p. 611]
tumaē ciya maha siṭṭhaṁ avahariō puvvavēriyasurēṇa
tō cittavēgakhayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi? // SurSuCa.120

ēyaṁ taṁ sañjāyaṁ tā puṇaravi putta! tāō vijjāō
sāhēsu, cayasu sōgaṁ niyayapaē jēṇa ṭhāvēmi // SurSuCa.121

mōttūṇa visayasaṅgaṁ bhavabhamaṇubbhantamāṇasā amhē
icchāmō pavvajjaṁ niravajjaṁ sampayaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.122

iya surasundari! jāva ya tāō vajjaraï tāva sahasatti
damaghōsavandaṇatthaṁ dharaṇindō āgaō tattha // SurSuCa.123

daṭhṭhūṇamayarakēuṁ suiraṁ nijjhāiūṇa vajjaraï
jāṇasi kumāra! sō haṁ puvvabhavē āsi tuha jaṇaō // SurSuCa.124

bhīmarahō nāmēṇaṁ majjha ya aïvallahō tumaṁ āsi
kusumāvalisambhūō kaṇagarahō nāma puttotti // SurSuCa.125


[p. 612]
sañjāē ummāē sabhāriyāē tumammi nīsariē
niuṇaṁ gavēsiōvi hu jāhē sampāviō na tumaṁ // SurSuCa.126

tāhē tuha lahubhāyaṁ vajjarahaṁ ṭhāviūṇaṁ rajjammi
vēraggabhāviyamaṇō pavvaïō gurusamīvammi // SurSuCa.127

[yugmam]
kāūṇaṁ pavvajjaṁ sōhammē suravarō ahaṁ jāō
sattapaliōvamāū tattō caïūṇa iha bharahē // SurSuCa.128

campāē puravarīē rannō dahivāhaṇassa bhajjāē
kusumasirīē gabbhē uvavannō dāragattāē // SurSuCa.129

[yugmam]
jāō ya uciyasamaē nāmaṁ ca kayaṁ pahaṅkarō majjha
ētthantarami nihaō majjapasattō piyā majjha // SurSuCa.130

rajjāhilāsivimalēṇa mantiṇā 'hiṭṭhiyaṁ sayaṁ rajjaṁ
naṭṭhā bhaēṇa jaṇaṇī timāsajāyaṁ mamaṁ ghittuṁ // SurSuCa.131

[yugmam]

[p. 613]
pattā vijayapurammī rannō saṅkhassa bhāuṇō pāsē
jōvvamapattō ya ahaṁ saṅkhēṇa samaṁ gaō tattha // SurSuCa.132

kāūṇa ya saṅgāmaṁ vimalaṁ haṇiūṇa samaramajjhammi
campāē niyarajjē jāō rāyā ahaṁ tāhē // SurSuCa.133

vimalataṇayāvi naṭṭhā gantuṁ nayarammi hatthisīsammi
ōlaggiuṁ payattā jiyasattuṁ nāma naranāhaṁ // SurSuCa.134

balagavviō ya ahayaṁ samayaṁ hatthīhiṁ tattha khēllāmi
tēṇa ya majjha pasiddhī jāyā savvēsu dēsēsu // SurSuCa.135

natthi pahaṅkaratullō mahābalō ēttha bharahakhittammi
ruṭṭhaṁ mattagaïndaṁ dharēi jō ēgabāhāē // SurSuCa.136

rajjaṁ pabhūyakālaṁ ahampi campāi tattha kāūṇaṁ
sugurusamīvē buddhō rajjē ṭhaviūṇa niyaputtaṁ // SurSuCa.137

[yugmam]

[p. 614]
jāō samaṇō tattō abhiggahō ērisō maē gahiō
gurumūlē jājīvaṁ māsaṁ māsāu bhōttavvaṁ // SurSuCa.138

aha annayā kayāivi viharantō hatthisīsaē pattō
pāraṇadiṇē paviṭṭhō bhikkhaṭṭhā tattha nayarammi // SurSuCa.139

aha dittasaṇḍapaḍipēlliō ahaṁ nivaḍiō dharāvaṭṭhē
hasiō vimalassa suēhiṁ pāvakammēhiṁ puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.140

taṁ katthaṁ balaṁ sampaï gaïndapaḍipēlliṇēkkarasiyaṁ tē?
iya bhaṇamāṇā tāhē hantuṁ uddhāiyā savvē // SurSuCa.141

piivēraṁ sumarantā samāgayā laüḍapattharavihatthā
daṭṭhūṇa ya tē kuviō ahampi annāṇadōsēṇa // SurSuCa.142

ghēttūṇa khambhamēgaṁ tattō uddhāiō iya bhaṇantō
rē! rē! sīhassa balaṁ khaṇḍijjaï kiṁ siyālēhiṁ? // SurSuCa.143


[p. 615]
jaïvi ahaṁ kisadēhō tahavi hu gammō na tumha tā hōha
khaṇamēgaṁ saṁmuhayā piumaggaṁ jēṇa pēsēmi // SurSuCa.144

hayamahiē tē kāuṁ pacchāyāvāō aṇasaṇaṁ kāuṁ
lajjāē duccariyaṁ na ya taṁ siṭṭhaṁ gurujaṇassa // SurSuCa.145

tattō appaḍikkantō khaṇḍiyacaraṇō maō taō kumara!
uvavannō dharaṇindō sampaï sō haṁ ihāyāō // SurSuCa.146

tā mā kuṇasu visāyaṁ maē vidinnāō tujjha sijjhantu
pannattimāiyāō asāhiyāōvi vijjāō // SurSuCa.147

iya tavvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ mahāpasāutti jampiuṁ kumarō
karakaramalamaülasōhō paḍiō dharaṇindapāēsu // SurSuCa.148

nahayarasandōhasamanniēṇa tāēṇa kayamahāmahimō
dharaṇindō sampattō saṭṭhāṇaṁ pariyaṇasamēō // SurSuCa.149


[p. 616]
vijjāharasahiēṇaṁ mahāvibhūīi cittavēgēṇa
ahisittō niyayapaē kumarō taha cittagaïṇāvi // SurSuCa.150

aha khayaracakkavaṭṭī jāō vēyaḍḍhapavvaē ēsō
sayalakhayarēhiṁ tattō dinnāō niyayadhūyāō // SurSuCa.151

tō bhaṇaï mayarakēū na tāva pariṇēmi annakannāō
jāva na sā pariṇīyā dhūyā naravāhaṇanivassa // SurSuCa.152

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō iṇhiṁ gantuṁ kusagganayarammi
naravāhaṇaṁ vimaggiya varēmi surasundari tumha // SurSuCa.153

tō bhaṇaï mayarakēū ēvaṁ sigghaṁ karēsu, amhēvi
tāyāṇunnaṁ ghēttuṁ gacchāmō hatthiṇapurammi // SurSuCa.154

vandāmō payajuyalaṁ adiṭṭhapuvvāṇa jaṇaṇijaṇayāṇaṁ
iya bhaṇiē uppaïō gayaṇēṇaṁ bhāṇuvēgō sō // SurSuCa.155


[p. 617]
aha mayarakēu-rāyā bhaṇiyō tāēṇa putta! ajjēva
kijjaü vigāla-samaē sōhaṇa-vēlā-muhuttammi // SurSuCa.156

jaṇāṇi-jaṇāyāṇa daṁsaṇamiya bhaṇiē sayalakhayaraniyarēṇa
aha kāuṁ pāraddhā takkhaṇamāgamaṇa-sāmaggī // SurSuCa.157

[yugmam]
ētthantarammi ahamavi tāyaṁ āpucchiūṇa vēgēṇa
surasundari! tuha pāsē paütti-kahaṇatthamāyāyā // SurSuCa.158

ēvaṁ piyaṁvayāē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa dāsa-cēḍīhiṁ
gantuṁ rannō siṭṭhaṁ aha rāyā harisa-paḍihatthō // SurSuCa.159

varagīyavihiyavāiyaravēṇa varavilayanaṭṭajuttēṇaṁ
kayavivihakōuēhiṁ ya jaṇayantō paüra-saṅkhōhaṁ // SurSuCa.160

nīhariō nayarāō caüraṅgabalēṇa gayavarārụ̄dhō
savvāē vibhūīē antōgaïyāē taṇayassa // SurSuCa.161


[p. 618]
vijjāharasēnnampi hu ummiṭṭaṁ tāva gayaṇamaggammi
dhaya-chatta-cindha-paüraṁ-nāṇaviha-vāhaṇārūḍhaṁ // SurSuCa.162

tanmajjhē ya vimāṇaṁ puraō dhāvantakhayarasaṅghāyaṁ
maṇi-maya-khambha-saṇāhaṁ vicittavararūvayāinnaṁ // SurSuCa.163

khayarēsamayarakēū puraō daṭṭhūṇa naravaïṁ sahasā
avayariuṁ gayaṇāō paḍiō pāēsu jaṇayassa // SurSuCa.164

aha amarakēu rāyā taṇayaṁ āliṅgiūṇa sasiṇēhaṁ
āṇanda-bāha-salilaṁ muñcantō cumbaï sirammi // SurSuCa.165

sambhāsiūṇa savvaṁ jahārihaṁ pūiūṇa khayara-varē
aha nayarammi paviṭṭō thuvvantō māgaha-saēhiṁ // SurSuCa.166

kayamaṅgalōvayārō pavēsiō niyayamandirē rannā
sēsakhayarāṇa dinnā jahōciyaṁ pavara-āvāsā // SurSuCa.167


[p. 619]
kaïvaya-khayara samēō nīō antēurammi nara-vaïṇā
suyadaṁsaṇūsūyāē paḍiō jaṇaṇīi calaṇēsu // SurSuCa.168

kōmalakarēhiṁ ghēttuṁ nivēsiō tīi niyayaücchaṅgē
āliṅgiō ya bahusō ya cumbiō uttimaṅgammi // SurSuCa.169

āṇanda-vāha-salilaṁ muñcanti bhaṇaï vajjaghaḍiyaṁ tē
jaṇaṇīi putta! hiyayaṁ jīvaï jā tujjha virahammi // SurSuCa.170

tō bhaṇaï mayarakēu kiṁ kīraï amba! viviha-laliyassa
vihiṇō paravvasāṇaṁ jāyaï jaṁ ērisaṁ dukkhaṁ // SurSuCa.171

parithūla-muttiyāvali-vihiya-caükkammi tāhi ṭhaviūṇa
siṁhāsaṇamaṇavajjaṁ maṇi-rayaṇa-pahāhiṁ vicchuriyaṁ // SurSuCa.172

tatthūvaviṭṭhassa taō maṅgallāiṁ kayāiṁ taṇayassa
dēvīē suya-saṅgama-harisa-vasubbhinna-pulayāē // SurSuCa.173


[p. 620]
taṁ kimpi āsi taïyā tēsiṁ taṇayassa saṅgamē sōkkhaṁ
kahiṁupiṁ jaṁ na tīraï saṅkāsaṁ muttisōkkhēṇa // SurSuCa.174

ittō ya kusaggapurē gantūṇaṁ bhāṇuvēga-khayarēṇa
naravāhaṇassa rannō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantā // SurSuCa.175

naravāhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēya-nimittaṁ surakkhiyā ēsā
maggantāṇavi puvviṁ na ya dinnā anna-rāīṇa // SurSuCa.176

tīē jamma-diṇēcciyaṁ āiṭṭhaṁ āsi divva-nāṇīhi
ēsā kannā hōhī vijjāhara-cakkiṇō bhajjā // SurSuCa.177

santtujaya-ruddhassiha maha dinnaṁ jēṇa jīviyaṁ taïyā
surasundarīvi dinnā tassa maē kimiha pucchāē? // SurSuCa.178

vāhariō jōisiō bhaṇiō nīsēsa-dōsa-parisuddhaṁ
vīvāhalaggadivasaṁ sāhēsu nirūviūṇamha // SurSuCa.179


[p. 621]
tēṇavi bhaṇiyaṁ nara-vara! iō diṇāō taïjja divasammi
aïsōhaṇaṁ tu laggaṁ rayaṇīē carimajāmammi // SurSuCa.180

ērisa-guṇa-sañjuttaṁ annaṁ laggaṁ na labbhaē sigghaṁ
rannāvi taō bhaṇiyaṁ āsannamiṇaṁ tu kahamēttha // SurSuCa.181

sakkijjaï nīsēsā kāuṁ vīvāhakaraṇasāmaggī
tō bhāṇuvēga! sahasu kō kīraï iha uvāutti? // SurSuCa.182

aha tēṇavi paḍibhaṇiyaṁ gammaü naranāha! hatthiṇapurammi
tattha ya sampattāṇaṁ savvampi hu sundaraṁ hōhī? // SurSuCa.183

aha bhāṇuvēga - vihiē divva-vimāṇammi pariyaṇasamēō
takkāluciyaṁ ghittuṁ sayalaṁ vīvāhaüvagaraṇaṁ // SurSuCa.184

hatthiṇapurammi pattō ēttō cittagaïcittavēgāvi
vijjāharōha-sahiyā pattā vinnāyavuttantā // SurSuCa.185


[p. 622]
aha amarakēū rāyā tēsiṁ kāūṇa sayala-paḍivattiṁ
bahukhajjapijjajuttaṁ kāraï vīvāha-sāmaggiṁ // SurSuCa.186

niya-kula-kamāgaēṇaṁ vihiṇā pattammi laggadiyahammi
āṇandiyapaüra-jaṇaṁ naccantavilāsiṇisaṇāhaṁ // SurSuCa.187

vajjanta-vajja-āujja-gahira-saṁsadda-pūriya-diyantaṁ
vattaṁ pāṇi-ggahaṇaṁ mahāvibhūīē aha tēsiṁ // SurSuCa.188

samuciyapaḍivattīē khayarā saṁmāṇiyā narindēṇa
dinnaṁ ca mahā-dāṇaṁ paürāī bhōjiō lōō // SurSuCa.189

jiṇa-mandirēsu vihiyā mahimā paramāyarēṇa savvēsu
jiṇa paḍimāṇaṁ vatthāēhiṁ viviyā mahā-pūyā // SurSuCa.190

vara-vattha-patta-kambala-asaṇāīēhiṁ samaṇasaṅghōvi
savvōvāhi-visuddhēhiṁ pūiō paramabhattīē // SurSuCa.191


[p. 623]
gaya-turaya-pavara-sandaṇa-gāmāgara-nagara-paṭṭaṇāīyaṁ
dinnaṁ sāmantāṇaṁ jahōciyaṁ tattha naravaïṇā // SurSuCa.192

aha annādiṇē rāyā mahāvibhūīi pariyaṇasamēō
surissa vandaṇatthaṁ nīhariō khayarasañjuttō // SurSuCa.193

abhivandiūṇa sūriṁ avasēsa-tavassiṇē ya savvēvi
uvaviṭṭhā aha guruṇā kahiō jiṇadēsiō dhammō // SurSuCa.194

aha vandiūṇa sūriṁ dēvī kamalāvaī imaṁ bhaṇaï
bhayavaṁ! annammi bhavē āsi kayaṁ ki maē pāvaṁ? // SurSuCa.195

suyavirahajaṇiyadukkhaṁ jassa vasāō sudussahaṁ pattaṁ?
aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ dēvāṇupiē! nisāmēsu // SurSuCa.196

jō sō 'varakaṅkāē ammaḍa vaṇiotti āsi mē kahiō
maṇḍaṇa-pabhiīṇa piyā acchutta-bhāriyā-sahiō // SurSuCa.197


[p. 624]
sō bhamiūṇa bhavōhaṁ maru-dēsē harisaūya gāmammi
mēharō ajjuṇa nāmō ihēva bharahammi uvavannō // SurSuCa.198

acchuttāvi hu tattō bhamiuṇa bhavēsu viviha-rūvēsu
mahilā ajjuṇagassa u bandhusirī nāma uvavannā // SurSuCa.199

avarōppara piīē kisi--kamma-rayāṇa vaccaē kālō
dōṇhavi dayāparāṇaṁ payaīē taṇu-kasāyāṇāṁ // SurSuCa.200

pattē pāusa-kālē paḍiē aha paṇiyammi paürammi
niya palihaīi dōhivi kisi-kammaṁ kāumāḍhattaṁ // SurSuCa.201

tattha ya ēgō kamalō sagabbha hariṇīē saṅgaō vasaï
palihaïparipērantē caraï taṇaṁ tīi sañjuttō // SurSuCa.202

aha annayā paviṭṭhaṁ khittē daṭṭhūṇa hariṇajuyalaṁ taṁ
ajjuṇaō hakkantō caliō nīsāraṇaṭhṭhāē // SurSuCa.203


[p. 625]
ajjuṇa-bhaēṇa hariṁṇī guru-hārā vēga-dhāviyā sahasā
sañjāya-pasava-samayā viyaṇā-vihalaṅghalā paḍiyā // SurSuCa.204

naṭṭhō sāraṅgōvi hu puṇō puṇō ajjuṇaṁ niruvintō
daïyā-viōga-vihuriya-hiyaō guru-sōya-santattō // SurSuCa.205

karuṇāparēṇa nīyā hariṇīvi hu ajjuṇēṇa niyaṭhāṇaṁ
sīyalajalēṇa sittā mucchā-viramē pasūyā ya // SurSuCa.206

jāyaṁ kōḍḍāvaṇayaṁ hariṇa-silimba tu muddhaḍa-sahāvaṁ
hariṇīi vaṭṭiyaṁ taṁ dinnō ya thaṇō taō tassa // SurSuCa.207

daṭṭhūṇa taṁ suruvaṁ vilāsa-susiṇiddha-nayaṇa-sōhillaṁ
bandhusirīē bhaṇiyaṁ maha hōi khillaṇaṁ ēyaṁ // SurSuCa.208

tattō ya vāma-pāē baddhaṁ taṁ kōmalāi rajjūē
hariṇīvi vigaya-viyaṇā bhaēṇa naṭṭhā tayaṁ mōttuṁ // SurSuCa.209


[p. 626]
miliyā kamalassa taō puṇō puṇō ēi tammi ṭhāṇammi
sisu-nēhāō, na puṇō alliyaï bhaēṇa sā tattha // SurSuCa.210

uvviggamaṇā varaī silimba-nēhēṇa vimaṇa-dummaṇiyā
na caraï taṇaṁ na ya piyaï pāṇiyaṁ bhamaï khijjantī // SurSuCa.211

bīyadiṇēvi hu hariṇiṁ durụdhullanti tahēva daṭṭhūṇaṁ
jāya-karuṇāē mukkō sa silimbō bandhusiriyāē // SurSuCa.212

aha sō bandhaṇa-mukkō gantuṁ māūṇa sabhaya-nēhāē
miliō daṭṭhūṇa tayaṁ sāraṅgī nivvuyā jāyā // SurSuCa.213

majjhima-guṇa-sañjuttō dayāpabhāvāō ajjuṇō tattō
mariūṇa samuppannō ēsō rāyā amarakēū // SurSuCa.214

bandhusirīvi hu tattō nibaddha-maṇuyāuyā mayā pacchā
iha uppannā bhaddē! dēvī kamalāvaī taṁ si // SurSuCa.215


[p. 627]
jāyā ya tumha dōṇhavi puvvabhavabbhāsaō garuya-pīī
jīva-dayā-karaṇāō viulā bhōgā samaṇupattā // SurSuCa.216

kamalō hariṇīē samaṁ viōiō jaṁ ca tattha khaṇamēgaṁ
takkammudayā rannō jāō tumhaṁ saha viōgō // SurSuCa.217

jaṁ ca kaō ēṇīē virahō līvēṇa aṭṭha pāhariō
tattha ya taē nibaddhaṁ kammaṁ suya-viraha-dukkha-phalaṁ // SurSuCa.218

udayāō tassa jāō virahō taṇaēṇa jāya-mēttēṇa
khīṇaṁ ca tayaṁ sampaï aṭṭhahiṁ lakkhēhiṁ varisāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.219

khaṇamitta-sañciyampi hu dēi vivāgaṁ sudīha-kālīyaṁ
suhamasuhaṁ vā kammaṁ bhāva-visēsēṇa jīvāṇa // SurSuCa.220

iya nāūṇa vivāgaṁ pamāya- nivvattiyassa kammassa
dūrēṇa kamma-bandhassa kāraṇaṁ muyaha jattēṇa // SurSuCa.221


[p. 628]
iya guru-vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ parisā savvāvi tattha saṁviggā
dikkhābhimuhī jāyā bhīyā saṁsāra-dukkhāṇa // SurSuCa.222

naravaï-dēvīṇa puṇō visuddha-lēsāhiṁ vaṭṭamāṇāṇa
jāyaṁ jāī-saraṇaṁ īhāpōhaṁ karēntāṇa // SurSuCa.223

sumariya-puvva-bhavāṇaṁ āgaya-saṁvēga-bhāviya-maṇāṇa
caraṇāvaraṇa-khayāō sañjāō caraṇa-pariṇāmō // SurSuCa.224

tattō ya amarakēū puttaṁ ahisiñciūṇa rajjammi
takkāluciyaṁ kāuṁ karaṇijjaṁ tivva-saṁvēgō // SurSuCa.225

aṇusāsiūṇa puttaṁ āpucchittā ya pariyaṇaṁ sayalaṁ
kamalāvaīē sahiō pavvaïō guru-samīvammi // SurSuCa.226

siridēvaṁ niya-puttaṁ kuḍumba-cintāē saṇṭhavēūṇa
rannā saha pavvaïō dhaṇadēvō bhāriyā-sahiō // SurSuCa.227


[p. 629]
khayarōvi cittavēgō cittagaï-ppamuha-khayara-sañjuttō
nivvinna-kāma-bhōgō pavvaïō sūri-pāsammi // SurSuCa.228

khayarīvi kaṇagamālā pavvaïyā sūri-vayaṇa-paḍibuddhā
sahiyā piyaṅgumañjarimāīhiṁ pabhūya-khayarīhiṁ // SurSuCa.229

naravāhaṇōvi rāyā rajjaṁ dāūṇa mayarakēussa
pavvaïō paya-bhūlē kēvaliṇō suppaïṭṭhassa // SurSuCa.230

rannā saha pavvaïyā khayara-narindāṇa dasa sahassāō
kamalāvaï-pamuhāṇaṁ vīsa-sahasāiṁ mahilāṇa // SurSuCa.231

iya tīsa-sahassāiṁ samayaṁ pavvāviyāiṁ kēvaliṇā
saṁnihiya-dēvayāē uvaṇīyaṁ tēsiṁ muṇi-ligaṁ // SurSuCa.232

tā bhaṇaï mayarakēū caraṇaṁ paḍivajjiuṁ asattō mhi
gihi-pāuggaṁ dhammaṁ tā bhayavaṁ! amha sāhēsu // SurSuCa.233


[p. 630]
bhaṇiyaṁ guruṇā nisuṇasu thūlaga-jīvāṇa niravarāhāṇa
nisiranti jē na daṇḍaṁ tēvi hu pāvinti nivvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.234

thūlamasaccaṁ bhāsaṁ maṇa-vaï-kāēhiṁ jē na kappēnti
sura-maṇuēsara-sōkkhaṁ bhōttūṇa vayanti tē mōkkhaṁ // SurSuCa.235

thūlamadattaṁ vajjanti jē sayā tiviha-karaṇa-jōgēhiṁ
savvatthakkhaya-vittā hōūṇa vayanti tē siddhiṁ // SurSuCa.236

santōsō sa-kalattē ahavā para-dāra-vajjaṇamudāraṁ
kāuṁ suraṅgaṇāō bhōttūṇa vayanti nivvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.237

icchā-parimāṇaṁ sēviūṇa laddhūṇa viula-riddhīō
dēva-narēsara-bhāvē kamēṇa gacchanti nivvāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.238

ēmāi-vittharēṇaṁ gihi-dhammē sāhiyammi kēvaliṇā
tō bhaṇaï mayarakēū hōmi samatthō imaṁ kāu // SurSuCa.239


[p. 631]
tattō ya guru-samīvē surasundarī-mayarakēu-pamuhēhiṁ
sammatta-rayaṇa-mūlō sāvaga-dhammō-pavannōti // SurSuCa.240

aha cittavēga-pamuhā muṇiṇa sūrissa pāya-mūlammi
gahaṇāsēvaṇa-rūvaṁ sikkhaṁ abbhasiumāḍhattā // SurSuCa.241

kamalāvaï-pamuhāō ajjāō suvvayāi-gaṇiṇīē
pāsammi sāhu-kiriyaṁ sikkhanti paḍhanti aṅgāiṁ // SurSuCa.242

chaṭṭhaṭṭhama-dasama-duvālasāiṁ vivihaṁ tavaṁ pakuvvanti
viṇayaṁ guruṇa sammaṁ vēyāvaccaṁ ca savvēvi // SurSuCa.243

aha cittavēga-muṇiṇā cōddasa-puvvāiṁ tattha pạdhiyāiṁ
bhinnakkhara-puvvadharō jāō acirēṇa kālēṇa // SurSuCa.244

aha suppaïṭṭha-sūriṁ ṭhaviūṇa cittavēga-muṇiṁ
kaya-aṇasaṇō mahappā nivvāṇamaṇuttaraṁ pattō // SurSuCa.245


[p. 632]
aha cittavēga-sūrī gāmāgara-nagara-maṇḍiyaṁ vasuhaṁ
viharaï-suppaḍibaddhō bōhintō bhaviya-jaṇa-niyaraṁ // SurSuCa.246

ajjāvi kaṇagamālā suvvaya-gaṇiṇīē sagga-pattāē
ahisittā mayahariyā sāhūṇi-gaṇa-bahu-mayā-tattha // SurSuCa.247

bōhintō bhavva-lōyaṁ tava-sūsiya-taṇū catta-nīsēsa-rāgō
sajjhāṇaḍ̣dhō muṇīṇaṁ sa-samaya-vihiṇā sāraṇāī karintō
sūrīsō cittavēgō samaṇa-parivuḍō dēsayantō jaṇāṇaṁ
dhammaṁ titthēsaruttaṁ viharaï vasuhaṁ sañjamujjōya-juttō // SurSuCa.248

sāhu-dhaṇēsara-viraïya-subōha-gāhā-samūha-rammāē
rāgāggi-dōsa-visahara-pasamaṇa-jala-manta-bhūyāē // SurSuCa.249

ēsōvi hu khayarāhiva-cārittāsēvaṇō parisamattō
surasundarī-kahāē pannarasō iha paricchēō // SurSuCa.250



---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 633]
[|| ṣōḍaśaḥ paricchēdaḥ]

rāyā vi mayarakēū pariṇittā khayara-dinna-kannāō
dāūṇa naha-yarāṇaṁ jahōciyaṁ gāma-nagarāiṁ // SurSuCa.1

āṇā-niddēsakarē kāumasēsaddha-bharaha-rāyāṇō
nīsēsa-dēsa-visaraṁ vihāya gaya-ḍamara-cōra-bhayaṁ // SurSuCa.2

uttuṅga-dhavala-maṇahara-cēiya-bhavaṇēhiṁ maṇḍiyaṁ kāuṁ
āriya-dēsa-samubbhava-gāmāgara-nagara-sandōhaṁ // SurSuCa.3

kara-bhara-suṅka-vimukkaṁ sāvaya-visaraṁ karittu nīsēsaṁ
ucchāittā savvē jiṇa-sāsaṇa-saṅgha-paḍiṇīē // SurSuCa.4


[p. 634]
akkhaliyaṁ ca vihāraṁ viyarittā muṇi-jaṇassa dēsēsu
sāhaṁmmiya-vacchallē niya-sāmantē niōittā // SurSuCa.5

kāuṁ sattāgārāiṁ vivaha-ruvāiṁ ṭhāṇa-ṭhāṇēsu
dijjanta-jantu-patthiya-samattha-vara-vatthu-satthāiṁ // SurSuCa.6

pālēi rajjamaṇavajja-kajja-paya-pālaṇikka-vāvāraṁ
kaya-duṭṭha-dhaṭṭha-ulluṇṭha-vaṇṭha-kaya-ugga-niggahaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.7

paṇaya-jaṇa-jaṇiya-tōsaṁ vasīkayāsēsa-sattu-santāṇaṁ
āṇandiya-jiya-satthaṁ kaya-suttha-samattha-dugga-pahaṁ // SurSuCa.8

iya mayarakēu-rannō surasundari-pamuha-dēvi-jutassa
dhammattha-kāma-sāraṁ visaya-suhaṁ aṇuhavantassa // SurSuCa.9


[p. 635]
kaïyāvi hu jiṇa-bhavaṇē nimmala-pasaranta-dasa-disi-maūhē
vimala-silā-yala-ghaḍiē bhattīē kārayantassa // SurSuCa.10

annōnna-vanna-kaliē nimmala-maṇi-rayaṇa-hēma-nimmaviē
saṁsāra-jalahi-majjanta-jantu-santaraṇa-bōhitthē // SurSuCa.11

vara-vinnāṇiya-nivahēṇa dinna-bahu-davva-jāya-harisēṇaṁ
kaïyāvi hu jiṇa-bimbē vara-ruvē kārayantassa // SurSuCa.12

āgama-vihiṇā kaya-satta-rakkhaṇaṁ vihiya-saṅgha-vara-pūyaṁ
jiṇa-bimbāṇa païṭṭhaṁ kaïyāvi hu āisantassa // SurSuCa.13

ghaṇasāra-sāra-gōsīsa-mīsa-hariyandaṇāi-davvēhiṁ
kuṇamāṇassa kayāivi jiṇinda-paḍimā-samālabhaṇaṁ // SurSuCa.14

nisiranta-bahala-parimala-dasaddha-vannēṇa kusuma-niyarēṇa
kaïyāvi bahu-viyappaṁ jiṇa-pūyaṁ virayamāṇassa // SurSuCa.15


[p. 636]
pavara-vara-paṭṭaṇuggaya-aṇaggha-samuhaggha-vasaṇa-sōhillaṁ
ullōcaṁ jiṇa-bhavaṇē kaïyāvi hu kārayantassa // SurSuCa.16

mōiya cārāgāraṁ jiṇinda-vara-mandirēsu sāṇandaṁ
kaïyāvi hu raha-jattaṁ jattēṇa pēcchamāṇassa // SurSuCa.17

jattā-samaya-samāgaya-kiviṇāṇāhāi-dīṇa-lōyassa
vara-variya-viyaraṇāō maṇōrahē pūrayantassa // SurSuCa.18

raha-jattāgaya-sāhammiyāṇa kaïyāvi guru-pamōēṇa
bhōyaṇa-vatthābharaṇāi-dāṇaō tappamāṇassa // SurSuCa.19

antēura-majjha-gayassa viviha-līlā-vilāsa-kaliyāhiṁ
bhajjāhiṁ saha kayāivi suraha-suhaṁ sēvamāṇassa // SurSuCa.20

pattaṭṭha-vara-vilāsiṇi-vihiya-vivihaṅgahāra-sōhillaṁ
kaïyāvi hu vara-gēyaṁ pēkkhaṇayaṁ pēkkhamāṇassa // SurSuCa.21


[p. 637]
annampi ēvamāiṁ visiṭṭha-lōyassa saṁmayaṁ jaṁ jaṁ
puvva-purisāṇucinnaṁ aviruddhaṁ niyaya-vaṁsassa // SurSuCa.22

niyaya-avatthā-sarisaṁ salāhaṇijjaṁ ca sajjaṇa-jaṇassa
lōyāgamāviruddha aṇucinna puvva-rāīhiṁ // SurSuCa.23

niya-niya kālē savvaṁ taṁ taṁ kamasō pakuvvamāṇassa
suha-sāgarāvagāḍhassa rāiṇō dukkha-rahiyassa // SurSuCa.24

surasundarīē samayaṁ siṇēha-sārassa puvva-lakkhāiṁ
bōlīṇāiṁ kaïvi hu jiṇa-sāsaṇa-bhatti-juttassa // SurSuCa.25

aha annayā kayāivi rayaṇīē rāiṇā saha pasuttā
pāhāuya-vēlāē picchaï surasundarī suviṇaṁ // SurSuCa.26

kila kōvi kasiṇa-sappō ḍasiūṇa mamaṁ narinda-sañjuttaṁ
maha udarammi paviṭṭhō ēyaṁ daṭṭhūṇa paḍibuddhā // SurSuCa.27


[p. 638]
bhīyā jāva vicintaï na sundaraṁ handi! sumiṇamēyanti
tā kiṁ amaṅgalēṇaṁ imiṇā siṭṭhēṇa-nara-vaïṇō // SurSuCa.28

tāva paḍu-paḍaha-paḍirava-payaḍiya-gīya-jjhuṇīhiṁ saṁvaliyaṁ
takkāla-niuttēhi pahayaṁ pāhāuyaṁ tūraṁ // SurSuCa.29

tassavaṇā paḍibuddhō cintiya cittammi pañca-navakāraṁ
kāuṁ sarīra-sōyaṁ takkāluciyaṁ mayarakēū // SurSuCa.30

maṇi-rayaṇa-paṇaṭṭha-tamaṁ jugāi-jiṇa-paḍima-maṇḍiyaṁ viyaḍaṁ
cēiya-bhavaṇaṁ gantuṁ vihiṇā pūittu jiṇa-bimbaṁ // SurSuCa.31

cī-vandaṇaṁ karittā paccakkhāṇaṁ ca taduciyaṁ kāuṁ
vāra-vilāsiṇi-paürē atthāṇē tāhi sampattō // SurSuCa.32

takkālamaṅgalīē vara-vāra-vilāsiṇīhi vihiyammi
khaṇamēgaṁ atthāṇaṁ dāūṇa samuṭṭhiō rāyā // SurSuCa.33


[p. 639]
vijjā-vihiya-vimāṇō surasundarī-pamuha-bhāriyā-sahiō
himagiri-siharē khayarōha-saṅgaō sō gaō jhatti // SurSuCa.34

kīḍā-nimittamaha sō aṇēga-gōsīsa-sāhi-saṅkinnē
ōinnō ujjāṇē nandaṇa-vaṇa-sarisa-sōhillē // SurSuCa.35

maṇimaya-silā-yalēsu kayalī-vaṇa-parigaēsu rammēsu
ukkiṭṭha-gīya-vāiya-pēkkhaṇayakkhitta-cittassa // SurSuCa.36

siri-mayarakēu-khayarāhivassa antēurāi-sahiyassa
himavanta-pavvaē aha pattō majjhaṇha-samaütti // SurSuCa.37

bhōyaṇa-vēlā vaṭṭaï vinnattō tattha sūvayārēṇa
pūiya-jiṇinda-bimbō vihiṇā cī-candaṇaṁ kāuṁ // SurSuCa.38

nahayara-niyara-parigaō bhōttūṇamaṇaggha-pavaramāhāraṁ
surasundarīē sahiō kayalī-harayaṁ aha paviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.39


[p. 640]
sayaṇīyammi pasuttō suraya-suhaṁ sēviūṇa khaṇamēgaṁ
paḍibuddhāē surasundarīi aha nara-vaī bhaṇiō // SurSuCa.40

piyayama! tāva khaṇantaramacchāmō vibuha-jaṇa-viṇōēṇa
tā vaḍhasu kiñci paṇhōttaranti, aha nara-vaī bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.41

kō jāi nahē, ahilasaï kiṁ jaṇō, kattha vaccaï sasaṅkō?
païdiyahaṁ saï kammi va surasundarī! salahijjaē pīī? // SurSuCa.42

surasundarīi bhaṇiyaṁ tantāvaliyaṁ kahēsu maṇa-daïya!
bhaṇaï nivō 'tītaṁ tē, laddhaṁ dēvīi ‘vī-saṁ-bhē’ // SurSuCa.43

bhaṇiyaṁ rannā turiyaṁ laddhaṁ paṇhōttaraṁ imaṁ dēvi!
tā bhaṇasu tumaṁ sampaï dēvīē tāhi saṁlattaṁ // SurSuCa.44


[p. 641]
kō tīsāē paḍhamō kammi va rāyā viṇassaï viṇaṭṭhō
kiṁ sakkayaṁ vōlīṇaṁ kassa va daïō tuhaṁ nāha! // SurSuCa.45

āmantijjaü lacchī kā vā gēyammi sūsarā hōi
tumaē vidinna paṇhōttarassa tantāvalī kā vā? // SurSuCa.46

bhaṇiyaṁ rannā avvō! dēvī paṇhōttarēsu aïkusalā
jaṁ tantāvaliyāvi hu vihiyā paṇhōttaraṁ jhati? // SurSuCa.47

vatthaṁ duhāṇulōmēṇa taha ya paḍilōmaō bhavē vatthaṁ
aṇulōmēṇa samatthaṁ caüha kayaṁ dēvi tī-taṁ-tē // SurSuCa.48

puṇō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ—

kiṁ savva-jaṇō icchaï sakkandaṇa-paharaṇaṁ ca bōhēsu
pahiēhiṁ kiṁ va ghēppaï sāhijjaü dēvi! ēyampi? // SurSuCa.49


[p. 642]
surasundarīi bhaṇiyaṁ pavaḍḍhamāṇakkharaṁ imaṁ dēva!
‘saṁ-ba-la’ muttaramētthaṁ rannā bhaṇiyaṁ piē! bhaṇasu // SurSuCa.50

āmantijjaü lacchī kattha vasantāṇa nāsaē buddhī
kattha na nāsaï suhaḍō piyayama! sāhēsu ēyaṁ bhē? // SurSuCa.51

bhaṇiyaṁ rannā sundari! paḍilōmaṁ vaḍḍhamāṇa vannamiṇaṁ
‘saṁ-gā-mē’ iti, tattō, rannā bhaṇiyaṁ piē! bhaṇasu // SurSuCa.52

kiṁ dharaï punna-candō, kiṁvā icchanti pāmarā khittē
āmantasu anta-guruṁ kiṁvā sōkkhaṁ puṇō sōkkhaṁ? // SurSuCa.53

daṭṭhūṇa kiṁ visaṭṭaï kusuma-vaṇaṁ jaṇiya-jaṇa-maṇāṇandaṁ
kaha ṇu ramijjaï paḍhama para-mahilā jāra-purisēhiṁ? // SurSuCa.54


[p. 643]
surasundarīi cintiya bhaṇiyaṁ ēyampi jāṇiyaṁ dēva!
duvatthaṁ du-samatthaṁ uttaramētthaṁ ‘sa-saṁ-kaṁ’ tē // SurSuCa.55

iya paṇhōttara-bhindaṇa-karaṇikka-rasāṇavagga-hiyayāṇa
dēvī-nivāṇa tahiyaṁ samāgaō kasiṇa-guru-sappō // SurSuCa.56

aha puvva-vēriēṇavi sappēṇaṁ tēṇa dōṇṇivi jaṇāiṁ
duṭṭhēṇa paṭṭhi-dēsē daṭṭhāiṁ garuya-rōsēṇa // SurSuCa.57

sappō sappotti payampirīi dēvīi kalayalaṁ sōccā
aha khagga-vagga-hatthā samāgayā aṅga-rakkhā sē // SurSuCa.58

bhuyagōvi hu bhaya-sambhama-vēvira-dēhō kayāvarāhotti
nāsantō haṇiūṇaṁ khaḍākhaṇḍīkaō tēhiṁ // SurSuCa.59

tayaṇantaramucchaliō mahanta-kōlāhalō pariyaṇassa
samayaṁ ciya niva-dēvī-dēha-ṭṭhiya-visa-viyārēṇa // SurSuCa.60

taō. 


[p. 644]
vāhippanti pahāṇā gāruḍiyā gāruḍēsu pattaṭṭhā
kīranti manta-jāvā āṇāvijjanti mūlīō // SurSuCa.61

abhimantiya-tōēṇaṁ dijjantacchinna-salila-dhārāō
bajjhanti kaṇḍayāiṁ paüṇīkīranti agayāī // SurSuCa.62

iya gāruḍiyasaṇāhē nahayaranivahammi āulībhūē
ghaya-sittēvva huyāsē pabalībhūē visa-viyārē // SurSuCa.63

naranāhō avvattaṁ divva-maṇiṁ āṇahatti bhaṇamāṇō
pikkhantāṇaṁ khayarāṇa tattha jāō vigayaciṭṭhō // SurSuCa.64

ētthantarammi vinnāya-vaïyarā rāiṇō piyā bhagiṇī
pabhaṇaï piyaṁvayā vacca vacca lahu bāhuvēga! tumaṁ // SurSuCa.65

gantūṇa bhāṇuvēgassa nandaṇaṁ candavēgakhayarēsaṁ
maha vayaṇēṇa maggasu nayarē siri kuñjarāvattē // SurSuCa.66


[p. 645]
bhaṇasu ya jō sō vijjā-pasāhaṇujjaēṇa rakkhaṭṭhā
tumaē nīō puvviṁ divva-maṇī maha samīvāō // SurSuCa.67

sō ̣dhōijjaü sigdha iya bhaṇiō sō gaō turiya-vēgō
gantuṁ khaṇantarāō samāgaō candavēgēṇa // SurSuCa.68

khayarēṇa samaṁ tāhē maṇi-salila-payāṇa-puvvayaṁ vihiyaṁ
nīsēsa-visa-vigārēṇa vajjiyaṁ juvalayaṁ jugavaṁ // SurSuCa.69

tuṭṭhō nahayara-vaggō piyaṁvayā taha ya pariyaṇa-samaggā
rāyāvi bhava-sarūvaṁ cintētō āgaō nagaraṁ // SurSuCa.70

aviya. 

ēttō tattō vivihāvayāhiṁ ghippanta-jīva-sārāṇaṁ
saraṇaṁ natthi jiyāṇaṁ jiṇinda-dhammaṁ pamōttūṇa // SurSuCa.71

sūla-ahi-visa-visūiya-pāṇiya-satthaggi-sambhamēhiṁ ca
dēhantara-saṅkamaṇaṁ karēi jīvō muhuttēṇa // SurSuCa.72


[p. 646]
tā ērisammi cavalammi jīviē visaya-mōhiyā jīvā
mōha-mahā-gaha-ghatthā tahavi hu dhammē pamāyanti // SurSuCa.73

aha nahayara-nivahēṇaṁ vōlīṇā āvayatti tuṭṭhēṇaṁ
gayapuramāgantūṇaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ kayaṁ rannō // SurSuCa.74

sura-sundarīvi dēvī diyahaṁ taṁ cēva paḍhamayaṁ kāuṁ
gabbhavaī sañjāyā ninnēhā niyaya-daïyammi // SurSuCa.75

aviya. 

jaha jaha vaḍḍhaï gabbhō taha taha dēvīvi gabbha-māhappā
niṭṭhūra-hiyayā cintaï mārēmi nivaṁ sahatthēṇa // SurSuCa.76

taō. 

ābhāsiyāvi rūsaï niṭṭhuramullavaï nēcchaē bhōgaṁ
daṭṭhōṭṭha-bhiuḍi-bhīmā diṭṭhammi parammuhā ṭhāī // SurSuCa.77

taṁ vivarīya-sarūvaṁ daṭṭhūṇa piyaṁvayā bhaṇaï bhaddē
kīsa tumē ninnēhā bahu mannasi nēva rāyāṇaṁ? // SurSuCa.78


[p. 647]
surasudaṁrīi bhaṇiyaṁ dōsēṇa imassa pāva-gabbhassa
maha maḍḍāi paōsō uppajjaï pāva-kammāē // SurSuCa.79

tā gantuṁ nara-vaïṇō sāhijjasu jēṇa annahābhāvaṁ
na karēi majjha uvariṁ viyaliya-nēhaṁ mamaṁ daṭṭhuṁ // SurSuCa.80

annaṁ ca bhaṇasu daïyaṁ daṭṭhavvā nēva pāva-kammā haṁ
jāva na jāi pasavō pāvaya-gabbhassa gabbhassa // SurSuCa.81

gantuṁ piyaṁvayāē siṭṭhaṁ savvampi mayarakēussa
taṁ sōuṁ rāyāvi hu vimhiya-cittō imaṁ bhaṇaï // SurSuCa.82

avvō! jā maha virahaṁ dēvī nimisampi sọ̄dhumasamatthā
sā gabbhassa pabhāvā adaṁsaṇaṁ niṭṭhurā mahaï // SurSuCa.83

tā kiṁ na hōjja so cciya puvva-viruddhō subandhu-jīvō 'yaṁ
bhaviyavvāyā-vasēṇaṁ uvavannō dēvī-kucchīē? // SurSuCa.84


[p. 648]
ēmāi cintayantō dēvīē adinna-daṁsaṇō rāyā
niya-vaïriya-saṅkāē jāvacchaï dūmiō cittē // SurSuCa.85

tāva ya dēviṁ daṭṭhuṁ asuhajjhavasāya-dāruṇaṁ rannō
mannē piya-mittā iva sāma-muhā sē thaṇā jāyā // SurSuCa.86

nara-vara-vara-suha-saṅgama-suha-virahukkaṇṭhiyēva dēvīē
ujjhiya sāma-cchaya gaṇḍa-yalaṁ paṇḍuraṁ jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.87

savvēhivi garuyattaṁ pattaṁ na maētti laddha-patthāvaṁ
vitthariyaṁ sē udaraṁ nara-vaïṇō vēri-uggamaṇē // SurSuCa.88

daṭṭhūṇava udarassavi garuyattaṁ jāya-tivva-abhimāṇaṁ
vaḍḍhaï niyamba-bimbaṁ mā jiṇijjatti cintāē // SurSuCa.89

kamasō pasavaṇa-samaē sampattē sasaharammi mūlatthē
pāva-ggahāvalōiya-laggē laggāi viṭṭhīē // SurSuCa.90


[p. 649]
surasundarī-pasūyā mahayā kicchēṇa dārayaṁ tāhē
hittha-hiyaēṇa rannā vāhariō pavara-jōisiō // SurSuCa.91

puṭṭhō ya kahasu taṇayassa guṇa-gaṇaṁ ēyassa samaya-jāyassa
ghūṇiya-sirēṇa tēṇavi bhaṇiyaṁ nara-nāha! nisuṇēsu // SurSuCa.92

ērisa-samaē jāō jaṇayassa na sundarō havaï bālō
vaḍḍhantō piu-gēhē haṇaï kulaṁ rāya-lacchiṁ ca // SurSuCa.93

dēva! na rūsēyavvaṁ jāva tumaṁ nēva pēcchasē ēyaṁ
tāvacciya tuha kusalaṁ pāṇāṇavi saṁsaō diṭṭhē // SurSuCa.94

rannā bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddaya! kō kōvō ēttha vatthu-paramatthē
sattha-samatthiya-majjhattha-tatta-buddhīhiṁ kahiyammi? // SurSuCa.95

kaya-uvayārammi gaē sa-ṭṭhāṇaṁ aha nivēṇa vāhittā
bhaṇiyā suhāsaṇatthā piyaṁvayā sōya-taviēṇa // SurSuCa.96


[p. 650]
paḍhama-suya-jamma-diyahē harisō kira hōi jaṇaṇi-jaṇayāṇaṁ
taṁ puṇa divva-vasēṇaṁ amhaṁ annārisaṁ jāyaṁ // SurSuCa.97

tā bhaddē! taṁ gacchasu bālaṁ ghittūṇa dhāvi-sañjuttaṁ
niya-sāsuraē sigghaṁ vuḍ̣dhiṁ tatthēva nēyavvō // SurSuCa.98

tīē tahatti bhaṇiuṁ nīō suranandaṇammi nayarammi
siṭṭhō tavvuttantō khayarāhiva-niyaya-daïyassa // SurSuCa.99

jalaṇappaha-khayarāhiva-piya-bhajjā-cittalēha-taṇayassa
jalakantassa u savvō tēṇavi bahu manniyā ēsā // SurSuCa.100

tāhē jalakantēṇavi jammaṇa-mahimāi-sayala-kāyavvaṁ
kāūṇa kayaṁ nāmaṁ suha-diyahē mayaṇavēgotti // SurSuCa.101

kamasō pavaḍḍhamāṇō pattō sō jōvvaṇaṁ mayaṇavēgō
aviṇīō dussīlō akacca-niraō kayagghō ya // SurSuCa.102


[p. 651]
jalakanta-khayara-puttō kañcaṇadēvīi gabbha-sambhūō
jalavēgō sē mittō jāō sahapạdhiya-ramiutti // SurSuCa.103

surasundarīi kaïyāvi sīha-sumiṇēṇa sūiō taṇaō
uppannō bīōvi ya suha-tihi-nakkhatta-jōgammi // SurSuCa.104

ruvēṇa aṇaṅga-samō sūrō cāī piyaṁvaō dakkhō
nāmēṇa 'ṇaṅgakēū suviṇīō jaṇaṇi-jaṇayāṇa // SurSuCa.105

kamasō jōvvaṇa-pattō juvarāya-payammi ṭhāviō ēsō
sāhiya-vijjō viyaraï icchāē khayara-nayarēsu // SurSuCa.106

mahu-māsē sampattē rāyā antēurēṇa sañjuttō
aṭṭhāhiya-mahimaṭṭhā pattō vēyaḍḍha-kūḍammi // SurSuCa.107

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ pattā vēyaḍḍha-vāsiṇō khayarā
gandhavva-naṭṭha-paürā vaṭṭaï aṭṭhāhiyā jāva // SurSuCa.108


[p. 652]
tāva ya gaṅgāvattāu āgayā khayara-niyara-paricariyā
vara-rūvavaī kannā aṇaṅgavēgatti nāmēṇa // SurSuCa.109

diṭṭhā sā juvarannā tīēvi siṇiddha-diṭṭhi-pāēṇa
viddhō aṇaṅga-bāṇēhiṁ jhatti āyallayaṁ pattō // SurSuCa.110

pucchaï aṇaṅgakēū vasantanāmaṁ vayasiyaṁ, bhadda!
kassēsā vara-vilayā kassa va dhūyā ō kiṁnāmā? // SurSuCa.111

bhaṇiyaṁ vasantaēṇaṁ gaṅgāvattammiṁ āsi vara-rāyā
siri-gandhavāhaṇotti ya mahilā mayaṇāvalī tassa // SurSuCa.112

tīē ya tiṇṇi taṇayā paḍhamō nahavāhaṇō, mayarakēū
taïō ya mēhanāō vijjā-bala-gavviā sūrā // SurSuCa.113

piuṇā saha pavvaïē jāē nahavāhaṇē, mayarakēū
jāō rāyā sōvi ya viyaṇē vijjaṁ pasāhintō // SurSuCa.114


[p. 653]
piuṇā tujjha pamāēṇa māriō chinna-vaṁsa-jālīē
guru-karuṇāgaēṇaṁ tuha piuṇā ṭhāviō rajjē // SurSuCa.115

ēsō u mēhanāō, dinnāṇi pabhūya-gāma-nayarāṇi
cittagaï-khayara-dhūyā dinnā paümōyarā pavarā // SurSuCa.116

tīē ēsā dhūyā kannā nāmēṇa mayaṇavēgatti
ēyaṁ ca kumara! maggaï piyaṁyamāē piyayamassa // SurSuCa.117

jalakantassa u puttō kañcaṇadēvīi kucchi-sambhūō
jalavēgō, kiṁ dinnā navitti sammaṁ na yāṇāmi // SurSuCa.118

iya sōūṇa kumārō vajjaraï vasanta! suṇasu maha vayaṇaṁ
ēyaṁ kannā-rayaṇaṁ viṇā u maha natthi jīyāsā // SurSuCa.119

jaï jīviēṇa kajjaṁ ahayaṁ vā vallahō jaï ya tujjha
tā gantūṇaṁ tāyaṁ taha bhaṇasu jahā lahuṁ lahaï // SurSuCa.120


[p. 654]
aha sō bāla-vayaṁsō nāūṇaṁ nicchayaṁ kumārassa
gantūṇa ya taṁ rannō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhaē savvaṁ // SurSuCa.121

rannāvi mēhanāō vāhariūṇaṁ vimaggiō kannaṁ
tēṇavi ya tassa dinnā viyasiya-vayaṇāravindēṇa // SurSuCa.122

gaṅgāvattē vattaṁ pāṇiggahaṇaṁ mahā-vibhūīē
nīyā ya mayaṇavēyā kumarēṇaṁ niyaya-nayarammi // SurSuCa.123

sōūṇa pāṇiggahaṇaṁ jalavēgō dumiō ya cittēṇa
kannā-viōya-duhiō dukkhaṁ naraōvamaṁ pattō // SurSuCa.124

ruṭṭhō aṇaṅgakēussa cintaē viviha-māraṇōvāē
laddhōvāō gantūṇa sāhaē mayaṇavēgassa // SurSuCa.125

mitta! tumaṁ na viyāṇasi jēṭṭha-suō taṁ hi mayarakēussa
surasundarīi puttō ihāṇiō janma-divasammi // SurSuCa.126


[p. 655]
avamanniō si mittaya! jaṇaēṇa tumaṁ suniṭṭhura-maṇēṇa
tujjha kaṇiṭṭhō bhāyā juvarajjē jēṇa ahisittō // SurSuCa.127

māyā-vittāṇi ya tujjha daṁsaṇaṁ kahavi nēya icchanti
vēriya-sarisaṁ dhārēnti jēṇa dūra-ṭṭhiyaṁ niccaṁ // SurSuCa.128

na ya lahasi tumaṁ gantuṁ tīi disāēvi jattha tuha jaṇaō
tā piu-paribhūēṇaṁ vayaṁsa! kiṁ tujjha jīēṇa? // SurSuCa.129

ēmāi-vayaṇa-mahu-sappi-hōmiō tassa guru-paōsaggī
jaliō jamma-parampara-nibaddha-sambandha-jōgēṇa // SurSuCa.130

aha sō rōsa-vasaṭṭō pabhaṇaï daṁsēhi vēriyaṁ piyaraṁ
daṁsēmi avannāē jēṇa phalaṁ tassa pāvassa // SurSuCa.131

bhaṇaï taō jalakantō sō tujjha piyā aṇēga-khayarēhiṁ
rakkhijjaï tikkhāliya-khagga-gayāvagga-hatthēhiṁ // SurSuCa.132


[p. 656]
rūva-parivattiṇiṁ mitta! gēṇha ēyaṁ kulāgayaṁ vijjaṁ
jēṇa jahicchiya-atthassa sāhagō hōsi aïrēṇa // SurSuCa.133

dinnā ya tēṇa vijjā rannaṁ gantūṇa sāhiyā kamasō
gayapuramāgamma ṭhiō cēḍī-rūpēṇa dēvi-gihē // SurSuCa.134

surasundarīi cēḍī laliyaṁ hariūṇa dūra-dēsammi
mōttūṇa tīi rūvēṇa sō ṭhiō niva-vahaṭṭhāē // SurSuCa.135

kasiṇāhi-ḍasaṇa-divasāu nara-vaī divva-aṅgulīēṇa
kara-saṇṭhiēṇa ciṭṭhaï surayāiyaṁ pamōttūṇaṁ // SurSuCa.136

aha annayā narindō bhōttūṇaṁ khayara-kañcui-samaggō
dēvī-gharaṁ paviṭṭhō diṭṭhō cēḍīi pāvāē // SurSuCa.137

mōttūṇaṁ aṅgarakkhē bāhiṁ dēvīē vihiya-maṅgillō
vāsa-harammi paviṭṭhō rayaṇa-vicittammi dēvi-juō // SurSuCa.138


[p. 657]
parihāsāihiṁ khaṇaṁ acchittā suraya-sēvaṇārambhē
millaï aṅgulīyaṁ dēvī ābharaṇa-ṭhāṇammi // SurSuCa.139

pāraddhammi ya suraē sahasā āyaḍ̣dhiūṇa karavālaṁ
cēḍī-vēsēṇa ṭhiō taṇaya-kayantō tahiṁ pattō // SurSuCa.140

jaṇaṇī-surayāsattaṁ jaṇayaṁ ghāēumujjaō taṇaō
hā! hā! kaṭṭhaṭhamakajjaṁ dhiratthu saṁsāra-vāsassa // SurSuCa.141

jāṇatō niya-puttō piyaraṁ ghāēi jaṇaṇi-sañjuttaṁ
dōsa-paraddhō jamhā ahō! durantō imō dōsō // SurSuCa.142

rāgāō hōi dōsō dōsāō hōi vēra-sambandhō
vērāō pāṇi-ghāō tattō guru-kamma-bandhotti // SurSuCa.143

kamma-gurū pāṇi-gaṇō nivaḍaï tiri-naraya-dukkha-gahaṇammi
dukkha-paraddhō pāvaṁ kuṇamāṇō bhamaï puṇaruttaṁ // SurSuCa.144


[p. 658]
narayāō tiriyattē tiriyattāō puṇōvi narayammi
dukkha-saya-sampaüttaṁ bhava-pariyaṭṭaṁ kuṇaï jīvō // SurSuCa.145

ēvaṁ nāūṇa jaṇā rāga-ddōsāṇa vajjaṇaṁ kuṇaha
bhava-saya-kilēsa-bahulaṁ saṁsāraṁ jēṇa uttaraha // SurSuCa.146

ugginna-khaggamabalaṁ avalōiya naravaīvi vimhahiō
cintēi ahō! dhaṭṭhā majjha vahaṭṭhā iha paviṭṭhā // SurSuCa.147

lallakka-mukka-huṅkāra-puvvayaṁ thaṁmaṇīē vijjāē
thaṁmiya-dēhā jāyā nicciṭṭhā citta-muttivva // SurSuCa.148

dēvīvi vimhiya-maṇā bhaṇaï ya laliē! kimēvamāraddhaṁ
pāvē! kēṇa paüttā duṭṭhēṇaṁ ghāiyā rannō? // SurSuCa.149

rannā bhaṇiyaṁ itthīē sāhasaṁ ērisaṁ na sambhavaï
tā dēvi! kōvi duṭṭhō diṭṭhō kālēṇa purisō 'yaṁ // SurSuCa.150


[p. 659]
para-vijjā-cchēyakariṁ vijjaṁ āvāhiūṇa nara-vaïṇā
cira-kāla-sāhiyāō chinnāō tassa vijjāō // SurSuCa.151

tacchēyāō jāō payaïtthō sō pakampamāṇa-taṇū
bhaṇiyaṁ nivēṇa aṇuharaï dēvi! ēsō kumārassa // SurSuCa.152

tā nūṇaṁ sō ēsō paḍhamō tuha puttaō na annotti
taṁ suṇiya imā jāyā bhaya-lajjā-sōya-sambhantā // SurSuCa.153

tammi ya diṇammi suranandaṇāō jalakanta-santiō dūō
phuḍa-vayaṇō nāmēṇaṁ samāgaō rāya-kajjēṇa // SurSuCa.154

sō vāhariō rannā puṭṭhō kiṁ bhadda! hōi sō ēsō
sō jō piyaṁvayāē pāsē sampēsiō āsi? // SurSuCa.155

jamma-diṇē nēmittiya-vayaṇāō jāyamēttaō puttō
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa ēvaṁ ēsō mayaṇavēgotti // SurSuCa.156


[p. 660]
sōūṇa tassa vayaṇaṁ rāyā sōyāurō vicintēī
ajjavi puvva-viruddhō vaïrī paṭṭhiṁ na chaḍḍaï // SurSuCa.157

dhī! saṁsāra-sahāvō puttōvi hu dāruṇō havaï vaïrī
piccha akāraṇa-kuviō vavasaï ēyārisaṁ pāvaṁ // SurSuCa.158

mantīhiṁ samaṁmantaṁ guttaṁ kāūṇa tāṇa vayaṇēṇaṁ
kaṭṭha-harē sō chụdhō nara-vaï-hiya-purisa-kaya-rakkhō // SurSuCa.159

tatthavi kalusiya-hiyaō piya-vaha-pariṇāma-nicchaya-maīō
kōhēṇa dhamadhamantō kicchēṇaṁ gamaï diyahāiṁ // SurSuCa.160

aha annayā kayāivi pajjōsavaṇā-diṇammi sampattē
cārāgāra-nara-gaṇē visujjhamāṇē nivāṇāē // SurSuCa.161

sumaraï taṇayaṁ jēṭṭhaṁ kaṭṭha-harē saṇṭhiyaṁ nara-varindō
cintaï hā! kaṭṭhaṁ na hu juttaṁ majjha ērisayaṁ // SurSuCa.162


[p. 661]
jaïvi hu kayāvarāhō dussīlō handi! nandaṇō majjha
tahavi hu tammi niruddhē rajja-suhaṁ na pasaṁsāmi // SurSuCa.163

pajjōsavaṇāvi hu maha na ya sujjhaï tammi bandhaṇa-ṭhiyammi
iya citiūṇa mukkō pēsala-vayaṇēhiṁ ālaviō // SurSuCa.164

muñcasu putta! visāyaṁ kuṇasu pasāyaṁ kumāra-bhuttīē
dikkhāi gahaṇa-samaē niyaya-paē taṁ ṭhavissāmi // SurSuCa.165

dēsantē gāma-sayaṁ dāuṁ paccaïya-niyaya-nara-sahiō
paṭṭhaviō sōvi gaō amukka vērō niya-maṇammi // SurSuCa.166

cintēi sō kayagdhō vivihōvāēhiṁ māraṇaṁ piuṇō
rattīē lahaï niddaṁ na ya sō kūḍāiṁ cintēntō // SurSuCa.167

tattha ya pavvaya-gahaṇē pallī-pāsammi saṁvasantassa
mūlīē gavēsantō dhūma-muhō āgaō jōgī // SurSuCa.168


[p. 662]
uvayariō sō tēṇaṁ sayaṇāsaṇa-bhōyaṇāīhiṁ
tuṭṭhēṇa tēṇa dinnaṁ addissaṁ añjaṇaṁ tassa // SurSuCa.169

añjiya-lōyaṇa-juyalō addissō sō maṇēṇa cintēi
mārēmi vēriyaṁ taṁ jēṇa maṇaṁ nivvuiṁ lahaï // SurSuCa.170

ēsa maha rajja-lambhō hantavvō jaṁ piyā sa-hatthēṇa
vēriya-jaṇēṇa dinnaṁ rajjaṁ narayaṁ visēsēi // SurSuCa.171

aha sō addissa-taṇū vañciya sayalampi rakkhaṇa-narōhaṁ
āgamma gayapurammī rannō chiddaṁ palōēi // SurSuCa.172

vaccōhara-ṭṭhiō sō sarīra-cintatthamāgayaṁ piyaraṁ
maṇi-rahiyaṁ paṭṭhīē pāvō churiyāē // SurSuCa.173

duṭṭhaṁ apicchamāṇō ya nara-vaī takkhaṇēṇa nikkhantō
pabhaṇaï rumbhaha dāṁraṁ addissō acchaē kōvi // SurSuCa.174


[p. 663]
haṇa haṇa bhaṇamāṇēhiṁ kuntaggāhēhiṁ ruddha-dārammi
maraṇa-bhayāō paḍiō vēṭṭhaya kūvē mayaṇavēgō // SurSuCa.175

pāvaṁ citēi narō vēriya-lōyassa kūra-pariṇāmō
navaraṁ nivaḍaï tassēva dukkhayaṁ iyara-punnēhiṁ // SurSuCa.176

rāyāviṁ aṅgarakkhēhiṁ takkhaṇaṁ vẹ̄dhiō parūḍha-vaṇō
jāō maṇi-salilēṇaṁ siñcantō vēyaṇā-rahiō // SurSuCa.177

dēsantāō pattā bhaṇanti parirakkhagā narā dēva!
addissō hōūṇaṁ naṭṭhō mayaṇavēgō mha // SurSuCa.178

aha rāyā saṁviggō cintaï taṇayassa vilasiyaṁ ēyaṁ
jāṇantō kiṁ ajjavi nirujjamō dhamma-karaṇammi? // SurSuCa.179

bhōgāsattō jiṇa-dhamma-vajjiō kahavi jaï maō hontō
aṭṭa-jjhāṇōvagaō kā majjha gaī taō hontā? // SurSuCa.180


[p. 664]
aha annayā kayāivi vinnattō sō niutta-khayarēṇa
kusumāyarammi sūrī samāgaō cittavēgotti // SurSuCa.181

pahasiya-vayaṇō-rāyā-dāūṇaṁ pāriōsiyaṁ tassa
antaürēṇa sahiō sampattō sūri-pāsammi // SurSuCa.182

ti payakkhiṇiūṇa muṇiṁ vandaï viṇaōṇamanta-sira-kamalō
taha amarakēumāī vandiya bhattīi uvaviṭṭhō // SurSuCa.183

saṁsāruvvēyakarī rāga-ddōsāi-sattu-nimmahaṇī
saṁvēgakarī vihiyā vittharaō dēsaṇā guruṇā // SurSuCa.184

taṁ sōuṁ saṁviggō pucchaï rāyā kahēhi mē bhayavaṁ!
kiṁ vahaï vēra-bhāvaṁ maha puttō mayaṇavēgotti? // SurSuCa.185

kattha va ciṭṭhaï sampaï, pabhaṇaï sūrī suṇēhi nara-nāha!
jō sō subandhu-jīvō āsi surō kālabāṇō tē // SurSuCa.186


[p. 665]
kāuṁ vijjā-cchēyaṁ surasundarī-haraṇa-samaya-khīṇāū
uppannō vaṇa-mahisō davēṇa daḍ̣dhō maō rannē // SurSuCa.187

khaya-kimi-kulāulāē gabbhē chuhiyāē sāramēīē
jāō suṇaō tāva ya pañcama-divasē mayā jaṇaṇī // SurSuCa.188

ḍimbha-kayatthaṇa-duhiō bhukkhāi maō taōvi vippa-gihē
jāō gali-gōrahaō tōttaya-ghāēhiṁ viddaviō // SurSuCa.189

galiyattaṇa-khinnēṇaṁ dinnō vippēṇa ghañciya-varassa
tila-jantammi vahantō ahōnisiṁ dubbalō jāō // SurSuCa.190

kimi-kāya-khaïya-dēhō pāē ghasiūṇa dīharaṁ kālaṁ
gōsīsa-taru-gaṇaḍ̣dhē himavantē pannagō jāō // SurSuCa.191

ḍasiō tēṇa nara-vara! paṇhōttara-vāvaḍō saha piyāē
tuha aṅgarakkha-nihaō uppannō mayaṇavēgō sō // SurSuCa.192


[p. 666]
puvva-kaya-vēra-vasaō puttōvi vahujjaō imō tēṇa
addissō haṇaï tumaṁ so cciya vaccō-harē taïyā // SurSuCa.193

kōtakkantō bhaya-sambhamēṇa paḍiō sa vacca-kūvammi
vaccāhārō tahiyaṁva sō ṭhiō dīharaṁ kālaṁ // SurSuCa.194

asuddha-visōhaya-purisēhiṁ-dāra-pihaṇē kayāi avaṇīē
rattīē niggaō sō naṭṭhō ya bhaēṇa tuha rāya! // SurSuCa.195

pāvōdaēṇa aṇuciya-āhāra-nisēvaṇēṇa sē kōḍhaṁ
jāyaṁ vēyaṇa-paüraṁ sampaï sō bhamaï dukkhattō // SurSuCa.196

sōūṇa sūri-vayaṇaṁ saṁviggō jāya-viraï-pariṇāmō
surasundari-bīya-suyaṁ aṇaṅgakēuṁ ṭhaviya rajjē // SurSuCa.197

jiṇa-cēiyāṇa pūyaṁ kāuṁ dāūṇa viviha-dāṇāiṁ
vatthāsaṇāiēhiṁ sammāṇēūṇa muṇi-saṅghaṁ // SurSuCa.198


[p. 667]
bahu-vijjāhara-sahiō pavvaïō jāya-tivva-saṁvēgō
suha-laggē sampattē paya-mūlē cittavēgassa // SurSuCa.199

surasundarīvi sōuṁ vēra-nimittaṁ sudāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ
pavvaïyā gaṇiṇīē paya-mūlē kaṇagamālāē // SurSuCa.200

iya tinnivi miliyāō vaya-paḍivattīē puvva-bhagiṇīō
tāṇaṁ ca puvva-daïyā mittā tē tinnivi miliyā // SurSuCa.201

cittagaï-vāyagassa ō pāsē pạdhiūṇa aṅga-suttāiṁ
atthaṁ suṇēi mūlē guruṇō siri-cittavēgassa // SurSuCa.202

kālēṇa mayarakēū suttattha-visāraō mahā-sattō
pañcavihampi ya tulaṇaṁ karēi ēgāgi-paḍimaṭṭhā // SurSuCa.203

tava-bhāvaṇāē bhāviya attāṇaṁ satta-bhāvaṇabbhāsaṁ
kuṇamāṇō pēyavaṇē rattīē ṭhāi ussaggaṁ // SurSuCa.204


[p. 668]
ētthaṁrammi sūrī viharantō pāviō puriṁ campaṁ
paḍimāē mayarakēū païdiyahaṁ ṭhāi pēyavaṇē // SurSuCa.205

cittagaï-vāyagōvi ya vāyaṇa-samayammi sāhu-majjha-gaō
vigaha-pamāyāsattō hariō kēṇāvi dēvēṇa // SurSuCa.206

aha muṇiṇō vimhaïyā guruṇa sāhinti haraṇa-vuttantaṁ
uvaüttō puvva-gaē nāuṁ taṁ vaïyaraṁ sūrī // SurSuCa.207

āmantiūṇa samaṇē pavattiṇiṁ sayala-sāhuṇi-samēyaṁ
vajjaraï gurū ajjā! vajjaha vēraṁ sudūrēṇa // SurSuCa.208

jō sō mōhila-jīvō sumaṅgalō para-bhavammi ruṭṭhēṇa
dhaṇavaï-jīva-surēṇa haya-vijjō māṇusa-nagassa // SurSuCa.209

paraō mukkō taïyā hiḍantō maṇuya-virahiē rannē
ḍasiō kukkuḍa-sappēṇa sō maō bhamaï saṁsārē // SurSuCa.210


[p. 669]
nāyara-tiriya-narēsuṁ dāruṇa-dukkhāiṁ tattha aṇuhaviuṁ
siddhatthapurē jāō surahō sō kaṇagavaï-puttō // SurSuCa.211

khaya-vāhīē mayammī suggīvē nara-vaī imō jāō
takkammudayā rajjaṁ ahiṭṭhiṁyaṁ suppaïṭaṭhēṇaṁ // SurSuCa.212

rajja-bbhaṭṭhō campāē āgaō kittidhamma-nara-vaïṇā
dēsantē gāma-sayaṁ dinnaṁ sē dhūya-taṇayassa // SurSuCa.213

dunnayakārī bhīmēṇa rāiṇā kittighamma-taṇaēṇa
nivvāsiō aḍantō nivvinnō tāva-sō jāō // SurSuCa.214

kāūṇa ya bāla-tavaṁ jōisavāsī saṇiccharō jāō
sariūṇa puvva-vaïraṁ ihāgaō cittagaï-pāsē // SurSuCa.215

chiddaṁ gavēsayantō vigaha-pamattō ya vāyagō ajja
avahariuṁ pakkhittō surēṇa sō lavaṇa-jalahimmi // SurSuCa.216


[p. 670]
suha-pariṇāmō bhayavaṁ sukka-jjhāṇēṇa daḍḍha-kammaṁsō
sampaï bhava-bhaya-mukkō antagaḍō kēvalī jāō // SurSuCa.217

sōūṇa sūri-vayaṇaṁ samaṇā samaṇī ya parama-saṁviggā
tāvaya pēyavaṇāō samāgaō amarakēu muṇī // SurSuCa.218

bhaṇaï ya guru-āṇāē dhaṇadēva-juō ahaṁ tu pēyavaṇē
bhayavaṁ! gaō pahāē pāsē muṇi-mayarakēussa // SurSuCa.219

tahiyaṁ ya na sō diṭṭhō diṭṭhā ya ciyā phuranta-iṅgālā
gandhōdaga-kusuma-vāsaṁ ca nivaḍiyaṁ dīsaē tattha // SurSuCa.220

duguṇāṇiya saṁvēgō pabhaṇaï sūrīvi nāya-paramatthō
dukkhattō hiṇḍantō ihāgaō mayaṇavēgō sō // SurSuCa.221

pēyavaṇē paḍimatthaṁ piyaraṁ daṭṭhaṇa cintaē pāvō
iṇhiṁ karēmi sahalaṁ niya-jamma-vēriyaṁ hantuṁ // SurSuCa.222


[p. 671]
dāruya-bhariyaṁ sagaḍaṁ bhaggaṁ mōttūṇa tattha sāgaḍiō
ussūranti païṭṭhō vasamē ghittūṇa nayarīē // SurSuCa.223

jāē tamandhayāraṁ tahi ō kaṭṭhēṁhiṁ tēṁṇa pāvēṇa
pacchāiūṇa daḍ̣dhō cīyā-jalaṇēṇa sō sāhū // SurSuCa.224

dēhaṁ sa dahaï sihī sukka-jjhāṇēṇa sōvi kammāiṁ
avicala-cittō bhayavaṁ antagaḍō kēvalī jāō // SurSuCa.225

ēvaṁ samullavantassa sūriṇō ullasanta-viriyassa
khaviē kamma-caükkē uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ // SurSuCa.226

taha amarakēu-muṇiṇō dhaṇadēva-jaïssa kaṇagamālāē
kamalāvaï-surasundari-piyaṅguvaramañjarīē ya // SurSuCa.227

suha-bhāvāṇamimāṇaṁ uppaṇṇaṁ kēvalaṁ varaṁ nāṇaṁ
dēvēhiṁ kayā mahimā mōkkhaṁ pattāṇi kālēṇa // SurSuCa.228


[p. 672]
pāvēṇa mayaṇavēgō bhamihī saṁsāra-sāyaramaṇantaṁ
tā bhō bhavvā! ujjhaha rāga-ddōsē mahā-sattū // SurSuCa.229

ittha ya kahā samappaï surasundari-nāmiyā purā bhaṇiyā
rāga-ddōsē-vimukkaṁ paṇamaha bhatīi jiṇaïndaṁ // SurSuCa.230

nicca-palōyaṇa-nirayā taggaya-cittā vimukka-vāvārā
attha-payāṇa-rahiyā jāsiṁ vayaṇampi na lahanti // SurSuCa.231

niya-attha-payāṇēvi hu rasa-rahiyāō na dinti sabbhāvaṁ
paramattha-virahiyāṇaṁ annattha-nibaddha-cinnāō // SurSuCa.232

tāsu vara-vēsiyāsuva suvanna-rayaṇucchalanta-sōhāsu
bahala-niratara-vannaya-sañjāya-sarīra-sōhāsu // SurSuCa.233

āsattaṁ suviyaḍ̣dhāṇa māṇasaṁ jaïvi aṇudiṇaṁ nūṇaṁ
tahavi hu maha vinnattiṁ suṇantu iha sajjaṇā saralā // SurSuCa.234


[p. 673]
niralaṅkārācchandāṇuvattiṇī laliya-kōmala-sarīrā
dāliddiya-vara-kula-bāliyavva ēsā kahā tumha // SurSuCa.235

uvaṇīyā suyaṇāṇaṁ annāsattāvi vārayaṁ dāuṁ
aviyaḍạdhāvi viyaḍ̣dhā jaha hōi tahā jaïjjāha // SurSuCa.236

āsi jiṇō jaya-bandhū titthayarō vaddhamāṇa-nāmotti
saṁsāra-jalahi-majjanta-jantu-jaṇa-jāṇavatta-samō // SurSuCa.237

sīsō tassa suhammō tattō jambū taō ya pabhavotti
ēvaṁ sūrīṇa paramparāē tā jāva vaïrotti // SurSuCa.238

sāhāē tassa sūrī jiṇēsarō nāma āsi vikkhāō
tattō ya nimmala-guṇō ujjhāō allaō nāma // SurSuCa.239

sīsō ya tassa sūrī sūrōvva sayāvi jaṇiya-dōsantō
āsi siri-vaddhamāṇō pavaḍḍhamāṇō guṇa-sirīē // SurSuCa.240


[p. 674]
rāgō ya jassa dhammē āsi paōsō ya jassa pāvammi
tullō ya mitta-sattusu tassa ya jāyā duvē sīsā // SurSuCa.241

duvvāra-vāi-vāraṇa-maraṭṭa-niṭṭavaṇa-niṭṭhura-maïndō
jiṇa-bhaṇiya-suddha-siddhanta-dēsaṇā-karaṇa-tallicchō // SurSuCa.242

jassa ya aīva-sulaliya-paya-sañcārā pasanna-vāṇīyā
aïkōmalā silēsē vivihālaṅkāra-sōhillā // SurSuCa.243

līlāvaïtti-nāmā suvanna-rayaṇōha-hāri-sayalaṅgā
vēsavva-kahā viyaraï jayammi kaya-jaṇa-maṇāṇandā // SurSuCa.244

ēgā tāṇa jiṇēsara-sūrī sūrōvva ukkaḍa-payāvō
tassa siri buddhisāgarasūrī ya sahōyarō bīō // SurSuCa.245

punnaṁ-saradindu-sundara-niya-jasa-pabbhāra-bhariya-bhuvaṇa-yalō
jiṇa-bhaṇiya-sattha-paramāttha-vittharāsatta-suha-cittō // SurSuCa.246


[p. 675]
jassa ya muha-kuharāō viṇiggayā attha-vāri-sōhillā
buha-cakkavāya-kaliyā raṅganta-suphakkiya-taraṅgā // SurSuCa.247

taḍaruha-avasadda-mahīruhōha-ummūlaṇammi susamatthā
ajjhāya-pavara-titthā-pañcagganthī naī pavarā // SurSuCa.248

tēsiṁ sīsa-varō dhaṇēsara-muṇī ēyaṁ kahaṁ pāyaḍaṁcaḍḍāvalli-purī-ṭhiō sa-guruṇō āṇāē pāḍhantarā
kāsī vikkama-vaccharammi ya gaē bāṇaṅka-sunnōḍupēmāsē bhaddavaē gurummi kasiṇē bīyā-dhaṇiṭṭhā-diṇē // SurSuCa.249

sāhu-dhaṇēsara-viraïya-subōha-gāhā-samūha-rammāē
rāgaggi-dōsa-visahara-pasamaṇa-jala-manta-bhūyāē // SurSuCa.250

ēsōvi puvva-sūiya-nivvāṇa-vihāṇa-vannaṇō nāma
surasundarī kahāē sōlasamō iha paricchēō // SurSuCa.251
